the PLUMED SERPENT 

 

 by 

 

 D. H. Lawrence 

 
 CHAPTER I 

 beginning of a bull - fight 

 

 it be the Sunday after Easter , and the last bull - fight of the season in Mexico City . four special bull have be bring over from Spain for the occasion , since spanish bull be more fiery than Mexican . perhaps it be the altitude , perhaps just the spirit of the western continent which be to blame for the lack of ' pep ' , as Owen put it , in the native animal . 

 although Owen , who be a great socialist , disapprove of bull - fight , ' we have never see one . we shall have to go , ' he say . 

 ' oh yes , I think we must see it , ' say Kate . 

 ' and it be our last chance , ' say Owen . 

 away he rush to the place where they sell ticket , to book seat , and Kate go with he . as she come into the street , her heart sink . it be as if some little person inside she be sulk and resist . neither she nor Owen speak much spanish , there be a fluster at the ticket place , and an unpleasant individual come forward to talk American for they . 

 it be obvious they ought to buy ticket for the ' Shade . ' but they want to economize , and Owen say he prefer to sit among the crowd , therefore , against the resistance of the ticket man and the onlooker , they buy reserve seat in the ' Sun . ' 

 the show be on Sunday afternoon . all the tram - car and the frightful little Ford omnibus call camion be label Torero , and be surge away towards Chapultepec . Kate feel that sudden dark feeling , that she do not   want to go . 

 ' I be not very keen on go , ' she say to Owen . 

 ' oh , but why not ? I do not   believe in they on principle , but we have   never see one , so we shall have to go . ' 

 Owen be an American , Kate be irish . ' never have see one ' mean ' have to go . ' but it be american logic rather than irish , and Kate only let herself be overcome . 

 villier of course be keen . but then he too be american , and he too have never see one , and be young , more than anybody he have to go . 

 they get into a Ford taxi and go . the bust car career away down the wide dismal street of asphalt and stone and Sunday dreariness . stone building in Mexico have a peculiar hard , dry dreariness . 

 the taxi draw up in a side street under the big iron scaffolding of the stadium . in the gutter , rather lousy man be sell pulque and sweet , cake , fruit , and greasy food . crazy motorcar rush up and hobble away . little soldier in wash - out cotton uniform , pinky drab , hang around an entrance . above all loom the network iron frame of the huge , ugly stadium . 

 Kate feel she be go to prison . but Owen excitedly surge to the entrance that correspond to his ticket . in the depth of he , he too do not   want to go . but he be a bear American , and if anything be on show , he have to see it . that be ' life . ' 

 the man who take the ticket at the entrance , suddenly , as they be pass in , stand in front of Owen , put both his hand on Owen 's chest , and paw down the front of Owen 's body . Owen start , bridle , transfix for a moment . the fellow stand aside . Kate remain petrified . 

 then Owen jerk into a smile composure as the man wave they on . ' feel for fire - arm ! ' he say , roll his eye with pleased excitement at Kate . 

 but she have not get over the shock of horror , fear the fellow might paw she . 

 they emerge out of a tunnel in the hollow of the concrete - and - iron amphitheatre . a real gutter - lout come to look at their counterslip , to see which seat they have book . he jerk his head downwards , and slouch off . now Kate know she be in a trap - a big concrete beetle trap . 

 they drop down the concrete step till they be only three tier from the bottom . that be their row . they be to sit on the concrete , with a loop of thick iron between each numbered seat . this be a reserved place in the ' Sun . ' 

 Kate sit gingerly between her two iron loop , and look vaguely around . 

 ' I think it be thrill ! ' she say . 

 like most modern people , she have a will - to - happiness . 

 ' be not   it thrill ? ' cry Owen , whose will - to - happiness be almost a mania . ' do not   you think so , Bud ? ' 

 ' why , yes , I think it may be , ' say Villiers , non - committal . 

 but then Villiers be young , he be only over twenty , while Owen be over forty . the young generation calculate its ' happiness ' in a more business - like fashion . villier be out after a thrill , but he be not   go to say he would get one till he would get it . Kate and Owen - Kate be also nearly forty - must enthuse a thrill , out of a sort of politeness to the great Show - man , Providence . 

 ' look here ! ' say Owen . ' supposing we try to protect our extremity on this concrete - ' and thoughtfully he fold his rain - coat and lay it along the concrete ledge so that both he and Kate could sit on it . 

 they sit and gaze around . they be early . patch of people mottle the concrete slope opposite , like eruption . the ring just below be vacant , neatly sand ; and above the ring , on the encircle concrete , great advertisement for hat , with a picture of a city - man 's straw hat , and advertisement for spectacle , with pair of spectacle supinely fold , glare and shout . 

 ' where be the " Shade " then ? ' say Owen , twist his neck . 

 at the top of the amphitheatre , near the sky , be concrete box . this be the ' Shade ' , where anybody who be anything sit . 

 ' oh but , ' say Kate , ' I do not   want to be perch right up there , so far away . ' 

 ' why no ! ' say Owen . ' we be much well where we be , in our " Sun " , which be not   go to shine a great deal after all . ' 

 the sky be cloudy , prepare for the rainy season . 

 it be nearly three o'clock in the afternoon , and the crowd be fill in , but still only occupy patch of the bare concrete . the low tier be reserve , so the bulk of the people sit in the mid - way level , and gentry like our trio be more or less isolated . 

 but the audience be already a mob , mostly of fattish town man in black tight suit and little straw hat , and a mixing - in of the dark - face labourer in big hat . the man in black suit be probably employee and clerk and factory hand . some have bring their woman , in sky - blue chiffon with brown chiffon hat and face powder to look like white marshmallow . some be family with two or three child . 

 the fun begin . the game be to snatch the hard straw hat off some fellow 's head , and send it skim away down the slope of humanity , where some smart bounder down below would catch it and send it skim across in another direction . there be shout of jeer pleasure from the mass , which rise almost to a yell as seven straw hat be skimming , meteor - like , at one moment across the slope of people . 

 ' look at that ! ' say Owen . ' be not   that fun ! ' 

 ' no , ' say Kate , her little alter ego speak out for once , in spite of her will - to - happiness . ' no , I do not   like it . I really hate common people . ' 

 as a socialist , Owen disapprove , and as a happy man , he be disconcert . because his own real self , as far as he have any left , hat common rowdiness just as much as Kate do . 

 ' it be awfully smart though ! ' he say , try to laugh in sympathy with the mob . ' there now , see that ! ' 

 ' yes , it be quite smart , but I be glad it be not my hat , ' say villier . 

 ' oh , it be all in the game , ' say Owen largely . 

 but he be uneasy . he be wear a big straw hat of native make , conspicuous in the comparative isolation of the low tier . after a lot of fidgeting , he take off this hat and put it on his knee . but unfortunately he have a very definitely bald spot on a sunburnt head . 

 behind , above , sit a dense patch of people in the unreserved section . already they be throw thing . Bum ! come an orange , aim at Owen 's bald spot , and hit he on the shoulder . he glare round rather ineffectually through his big shell spectacle . 

 ' I would keep my hat on if I be you , ' say the cold voice of Villiers . 

 ' yes , I think perhaps it be wise , ' say Owen , with assumed nonchalance , put on his hat again . 

 Whereupon a banana skin rattle on Villiers ' tidy and ladylike little panama . he glare round coldly , like a bird that would stab with its beak if it get the chance , but which would fly away at the first real menace . 

 ' how I detest they ! ' say Kate . 

 a diversion be create by the entrance , opposite , of the military band , with their silver and brass instrument under their arm . there be three set . the chief band climb and sit on the right , in the big bare tract of concrete reserve for the Authorities . these musician wear dark grey uniform trim with rose colour , and make Kate feel almost reassure , as if it be Italy and not Mexico City . a silver band in pale buff uniform sit opposite our party , high up across the hollow distance , and still a third ' música ' thread away to the left , on the remote scatter hillside of the amphitheatre . the newspaper have say that the President would attend . but the president be scarce at bull - fight in Mexico , nowadays . 

 there sit the band , in as much pomp as they could muster , but they do not begin to play . great crowd now patch the slope , but there be still bare tract , especially in the Authorities ' section . only a little distance above Kate 's row be a mass of people , as it be impend ; a very uncomfortable sensation . 

 it be three o'clock , and the crowd have a new diversion . the band , due to strike up at three , still sit there in lordly fashion , sound not a note . 

 ' La música ! La música ! ' shout the mob , with the voice of mob authority . they be the People , and the revolution have be their revolution , and they have win they all . the band be their band , present for their amusement . 

 but the band be military band , and it be the army which have win all the revolution . so the revolution be their revolution , and they be present for their own glory alone . 

 Música pagada toca mal tono . 

 spasmodically , the insolent yelling of the mob rise and subside . La música ! La música ! the shout become brutal and violent . Kate always remember it . La música ! the band peacocke its nonchalance . the shouting be a great yell : the degenerate mob of Mexico City ! 

 at length , at its own leisure , the band in grey with dark rose facing strike up : crisp , martial , smart . 

 ' that be fine ! ' say Owen . ' but that be really good ! and it be the first time I have   hear a good band in Mexico , a band with any backbone . ' 

 the music be smart , but it be brief . the band seem scarcely to have start , when the piece be over . the musician take their instrument from their mouth with a gesture of dismissal . they play just to say they would play , make it as short as possible . 

 Música pagada toca mal tono . 

 there be a ragged interval , then the silver band pip up . and at last it be half - past three , or more . 

 Whereupon , at some give signal , the mass in the middle , unreserved seat suddenly burst and rush down on to the low , reserved seat . it be a crash like a burst reservoir , and the populace in black Sunday suit pour down round and about our astonished , frightened trio . and in two minute it be over . without any pushing or shove . everybody careful , as far as possible , not to touch anybody else . you do not   elbow your neighbour if he be get a pistol on his hip and a knife at his belly . so all the seat in the low tier fill in one rush , like the flowing of water . 

 Kate now sit among the crowd . but her seat , fortunately , be above one of the track - way that go round the arena , so at least she would not have anybody sit between her knee . 

 man go uneasily back and forth along this gangway past the foot , want to get in next their friend , but never venture to ask . three seat away , on the same row , sit a polish bolshevist fellow who have meet Owen . he lean over and ask the Mexican next to Owen if he might change seat with he . ' no , ' say the Mexican . ' I will sit in my own seat . ' 

 ' Muy bien , Señor , muy bien ! ' say the Pole . 

 the show do not begin , and man like lose mongrel still prowl back and forth on the track that be next step down from Kate 's foot . they begin to take advantage of the ledge on which rest the foot of our party , to squat there . 

 down sit a heavy fellow , plumb between Owen 's knee . 

 ' I hope they will not   sit on my foot , ' say Kate anxiously . 

 ' we will not   let they , ' say villier , with bird - like decision . ' why do not   you shove he off , Owen ? shove he off ? ' 

 and villier glare at the mexican fellow ensconce between Owen 's leg . Owen flush , and laugh uncomfortably . he be not good at shove people off . the Mexican begin to look round at the three angry white people . 

 and in another moment , another fat Mexican in a black suit and a little black hat be lower himself into villier ' foot - space . but villier be too quick for he . he quickly bring his foot together under the man 's sink posterior , so the individual subside uncomfortably on to a pair of boot , and at the same time feel a hand shove he quietly but determinedly on the shoulder . 

 ' no ! ' villier be say in good American . ' this place be for my foot ! get off ! you get off ! ' 

 and he continue , quietly but very emphatically , to push the Mexican 's shoulder , to remove he . 

 the Mexican half raise himself , and look round murderously at villier . physical violence be be offer , and the only retort be death . but the young American 's face be so cold and abstract , only the eye show a primitive , bird - like fire , that the Mexican be nonplus . and Kate 's eye be blaze with irish contempt . 

 the fellow struggle with his mexican city - breed inferiority complex . he mutter an explanation in Spanish that he be only sit there for a moment , till he could join his friend - wave a hand towards a low tier . villier do not understand a word , but he reiterate : 

 ' I do not   care what it be . this place be for my foot , and you do not   sit there . ' 

 oh , home of liberty ! oh , land of the free ! which of these two man be to win in the struggle for conflicting liberty ? be the fat fellow free to sit between villier ' foot , or be villier free to keep his foot - space ? 

 there be all sort of inferiority complex , and the city Mexican have a very strong sort , that make he all the more aggressive , once it be rouse . therefore the intruder lower his posterior with a heavy , sudden bounce on villier ' foot , and villier , out of very distaste , have have to extricate his foot from such a compression . the young man 's face go white at the nostril , and his eye take on that bright abstract look of pure democratic anger . he push the fat shoulder more decisively , repeat : 

 ' go away ! go away ! you be not to sit there . ' 

 the Mexican , on his own ground , and heavy on his own base , let himself be shove , oblivious . 

 ' Insolence ! ' say Kate loudly . ' insolence ! ' 

 she glare at the fat back in the shoddily - fitting black coat , which look as if a woman dressmaker have make it , with loathing . how could any man 's coat - collar look so homemade , so en famille ! 

 villier remain with a fix , abstract look on his thin face , rather like a death 's head . all his American will be summon up , the bald eagle of the north bristling in every feather . the fellow should not sit there . - but how to remove he ? 

 the young man sit tense with will to annihilate his beetle - like intruder , and Kate use all her irish malice to help he . 

 ' do not   you wonder who be his tailor ? ' she ask , with a flicker in her voice . 

 villier look at the femalish black coat of the Mexican , and make an arch grimace at Kate . 

 ' I should say he have not   one . perhaps do it himself . ' 

 ' very likely ! ' Kate laugh venomously . 

 it be too much . the man get up and betook himself , rather diminish , to another spot . 

 ' Triumph ! ' say Kate . ' can not   you do the same , Owen ? ' 

 Owen laugh uncomfortably , glance down at the man between his knee as he might glance at a dog with rabie , when it have its back to he . 

 ' apparently not yet , unfortunately , ' he say , with some constraint , turn his nose away again from the Mexican , who be use he as a sort of chair - back . 

 there be an exclamation . two horseman in gay uniform and bear long staff have suddenly ride into the ring . they go round the arena , then take up their post , sentry - wise , on either side the tunnel entrance through which they have come in . 

 in march a little column of four toreador wear tight uniform plaster with silver embroidery . they divide , and march smartly in opposite direction , two and two , around the ring , till they come to the place face the section of the Authorities , where they make their salute . 

 so this be a bull - fight ! Kate already feel a chill of disgust . 

 in the seat of the Authorities be very few people , and certainly no sparkling lady in high tortoise - shell comb and lace mantilla . a few common - look people , bourgeois with not much taste , and a couple of officer in uniform . the President have not come . 

 there be no glamour , no charm . a few commonplace people in an expanse of concrete be the elect , and below , four grotesque and effeminate - look fellow in tight , ornate clothe be the hero . with their rather fat posterior and their squiff of pigtail and their clean - shaven face , they look like eunuchs , or woman in tight pant , these precious toreador . 

 the last of Kate 's illusion concern bull - fight come down with a flop . these be the darling of the mob ! these be the gallant toreador ! gallant ? just about as gallant as assistant in a butcher 's shop . Lady - killers ? Ugh ! 

 there be an ah ! of satisfaction from the mob . into the ring suddenly rush a smallish , dun - colour bull with long flourish horn . he run out , blindly , as if from the dark , probably think that now he be free . then he stop short , see he be not free , but surround in an unknown way . he be utterly at a loss . 

 a toreador come forward and switch out a pink cloak like a fan not far from the bull 's nose . the bull give a playful little prance , neat and pretty , and charge mildly on the cloak . the toreador switch the cloak over the animal 's head , and the neat little bull trot on round the ring , look for a way to get out . 

 see the wooden barrier around the arena , find he be able to look over it , he think he might as well take the leap . so over he go into the corridor or passage - way which circle the ring , and in which stand the servant of the arena . 

 just as nimbly , these servant vault over the barrier into the arena , that be now bull - less . 

 the bull in the gangway trot inquiringly round till he come to an opening on to the arena again . so back he trot into the ring . 

 and back into the gangway vault the servant , where they stand again to look on . 

 the bull trot waveringly and somewhat irritated . the toreador wave their cloak at he , and he swerve on . till his vague course take he to where one of the horseman with lance sit motionless on his horse . 

 instantly , in a pang of alarm , Kate notice that the horse be thickly blindfold with a black cloth . yes , and so be the horse on which sit the other picador . 

 the bull trot suspiciously up to the motionless horse bear the rider with the long pole ; a lean old horse that would never move till Doomsday , unless someone shove it . 

 o shade of Don Quixote ! oh four spanish horseman of the Apocalypse ! this be surely one of they . 

 the picador pull his feeble horse round slowly , to face the bull , and slowly he lean forward and shove his lance - point into the bull 's shoulder . the bull , as if the horse be a great wasp that have sting he deep , suddenly lower his head in a jerk of surprise and lift his horn straight up into the horse 's abdomen . and without more ado , over go horse and rider , like a tottering monument upset . 

 the rider scramble from under the horse and go run away with his lance . the old horse , in complete daze amazement , struggle to rise , as if overcome with dumb incomprehension . and the bull , with a red place on his shoulder well a trickle of dark blood , stand look around in equally hopeless amazement . 

 but the wound be hurt . he see the queer sight of the horse half rear from the ground , try to get to its foot . and he smell blood and bowel . 

 so rather vaguely , as if not quite know what he ought to do , the bull once more lower his head and push his sharp , flourish horn in the horse 's belly , work they up and down inside there with a sort of vague satisfaction . 

 Kate have never be take so completely by surprise in all her life . she have still cherish some idea of a gallant show . and before she know where she be , she be watch a bull whose shoulder trickle blood gore his horn up and down inside the belly of a prostrate and feebly plunge old horse . 

 the shock almost overpower she . she have come for a gallant show . this she have pay to see . human cowardice and beastliness , a smell of blood , a nauseous whiff of bursten bowel ! she turn her face away . 

 when she look again , it be to see the horse feebly and dazedly walk out of the ring , with a great ball of its own entrail hang out of its abdomen and swing reddish against its own leg as it automatically move . 

 and once more , the shock of amazement almost make her lose consciousness . she hear the confused small applause of amusement from the mob . and that Pole , to whom Owen have introduce she , lean over and say to she , in horrible English : 

 ' now , Miss Leslie , you be see Life ! now you will have something to write about , in your letter to England . ' 

 she look at his unwholesome face in complete repulsion , and wish Owen would not introduce she to such sordid individual . 

 she look at Owen . his nose have a sharp look , like a little boy who may make himself sick , but who be watch at the shamble with all his eye , know it be forbid . 

 villier , the young generation , look intense and abstract , get the sensation . he would not even feel sick . he be just get the thrill of it , without emotion , coldly and scientifically , but very intent . 

 and Kate feel a real pang of hatred against this americanism which be coldly and unscrupulously sensational . 

 ' why do not   the horse move ? why do not   it run away from the bull ? ' she ask in repel amazement , of Owen . 

 Owen clear his throat . 

 ' do not   you see ? it be blindfold , ' he say . 

 ' but can not   it smell the bull ? ' she ask . 

 ' apparently not . - they bring the old wreck here to finish they off . - I know it be awful , but it be part of the game . ' 

 how Kate hat phrase like ' part of the game . ' what do they mean , anyhow ! she feel utterly humiliate , crush by a sense of human indecency , cowardice of two - legged humanity . in this ' brave ' show she feel nothing but reek cowardice . her breeding and her natural pride be outraged . 

 the ring servant have clean away the mess and spread new sand . the toreador be play with the bull , unfurl their foolish cloak at arm 's length . and the animal , with the red sore run on his shoulder , foolishly caper and run from one rag to the other , here and there . 

 for the first time , a bull seem to she a fool . she have always be afraid of bull , fear temper with reverence of the great Mithraic beast . and now she see how stupid he be , in spite of his long horn and his massive maleness . blindly and stupidly he run at the rag , each time , and the toreador skip like fat - hippe girl show off . probably it need skill and courage , but it look silly . 

 blindly and foolishly the bull run duck its horn each time at the rag , just because the rag flutter . 

 ' run at the man , idiot ! ' say Kate aloud , in her overwrought impatience . ' run at the man , not at the cloak . ' 

 ' they never do , be not   it curious ! ' reply Villiers , with cool scientific interest . ' they say no toreador will face a cow , because a cow always go for he instead of the cloak . if a bull do that there would be no bull - fight . imagine it ! ' 

 she be bore now . the nimbleness and the skip trick of the toreador bore she . even when one of the banderillero rear himself on tiptoe , his plump posterior much in evidence , and from his erectness push two razor - sharp dart with frill at the top into the bull 's shoulder , neatly and smartly , Kate feel no admiration . one of the dart fall out , anyway , and the bull run on with the other swinging and waggle in another bleed place . 

 the bull now want to get away , really . he leap the fence again , quickly , into the attendant ' gangway . the attendant vault over into the arena . the bull trot in the corridor , then nicely leap back . the attendant vault once more into the corridor . the bull trot round the arena , ignore the toreador , and leap once more into the gangway . over vault the attendant . 

 Kate be begin to be amuse , now that the mongrel man be skip for safety . 

 the bull be in the ring again , run from cloak to cloak , foolishly . a banderillero be get ready with two more dart . but at first another picador put nobly forward on his blindfold old horse . the bull ignore this little lot too , and trot away again , as if all the time look for something , excitedly look for something . he stand still and excitedly paw the ground , as if he want something . a toreador advance and swing a cloak . up prance the bull , tail in air , and with a prancing bind charge - upon the rag , of course . the toreador skip round with a ladylike skip , then trip to another point . very pretty ! 

 the bull , in the course of his trotting and prance and pawing , have once more come near the bold picador . the bold picador shove forward his ancient steed , lean forwards , and push the point of his lance in the bull 's shoulder . the bull look up , irritated and arrest . what the devil ! 

 he see the horse and rider . the horse stand with that feeble monumentality of a milk horse , patient as if between the shaft , wait while his master deliver the milk . how strange it must have be to he when the bull , give a little bound like a dog , duck its head and dive its horn upwards into his belly , roll he over with his rider as one might push over a hat - stand . 

 the bull look with irritable wonder at the incomprehensible medley of horse and rider kick on the ground a few yard away from he . he draw near to investigate . the rider scramble out and bolt . and the toreador , run up with their cloak , draw off the bull . he go caracole round , charge at more silk - line rag . 

 meanwhile an attendant have get the horse on its foot again , and be lead it totteringly into the gangway and round to the exit , under the Authorities . the horse crawl slowly . the bull , run from pink cloak to red cloak , rag to rag , and never catch anything , be get excite , impatient of the rag game . he jump once more into the gangway and start run , alas , on towards where the wound horse be still limp its way to the exit . 

 Kate know what be come . before she could look away , the bull have charge on the limping horse from behind , the attendant have flee , the horse be up - end absurdly , one of the bull 's horn between his hind leg and deep in his inside . down go the horse , collapse in front , but his rear be still heave up , with the bull 's horn work vigorously up and down inside he , while he lie on his neck all twist . and a huge heap of bowel come out . and a nauseous stench . and the cry of pleased amusement among the crowd . 

 this pretty event take place on Kate 's side of the ring , and not far from where she sit , below she . Most of the people be on their foot crane to look down over the edge to watch the conclusion of this delightful spectacle . 

 Kate know if she see any more she would go into hysteric . she be get beside herself . 

 she look swiftly at Owen , who look like a guilty boy spellbound . 

 ' I be go ! ' she say , rise . 

 ' go ! ' he cry , in wonder and dismay , his flushed face and his bald flushed forehead a picture , look up at she . 

 but she have already turn , and be hurry away towards the mouth of the exit - tunnel . 

 Owen come run after she , fluster , and draw in all direction . 

 ' really go ! ' he say in chagrin , as she come to the high , vaulted exit - tunnel . 

 ' I must . I have   get to get out , ' she cry . ' do not   you come . '

 the scene be create a very hostile attitude in the audience . to leave the bull - fight be a national insult . 

 ' do not   come ! really ! I shall take a tram - car , ' she say hurriedly . 

 ' really ! do you think you will be all right ? ' 

 ' perfectly . you stay . good - bye ! I can not   smell any more of this stink . ' 

 he turn like Orpheus look back into hell , and wavering make towards his seat again . 

 it be not so easy , because many people be now on their foot and crowd to the exit vault . the rain which have sputter a few drop suddenly fall in a downward splash . People be crowd to shelter ; but Owen , unheeding , fight his way back to his seat , and sit in his rain - coat with the rain pour on his bald head . he be as nearly in hysteric as Kate . but he be convince that this be life . he be see life , and what can an American do more ! 

 ' they might just as well sit and enjoy somebody else 's diarrhoea ' be the thought that pass through Kate 's distracted but still irish mind . 

 there she be in the great concrete archway under the stadium , with the lousy press of the audience crowd in after she . face outward , she see the straight downpour of the rain , and a little beyond , the great wooden gate that open to the free street . oh to be out , to be out of this , to be free ! 

 but it be pour tropical rain . the little shoddy soldier be press back under the brick gateway , for shelter . and the gate be almost shut . perhaps they would not let she out . oh horror ! 

 she stand hover in front of the straight downpour . she would have dash out , but for the restraining thought of what she would look like when her thin gauze dress be plaster to her body by drench rain . on the brink she hover . 

 behind she , from the inner end of the stadium tunnel , the people be surge in in wave . she stand horrified and alone , look always out to freedom . the crowd be in a state of excitement , cut off in its sport , on tenterhook lest it should miss anything . thank goodness the bulk stay near the inner end of the vault . she hover near the outer end , ready to bolt at any moment . 

 the rain crash steadily down . 

 she wait on the outer verge , as far from the people as possible . her face have that draw , blank look of a woman near hysteric . she could not get out of her eye the last picture of the horse lie twist on its neck with its hindquarter hitch up and the horn of the bull goring slowly and rhythmically in its vital . the horse so utterly passive and grotesque . and all its bowel slip on to the ground . 

 but a new terror be the throng inside the tunnel entrance . the big arched place be fill up , but still the crowd do not come very near she . they press towards the inner exit . 

 they be mostly loutish man in city clothe , the mongrel man of a mongrel city . two man stand make water against the wall , in the interval of their excitement . one father have kindly bring his little boy to the show , and stand in fat , sloppy , paternal benevolence above they . they be pale mite , the eld about ten year old , highly dress up in Sunday clothe . and badly they need protect from that paternal benevolence , for they be oppress , peak , and a bit wan from the horror . to those child at least bull - fight do not come natural , but would be an acquire taste . there be other child , however , and fat mamma in black satin that be greasy and grey at the edge with an overflow of face - powder . these fat mamma have a please , excited look in their eye , almost sexual , and very distasteful in contrast to their soft passive body . 

 Kate shiver a little in her thin frock , for the ponderous rain have a touch of ice . she star through the curtain of water at the big rickety gate of the enclosure surround the amphitheatre , at the midget soldier cower in their shoddy , pink - white cotton uniform , and at the glimpse of the squalid street outside , now run with dirty brown stream . the vendor have all take refuge , in dirty - white cluster , in the pulque shop , one of which be sinisterly name : a ver que sale . 

 she be afraid more of the repulsiveness than of anything . she have be in many city of the world , but Mexico have an underlying ugliness , a sort of squalid evil , which make Naples seem debonair in comparison . she be afraid , she dread the thought that anything might really touch she in this town , and give she the contagion of its crawl sort of evil . but she know that the one thing she must do be to keep her head . 

 a little officer in uniform , wear a big , pale - blue cape , make his way through the crowd . he be short , dark , and have a little black beard like an imperial . he come through the people from the inner entrance , and clear his way with a quiet , silent unobtrusiveness , yet with the peculiar heavy indian momentum . even touch the crowd delicately with his gloved hand , and murmur almost inaudibly the Con permiso ! formula , he seem to be keep himself mile away from contact . he be brave too : because there be just the chance some lout might shoot he because of his uniform . the people know he too .  ' oh really ! '

 ' yes indeed ! ' say the General . 

 there be a pause . 

 ' and the gentleman who be with you , they be - ? '

 ' ah Americans ! ah yes ! '

 ' Owen Rhys ! ah yes ! I think I see in the newspaper you be here in town - visit Mexico . '

 she tell he a time , and add :

I do think Mexico City be evil , underneath . '

 CHAPTER II 

 Tea - party in Tlacolula 

 

 Owen come back to the hotel at about half - past six , tired , excited , a little guilty , and a good deal distress at have let Kate go alone . and now the whole thing be over , rather dreary in spirit .

 ' I get on perfectly . go to Sanborn 's for tea , and have strawberry shortcake - so good ! '

I have such awful qualm after I would let you go . imagine all the thing that be suppose to happen in Mexico - chauffeur drive away with you into some horrible remote region , and rob you and all that - but then I know really you would be all right . oh , the time I have - the rain ! - and the people throw thing at my bald patch - and those horse - be not   that horrible ? - I wonder I be still alive . ' and he laugh with tired excitement , put his hand over his stomach and roll his eye . 

 ' be not   you drench ? ' she say . 

 ' drench ! ' he reply . ' or at least I be . I have   dry off quite a lot . my rain - coat be no good - I do not   know why I do not   buy another . oh , but what a time ! the rain stream on my bald head , and the crowd behind throw orange at it . then simply gore in my inside about let you go alone . yet it be the only bull - fight I shall ever see . I come then before it be over . Bud would not   come . I suppose he be still there . '

' Plucky ! they with all their knife and their spear and cloak and dart - and they know just how a bull will behave . it be just a performance of human being torture animal , with those common fellow show off , how smart they be at hurt a bull . dirty little boy maim fly - that be what they be . only grown - up , they be bastard , not boy . oh , I wish I could be a bull , just for five minute . Bastard , that be what I call it ! '

Greedy even for the most sordid sensation . 

 whereas she feel as if she have eat something which be give her ptomaine poisoning . if that be life ! 

 ah man , man ! they all have this soft rottenness of the soul , a strange perversity which make even the squalid , repulsive thing seem part of life to they . life ! and what be life ? a louse lie on its back and kicking ? Ugh ! 

 at about seven o'clock Villiers come tap . he look wan , peak , but like a bird that have successfully peck a bellyful of garbage .

 villier disappear with a wicked little laugh . and as she sit her hand tremble with outrage and passion . a - moral ! how could one be a - moral , or non - moral , when one 's soul be revolt ! how could one be like these Americans , pick over the garbage of sensation , and gobble it up like carrion bird ! at the moment , both Owen and Villiers seem to she like carrion bird , repulsive .

 Kate remember the little General ; he be a good deal small than herself . she remember his erect , alert little figure , something birdlike , and the face with eye slant under arched eyebrow , and the little black tuft of an imperial on the chin : a face with a peculiar chinese suggestion , without be chinese in the least , really . an odd , detach , yet cocky little man , a true little Indian , speak Oxford English in a rapid , low , musical voice , with extraordinarily gentle intonation . yet those black , inhuman eye !

 but it have annoy Kate to see this General and this woman eat chicken and asparagus and jelly in the Pullman , pay fifteen peso for a rather poor dinner , when for a peso - and - a - half apiece they could have eat a well meal , and real Mexican , at the meal - stop station . and all the poor , barefoot people clamour on the platform , while the ' General ' , who be a man of their own sort , nobly swallow his asparagus on the other side of the window - pane .

 be rather late , Owen and Kate bump out to Tlacolula in a Ford taxi . it be a long way , a long way through the peculiar squalid ending of the town , then along the straight road between tree , into the valley . the sun of April be brilliant , there be pile of cloud about the sky , where the volcano would be . the valley stretch away to its sombre , atmospheric hill , in a flat dry bed , parch except where there be some crop be irrigate . the soil seem strange , dry , blackish , artificially wet , and old . the tree rise high , and hung bare bough , or withered shade . the building be either new and alien , like the Country Club , or crack and dilapidate , with all the plaster fall off . the fall of thick plaster from crack building - one could almost hear it ! 

 Yellow tram - car rush at express speed away down the fence - in car - line , rush round towards Xochimilco or Tlalpam . the asphalt road run outside these line , and on the asphalt rush incredibly dilapidate Ford omnibus , crowd with blank dark native in dirty cotton clothe and big straw hat . at the far edge of the road , on the dust - track under the tree , little donkey under huge load loitered towards the city , drive by man with blacken face and bare , blacken leg . three - fold go the traffic ; the roar of the tram - train , the clatter of the automobile , the straggle of ass and of outside - seem individual .

 they go through the tree - fill plaza of Tlacolula , where native be squat on the ground , sell fruit or sweet , then down a road between high wall . they pull up at last at big gate - door , beyond which be a heavy pink - and - yellow house , and beyond the house , high , dark cypress tree .

 Kate go up the jet - like stone staircase , through the leather door . Mrs Norris come forward on the terrace of the upper patio to receive her guest . 

 ' I be so glad , my dear , that you come . I should have ring you up before , but I have   have such trouble with my heart . and the doctor want to send I down to a low altitude ! I say to he , I have   no patience ! if you be go to cure I , cure I at an altitude of seven thousand foot or else admit your incompetence at once . ridiculous , this rush up and down from one altitude to another . I have   live at this height all these year . I simply refuse to be bundle down to Cuernavaca or some other place where I do not   want to go . well , my dear , and how be you ? ' 

 Mrs Norris be an elderly woman , rather like a conquistador herself in her black silk dress and her little black shoulder - shawl of fine cashmere , with a short silk fringe , and her ornament of black enamel . her face have go slightly grey , her nose be sharp and dusky , and her voice hammer almost like metal , a slow , distinct , peculiar hard music of its own . she be an archaeologist , and she have study the Aztec remain so long , that now some of the black - grey look of the lava rock , and some of the experience of the aztec idol , with sharp nose and slightly prominent eye and an expression of tomb - like mockery , have pass into her face . a lonely daughter of culture , with a strong mind and a dense will , she have browse all her life on the hard stone of archaeological remain , and at the same time she have retain a strong sense of humanity , and a slightly fantastic humorous vision of her fellow man .

Mrs Norris be one of the few individual . true , she play her social game all the time . but she be an odd number ; and all alone , she could give the even number a bad time .

 ' Judge and Mrs Burlap . '

 the Judge stamp his stick on the ground in a speechless access of irritability . 

 ' they paste on my luggage , ' say the Major , ' when I come through Vera Cruz : La degenerada medium clasa , Será regenerada , por mi , Montes . the degenerate middle class shall be regenerate by I , Montes . ' 

 ' Poor Montes ! ' say Kate . ' he seem to have get his work cut out . ' 

 ' he have indeed ! ' say Mrs Norris . ' poor man , I wish he might come in peacefully and put a strong hand on the country . but there be not much hope , I be afraid . ' 

 there be a silence , during which Kate feel that bitter hopelessness that come over people who know Mexico well . a bitter barren hopelessness . 

 ' how can a man who come in on a labour vote , even a doctored one , put a strong hand on a country ! ' snap the Judge . ' why he come in on the very cry of Down with the strong hand ! ' and again the old man stamp his stick in an access of extreme irritability . 

 this be another characteristic of the old resident of the city : a state of intense , though often suppress irritation , an irritation amount almost to rabie . 

 ' oh , but may not   it be possible that he will change his view a little on come into power ? ' say Mrs Norris . ' so many president have do so . ' 

 ' I should say very probable , if ever he get into power , ' say young Henry . ' he will have all his work cut out save Socrates Tomás , he will not   have much time leave for save Mexico . ' 

 ' he be a dangerous fellow , and will turn out a scoundrel , ' say the Judge . 

 ' Myself , ' say Owen , ' as far as I have follow he , I believe he be sincere , and I admire he . ' 

 ' I think it be so nice , ' say Kate , ' that they receive he in New York with loud music by the Street Sweepers ' Band . the Street Sweepers ' Band they send to receive he from the ship ! ' 

 ' you see , ' say the Major , ' no doubt the Labour people themselves wish to send that particular band . ' 

 ' but to be President Elect , and to be receive by the Street Sweepers ' Band ! ' say Kate . ' no , I can not   believe it ! ' 

 ' oh , it actually be so , ' say the Major . ' but that be Labour hail Labour , surely . ' 

 ' the late rumour , ' say Henry , ' be that the army will go over en bloc to General Angulo about the twenty - third , a week before the inauguration . ' 

 ' but how be it possible ? ' say Kate , ' when Montes be so popular ? ' 

 ' monte popular ! ' they all cry at once . ' why ! ' snap the Judge , ' he be the most unpopular man in Mexico . ' 

 ' not with the Labour Party ! ' say Owen , almost at bay . 

 ' the Labour Party ! ' the Judge fairly spat like a cat . ' there be no such thing . what be the Labour Party in Mexico ? a bunch of isolated factory hand here and there , mostly in the State of Vera Cruz . the Labour Party ! they have   do what they could already . we know they . ' 

 ' that be true , ' say Henry . ' the Labourites have try every little game possible . when I be in Orizaba they march to the Hotel Francia to shoot all the gringoe and the Gachupines . the hotel manager have pluck enough to harangue they , and they go off to the next hotel . when the man come out there to talk to they , they shoot he before he get a word out . it be funny , really ! if you have to go to the Town Hall , and you be dressed in decent clothe , they let you sit on a hard bench for hour . but if a street - sweeper come in , or a fellow in dirty cotton drawer , it be Buenos dia ! señor ! Pase uste ! Quiere Usted algo ? - while you sit there wait their pleasure . oh , it be quite funny . ' 

 the Judge tremble with irritation like an access of gout . the party sit in gloomy silence , that sense of doom and despair overcome they as it seem to overcome all people who talk seriously about Mexico . even Owen be silent . he too have come through Vera Cruz , and have have his fright ; the porter have charge he twenty peso to carry his trunk from the ship to the train . twenty peso be ten dollar , for ten minute ' work . and when Owen have see the man in front of he arrest and actually send to jail , a mexican jail at that , for refuse to pay the charge , ' the legal charge ' , he himself have stump up without a word . 

 ' I walk into the National Museum the other day , ' say the Major quietly . ' just into that room on the patio where the stone be . it be rather a cold morning , with a Norte blowing . I would be there about ten minute when somebody suddenly poke I on the shoulder . I turn round , and it be a lout in tight boot . you spik English ? I say yes ! then he motion I to take my hat off : I would get to take my hat off . what for ? say I , and I turn away and go on look at their idol and thing : ugly set of stuff in the world , I believe . then up come the fellow with the attendant - the attendant of course wear his cap . they begin gabble that this be the National Museum , and I must take off my hat to their national monument . imagine it : those dirty stone ! I laugh at they and jam my hat on tight and walk out . they be really only monkey when it come to nationalism . ' 

 ' exactly ! ' cry Henry . ' when they forget all about the Patria and Mexico and all that stuff , they be as nice a people as you would find . but as soon as they get national , they be just monkey . a man up from Mixcoatl tell I a nice story . Mixcoatl be a capital way in the South , and they have   get a sort of Labour bureau there . well , the Indians come in from the hill , as wild as rabbit . and they get they into that bureau , and the Laboristas , the agitator fellow , say to they : now , Señores , have you anything to report from your native village ? have not   you anything for which you would like redress ? then of course the Indians start complain about one another , and the Secretary say : wait a minute , gentleman ! let I ring up the Governor and report this . so he go to the telephone and start ring : ringing : ah ! be that the Palace ? be the Governor in ? tell he Señor Fulano want to speak to he ! the Indians sit gap with open mouth . to they it be a miracle . ah ! be that you , Governor ! good morning ! how be you ? can I have your attention for a moment ? many thank ! well I have   get some gentleman here down from Apaxtle , in the hill : José Garcia , Jesús Querido , etc . - and they wish to report so - and - so . yes ! yes ! that be it ! yes ! what ? you will see that justice be do and the thing be make right ? ah señor , many thank ! in the name of these gentleman from the hill , from the village of Apaxtle , many thank . 

 ' there sit the Indians star as if heaven have open and the Virgin of Guadalupe be stand tiptoe on their chin . and what do you expect ? the telephone be a dummy . it be not   connect with anywhere . be not   that rich ? but it be Mexico . ' 

 the moment 's fatal pause follow this funny story . 

 ' oh but ! ' say Kate , ' it be wicked ! it be wicked . I be sure the Indians would be all right , if they be leave alone . ' 

 ' well , ' say Mrs Norris , ' Mexico be not   like any other place in the world . ' 

 but she speak with fear and despair in her voice . 

 ' they seem to want to betray everything , ' say Kate . ' they seem to love criminal and ghastly thing . they seem to want the ugly thing . they seem to want the ugly thing to come up to the top . all the foulness that lie at the bottom , they want to stir up to the top . they seem to enjoy it . to enjoy make everything fouler . be not   it curious ! ' 

 ' it be curious , ' say Mrs Norris . 

 ' but that be what it be , ' say the Judge . ' they want to turn the country into one big crime . they do not   like anything else . they do not   like honesty and decency and cleanliness . they want to foster lie and crime . what they call liberty here be just freedom to commit crime . that be what Labour mean , that be what they all mean . free crime , nothing else . ' 

 ' I wonder all the foreigner do not   go away , ' say Kate . 

 ' they have their occupation here , ' snap the Judge . 

 ' and the good people be all go away . they have nearly all go , those that have anything leave to go to , ' say Mrs Norris . ' some of we , who have our property here , and who have make our life here , and who know the country , we stay out of a kind of tenacity . but we know it be hopeless . the more it change , the bad it be . - ah , here be Don Ram n and Don Cipriano . so pleased to see you . let I introduce you . ' 

 Don Ram n Carrasco be a tall , big , handsome man who give the effect of bigness . he be middle aged , with a large black moustache and large , rather haughty eye under straight brow . the General be in civilian clothe , look very small beside the other man , and very smartly build , almost cocky . 

 ' come , ' say Mrs Norris . ' let we go across and have tea . ' 

 the Major excuse himself , and take his departure . 

 Mrs Norris gather she little shawl round her shoulder and lead through a sombre antechamber to a little terrace , where creeper and flower bloom thick on the low wall . there be a bell - flower , red and velvety , like blood that be dry : and cluster of white rose : and tuft of bougainvillea , papery magenta colour . 

 ' how lovely it be here ! ' say Kate . ' have the great dark tree beyond . ' 

 but she stand in a kind of dread .

' and go across in her little black shawl , she push the bougainvillea away from the rust - scarlet bell - flower , stroke the little white rose to make they intervene .

 ' do you really ! ' say Mrs Norris , automatically , pay no heed to such a remark . 

 the sky be blue overhead , but on the low horizon be a thick , pearl haze . the cloud have go .

 ' no , not at this season . but look , through the tree there , you see Ajusco ! ' 

 Kate look at the sombre - seem mountain , between the huge dark tree . 

 on the low stone parapet be aztec thing , obsidian knife , grimace squat idol in black lava , and a queer thickish stone stick , or bâton . Owen be balance the latter : it feel murderous even to touch . 

 Kate turn to the General , who be near she , his face expressionless , yet alert . 

 ' aztec thing oppress I , ' she say . 

 ' they be oppressive , ' he answer , in his beautiful cultured English , that be nevertheless a tiny bit like a parrot talking . 

 ' there be no hope in they , ' she say . 

 ' perhaps the Aztecs never ask for hope , ' he say , somewhat automatically .

 ' I would like to give they hope , ' she say . ' if they have hope , they would not   be so sad , and they would be clean , and not have vermin . '

 ' no , ' she say . ' they oppress I , like a weight on my heart . they make I irritable , and I want to go away . ' 

 ' from Mexico ? ' 

 ' yes . I feel I want to go away from it and never , never see it again . it be so oppressive and gruesome . ' 

 ' try it a little long , ' he say . ' perhaps you will feel differently . but perhaps not , ' he end vaguely , driftingly . 

 she could feel in he a sort of yearn towards she . as if a sort of appeal come to she from he , from his physical heart in his breast . as if the very heart give out dark ray of seek and yearning . she glimpse this now for the first time , quite apart from the talking , and it make she shy . 

 ' and do everything in Mexico oppress you ? ' he add , almost shyly , but with a touch of mockery , look at she with a troubled naïve face that have its age heavy and resistant beneath the surface . 

 ' almost everything ! ' she say . ' it always make my heart sink . like the eye of the man in the big hat - I call they the peon . their eye have no middle to they . those big handsome man , under their big hat , they be not   really there . they have no centre , no real i. their middle be a rag black hole , like the middle of a maelstrom . ' 

 she look with her troubled grey eye into the black , slanting , watchful , calculate eye of the small man opposite she . he have a pained expression , puzzle , like a child . and at the same time something obstinate and mature , a demonish maturity , oppose she in an animal way . 

 ' you mean we be not   real people , we have nothing of our own , except killing and death , ' he say , quite matter of fact . 

 ' I do not   know , ' she say , startle by his interpretation . ' I only say how it make I feel . ' 

 ' you be very clever , Mrs Leslie , ' come Don Ram n 's quiet , but heavy teasing voice behind she . ' it be quite true . whenever a mexican cry Viva ! he end up with Muera ! when he say Viva ! he really mean Death for Somebody or other ! I think of all the mexican revolution , and I see a skeleton walk ahead of a great number of people , wave a black banner with Viva la Muerte ! write in large white letter . long live death ! not Viva Cristo Rey ! but Viva Muerte Rey ! Vamos ! Viva ! ' 

 Kate look round . Don Ram n be flash his knowing brown spanish eye , and a little sardonic smile lurk under his moustache . instantly Kate and he , Europeans in essence , understand one another . he be wave his arm to the last Viva !

 ' I never could be , ' she say hotly , and he laugh .

 she lead the way in her black little shawl and neat grey hair , go ahead like a Conquistador herself , and turn to look with her aztec eye through her pince - nez , to see if the other be come .

 an amused little smile quickly light his face , though his eye do not smile . they look at she with a black , sharp look . 

 ' as you wish , ' he say . ' you know General be a term of disgrace in Mexico . shall we say Don Cipriano ? '

 and he seem pleased . 

 it be a round tea - table , with shiny silver tea - service , and silver kettle with a little flame , and pink and white oleander . the little neat young footman carry the tea - cup , in white cotton glove . Mrs Norris pour tea and cut cake with a heavy hand . 

 Don Ram n sit on her right hand , the Judge on she left . Kate be between the Judge and Mr Henry . everybody except Don Ram n and the Judge be a little nervous . Mrs Norris always put her visitor uncomfortably at their ease , as if they be captive and she the chieftainess who have capture they . she rather enjoy it , heavily , archaeologically queen at the head of the table . but it be evident that Don Ram n , by far the most impressive person present , like she . Cipriano , on the other hand , remain mute and disciplined , perfectly familiar with the tea - table routine , superficially quite at ease , but underneath remote and unconnected . he glance from time to time at Kate . 

 she be a beautiful woman , in her own unconventional way , and with a certain richness . she be go to be forty next week . use to all kind of society , she watch people as one read the page of a novel , with a certain disintereste amusement . she be never in any society : too irish , too wise . 

 ' but of course nobody live without hope , ' Mrs Norris be say banteringly to Don Ram n. ' if it be only the hope of a real , to buy a litre of pulque . ' 

 ' ah , Mrs Norris ! ' he reply in his quiet , yet curiously deep voice , like a violoncello : ' if pulque be the high happiness ! ' 

 ' then we be fortunate , because a tost n will buy paradise , ' she say . 

 ' it be a bon mot , Señora mía , ' say Don Ram n , laugh and drink his tea . 

 ' now will not   you try these little native cake with sesame seed on they ! ' say Mrs Norris to the table at large . ' my cook make they , and her national feeling be flatter when anybody like they . Mrs Leslie , do take one . ' 

 ' I will , ' say Kate . ' do one say Open Sesame ! ' 

 ' if one wish , ' say Mrs Norris .

 ' do you see that article by Willis Rice Hope , in the Excelsior ? ' suddenly snarl the Judge , to his hostess . 

 ' I do . I think it very sensible . ' 

 ' the only sensible thing that be be say about these Agrarian Laws . sensible ! I should think so . why Rice Hope come to I , and I put he up to a few thing . but his article say everything , do not   miss an item of importance . ' 

 ' quite ! ' say Mrs Norris , with rather stony attention . ' if only say would alter thing , Judge Burlap . '

 ' fortunately , ' she say , ' they do not   come out to Tlacolula , so we need not   think about they . Mrs Henry , let I give you some more tea . '

' my father have we all speak four language by the time we be twelve , and we have none of we ever quite recovered . my stocking be all dye blue for I before I put my hair up . by the way ! how have you be for walking , Judge ? you hear of the time I have with my ankle ? '

'

 ' do nobody help you ? ' ask Kate . 

 ' oh no ! if anyone have an accident in this country , you must never , never help . if you touch they even , you may be arrest for cause the accident . '

 ' be that true ? ' say Kate to Don Ram n.

' I be an American , and I may any day turn bolshevist , to save my peso , so I can repeat what I hear a man say yesterday . he say there be only two great disease in the world to - day - bolshevism and americanism ; and americanism be the bad of the two , because Bolshevism only smash your house or your business or your skull , but americanism smash your soul . ' 

 ' who be he ? ' snarl the Judge . 

 ' I forget , ' say Henry , wickedly .

 ' well , ' say Mrs Norris . ' the cult of the dollar , in my experience , be far more intense in the country that have not   get the dollar , than in the United States . ' 

 Kate feel that the table be like a steel disc to which they be all , as victim , magnetize and bind .

 they troop out , gasp with relief , to the terrace . the Judge hobble behind , and Kate have to linger sympathetically to keep he company . 

 they be on the little terrace . 

 ' be not   this strange stuff ! ' say Kate , pick up one of the aztec stone knife on the parapet . ' be it a sort of jade ? ' 

 ' Jade ! ' snarl the Judge . ' Jade 's green , not black . that be obsidian . ' 

 ' Jade can be black , ' say Kate . ' I have   get a lovely little black tortoise of jade from China . '

 ' Jade 's bright green . ' 

 Owen , who have the ear of a lynx , have hear . 

 ' what be that ? ' he say . 

 ' surely there be more than green jade ! ' say Kate . 

 ' what ! ' cry Owen . ' More ! why there be every imaginable tint - white , rise , lavender - ' 

 ' and black ? ' say Kate . 

 ' black ? oh yes , quite common . why you should see my collection . the most beautiful range of colour ! only green jade ! ha - ha - ha ! ' - and he laugh a rather stage laugh .

 evening be fall . the garden be draw up tall , under the huge dark tree on the one side , and the tall , reddish - and - yellow house on the other . it be like be at the bottom of some dusky , flower garden down in Hades .  Mrs Norris be almost regal , stonily , aztec - regal .

Nearer , on this side of the road , stand another little gang , of workman in town clothe . 

 ' there you have they , ' say the Judge , flourish his stick with utter vindictiveness . ' there be the two lot of them . ' 

 ' what two lot ? ' say Kate , surprised .

 whereas the other bloodless , acidulous couple from the Middle - West , with their nasty whiteness . . . ! 

 she think of the little tale the native tell . when the Lord be make the first man , he make they of clay and put they into the oven to bake . they come out black . they be bake too much ! say the Lord . so he make another batch , and put they in . they come out white . they be bake too little ! he say . so he have a third try . these come out a good warm brown . they be just right ! say the Lord . 

 the couple from the Middle - West , that wither baby - face and that limp Judge , they be not   bake . they be hardly bake at all . 

 Kate look at the dark face under the arc - lamp . they frighten she . they be a sort of menace to she . but she feel they be at least bake hot and to a certain satisfactory colour .

 ' we may as well , ' she say . 

 away gallivant the Ford , full speed to Hell . 

 ' do tell he not so fast , ' say Kate . 

 ' I do not   know how , ' say Owen . 

 he shout in good English : 

 ' Hey ! chauffeur ! not so fast ! do not   drive so fast . ' 

 ' no presto . troppo presto . Va troppo presto ! ' say Kate .

 ' be not   that a ghastly tea - party ! ' say Owen . 

 ' ghastly ! ' say Kate . 

 

 

 CHAPTER III 

 Fortieth Birthday 

 

 Kate wake up one morning , age forty . she do not hide the fact from herself , but she keep it dark from the other . 

 it be a blow , really . to be forty ! one have to cross a dividing line . on this side there be youth and spontaneity and ' happiness . ' on the other side something different : reserve , responsibility , a certain standing back from ' fun . ' 

 she be a widow , and a lonely woman now . have marry young , her two child be grow up . the boy be twenty - one , and her daughter nineteen . they stay chiefly with their father , from whom she have be divorce ten year before , in order to marry James Joachim Leslie . now Leslie be dead , and all that half of life be over . 

 she climb up to the flat roof of the hotel . it be a brilliant morning , and for once , under the blue sky of the distance , Popocatepetl stand aloof , a heavy giant presence under heaven , with a cape of snow . and roll a long dark roll of smoke like a serpent . 

 Ixtaccihuatl , the White Woman , glitter and seem near , but the other mountain , Popocatepetl , stand far back , and in shadow , a pure cone of atmospheric shadow , with glint flash of snow . there they be , the two monster , watch gigantically and terribly over their lofty , bloody cradle of man , the Valley of Mexico . Alien , ponderous , the white - hung mountain seem to emit a deep purring sound , too deep for the ear to hear , and yet audible on the blood , a sound of dread . there be no soar or uplift or exaltation , as there be in the snowy mountain of Europe . rather a ponderous , white - shoulder weight , press terribly on the earth , and murmur like two watchful lion . 

 superficially , Mexico might be all right : with its suburb of villas , its central fine street , its thousand of motor - car , its tennis , and its bridge - party . the sun shine brilliantly every day , and big bright flower stand out from the tree . it be a holiday . 

 until you be alone with it . and then the undertone be like the low , angry , snarl purring of some jaguar spot with night . there be a ponderous , down - press weight upon the spirit : the great fold of the dragon of the Aztecs , the dragon of the Toltecs wind around one and weigh down the soul . and on the bright sunshine be a dark steam of an angry , impotent blood , and the flower seem to have their root in spilt blood . the spirit of place be cruel , down - dragging , destructive . 

 Kate could so well understand the Mexican who have say to she : El grito mexicano es siempre el grito del odio - the mexican shout be always a shout of hate . the famous revolution , as Don Ram n say , begin with Viva ! but end always with Muera ! death to this , death to the other ; it be all death ! death ! death ! as insistent as the aztec sacrifice . something for ever gruesome and macabre . 

 why have she come to this high plateau of death ? as a woman , she suffer even more than man suffer : and in the end , practically all man go under . once , Mexico have have an elaborate ritual of death . now it have death , ragged , squalid , vulgar , without even the passion of its own mystery . 

 she sit on a parapet of the old roof . the street beyond be like a black abyss , but around she be the rough glare of uneven flat roof , with loose telephone wire trail across , and the sudden , deep , dark well of the patio , show flower bloom in shade . 

 just behind be a huge old church , its barrel roof hump up like some crouch animal , and its dome , like bubble inflate , glitter with yellow tile , and blue and white tile , against the intense blue heaven . quiet native woman in long skirt be move on the roof , hang out washing or spread it on the stone . chicken perch here and there . an occasional bird soar huge overhead , trail a shadow . and not far away stand the brownish tower - stump of the Cathedral , the profound old bell tremble huge and deep , so soft as to be almost inaudible , upon the air . 

 it ought to have be all gay , allegro , allegretto , in that sparkle of bright air and old roof surface . but no ! there be the dark undertone , the black , serpent - like fatality all the time . 

 it be no good Kate 's wonder why she have come . over in England , in Ireland , in Europe , she have hear the consummatum e of her own spirit . it be finish , in a kind of death agony . but still this heavy continent of dark - soule death be more than she could bear . 

 she be forty : the first half of her life be over . the bright page with its flower and its love and its station of the Cross end with a grave . now she must turn over , and the page be black , black and empty . 

 the first half of her life have be write on the bright , smooth vellum of hope , with initial letter all gorgeous upon a field of gold . but the glamour have go from station to station of the Cross , and the last illumination be the tomb . 

 now the bright page be turn , and the dark page lie before she . how could one write on a page so profoundly black ?

Owen and Villiers and a young Mexican be wait for she . they set off through the busy street of the town , where automobile and the little omnibus call camione run wild , and where the native in white cotton clothe and sandal and big hat linger like heavy ghost in the street , among the bourgeoisie , the young lady in pale pink crêpe de chine and high heel , the man in little shoe and american straw hat . a continual bustle in the glitter of sunshine .

 Kate know the italian fruit vendor , vigorously polish their orange on their coat - sleeve . such a contrast , the big , handsome Indian , sit so soft and as it be lonely by the kerb , softly , lingeringly polish his yellow orange to a clean gleam , and lingeringly , delicately arrange the little pile , the pyramid for two or three cent each . 

 Queer work , for a big , handsome , male - look man . but they seem to prefer these childish job . 

 the University be a spanish building that have be do up spick and span , and give over to the young artist to decorate . since the revolution , nowhere have authority and tradition be so finally overthrow as in the mexican field of science and art . science and art be the sport of the young . go ahead , my boy ! 

 the boy have go ahead . but even then , the one artist of distinction be no long a boy , and he have serve a long apprenticeship in Europe .

 Kate think of the man polish his orange half - an - hour before : his peculiar beauty , a certain richness of physical being , a ponderous power of blood within he , and a helplessness , a profound unbelief that be fatal and demonish . and all the liberty , all the progress , all the socialism in the world would not help he . Nay , it would only help far to destroy he .

' in Mexico you can not   keep a balance , because thing be so bad . in other country , yes , perhaps you can remain balanced , because thing be not so bad as they be here . but here they be so very bad , you can not   be human . you have to be mexican . you have to be more mexican than human , no ? you can not   do no other . you have to hate the capitalist , you have to , in Mexico , or nobody can live . we can not   live . nobody can live . if you be mexican you can not   be human , it be impossible . you have to be a socialist Mexican , or you have to be a capitalist Mexican , and you hate . what else be there to be do ? we hate the capitalist because he ruin the country and the people . we must hate he . ' no , I do not   like it . you be not   Mexico . you be not   even Mexican , really . you be just half spaniard full of european idea , and you care for assert your own idea and nothing else . you have no real bowel of compassion . you be no good .  perhaps something come out of the earth , the dragon of the earth , some effluence , some vibration which militate against the very composition of the blood and nerve in human being . perhaps it come from the volcano . or perhaps even from the silent , serpent - like dark resistance of those mass of ponderous native whose blood be principally the old , heavy , resistant indian blood .

 this little item be among the spanish information , and be head : the Gods of Antiquity Return to Mexico . 

 

 ' there be a ferment in the village of Sayula , Jalisco , on the Lake of Sayula , owe to an incident of more or less comic nature , yesterday morning towards mid - day . the woman who inhabit the shore of the lake be to be see each day soon after sunrise descend to the water 's edge with large bundle . they kneel on the rock and stone , and in little group , like water - fowl , they wash their dirty linen in the soft water of the lake , pause at time as an old canoa sail by with large single sail . the scene be little change since the day of Montezuma , when the native of the lake worship the spirit of the water , and throw in little image and idol of baked clay , which the lake sometimes return to the descendant of the dead idolater , to keep they in mind of practice not yet altogether forget . 

 ' as the hot sun rise in the sky , the woman spread their washing on the sand and pebble of the shore , and retire to the shade of the willow tree that grow so gracefully and retain their verdant hue through the dry season of the year . while thus repose after their labour , these humble and superstitious woman be astonish to see a man of great stature rise naked from the lake and wade towards the shore . his face , they say , be dark and bearded , but his body shine like gold . 

 ' as if unaware of any watchful eye , he advance calmly and majestically towards the shore . there he stand a moment , and select with his eye a pair of the loose cotton pant wear by the peasant in the field , that be spread whiten in the sun , he stoop and proceed to cover his nakedness with the say garment . 

 ' the woman who thus see her husband 's apparel rob beneath her eye , rise , call to the man and summon the other woman . whereupon the stranger turn his dark face upon they , and say in a quiet voice : " why be you cry ? be quiet ! it will be give back to you . your god be ready to return to you . Quetzalcoatl and Tlaloc , the old god , be minded to come back to you . be quiet , do not   let they find you cry and complain . I have come from out of the lake to tell you the god be come back to Mexico , they be ready to return to their own home . " 

 ' little comfort by this speech , the woman who have lose her washing be overcome and say no more . the stranger then appropriate a cotton blouse , which he don , and disappear . 

 ' after a while , the simple woman gather courage to return to their humble dwelling . the story thus reach the ear of the police , who at once set out to search for the thief . 

 ' the story , however , be not yet conclude . the husband of the poor woman of the lake - shore , return from his labour in the field , approach the gate of the village towards sunset , thinking , no doubt , of nothing but repose and the evening meal . a man in a black serape step towards he , from the shadow of a break wall , and ask : be you afraid to come with I ? the labourer , a man of spirit , promptly reply : no , señor ! he therefore follow the unknown man through the broken wall and through the bush of a deserted garden . in a dark room , or cellar , a small light be burn , reveal a great basin of gold , into which four little man , small than child , be pour sweet - scented water . the astounded peasant be now tell to wash and put on clean clothe , to be ready for the return of the god . he be seat in the golden basin and wash with sweet - smell soap , while the dwarf pour water over he . this , they say , be the bath of Quetzalcoatl . the bath of fire be yet to come . they give he clean clothing of pure white cotton , and a new hat with star embroidery , and sandal with strap of white leather . but beside this , a new blanket , white with bar of blue and black , and flower like star at the centre , and two piece of silver money . go , he be tell . and when they ask you , where do you get your blanket ? answer that Quetzalcoatl be young again . the poor fellow go home in sore fear , lest the police should arrest he for possess steal good . 

 ' the village be full of excitement , and Don Ram n Carrasco , our eminent historian and archaeologist , whose hacienda lie in the vicinity , have announce his intention of proceeding as soon as possible to the spot to examine the origin of this new legend . meanwhile , the police be watch attentively the development of affair , without take any step for the moment . indeed , these little fantasy create a pleasant diversion in the regular order of banditry , murder , and outrage , which it be usually our duty to report . '

 the name Quetzalcoatl , too , fascinate she . she have read bit about the god . Quetzal be the name of a bird that live high up in the mist of tropical mountain , and have very beautiful tail - feather , precious to the aztec . Coatl be a serpent . Quetzalcoatl be the Plumed Serpent , so hideous in the fanged , feather , writhe stone of the National Museum . 

 but Quetzalcoatl be , she vaguely remember , a sort of fair - faced bearded god ; the wind , the breath of life , the eye that see and be unseen , like the star by day . the eye that watch behind the wind , as the star beyond the blue of day . and Quetzalcoatl must depart from Mexico to merge again into the deep bath of life . he be old . he have go eastward , perhaps into the sea , perhaps he have sail into heaven , like a meteor return , from the top of the Volcano of Orizaba : go back as a peacock stream into the night , or as a bird of Paradise , its tail gleaming like the wake of a meteor . Quetzalcoatl ! who know what he mean to the dead aztec , and to the old Indians , who know he before the Aztecs raise their deity to height of horror and vindictiveness ? 

 all a confusion of contradictory gleam of meaning , Quetzalcoatl . but why not ? her irish spirit be weary to death of definite meaning , and a God of one fix purport . god should be iridescent , like the rainbow in the storm . man create a God in his own image , and the god grow old along with the man that make they . but storm sway in heaven , and the god - stuff sway high and angry over our head . god die with man who have conceive they . but the god - stuff roar eternally , like the sea , with too vast a sound to be hear . like the sea in storm , that beat against the rock of living , stiffen man , slowly to destroy they . or like the sea of the glimmering , ethereal plasm of the world , that bath the foot and the knee of man as earth - sap bathe the root of tree . Ye must be bear again . even the god must be bear again . we must be bear again . 

 in her vague , woman 's way , Kate know this . she have live her life . she have have her lover , her two husband . she have her child .
