 ' why ! ' he reply . ' it might . die out and become americanized . ' 

 ' I quite see the danger of americanization , ' say Owen . ' that would be ghastly . almost well die out . ' 

 Owen be so american , he invariably say these thing . 

 ' but ! ' say Kate . ' the Mexicans look so strong ! ' 

 ' they be strong to carry heavy load , ' say Don Ram n. ' but they die easily . they eat all the wrong thing , they drink the wrong thing , and they do not   mind die . they have many child , and they like their child very much . but when the child die , the parent say : ah , he will be an angelito ! so they cheer up and feel as if they have be give a present . sometimes I think they enjoy it when their child die . sometimes I think they would like to transfer Mexico en bloc into Paradise , or whatever lie behind the wall of death . it would be well there ! ' 

 there be a silence . 

 ' but how sad you be ! ' say Kate , afraid . 

 Doña Isabel be give hurried order to the manservant . 

 ' whoever know Mexico below the surface , be sad ! ' say Julio Toussaint , rather sententiously , over his black cravat . 

 ' well , ' say Owen , ' it seem to I , on the contrary , a gay country . a country of gay , irresponsible child . or rather , they would be gay , if they be properly treat . if they have comfortable home , and a sense of real freedom . if they feel that they could control their life and their own country . but be in the grip of outsider , as they have be for hundred of year , life of course seem hardly worth while to they . naturally , they do not   care if they live or die . they do not   feel free . ' 

 ' free for what ? ' ask Toussaint . 

 ' to make Mexico their own . not to be so poor and at the mercy of outsider . ' 

 ' they be at the mercy of something bad than outsider , ' say Toussaint . ' let I tell you . they be at the mercy of their own nature . it be this way . fifty per cent of the people in Mexico be pure Indian : more or less . of the rest , a small proportion be foreigner or Spaniard . you have then the mass which be on top , of mixed blood , Indian and Spaniard mixed , chiefly . these be the Mexicans , those with the mixed blood . now , you take we at this table . Don Cipriano be pure Indian . Don Ram n be almost pure Spaniard , but most probably he have the blood of Tlaxcalan Indians in his vein as well . Señor Mirabal be mixed French and Spanish . Señor Garcia most probably have a mixture of indian blood with Spanish . I myself have French , spanish , Austrian , and indian blood . very well ! now you mix blood of the same race , and it may be all right . Europeans be all Aryan stock , the race be the same . but when you mix european and American Indian , you mix different blood race , and you produce the half - breed . now , the half - breed be a calamity . for why ? he be neither one thing nor another , he be divide against himself . his blood of one race tell he one thing , his blood of another race tell he another . he be an unfortunate , a calamity to himself . and it be hopeless . 

 ' and this be Mexico . the Mexicans of mixed blood be hopeless . well then ! there be only two thing to be do . all the foreigner and the Mexicans clear out and leave the country to the Indians , the pure - blooded Indians . but already you have a difficulty . how can you distinguish the pure - blooded Indian , after so many generation ? or else the half - breed or mix - blood Mexicans who be all the time on top shall continue to destroy the country till the Americans from the United States flood in . we be as California and New Mexico now be , swamp under the dead white sea . 

 ' but let I tell you something far . I hope we be not Puritans . I hope I may say that it depend on the moment of coition . at the moment of coition , either the spirit of the father fuse with the spirit of the mother , to create a new being with a soul , or else nothing fuse but the germ of procreation . 

 ' now consider . how have these Mexicans of mixed blood be beget , for century ? in what spirit ? what be the moment of coition like ? answer I that , and you have tell I the reason for this Mexico which make we despair and which will go on make everybody despair , till it destroy itself . in what spirit have the spanish and other foreign father get child of the indian woman ? what sort of spirit be it ? what sort of coition ? and then , what sort of race do you expect ? ' 

 ' but what sort of a spirit be there between white man and white woman ! ' say Kate . 

 ' at least , ' reply the didactic Toussaint , ' the blood be homogeneous , so that consciousness automatically unroll in continuity . ' 

 ' I hate its unrolling in automatic continuity , ' say Kate . 

 ' perhaps ! but it make life possible . without develop continuity in consciousness , you have chaos . and this come of mixed blood . ' 

 ' and then , ' say Kate , ' surely the indian man be fond of their woman ! the man seem manly , and the woman seem very lovable and womanly . ' 

 ' it be possible that the indian child be pure - blooded , and there be the continuity of blood . but the indian consciousness be swamp under the stagnant water of the white man 's Dead Sea consciousness . take a man like Benito Juarez , a pure indian . he flood his old consciousness with the new white idea , and there spring up a whole forest of verbiage , new law , new constitution and all the rest . but it be a sudden weed . it grow like a weed on the surface , sap the strength of the indian soil underneath , and help the process of ruin . no , madam ! there be no hope for Mexico short of a miracle . ' 

 ' ah ! ' cry Mirabal , flourish his wine - glass . ' be not   that wonderful , when only the miracle will save we ! when we must produce the miracle ? we ! we ! we must make the miracle ! ' he hit his own breast emphatically . ' ah , I think that be marvellous ! ' and he return to his turkey in black sauce . 

 ' look at the Mexicans ! ' Toussaint flare on . ' they do not   care about anything . they eat food so hot with chili , it burn hole in their inside . and it have no nourishment . they live in house that a dog would be ashamed of , and they lie and shiver with cold . but they do not   do anything . they could make , easily , easily , a bed of maize leaf or similar leaf . but they do not   do it . they do not   do anything . they roll up in a thin serape and lie on a thin mat on the bare ground , whether it be wet or dry . and mexican night be cold . but they lie down like dog , anyhow , as if they lie down to die . I say dog ! but you will see the dog look for a dry shelter place . the Mexicans , no ! anywhere , nothing , nothing ! and it be terrible . it be terrible ! as if they want to punish themselves for be alive ! ' 

 ' but then , why do they have so many child ? ' say Kate . 

 ' why do they ? the same , because they do not   care . they do not   care . they do not   care about money , they do not   care about make anything , they do not   care about nothing , nothing , nothing . only they get an excitement out of woman , as they do out of chili . they like to feel the red pepper burn hole in their inside , and they like to feel the other thing , the sex , burn hole in they too . but after the moment , they do not   care . they do not   care a bit . 

 ' and that be bad . I tell you , excuse I , but all , everything , depend on the moment of coition . at that moment many thing can come to a crisis : all a man 's hope , his honour , his faith , his trust , his belief in life and creation and God , all these thing can come to a crisis in the moment of coition . and these thing will be hand on in continuity to the child . believe I , I be a crank on this idea , but it be true . it be certainly absolutely true . ' 

 ' I believe it be true , ' say Kate , rather coldly . 

 ' ah ! you do ! well then ! look at Mexico ! the only conscious people be half - breed , people of mixed blood , beget in greed and selfish brutality . ' 

 ' some people believe in the mixed blood , ' say Kate . 

 ' ah ! they do , do they ? who ? ' 

 ' some of your serious - minded man . they say the half - breed be well than the Indian . ' 

 ' well ! well ! the Indian have his hopelessness . the moment of coition be his moment of supreme hopelessness , when he throw himself down the pit of despair . ' 

 the austrian , european blood , which fan into fire of conscious understanding , die down again , leave what be mexican in Julio Toussaint sink in irredeemable gloom . 

 ' it be true , ' say Mirabal , out of the gloom . ' the Mexicans who have any feeling always prostitute themselves , one way or another , and so they can never do anything . and the Indians can never do anything either , because they have not   get hope in anything . but it be always darkest before the dawn . we must make the miracle come . the miracle be superior even to the moment of coition . ' 

 it seem , however , as if he say it by an effort of will . 

 the dinner be end in silence . during the whirl of talk , or of passionate declaration , the servant have carry round the food and wine . Doña Isabel , completely oblivious of the thing that be be say , watch and direct the servant with nervous anxiety and excitement , her hand with their old jewellery tremble with agitation . Don Ram n have keep his eye on his guest ' material comfort , at the same time listen , as it be , from the back of his head . his big brown eye be inscrutable , his face impassive . but when he have anything to say , it be always with a light laugh and a teasing accent . and yet his eye brood and smoulder with an incomprehensible , unyielde fire . 

 Kate feel she be in the presence of man . here be man face to face not with death and self - sacrifice , but with the life - issue . she feel , for the first time in her life , a pang almost like fear , of man who be pass beyond what she know , beyond her depth . 

 Cipriano , his rather short but intensely black , curved eyelash lower over his dark eye , watch his plate , only sometimes look up with a black , brilliant glance , either at whomsoever be speak , or at Don Ram n , or at Kate . his face be changeless and intensely serious , serious almost with a touch of childishness . but the curious blackness of his eyelash lift so strangely , with such intense unconscious maleness from his eye , the movement of his hand be so odd , quick , light as he eat , so easily a movement of shooting , or of flash a knife into the body of some adversary , and his dark - colour lip be so helplessly savage , as he eat or briefly speak , that her heart stand still . there be something undeveloped and intense in he , the intensity and the crudity of the semi - savage . she could well understand the potency of the snake upon the aztec and Maya imagination . something smooth , undeveloped , yet vital in this man suggest the heavy - ebb blood of reptile in his vein . that be what it be , the heavy - ebb blood of powerful reptile , the dragon of Mexico . 

 so that unconsciously she shrink when his black , big , glitter eye turn on she for a moment . they be not , like Don Ram n 's , dark eye . they be black , as black as jewel into which one could not look without a sensation of fear . and her fascination be ting with fear . she feel somewhat as the bird feel when the snake be watch it . 

 she wonder almost that Don Ram n be not afraid . because she have notice that usually , when an Indian look to a white man , both man stand back from actual contact , from actual meeting of each other 's eye . they leave a wide space of neutral territory between they . but Cipriano look at Ram n with a curious intimacy , glitter , steady , warrior - like , and at the same time betray an almost menacing trust in the other man . 

 Kate realize that Ram n have a good deal to stand up to . but he keep a little , foil laugh on his face , and lower his beautiful head with the black hair touch with grey , as if he would put a veil before his countenance . 

 ' do you think one can make this miracle come ? ' she ask of he . 

 ' the miracle be always there , ' he say , ' for the man who can pass his hand through to it , to take it . ' 

 they finish dinner , and go to sit out on the veranda , look into the garden where the light from the house fall uncannily on the blossoming tree and the dark tuft of Yucca and the strange great writhing trunk of the Laurel de India . 

 Cipriano have sit down next to she , smoke a cigarette . 

 ' it be a strange darkness , the mexican darkness ! ' she say . 

 ' do you like it ? ' he ask . 

 ' I do not   know yet , ' she say . ' do you ? ' 

 ' yes . very much . I think I like well the time when the day be fall and the night come on like something else . then , one feel more free , do not   you think ? like the flower that send out their scent at night , but in the daytime they look at the sun and do not   have any smell . ' 

 ' perhaps the night here scar I , ' she laugh . 

 ' yes . but why not ? the smell of the flower at night may make one feel afraid , but it be a good fear . one like it , do not   you think ? ' 

 ' I be afraid of fear , ' she say . 

 he laugh shortly . 

 ' you speak such English English , ' she say . ' nearly all the Mexicans who speak English speak american English . even Don Ram n do , rather . ' 

 ' yes . Don Ram n graduate in Columbia University . but I be send to England , to school in London , and then to Oxford . ' 

 ' who send you ? ' 

 ' my god - father . he be an Englishman : Bishop Severn , Bishop of Oaxaca . you have hear of he ? ' 

 ' no , ' say Kate . 

 ' he be a very well - know man . he die only about ten year ago . he be very rich , too , before the revolution . he have a big hacienda in Oaxaca , with a very fine library . but they take it away from he in the revolution , and they sell the thing , or break they . they do not   know the value of they , of course . ' 

 ' and do he adopt you ? ' 

 ' yes ! in a way . my father be one of the overseer on the hacienda . when I be a little boy I come run to my father , when the Bishop be there , with something in my hand - so ! ' - and he make a cup of his hand . ' I do not   remember . this be what they tell I . I be a small child - three or four year of age - somewhere there . what I have in my hand ' be a yellow scorpion , one of the small one , very poisonous , no ? ' 

 and he lift the cup of his small , slender , dark hand , as if to show Kate the creature . 

 ' well , the Bishop be talk to my father , and he see what I have get before my father do . so he tell I at once , to put the scorpion in his hat - the Bishop 's hat , no ? of course I do what he tell I , and I put the scorpion in his hat , and it do not bite I . if it have sting I I should have die , of course . but I do not   know , so I suppose the alacran be not interested . the Bishop be a very good man , very kind . he like my father , so he become my god - father . then he always take an interest in I , and he send I to school , and then to England . he hop I should be a priest . he always say that the one hope for Mexico be if she have really fine native priest . ' he end rather wistfully . 

 ' and do not   you want to become a priest ? ' say Kate . 

 ' no ! ' he say sadly . ' no ! ' 

 ' not at all ? ' she ask . 

 ' no ! when I be in England it be different from Mexico . even God be different , and the blessed Mary . they be change so much , I feel I do not   know they any more . then I come to understand well , and when I understand I do not   believe any more . I use to think it be the image of Jesus , and the Virgin , and the Saints , that be do everything in the world . and the world seem to I so strange , no ? I could not   see that it be bad , because it be all so very strange and mysterious , when I be a child , in Mexico . only in England I learn about the law of life , and some science . and then when I know why the sun rise and set , and how the world really be , I feel quite different . ' 

 ' be your god - father disappoint ? ' 

 ' a little , perhaps . but he ask I if I would rather be a soldier , so I say I would . then when the revolution come , and I be twenty - two year old , I have to come back to Mexico . ' 

 ' do you like your god - father ? ' 

 ' yes , very much . but the revolution carry everything away . I feel I must do what my god - father wish . but I could see that Mexico be not the Mexico he believe in . it be different . he be too english , and too good to understand . in the revolution I try to help the man I believe be the good man . so you see , I have always be half a priest and half a soldier . ' 

 ' you never marry ? ' 

 ' no . I could not   marry , because I always feel my god - father be there , and I feel I have promise he to be a priest - all those thing , you know . when he die he tell I to follow my own conscience , and to remember that Mexico and all the Indians be in the hand of God , and he make I promise never to take side against God . he be an old man when he die , seventy - five . ' 

 Kate could see the spell of the old Bishop 's strong , rather grandiose personality upon the impressionable Indian . she could see the curious recoil into chastity , perhaps characteristic of the savage . and at the same time she feel the intense masculine yearning , couple with a certain male ferocity , in the man 's breast . 

 ' your husband be James Joachim Leslie , the famous irish leader ? ' he ask she : and add : ' you have no child ? ' 

 ' no . I want Joachim 's child so much , but I do not   have any . but I have a boy and a girl from my first marriage . my first husband be a lawyer , and I be divorce from he for Joachim . ' 

 ' do you like he - that first one ? ' 

 ' yes . I like he . but I never feel anything very deep for he . I marry he when I be young , and he be a good deal old than I. I be fond of he , in a way . but I - have never realize that one could be more than fond of a man , till I know Joachim . I think that be all one could ever expect to feel - that you just like a man , and that he be in love with you . it take I year to understand that a woman can not   love a man - at least a woman like I be can not   - if he be only the sort of good , decent citizen . with Joachim I come to realize that a woman like I can only love a man who be fight to change the world , to make it free , more alive . man like my first husband , who be good and trustworthy and who work to keep the world go on well in the same state they find it in , they let you down horribly , somewhere . you feel so terribly sell . everything be just a sell : it become so small . a woman who be not   quite ordinary herself can only love a man who be fight for something beyond the ordinary life . ' 

 ' and your husband fight for Ireland . ' 

 ' yes - for Ireland , and for something he never quite realize . he ruin his health . and when he be die , he say to I : Kate , perhaps I have   let you down . perhaps I have not   really help Ireland . but I could not   help myself . I feel as if I would bring you to the door of life , and be leave you there . kate , do not   be disappoint in life because of I . I do not   really get anywhere . I have not   really get anywhere . I feel as if I have make a mistake . but perhaps when I be dead I shall be able to do more for you than I have do while I be alive . say you will never feel disappointed ! ' 

 there be a pause . the memory of the dead man be come over she again , and all her grief . 

 ' and I do not   feel disappointed , ' she go on , her voice begin to shake . ' but I love he . and it be bitter , that he have to die , feel he have not   - have not . ' 

 she put her hand before her face , and the bitter tear come through her finger . 

 Cipriano sit motionless as a statue . but from his breast come that dark surge passion of tenderness the Indians be capable of . perhaps it would pass , leave he indifferent and fatalistic again . but at any rate for the moment he sit in a dark , fiery cloud of passionate male tenderness . he look at her soft , wet white hand over her face , and at the one big emerald on her finger , in a sort of wonder . the wonder , the mystery , the magic that use to flood over he as a boy and a youth , when he kneel before the babyish figure of the Santa Maria de la Soledad , flood he again . he be in the presence of the goddess , white - handed , mysterious , gleam with a moon - like power and the intense potency of grief . 

 then Kate hastily take her hand from her face and with head duck look for her handkerchief . of course she have not   get one . Cipriano lend she his , nicely fold . she take it without a word , and rub her face and blow her nose . 

 ' I want to go and look at the flower , ' she say in a strangle voice . 

 and she dash into the garden with his handkerchief in her hand . he stand up and draw aside his chair , to let she pass , then stand a moment look at the garden , before he sit down again and light a cigarette . 

 

 

 CHAPTER IV 

 to stay or not to stay 

 

 Owen have to return to the United States , and he ask Kate whether she want to stay on in Mexico . 

 this put she into a quandary . it be not an easy country for a woman to be alone in . and she have be beat her wing in an effort to get away . she feel like a bird round whose body a snake have coil itself . Mexico be the snake . 

 the curious influence of the country , pull one down , pull one down . she have hear an old American , who have be forty year in the Republic , say to Owen : ' no man who have not   a strong moral backbone should try to settle in Mexico . if he do , he will go to piece , morally and physically , as I have   see hundred of young Americans do . ' 

 to pull one down . it be what the country want to do all the time , with a slow , reptilian insistence , to pull one down . to prevent the spirit from soar . to take away the free , soar sense of liberty . 

 ' there be no such thing as liberty , ' she hear the quiet , deep , dangerous voice of Don Ram n repeat . ' there be no such thing as liberty . the great liberator be usually slave of an idea . the free people be slave to convention and public opinion , and more still , slave to the industrial machine . there be no such thing as liberty . you only change one sort of domination for another . all we can do be to choose our master . ' 

 ' but surely that be liberty - for the mass of people . ' 

 ' they do not   choose . they be trick into a new form of servility , no more . they go from bad to bad . ' 

 ' you yourself - be not   you free ? ' she ask . 

 ' I ? ' he laugh . ' I spend a long time try to pretend . I think I could have my own way . till I realize that have my own way mean only run about smell all the thing in the street , like a dog that will pick up something . of myself , I have no way . no man have any way in himself . every man who go along a way be lead by one of three thing : by an appetite - and I class ambition among appetite ; or by an idea ; or by an inspiration . ' 

 ' I use to think my husband be inspire about Ireland , ' say Kate doubtfully . 

 ' and now ? ' 

 ' yes ! perhaps he put his wine in old , rotten bottle that would not   hold it . no ! - Liberty be a rotten old wine - skin . it will not   hold one 's wine of inspiration or passion any more , ' she say . 

 ' and Mexico ! ' he say . ' Mexico be another Ireland . ah no , no man can be his own master . if I must serve , I will not serve an idea , which crack and leak like an old wine - skin . I will serve the God that give I my manhood . there be no liberty for a man , apart from the God of his manhood . Free Mexico be a bully , and the old , colonial , ecclesiastical Mexico be another sort of bully . when man have nothing but his will to assert - even his good - will - it be always bully . bolshevism be one sort of bullying , capitalism another : and liberty be a change of chain . ' 

 ' then what be to be do ? ' say Kate . ' just nothing ? ' 

 and with her own will , she want nothing to be do . let the sky fall ! 

 ' one be drive , at last , back to the far distance , to look for God , ' say Ram n uneasily . 

 ' I rather hate this search - for - God business , and religiosity , ' say Kate . 

 ' I know ! ' he say , with a laugh . ' I have   suffer from would - be - cocksure religion myself . ' 

 ' and you can not   really " find God " ! ' she say . ' it be a sort of sentimentalism , and creep back into old , hollow shell . ' 

 ' no ! ' he say slowly . ' I can not   find God , in the old sense . I know it be a sentimentalism if I pretend to . but I be nauseate with humanity and the human will : even with my own will . I have realize that my will , no matter how intelligent I be , be only another nuisance on the face of the earth , once I start exert it . and other people 's will be even bad . ' 

 ' oh ! be not   human life horrible ! ' she cry . ' every human be exert his will all the time - over other people , and over himself , and nearly always self - righteous ! ' 

 Ram n make a grimace of repulsion . 

 ' to I , ' he say , ' that be just the weariness of life ! for a time , it can be amusing : exert your own will , and resist all the other people 's will , that they try to put over you . but at a certain point a nausea set in at the very middle of I : my soul be nauseate . my soul be nauseate , and there be nothing but death ahead , unless I find something else . ' 

 Kate listen in silence . she know the road he have go , but she herself have not yet come to the end of it . as yet she be still strong in the pride of her own - her very own will . 

 ' oh , people be repulsive ! ' she cry . 

 ' my own will become even more repulsive at last , ' he say . ' my own will , merely as my own will , be even more distasteful to I than other people 's will . from be the god in my own machine , I must either abdicate , or die of disgust - self - disgust , at that . ' 

 ' how amusing ! ' she cry . 

 ' it be rather funny , ' he say sardonically . 

 ' and then ? ' she ask , look at he with a certain malevolent challenge . 

 he look back at she slowly , with an ironical light in his eye . 

 ' then ! ' he repeat . ' then ! - I ask , what else be there in the world , besides human will , human appetite ? because idea and ideal be only instrument of human will and appetite . ' 

 ' not entirely , ' say Kate . ' they may be disintereste . ' 

 ' may they ? if the appetite be not   interested , the will be . ' 

 ' why not ? ' she mock . ' we can not   be mere detached block . ' 

 ' it nauseate I - I look for something else . ' 

 ' and what do you find ? ' 

 ' my own manhood ! ' 

 ' what do that mean ? ' she cry , jeer . 

 ' if you look , and find your own womanhood , you would know . ' 

 ' but I have my own womanhood ! ' she cry . 

 ' and then - when you find your own manhood - your womanhood , ' he go on , smile faintly at she - ' then you know it be not your own , to do as you like with . you do not   have it of your own will . it come from - from the middle - from the God . beyond I , at the middle , be the God . and the God give I my manhood , then leave I to it . I have nothing but my manhood . the God give it I , and leave I to do far . ' 

 Kate would not hear any more . she break off into banality . 

 the immediate question , for she , be whether she would stay in Mexico or not . she be not really concerned with Don Ram n 's soul - or even her own . she be concern with her immediate future . should she stay in Mexico ? Mexico mean the dark - face man in cotton clothe , big hat : the peasant , peon , pelado , Indians , call they what you will . the mere native . 

 those pale - face Mexicans of the Capital , politician , artist , professional , and business people , they do not interest she . neither do the hacendado and the ranch - owner , in their tight trouser and weak , soft sensuality , pale victim of their own emotional undiscipline . Mexico still mean the mass of silent peon , to she . and she think of they again , these silent , stiff - back man , drive their string of ass along the country road , in the dust of Mexico 's infinite dryness , past broken wall , broken house , broken hacienda , along the endless desolation leave by the revolution ; past the vast stretch of maguey , the huge cactus , or aloe , with its gigantic rosette of upstarte , pointed leaf , that in its iron row cover mile and mile of ground in the Valley of Mexico , cultivate for the making of that bad - smell drink , pulque . the Mediterranean have the dark grape , old Europe have malt beer , and China have opium from the white poppy . but out of the mexican soil a bunch of black - tarnish sword burst up , and a great unfolded bud of the once - flower monster begin to thrust at the sky . they cut the great phallic bud and crush out the sperm - like juice for the pulque . Agua miel ! Pulque ! 

 but well pulque than the fiery white brandy distil from the maguey : mescal , tequila : or in the low land , the hateful sugar - cane brandy , aguardiente . 

 and the Mexican burn out his stomach with those beastly fire - water and cauterize the hurt with red - hot chili . swallow one hell - fire to put out another . 

 tall field of wheat and maize . Taller , more brilliant field of bright - green sugar - cane . and thread in white cotton clothe , with dark , half - visible face , the eternal peon of Mexico , his great white calico drawer flop round his ankle as he walk , or roll up over his dark , handsome leg . 

 the wild , sombre , erect man of the north ! the too - often degenerate man of Mexico Valley , their head through the middle of their ponchos ! the big man in Tlascala , sell ice - cream or huge half - sweeten bun and fancy bread ! the quick little Indians , quick as spider , down in Oaxaca ! the queer - look half - chinese native towards Vera Cruz ! the dark face and the big black eye on the coast of Sinaloa ! the handsome man of Jalisco , with a scarlet blanket fold on one shoulder ! 

 they be of many tribe and many language , and far more alien to one another than Frenchmen , English , and Germans be . Mexico ! it be not really even the beginning of a nation : hence the rabid assertion of nationalism in the few . and it be not a race . 

 yet it be a people . there be some indian quality which pervade the whole . whether it be man in blue overall and a slouch , in Mexico City , or man with handsome leg in skintight trouser , or the floppy , white , cotton - clothe labourer in the field , there be something mysteriously in common . the erect , prance walk , step out from the base of the spine with lift knee and short step . the jaunty balancing of the huge hat . the throw - back shoulder with a fold serape like a royal mantle . and most of they handsome , with dark , warm - bronze skin so smooth and living , their proudly - hold head , whose black hair gleam like wild , rich feather . their big , bright black eye that look at you wonderingly , and have no centre to they . their sudden , charming smile , when you smile first . but the eye unchanged . 

 yes , and she have to remember , too , a fair proportion of small , sometimes insignificant - look man , some of they scaly with dirt , who look at you with a cold , mud - like antagonism as they step cattishly past . poisonous , thin , stiff little man , cold and unliving like scorpion , and as dangerous . 

 and then the truly terrible face of some creature in the city , slightly swell with the poison of tequila , and with black , dim , swivel eye swing in pure evil . never have she see such face of pure brutish evil , cold and insect - like , as in Mexico City . 

 the country give she a strange feeling of hopelessness and of dauntlessness . unbroken , eternally resistant , it be a people that live without hope , and without care . Gay even , and laugh with indifferent carelessness . 

 they be something like her own Irish , but go to a much great length . and also , they do what the self - conscious and pretentious Irish rarely do , they touch her bowel with a strange fire of compassion . 

 at the same time , she fear they . they would pull she down , pull she down , to the dark depth of nothingness . 

 it be the same with the woman . in their full long skirt and bare foot , and with the big dark - blue scarf or shawl call a rebozo over their womanly small head and tight round their shoulder , they be image of wild submissiveness , the primitive womanliness of the world , that be so touching and so alien . many woman kneel in a dim church , all hood in their dark - blue rebozo , the pallor of their skirt on the floor , their head and shoulder wrap dark and tight , as they sway with devotion of fear and ecstasy ! a churchful of dark - wrap woman sink there in wild , humble supplication of dread and of bliss fill Kate with tenderness and revulsion . they crouch like people not quite create . 

 their soft , untidy black hair , which they scratch for lice ; the round - eyed baby joggle like a pumpkin in the shawl sling over the woman 's shoulder , the never - wash foot and ankle , again somewhat reptilian under the long , flounce , soil cotton skirt ; and then , once more , the dark eye of half - create woman , soft , appealing , yet with a queer void insolence ! something lurking , where the womanly centre should have be ; lurk snake - like . fear ! the fear of not be able to find full creation . and the inevitable mistrust and lurking insolence , insolent against a high creation , the same thing that be in the striking of a snake . 

 Kate , as a woman , fear the woman more than the man . the woman be little and insidious , the man be big and more reckless . but in the eye of each , the uncreated centre , where the evil and the insolence lurk . 

 and sometimes she wonder whether America really be the great death - continent , the great no ! to the european and asiatic , and even african yes ! be it really the great melting - pot , where man from the creative continent be smelt back again , not to a new creation , but down into the homogeneity of death ? be it the great continent of the undoing , and all its people the agent of the mystic destruction ! plucking , pluck at the created soul in a man , till at last it pluck out the grow germ , and leave he a creature of mechanism and automatic reaction , with only one inspiration , the desire to pluck the quick out of every live spontaneous creature . 

 be that the clue to America ? she sometimes wonder . be it the great death - continent , the continent that destroy again what the other continent have build up ? the continent whose spirit of place fight purely to pick the eye out of the face of God ? be that America ? 

 and all the people who go there , Europeans , Negroes , Japanese , Chinese , all the colour and the race , be they the spend people , in whom the God impulse have collapse , so they cross to the great continent of the negation , where the human will declare itself ' free ' , to pull down the soul of the world ? be it so ? and do this account for the great drift to the New World , the drift of spend soul pass over to the side of godless democracy , energetic negation ? the negation which be the life - breath of materialism . and would the great negative pull of the Americans at last break the heart of the world ? 

 this thought would come to she , time and again . 

 she herself , what have she come to America for ? 

 because the flow of her life have break , and she know she could not re - start it in Europe . 

 these handsome native ! be it because they be death - worshipper , Moloch - worshipper , that they be so uncowed and handsome ? their pure acknowledgment of death and their undaunted admission of nothingness keep so erect and careless . 

 white man have have a soul , and lose it . the pivot of fire have be quench in they , and their life have start to spin in the reversed direction , widdershin . that reverse look which be in the eye of so many white people , the look of nullity , and life wheel in the reversed direction . widdershin . 

 but the dark - face native , with their strange soft flame of life wheel upon a dark void : be they centreless and widdershin too , as so many white man now be ? 

 the strange , soft flame of courage in the black mexican eye . but still it be not knit to a centre , that centre which be the soul of a man in a man . 

 and all the effort of white man to bring the soul of the dark man of Mexico into final clinched being have result in nothing but the collapse of the white man . against the soft , dark flow of the Indian the white man at last collapse ; with his God and his energy he collapse . in attempt to convert the dark man to the white man 's way of life , the white man have fall helplessly down the hole he want to fill up . seek to save another man 's soul , the white man lose his own , and collapse upon himself . 

 Mexico ! the great , precipitous , dry , savage country , with a handsome church in every landscape , rise as it be out of nothing . a revolution - break landscape , with lingering , tall , handsome church whose dome be like inflation that be go to burst , and whose pinnacle and tower be like the tremble pagoda of an unreal race . gorgeous church wait , above the hut and straw hovel of the native , like ghost to be dismiss . 

 and noble ruin hacienda , with ruined avenue approach their broken splendour . 

 and the city of Mexico , great and small , that the Spaniards conjure up out of nothing . stone live and die with the spirit of the builder . and the spirit of Spaniards in Mexico die , and the very stone in the building die . the native drift into the centre of the plazas again , and in unspeakable empty weariness the spanish building stand around , in a sort of dry exhaustion . 

 the conquered race ! Cortés come with his iron heel and his iron will , a conqueror . but a conquered race , unless graft with a new inspiration , slowly suck the blood of the conqueror , in the silence of a strange night and the heaviness of a hopeless will . so that now , the race of the conqueror in Mexico be soft and boneless , child cry in helpless hopelessness . 

 be it the dark negation of the continent ? 

 Kate could not look at the stone of the National Museum in Mexico without depression and dread . snake coil like excrement , snake fange and feather beyond all dream of dread . and that be all . 

 the ponderous pyramid of San Juan Teotihuacan , the House of Quetzalcoatl wreathe with the snake of all snake , his huge fang white and pure to - day as in the lose century when his maker be alive . he have not die . he be not so dead as the spanish church , this all - enwreathe dragon of the horror of Mexico . 

 Cholula , with its church where the altar be ! and the same ponderousness , the same unspeakable sense of weight and downward pressure of the blunt pyramid . down - sink pressure and depression . and the great market - place with its linger dread and fascination . 

 Mitla under its hill , in the parch valley where a wind blow the dust and the dead soul of the vanish race in terrible gust . the carve court of Mitla , with a hard , sharp - angle , intricate fascination , but the fascination of fear and repellence . hard , four - square , sharp - edge , cutting , zig - zagge Mitla , like continual blow of a stone axe . without gentleness or grace or charm . oh America , with your unspeakable hard lack of charm , what then be your final meaning ? be it forever the knife of sacrifice , as you put out your tongue at the world ? 

 Charmless America ! with your hard , vindictive beauty , be you wait forever to smite death ? be the world your everlasting victim ? 

 so long as it will let itself be victimize . 

 but yet ! but yet ! the gentle voice of the native . the voice of the boy , like bird twitter among the tree of the plaza of Tehuacan ! the soft touch , the gentleness . be it the dark - finger quietness of death , and the music of the presence of death in their voice ? 

 she think again of what Don Ram n have say to she . 

 ' they pull you down ! Mexico pull you down , the people pull you down like a great weight ! but it may be they pull you down as the earth 's pull of gravitation do , that you can balance on your foot . maybe they draw you down as the earth draw down the root of a tree , so that it may be clinch deep in soil . man be still part of the Tree of Life , and the root go down to the centre of the earth . loose leaf , and aeroplane , blow away on the wind , in what they call freedom . but the Tree of Life have fix , deep , grip root . 

 ' it may be you need to be draw down , down , till you send root into the deep place again . then you can send up the sap and the leaf back to the sky , later . 

 ' and to I , the man in Mexico be like tree , forest that the white man fell in their coming . but the root of the tree be deep and alive and forever send up new shoot . 

 ' and each new shoot that come up overthrow a spanish church or an american factory . and soon the dark forest will rise again , and shake the spanish building from the face of America . 

 ' all that matter to I be the root that reach down beyond all destruction . the root and the life be there . what else it need be the word , for the forest to begin to rise again . and some man among man must speak the word . ' 

 the strange doom - like sound of the man 's word ! but in spite of the sense of doom on her heart , she would not go away yet . she would stay long in Mexico . 

 

 

 CHAPTER V 

 The Lake 

 

 Owen leave , villier stay on a few day to escort Kate to the lake . if she like it there , and could find a house , she could stay by herself . she know sufficient people in Mexico and in Guadalajara to prevent she from be lonely . but she still shrink from travel alone in this country . 

 she want to leave the city . the new President have come in quietly enough , but there be an ugly feeling of uppishness in the low class , the bottom dog clamber mangily to the top . Kate be no snob . man or woman , she care nothing about the social class . but meanness , sordidness she hat . she hat bottom dog . they all be mangy , they all be full of envy and malice , many have the rabie . ah no , let we defend ourselves from the bottom dog , with its mean growl and its yellow tooth . 

 she have tea with Cipriano before leave . 

 ' how do you get along with the government ? ' she ask . 

 ' I stand for the law and the constitution , ' he say . ' they know I do not   want anything to do with cuartelazos or revolution . Don Ram n be my chief . ' 

 ' in what way ? ' 

 ' later , you will see . ' 

 he have a secret , important to himself , on which he be sit tight . but he look at she with shin eye , as much as to say that soon she would share the secret , and then he would be much happy . 

 he watch she curiously , from under his wary black lash . she be one of the rather plump Irishwomen , with soft brown hair and hazel eye , and a beautiful , rather distant repose . her great charm be her soft repose , and her gentle , unconscious inaccessibility . she be tall and big than Cipriano : he be almost boyishly small . but he be all energy , and his eyebrow tilt black and with a barbarian conceit , above his full , almost insolent black eye . 

 he watch she continually , with a kind of fascination : the same spell that the absurd little figure of the doll Madonna have cast over he as a boy . she be the mystery , and he the adorer , under the semi - ecstatic spell of the mystery . but once he rise from his knee , he rise in the same strutting conceit of himself as before he kneel : with all his adoration in his pocket again . but he have a good deal of magnetic power . his education have not diminish it . his education lie like a film of white oil on the black lake of his barbarian consciousness . for this reason , the thing he say be hardly interesting at all . only what he be . he make the air around he seem dark , but rich and fuller . sometimes his presence be extraordinarily grateful , like a healing of the blood . and sometimes he be an intolerable weight on she . she gasp to get away from he . 

 ' you think a great deal of Don Ram n ? ' she say to he . 

 ' yes , ' he say , his black eye watch she . ' he be a very fine man . ' 

 how trivial the word sound ! that be another boring thing about he : his English seem so trivial . he be not   really express himself . he be only flip at the white oil that lie on his surface . 

 ' you like he well than the Bishop , your god - father ? ' 

 he lift his shoulder in a twisted , embarrassed shrug . 

 ' the same ! ' he say . ' I like he the same . ' 

 then he look away into the distance , with a certain hauteur and insolence . 

 ' very different , no ? ' he say . ' but in some way , the same . he know well what be Mexico . he know well what I be . Bishop Severn do not know the real Mexico : how could he , he be a sincere Catholic ! but Don Ram n know the real Mexico , no ? ' 

 ' and what be the real Mexico ? ' she ask . 

 ' well - you must ask Don Ram n. I can not   explain . ' 

 she ask Cipriano about go to the lake . 

 ' yes ! ' he say . ' you can go ! you will like it . go first to Orilla , no ? - you take a ticket on the railway to Ixtlahuacan . and in Orilla be an hotel with a german manager . then from Orilla you can go in a motor - boat , in a few hour , to Sayula . and there you will find a house to live in . ' 

 he want she to do this , she could tell . 

 ' how far be Don Ram n 's hacienda from Sayula ? ' she ask . 

 ' near ! about an hour in a boat . he be there now . and at the beginning of the month I be go with my division to Guadalajara : now there be a new governor . so I shall be quite near too . ' 

 ' that will be nice , ' she say . 

 ' you think so ? ' he ask quickly . 

 ' yes , ' she say , on her guard , look at he slowly . ' I should be sorry to lose touch with Don Ram n and you . ' 

 he have a little tension on his brow , haughty , unwilling , conceited , and at the same time , yearning and desirous . 

 ' you like Don Ram n very much ? ' he say . ' you want to know he more ? ' 

 there be a peculiar anxiety in his voice . 

 ' yes , ' she say . ' one know so few people in the world nowadays , that one can respect - and fear a little . I be a little afraid of Don Ram n : and I have the great respect for he - ' she end on a hot note of sincerity . 

 ' it be good ! ' he say . ' it be very good . you may respect he more than any other man in the world . ' 

 ' perhaps that be true , ' she say , turn her eye slowly to his . 

 ' yes ! yes ! ' he cry impatiently . ' it be true . you will find out later . and Ram n like you . he tell I to ask you to come to the lake . when you come to Sayula , when you be come , write to he , and no doubt he can tell you about a house , and all those thing . ' 

 ' shall I ? ' she say , hesitant . 

 ' yes . yes ! of course , we say what we mean . ' 

 curious little man , with his odd , inflammable hauteur and conceit , something burn inside he , that give he no peace . he have an almost childish faith in the other man . and yet she be not sure that he do not , in some corner of his soul , resent Ram n somewhat . 

 Kate set off by the night train for the west , with villier . the one Pullman coach be full : people go to Guadalajara and Colima and the coast . there be three military officer , rather shy in their new uniform , and rather swagger at the same time , make eye at the empty air , as if they feel they be conspicuous , and sit quickly in their seat , as if to obliterate themselves . there be two country farmer or rancher , in tight trouser and cartwheel hat stitch with silver . one be a tall man with a big moustache , the other be a small , grey man . but they both have the handsome , alive leg of the Mexicans , and the rather quench face . there be a widow bury in crape , accompany by a criada , a maid . the rest be townsman , Mexicans on business , at once shy and fussy , unobtrusive and self - important . 

 the Pullman be clean and neat , with its hot green - plush seat . but , full of people , it seem empty compare with a Pullman in the United States . everybody be very quiet , very soft and guard . the farmer fold their beautiful serape and lay they carefully on the seat , sit as if their section be a lonely little place . the officer fold their cloak and arrange dozen of little parcel , little cardboard hatbox and heterogeneous bundle , under the seat and on the seat . the business man have the oddest luggage , canvas hold - all embroider in wool , with long , touching motto . 

 and in all the crowd a sense of guardedness and softness and self - effacement : a curious soft sensibilité , touch with fear . it be already a somewhat conspicuous thing to travel in the Pullman ; you have to be on your guard . 

 the evening for once be grey : the rainy season really approach . a sudden wind whirl dust and a few spot of rain . the train draw out of the formless , dry , dust - smite area fringe the city , and wound mildly on for a few minute , only to stop in the main street of Tacubaya , the suburb - village . in the grey approach of evening the train halt heavily in the street , and Kate look out at the man who stand in group , with their hat tilt against the wind and their blanket fold over their shoulder and up to their eye , against the dust , motionless , stand like sombre ghost , only a glint of eye show between the dark serape and the big hat - brim ; while donkey - driver in a dust - cloud run frantically , with uplifted arm like demon , utter short , sharp cry to prevent their donkey from poke in between the coach of the train . silent dog trot in - and - out under the train , woman , their face wrap in their blue rebozos , come to offer tortilla fold in a cloth to keep they warm , or pulque in an earthenware mug , or piece of chicken smother in red , thick , oily sauce ; or orange or banana or pitahayas , anything . and when few people buy , because of the dust , the woman put their ware under their arm , under the blue rebozo , and cover their face and motionless watch the train . 

 it be about six o'clock . the earth be utterly dry and stale . somebody be kindle charcoal in front of a house . man be hurry down the wind , balance their great hat curiously . horseman on quick , fine little horse , gun sling behind , trot up to the train , lingered , then trot quickly away again into nowhere . 

 still the train stand in the street . Kate and Villiers get down . they watch the spark blow from the charcoal which a little girl be kindle in the street , to cook tortilla . 

 the train have a second - class coach and a first - class . the second class be jam - full of peasant , Indians , pile in like chicken with their bundle and basket and bottle , endless thing . one woman have a fine peacock under her arm . she put it down and in vain try to suppress it beneath her voluminous skirt . it refuse to be suppress . she take it up and balance it on her knee and look round again over the medley of jar , basket , pumpkin , melon , gun , bundle , and human being . 

 in the front be a steel car with a guard of little scrubby soldier in their dirty cotton uniform . some soldier be mount on top of the train with their gun : the look - out . 

 and the whole train , seethe with life , be curiously still , subdue . perhaps it be the perpetual sense of danger which make the people so hush , without clamour or stridency . and with an odd , hush politeness among they . a sort of demon - world . 

 at last the train move on . if it have wait forever , no one would have be deeply surprised . for what might not be ahead ? rebel , bandit , bridge blow up - anything . 

 however , quietly , stealthily , the train move out and along the great weary valley . the circle mountain , so relentless , be invisible save near at hand . in a few broken adobe hut a bit of fire spark red . the adobe be grey - black , of the lava dust , depress . into the distance the field spread dry , with here and there patch of green irrigation . there be a broken hacienda with column that support nothing . darkness be come , dust still blow in the shadow ; the valley seem encompass in a dry , stale , weary gloom . 

 then there come a heavy shower . the train be pass a pulque hacienda . the row of the giant maguey stretch bristle their iron - black barb in the gloom . 

 all at once , the light come on , the Pullman attendant come swiftly lower the blind , so that the brilliance of the window should attract no bullet from the dark outside . 

 there be a poor little meal at exorbitant price , and when this be clear away , the attendant come with a clash to make the bed , pull down the upper berth . it be only eight o'clock , and the passenger look up in resentment . but no good . the pug - face Mexican in charge , and his smallpox - pit assistant , insolently come in between the seat , insert the key overhead , and bring down the berth with a crash . and the mexican passenger humbly crawl away to the smoking - room or the toilet , like whip dog . 

 at half - past eight everybody be silently and with intense discretion go to bed . none of the collar - stud - snap bustle and ' homely ' familiarity of the United States . like subdued animal they all creep in behind their green serge curtain . 

 Kate hat a Pullman , the discreet indiscretion , the horrible nearness of other people , like so many larvae in so many section , behind the green serge curtain . above all , the horrible intimacy of the noise of go to bed . she hat to undress , struggle in the oven of her berth , with her elbow butt into the stomach of the attendant who be button up the green curtain outside . 

 and yet , once she be in bed and could put out her light and raise the window - blind , she have to admit it be well than a wagon - light in Europe : and perhaps the good that can be do for people who must travel through the night in train . 

 there be a rather cold wind , after the rain , up there on that high plateau . the moon have rise , the sky be clear . rock , and tall organ cactus , and more mile of maguey . then the train stop at a dark little station on the rim of the slope , where man swathe in dark serape hold dusky , ruddy lantern that light up no face at all , only dark gap . why do the train stay so long ? be something wrong ? 

 at last they be go again . under the moon she see beyond she a long downslope of rock and cactus , and in the distance below , the light of a town . she lie in her berth watch the train wind slowly down the wild , rugged slope . then she doze . 

 to wake at a station that look like a quiet inferno , with dark face come near the window , glitter eye in the half - light , woman in their rebozo run along the train balance dish of meat , tamale , tortilla on one hand , black - face man with fruit and sweet , and all call in a subdue , intense , hush hubbub . strange and glaring , she see eye at the dark screen of the Pullman , sudden hand thrust up something to sell . in fear , Kate drop her window . the wire screen be not enough . 

 the platform below the Pullman be all dark . but at the back of the train she could see the glare of the first - class window , on the dark station . and a man sell sweet - meat - Cajetas ! cajeta ! La de Celaya ! 

 she be safe inside the Pullman , with nothing to do but to listen to an occasional cough behind the green curtain , and to feel the faint bristling apprehension of all the Mexicans in their dark berth . the dark Pullman be full of a subdue apprehension , fear lest there might be some attack on the train . 

 she go to sleep and wake at a bright station : probably Queretaro . the green tree look theatrical in the electric light . opale ! she hear the man call softly . if Owen have be there he would have get up in his pyjama to buy opal . the call would have be too strong . 

 she sleep fitfully , in the shaken saloon , vaguely aware of station and the deep night of the open country . then she start from a complete sleep . the train be dead still , no sound . then a tremendous jerking as the Pullman be shunt . it must be Irapuato , where they branch to the west . 

 she would arrive at Ixtlahuacan soon after six in the morning . the man wake she at daybreak , before the sun have rise . Dry country with mesquite bush , in the dawn : then green wheat alternating with ripe wheat . and man already in the pale , ripen wheat reaping with sickle , cut short little handfuls from the short straw . a bright sky , with a bluish shadow on earth . parch slope with ragged maize stubble . then a forlorn hacienda and a man on horseback , in a blanket , drive a silent flock of cow , sheep , bull , goat , lamb , ripple a bit ghostly in the dawn , from under a tottering archway . a long canal beside the railway , a long canal pave with bright green leaf from which poke the mauve head of the lirio , the water hyacinth . the sun be lift up , red . in a moment it be the full , dazzle gold of a mexican morning . 

 Kate be dressed and ready , sit face villier , when they come to Ixtlahuacan . the man carry out her bag . the train drift in to a desert of a station . they get down . it be a new day . 

 in the powerful light of morning , under a turquoise - blue sky , she gaze at the helpless - look station , railway line , some stand truck , and a remote lifelessness . a boy seize their bag and run across the line to the station yard , which be pave with cobblestone , but overgrow with weed . at one side stand an old tram - car with two mule , like a relic . one or two man , swathe up to the eye in scarlet blanket , be cross on silent white leg . 

 ' adonde ? ' say the boy . 

 but Kate go to see her big luggage take out . it be all there .

 occasional man on horseback clatter suddenly by , occasional big man in scarlet serape go noiselessly on their own way , under the big hat . a boy on a high mule be deliver milk from red globe - shape jar sling on either side his mount . the street be stony , uneven , vacuous , sterile . the stone seem dead , the town seem make of dead stone . the human life come with a slow , sterile unwillingness , in spite of the low - hung power of the sun .

 the tram stop and they get down . the boy get down with the bag , and tell they they must go to the river to take a boat . 

 they follow obediently down the smash pavement , where every moment you might twist your ankle or break your leg . everywhere the same weary indifference and brokenness , a sense of dirt and of helplessness , squalor of far - go indifference , under the perfect morning sky , in the pure sunshine and the pure mexican air . the sense of life ebb away , leave dry ruin . 

 they come to the edge of the town , to a dusty , humped bridge , a broken wall , a pale - brown stream flow full . below the bridge a cluster of man . 

 each one want she to hire his boat . she demand a motor - boat : the boat from the hotel . they say there be not   one . she do not   believe it . then a dark - face fellow with his black hair down his forehead , and a certain intensity in his eye , say : yes , yes ; the hotel have a boat , but it be break . she must take a row - boat . in an hour and a half he would row she there . 

 ' how long ? ' say Kate . 

 ' an hour and a half . ' 

 ' and I be so hungry ! ' cry Kate . ' how much do you charge ? ' 

 ' two peso . ' he hold up two finger . 

 Kate say yes , and he run down to his boat . then she notice he be a cripple with inturne foot . but how quick and strong !
