 the crippled boatman be pull hard , with great strength and energy . when she speak to he in her bad Spanish and he find it hard to understand , he knit his brow a little , anxiously . and when she laugh he smile at she with such a beautiful gentleness , sensitive , wistful , quick . she feel he be naturally honest and truthful , and generous . there be a beauty in these man , a wistful beauty and a great physical strength . why have she feel so bitterly about the country ? 

 Morning be still young on the pale buff river , between the silent earthen bank . there be a blue dimness in the low air , and black water - fowl run swiftly , unconcernedly back and forth from the river 's edge , on the dry , baked bank that be treeless now , and wider . they have enter a wide river , from the narrow one . the blueness and moistness of the dissolve night seem to linger under the scatter pepper - tree of the far shore . 

 the boatman row short and hard upon the flimsy , soft , sperm - like water , only pause at moment swiftly to smear the sweat from his face with an old rag he keep on the bench beside he . the sweat run from his bronze - brown skin like water , and the black hair on his high - dome , indian head smoke with wetness . 

 ' there be no hurry , ' say Kate , smile to he . 

 ' what do the Señorita say ? ' 

 ' there be no hurry , ' she repeat . 

 he pause , smile , breathe deeply , and explain that now he be row against stream . this wide river flow out of the lake , full and heavy . see ! even as he rest a moment , the boat begin to turn and drift ! he quickly take his oar . 

 the boat move slowly , in the hush of departed night , upon the soft , full - flow buff water , that carry little tuft of float water - hyacinth . some willow - tree stand near the edge , and some pepper - tree of most delicate green foliage . beyond the tree and the level of the shore , big hill rise up to high , blunt point , bake incredibly dry , like biscuit . the blue sky settle against they nakedly ; they be leafless and lifeless save for the iron - green shafts of the organ cactus , that glisten blackly , yet atmospherically , in the ochreous aridity . this be Mexico again , stark - dry and luminous with powerful light , cruel and unreal . 

 on a flat near the river a peon , perch on the rump of his ass , be slowly drive five luxurious cow towards the water to drink . the big black - and - white animal step in a dream - pace past the pepper - tree to the bank , like move piece of light - and - shade : the dun cow trail after , in the incredible silence and brilliance of the morning . 

 Earth , air , water be all silent with new light , the last blue of night dissolve like a breath . no sound , even no life . the great light be strong than life itself . only , up in the blue , some turkey - buzzard be wheel with dirty - edge wing , as everywhere in Mexico . 

 ' do not   hurry ! ' Kate say again to the boatman , who be again mop his face , while his black hair run sweat . ' we can go slowly . ' 

 the man smile deprecatingly . 

 ' if the Señorita will sit in the back , ' he say . 

 Kate do not understand his request at first . he have row in towards a bend in the right bank , to be out of the current . on the left bank Kate have notice some man bath : man whose wet skin flash with the beautiful brown - rose colour and glitter of the naked native , and one stout man with the curious creamy - biscuit skin of the city Mexicans . low against the water across - stream she watch the glitter of naked man , half - immerse in the river . 

 she rise to step back into the stern of the boat , where villier be . as she do so , she see a dark head and the flash ruddy shoulder of a man swim towards the boat . she waver - and as she be sit down , the man stand up in the water and be wad near , the water washing at the loose little cloth he have round his loin . he be smooth and wet and of a lovely colour , with the rich smooth - muscle physique of the Indians . he be come towards the boat , push back his hair from his forehead . 

 the boatman watch he , transfix , without surprise , a little subtle half - smile , perhaps of mockery , round his nose . as if he have expect it ! 

 ' where be you go ? ' ask the man in the water , the brown river run softly at his strong thigh . 

 the boatman wait a moment for his patron to answer , then , see they be silent , reply in a low , unwilling tone : 

 ' Orilla . ' 

 the man in the water take hold of the stern of the boat , as the boatman softly touch the water with the oar to keep she straight , and he throw back his longish black hair with a certain effrontery . 

 ' do you know whom the lake belong to ? ' he ask , with the same effrontery . 

 ' what do you say ? ' ask Kate , haughtily . 

 ' if you know whom the lake belong to ? ' the young man in the water repeat . 

 ' to whom ? ' say Kate , fluster . 

 ' to the old god of Mexico , ' the stranger say . ' you have to make a tribute to Quetzalcoatl if you go on the lake . ' 

 the strange calm effrontery of it ! but truly Mexican . 

 ' how ? ' say Kate . 

 ' you can give I something , ' he say . 

 ' but why should I give something to you , if it be a tribute to Quetzalcoatl ? ' she stammer . 

 ' I be Quetzalcoatl 's man , I , ' he reply , with calm effrontery . 

 ' and if I do not   give you anything ? ' she say . 

 he lift his shoulder and spread his free hand , stagger a little , lose his footing in the water as he do so . 

 ' if you wish to make an enemy of the lake - ' he say , coolly , as he recover his balance . 

 and then for the first time he look straight at she . and as he do so , the demonish effrontery die down again , and the peculiar american tension slacken and leave he . 

 he give a slight wave of dismissal with his free hand , and push the boat gently forward . 

 ' but it do not   matter , ' he say , with a slight insolent jerk of his head sideways , and a faint , insolent smile . ' we will wait till the Morning Star rise . ' 

 the boatman softly but powerfully pull the oar . the man in the water stand with the sun on his powerful chest , look after the boat in half - see abstraction . his eye have take again the peculiar gleam far - awayness , suspend between the reality , which , Kate suddenly realize , be the central look in the native eye . the boatman , row away , be glance back at the man who stand in the water , and his face , too , have the abstract , transfigure look of a man perfectly suspend between the world 's two strenuous wing of energy . a look of extraordinary , arrest beauty , the silent , vulnerable centre of all life 's quivering , like the nucleus gleam in tranquil suspense , within a cell . 

 ' what do he mean , ' say Kate , ' by " we will wait till the Morning Star rise " ? ' 

 the man smile slowly . 

 ' it be a name , ' he say . 

 and he seem to know no more . but the symbolism have evidently the power to soothe and sustain he . 

 ' why do he come and speak to we ? ' ask Kate . 

 ' he be one of those of the god Quetzalcoatl , Señorita . ' 

 ' and you ? be you one too ? ' 

 ' who know ! ' say the man , put his head on one side . then he add : ' I think so . we be many . ' 

 he watch Kate 's face with that gleaming , intense semi - abstraction , a gleam that hang unwavering in his black eye , and which suddenly remind Kate of the morning star , or the evening star , hang perfect between night and the sun . 

 ' you have the morning star in your eye , ' she say to the man . 

 he flash she a smile of extraordinary beauty . 

 ' the Señorita understand , ' he say . 

 his face change again to a dark - brown mask , like semi - transparent stone , and he row with all his might . ahead , the river be widen , the bank be grow low , down to the water 's level , like shoal plant with willow - tree and with reed . above the willow - tree a square white sail be stand , as if erect on the land . 

 ' be the lake so near ? ' say Kate . 

 the man hastily mop his run wet face . 

 ' yes , Señorita ! the sailing - boat be wait for the wind , to come into the river . we will pass by the canal . ' 

 he indicate with a backward movement of the head a narrow , twist passage of water between deep reed . it make Kate think of the little river Anapo : the same mystery unbroken . the boatman , with crease half of sadness and half of exaltation in his bronze , still face , be pull with all his might . water - fowl go swim into the reed , or rise on wing and wheel into the blue air . some willow - tree hang a dripping , vivid green , in the stark dry country . the stream be narrow and winding . with a nonchalant motion , first of the right then of the left hand , Villiers be guide the boatman , to keep he from run aground in the winding , narrow water - way . 

 and this put villier at his ease , to have something practical and slightly mechanical to do and to assert . he be strike the american note once more , of mechanical dominance . 

 all the other business have leave he incomprehending , and when he ask Kate , she have pretend not to hear he . she sense a certain delicate , tender mystery in the river , in the naked man in the water , in the boatman , and she could not bear to have it subject to the tough american flippancy . she be weary to death of american automatism and american flippant toughness . it give she a feeling of nausea . 

 ' quite a well - build fellow , that one who lay hold of the boat . what do he want , anyway ? ' villier insist . 

 ' nothing ! ' say Kate . 

 they be slip out past the clay - colour , loose stony edge of the land , through a surge of ripple , into the wide white light of the lake . a breeze be come from the east , out of the upright morning , and the surface of the shallow , flimsy , dun - colour water be in motion . shoal - water rustle near at hand . out to the open , large , square white sail be step gingerly forward , and beyond the buff - colour , pale desert of water rise far - away blue , sharp hill of the other side , many mile away , pure pale blue with distance , yet sharp - edged and clear in form . 

 ' now , ' say the boatman , smile to Kate , ' it be easy . now we be out of the current . ' 

 he pull rhythmically through the frail - rippling , sperm - like water , with a sense of peace . and for the first time Kate feel she have meet the mystery of the native , the strange and mysterious gentleness between a scylla and a charybdis of violence ; the small poised , perfect body of the bird that wave wing of thunder and wing of fire and night in its flight . but central between the flash of day and the black of night , between the flash of lightning and the break of thunder , the still , soft body of the bird poise and soaring , forever . the mystery of the evening - star brilliant in silence and distance between the downward - surge plunge of the sun and the vast , hollow seething of inpoure night . the magnificence of the watchful morning - star , that watch between the night and the day , the gleam clue to the two opposite . 

 this kind of frail , pure sympathy , she feel at the moment between herself and the boatman , between herself and the man who have speak from the water . and she be not go to have it break by villier ' american joke . 

 there be a sound of break water . the boatman draw away , and point across to where a canoa , a native sailing - boat , be lie at an angle . she have run aground in a wind , and now must wait till another wind would carry she off the submerged bank again . another boat be come down the breeze , steer cautiously among the shoal , for the river outlet . she be pile high with petate , the native leaf mat , above her hollowed black side . and bare - legged man with loose white drawer roll up , and brown chest show , be run with pole as the shallow heave up again , push she off , and balance their huge hat with small , bird - like shake of the head . 

 beyond the boat , seaward , be rock outcrop and strange bird like pelican stand in silhouette , motionless . 

 they have be cross a bay of the lake - shore , and be near the hotel . it stand on a parch dry bank above the pale - brown water , a long , low building amid a tender green of banana and pepper - tree . everywhere the shore rise up pale and cruelly dry , dry to cruelty , and on the little hill the dark statue of the organ cactus poise in nothingness . 

 there be a break - down landing - place , and a boat - house in the distance , and someone in white flannel trouser be stand on the broken masonry . upon the filmy water duck and black water - fowl bobbed like cork . the bottom be stony . the boatman suddenly back the boat , and pull round . he push up his sleeve and hang over the bow , reach into the water . with a quick motion he grab something , and scramble into the boat again . he be hold in the pale - skin hollow of his palm a little earthenware pot , crust by the lake deposit . 

 ' what be it ? ' she say . 

 ' Ollita of the god , ' he say . ' of the old dead god . take it , Señorita . ' 

 ' you must let I pay for it , ' she say . 

 ' no , Señorita . it be your , ' say the man , with that sensitive , masculine sincerity which come sometimes so quickly from a native . 

 it be a little , rough round pot with protuberance . 

 ' look ! ' say the man , reach again for the little pot . he turn it upside - down , and she see cut - in eye and the sticking - out ear of an animal 's head . 

 ' a cat ! ' she exclaim . ' it be a cat . ' 

 ' or a coyote ! ' 

 ' a coyote ! ' 

 ' let us look ! ' say villier . ' why , how awfully interesting ! do you think it be old ? ' 

 ' it be old ? ' Kate ask . 

 ' the time of the old god , ' say the boatman . then with a sudden smile : ' the dead god do not   eat much rice , they only want little casserole while they be bone under the water . ' and he look she in the eye . 

 ' while they be bone ? ' she repeat . and she realize he mean the skeleton of god that can not die . 

 they be at the landing - stage ; or rather , at the heap of collapse masonry which have once be a landing - stage . the boatman get out and hold the boat steady while Kate and Villiers land . then he scramble up with the bag . 

 the man in white trouser , and a mozo appear . it be the hotel manager . Kate pay the boatman . 

 ' Adi s , Señorita ! ' he say with a smile . ' may you go with Quetzalcoatl . ' 

 ' yes ! ' she cry . ' good - bye ! ' 

 they go up the slope between the tattered banana , whose ragged leaf be make a hush , distant patter in the breeze . the green fruit curve out its bristly - soft bunch , the purple flower - bud depend stiffly . 

 the german manager come to talk to they : a young man of about forty , with his blue eye go opaque and stony behind his spectacle , though the centre be keen . evidently a German who have be many year out in Mexico - out in the lonely place . the rather stiff look , the slight look of fear in the soul - not physical fear - and the look of defeat , characteristic of the European who have long be subject to the unbroken spirit of place ! but the defeat be in the soul , not the will . 

 he show Kate to her room in the unfinished quarter , and order her breakfast . the hotel consist of an old low ranch - house with a veranda - and this be the dining - room , lounge , kitchen , and office . then there be a two - storey new wing , with a smart bathroom between each two bedroom , and almost up - to - date fitting : very incongruous . 

 but the new wing be unfinishe - have be unfinished for a dozen year and more , the work abandon when Porfirio Diaz flee . now it would probably never be finish . 

 and this be Mexico . whatever pretentiousness and modern improvement it may have , outside the capital , they be either smash or raw and unfinished , with rusty bone of iron girder stick out . 

 Kate wash her hand and go down to breakfast . before the long veranda of the old ranch - house the green pepper - tree drop like green light , and small cardinal bird with scarlet body and blaze impertinent head like poppy - bud flash among the pinkish pepper - head , close their brown wing upon the audacity of their glow redness . a train of geese pass in the glare sun , automatic , towards the eternal tremble of pale , earth - colour water beyond the stone . 

 it be a place with a strange atmosphere : stony , hard , break , with round cruel hill and the many - flute bunch of the organ - cactus behind the old house , and an ancient road trail past , deep in ancient dust . a touch of mystery and cruelty , the stoniness of fear , a lingering , cruel sacredness . 

 Kate loiter hungrily , and be glad when the Mexican in shirt - sleeve and patched trouser , another linger remnant of Don Porfirio 's day , bring she her egg and coffee . 

 he be mute as everything about the place seem mute , even the very stone and the water . only those poppy on wing , the cardinal bird , give a sense of liveliness : and they be uncanny . 

 so swiftly one 's mood change ! in the boat she have glimpse the superb rich stillness of the morning - star , the poignant intermediate flash its quiet between the energy of the cosmo . she have see it in the black eye of the native , in the sunrise of the man 's rich , still body , indian - warm . 

 and now again already the silence be of vacuity , arrest , and cruelty : the uncanny empty unbearableness of many mexican morning . already she be uneasy , suffer from the malaise which torture one inwardly in that country of cactus . 

 she go up to her room , pause at the corridor window to look out at the savage little hill that stand at the back of the hotel in desiccated heap , with the dark - green bulk of organ - cactus stick up mechanically and sinister , sombre in all the glare . Grey ground - squirrel like rat slither ceaselessly around . Sinister , strangely dark and sinister , in the great glare of the sun ! 

 she go to her room to be alone . below her window , in the brick and fall rubble of unfinished masonry , a huge white turkey - cock , dim - white , strut with his brown hen . and sometimes he stretch out his pink wattle and give vent to fierce , powerful turkey - yelps , like some strong dog yelping ; or else he ruffle all his feather like a great , soil white peony , and chuff , hiss here and there , rag the metal of his plumage . 

 below he , the eternal tremble of pale - earth , unreal water , far beyond which rise the stiff resistance of mountain lose their pristine blue . distinct , frail distance far off on the dry air , dim - seeing , yet sharp and edge with menace . 

 Kate take her bath in the filmy water that be hardly like water at all . then she go and sit on the collapsed masonry , in the shade of the boat - house below . small white duck bob about on the shallow water below she , or dive , raise cloud of submarine dust . a canoe come paddle in ; a lean fellow with sinewy brown leg . he answer Kate 's nod with the aloof promptness of an Indian , make fast his canoe inside the boat - house , and be go , step silent and barefoot over the bright green water - stone , and leave a shadow , cold as flint , on the air behind he . 

 no sound on the morning save a faint touching of water , and the occasional powerful yelping of the turkey - cock . Silence , an aboriginal , empty silence , as of life withhold . the vacuity of a mexican morning . resound sometimes to the turkey - cock . 

 and the great , lymphatic expanse of water , like a sea , trembling , trembling , tremble to a far distance , to the mountain of substantial nothingness . 

 near at hand , a ragged shifting of banana - tree , bare hill with immobile cactus , and to the left , an hacienda with peon 's square mud box of house . an occasional ranchero in skintight trouser and big hat ride trot through the dust on a small horse , or peon on the rump of their ass , in floppy white cotton , go like ghost . 

 always something ghostly . the morning pass all of a piece , empty , vacuous . all sound withhold , all life withhold , everything hold back . the land so dry as to have a quality of invisibility , the water earth - filmy , hardly water at all . the lymphatic milk of fish , somebody say . 

 

 

 CHAPTER VI 

 the move down the Lake 

 

 in Porfirio Diaz ' day , the lake - side begin to be the Riviera of Mexico , and Orilla be to be the Nice , or at least the Mentone of the country . but revolution start erupt again , and in 1911 Don Porfirio flee to Paris with , it be say , thirty million gold peso in his pocket : a peso be half a dollar , nearly half - a - crown . but we need not believe all that be say , especially by a man 's enemy . 

 during the subsequent revolution , Orilla , which have begin to be a winter paradise for the Americans , lapse back into barbarism and broken brickwork . in 1921 a feeble new start have be make . 

 the place belong to a german - mexican family , who also own the adjacent hacienda . they acquire the property from the American Hotel Company , who have undertake to develop the lake - shore , and who have go bankrupt during the various revolution . 

 the german - mexican owner be not popular with the native . an angel from heaven would not have be popular , these year , if he have be know as the owner of property . however , in 1921 the hotel be very modestly open again , with an american manager . 

 towards the end of the year , José , son of the german - mexican owner , come to stay with his wife and child in the hotel , in the new wing . José be a bit of a fool , as most foreigner be , after the first generation in Mexico . have business to settle , he go into Guadalajara to the bank and return with a thousand gold peso in a bag , keep the matter , as he think , a dead secret . 

 everyone have just go to bed , on a brilliant moonlight night in winter , when two man appear in the yard calling for José : they have to speak to he . José , suspect nothing , leave his wife and two child , and go down . in a moment he call for the american manager . the manager , think it be some bargaining to be do , also come down . as he come out of the door , two man seize he by the arm , and say : ' do not   make a noise ! ' 

 ' what be amiss ? ' say Bell , who have build up Orilla , and have be twenty year on the lake . 

 then he notice that two other man have hold of José . ' come , ' they say . 

 there be five Mexicans - Indians , or half - Indians - and the two captive . they go , the captive in slipper and shirtsleeve , to the little office away at the end of the other part of the hotel , which have be the old ranch - house . 

 ' what do you want ? ' ask Bell . 

 ' give we the money , ' say the bandit . 

 ' oh , all right , ' say the American . there be a few peso only in the safe . he open , show they , and they take the money . 

 ' now give we the rest , ' they say . 

 ' there be no more , ' say the manager , in all sincerity ; for José have not confess to the thousand peso . 

 the five peon then begin to search the poor little office . they find a pile of red blanket - which they appropriate - and a few bottle of red wine - which they drank . 

 ' now , ' they say , ' give we the money . ' 

 ' I can not   give you what there be not   to give , ' say the manager . 

 ' good ! ' they say , and pull out the hideous machete , the heavy knife of the Mexicans . 

 José , intimidate , produce the suit - case with the thousand peso . the money be wrap up in the corner of a blanket . 

 ' now , come with we , ' say the bandit . 

 ' where to ? ' ask the manager , begin at last to be scared . 

 ' only out on to the hill , where we will leave you , so that you can not telephone to Ixtlahuacan before we have time to get away , ' say the Indians . 

 outside , in the bright moon , the air be chill . the American shiver , in his trouser and shirt and a pair of bedroom slipper . 

 ' let I take a coat , ' he say . 

 ' take a blanket , ' say the tall Indian . 

 he take a blanket , and with two man hold his arm , he follow José , who be likewise hold captive , out of the little gate , across the dust of the road , and up the steep little round hill on which the organ cactus thrust up their sinister clump , like bunch of cruel finger , in the moonlight . the hill be stony and steep , the go slow . José , a fat young man of twenty - eight , protest in the feeble manner of the well - to - do Mexicans . 

 at last they come to the top of the hill . three man take José apart , leave Bell alone near a cactus clump . the moon shine in a perfect Mexican heaven . below , the big lake glimmer faintly , stretch its length towards the west . the air be so clear , the mountain across , thirty mile away , stand sharp and still in the moonlight . and not a sound nor a motion anywhere ! at the foot of the hill be the hacienda , with the peon asleep in their hut . but what help be there in they ? 

 José and the three man have go behind a cactus - tree that stick up straight like a great black bundle of pole , poise on one central foot , and cast a sharp , iron shadow . the American could hear the voice , talk low and rapidly , but could not distinguish the word . his two guard draw away from he a little , to hear what the other be say , behind the cactus . 

 and the American , who know the ground he stand on and the sky that hang over he , feel again the black vibration of death in the air , the black thrill of the death - lust . unmistakable he feel it seethe in the air , as any man may feel it , in Mexico . and the strange aboriginal fiendishness , awake now in the five bandit , communicate itself to his blood . 

 loosen his blanket , he listen tensely in the moonlight . and come the thud ! thud ! thud ! of a machete strike with lust in a human body , then the strange voice of José : ' perd neme ! - forgive I ! ' the murder man cry as he fall . 

 the American wait for no more . drop his blanket , he jump for the cactus cover , and stoop , take the down - slope like a rabbit . the pistol - shot ring out after he , but the Mexicans do not   as a rule take good aim . his bedroom slipper fly off , and barefoot , the man , thin and light , speed down over the stone and the cactus , down to the hotel . 

 when he get down , he find everyone in the hotel awake and shout . 

 ' they be kill José ! ' he say , and he rush to the telephone , expect every moment the five bandit would be on he . 

 the telephone be in the old ranch - building , in the dining - room . there be no answer - no answer - no answer . in her little bedroom over the kitchen , the cook - woman , the traitress , be yell . across in the new wing , a little distance away , José 's mexican wife be scream . one of the servant boy appear . 

 ' try and get the police in Ixtlahuacan , ' say the American , and he run to the new wing , to get his gun and to barricade the door . his daughter , a motherless girl , be cry with Jose 's wife . 

 there be no answer on the telephone . at dawn , the cook , who say the bandit would not hurt a woman , go across to the hacienda to fetch the peon . and when the sun rise , a man be send for the police . 

 they find the body of José , pierce with fourteen hole . the American be carry to Ixtlahuacan , and keep in bed , have cactus spine dig out of his foot by two native woman . 

 the bandit flee across the marsh . month later , they be identify by the steal blanket , away in Michoacan ; and , pursue , one of they betray the other . 

 after this , the hotel be close again , and have be reopen only three month when Kate arrive . 

 but villier come with another story . last year the peon have murder the manager of one of the estate across the lake . they have strip he and leave he naked on his back , with his sexual organ cut off and put into his mouth , his nose slit and pin back , the two half , to his cheek , with long cactus spine . 

 ' tell I no more ! ' say Kate . 

 she feel there be doom write on the very sky , doom and horror . 

 she write to Don Ram n in Sayula , say she want to go back to Europe . true , she herself have see no horror , apart from the bull - fight . and she have have some exquisite moment , as come to this hotel in the boat . the native have a certain mystery and beauty , to she . but she could not bear the unease , and the late sense of horror . 

 true , the peon be poor . they use to work for twenty cent , American , a day ; and now the standard price be fifty cent , or one peso . but then in the old day they receive their wage all the year round . now , only at harvest time or sow time . no work , no pay . and in the long dry season , it be mostly no work . 

 ' still , ' say the german manager of the hotel , a man who have run a rubber plantation in Tabasco , a sugar plantation in the state of Vera Cruz , and an hacienda grow wheat , maize , orange , in Jalisco : ' still , it be not   a question of money with the peon . it do not   start with the peon . it start in Mexico City , with a lot of malcontent who want to put their spoke in the wheel , and who lie hold of pious catchword , to catch the poor . there be no more in it than that . then the agitator go round and infect the peon . it be nothing but a sort of infectious disease , like syphili , all this revolution and socialism . ' 

 ' but why do no one oppose it , ' say Kate . ' why do not   the hacendado put up a fight , instead of cave in and run away ? ' 

 ' the mexican hacendado ! ' the man 's german eye give out a spark . ' the mexican gentleman be such a brave man , that while the soldier be violate his wife on the bed , he be hide under the bed and hold his breath so they shall not   find he . he be as brave as that . ' 

 Kate look away uncomfortably . 

 ' they all want the United States to intervene . they hate the Americans ; but they want the United States to intervene , to save they their money and their property . that be how brave they be ! they hate the Americans personally , but they love they because they can look after money and property . so they want the United States to annex Mexico , the beloved patria ; leave the marvellous green and white and red flag , and the eagle with the snake in its claw , for the sake of appearance and honour ! they be simply bottled full of honour ; of that sort . ' 

 always the same violence of bitterness , Kate think to - herself . and she be so weary of it . how , how weary she be of politic , of the very word ' labour ' and ' socialism ! ' and all that sort ! it suffocate she . 

 ' have you hear of the man of Quetzalcoatl ? ' ask Kate . 

 ' Quetzalcoatl ! ' exclaim the manager , give a little click of the final ' l ' , in a peculiar native fashion . ' that be another try - on of the Bolshevists . they think socialism need a god , so they be go to fish he out of this lake . he will do for another pious catchword in another revolution . ' 

 the man go away , unable to stand any more . 

 ' oh dear ! ' think Kate . ' it really be hard to bear . ' 

 but she want to hear more of Quetzalcoatl . 

 ' do you know , ' she say to the man later , show he the little pot , ' that they find those thing in the lake ? ' 

 ' they be common enough ! ' he say . ' they use to throw they in , in the idolatrous day . may still do so , for what I know . then get they out again to sell to tourist . ' 

 ' they call they ollita of Quetzalcoatl . ' 

 ' that be a new invention . ' 

 ' why , do you think ? ' 

 ' they be try to start a new thing , that be all . they have   get this society on the lake here , of the Men of Quetzalcoatl , and they go round singing song . it be another dodge for national - socialism , that be all . ' 

 ' what do they do , the Men of Quetzalcoatl ? ' 

 ' I can not   see they do anything , except talk and get excited over their own importance . ' 

 ' but what be the idea ? ' 

 ' I could not   say . do not   suppose they have any . but if they have , they will not   let on to you . you be a gringo - or a gringita , at the good . and this be for pure Mexicans . for los señore , the workman , and los caballeros , the peon . every peon be a caballero nowadays , and every workman be a señor . so I suppose they be go to get themselves a special god , to put the final feather in their cap . ' 

 ' where do it start , the Quetzalcoatl thing ? ' 

 ' down in Sayula . they say Don Ram n Carrasco be at the back of it . maybe he want to be the next President - or maybe he be aim higher , and want to be the first Mexican Pharaoh . ' 

 ah , how tired it make Kate feel ; the hopelessness , the ugliness , the cynicism , the emptiness . she feel she could cry aloud , for the unknown god to put the magic back into her life , and to save she from the dry - rot of the world 's sterility . 

 she think again of go back to Europe . but what be the good ? she know it ! it be all politic or jazzing or slushy mysticism or sordid spiritualism . and the magic have go . the young generation , so smart and interesting , but so without any mystery , any background . the young the generation , the flatter and more jazzy , more and more devoid of wonder . 

 no , she could not go back to Europe . 

 and no ! she refuse to take the hotel manager 's estimate of Quetzalcoatl . how should a hotel manager judge ? - even if he be not really an hotel manager , but a ranch - overseer . she have see Ram n Carrasco , and Cipriano . and they be man . they want something beyond . she would believe in they . anything , anything rather than this sterility of nothingness which be the world , and into which her life be drift . 

 she would send Villiers away , too . he be nice , she like he . but he , too , be widdershin , unwind the sensation of disintegration and anti - life . no , she must send he away . she must , she must free herself from these mechanical connection . 

 every one of they , like villier , be like a cog - wheel in contact with which all one 's working be reverse . everything he say , everything he do , reverse her real life - flow , make she go against the sun . 

 and she do not want to go against the sun . after all , in spite of the horror latent in Mexico , when you get these dark - face people away from wrong contact like agitator and socialism , they make one feel that life be vast , if fearsome , and death be fathomless . 

 horror might burst out of they . but something must burst out , sometimes , if man be not machine . 

 no ! no ! no ! no ! no ! she cry to her own soul . let I still believe in some human contact . let it not be all cut off for I ! 

 but she make up her mind to be alone , and to cut herself off from all the mechanical widdershin contact . villier must go back to his United States . she would be alone in her own milieu . not to be touch by any , any of the mechanical cogwheel people . to be leave alone , not to be touch . to hide , and be hide , and never really be speak to . 

 yet , at the same time , with her blood flow softly sunwise , to let the sunwise sympathy of unknown people steal in to she . to shut door of iron against the mechanical world . but to let the sunwise world steal across to she , and add its motion to she , the motion of the stress of life , with the big sun and the star like a tree hold out its leaf . 

 she want an old spanish house , with its inner patio of flower and water . turn inward , to the few flower wall in by shadow . to turn one 's back on the cog - wheel world . not to look out any more on to that horrible machine of the world . to look at one 's own quiet little fountain and one 's own little orange - tree , with only heaven above . 

 so , have soothe her heart , she write Don Ram n again , that she be come to Sayula to look for a house . she send villier away . and the next day she set off with a man - servant , in the old motor - boat of the hotel , down to the village of Sayula . 

 it be thirty - five mile to travel , down the long lake . but the moment she set off , she feel at peace . a tall , dark - face fellow sit in the stern of the boat , steer and attend to the motor . she sit on cushion in the middle . and the young manservant perch in the prow . 

 they start before sunrise , when the lake be bath in motionless light . odd tuft of water - hyacinth be travel on the soft spermy water , hold up a green leaf like a little sail of a boat , and nod a delicate , mauve - blue flower . 

 give I the mystery and let the world live again for I ! Kate cry to her own soul . and deliver I from man 's automatism . 

 the sun rise , and a whiteness of light play on the top of the mountain . the boat hug the north shore , turn the promontory on which the villa have start so jauntily , twenty year ago , but now be lapse back to wilderness . all be still and motionless in the light . sometimes on the little bare patch high up on the dry hill be white speck ; bird ? no , man in their white cotton , peon hoe . they be so tiny and so distinct , they look like white bird settle . 

 round the bend be the hot spring , the church , the inaccessible village of the pure Indians , who speak no Spanish . there be some green tree , under the precipitous , dry mountain - side . 

 so on and on , the motor - boat chug incessantly , the man in the bow coil up like a serpent , watch ; the fish - milk water gleam and throw off a dense light , so that the mountain away across be fuse out . and Kate , under the awning , go into a kind of sleep . 

 they be pass the island , with its ruin of fortress and prison . it be all rock and dryness , with great broken wall and the shell of a church among its hurtful stone and its dry grey herbage . for a long time the Indians have defend it against the Spaniards . then the Spaniards use the island as a fortress against the Indians . later , as a penal settlement . and now the place be a ruin , repellent , full of scorpion , and otherwise empty of life . only one or two fisherman live in the tiny cove face the mainland , and a flock of goat , speck of life creep among the rock . and an unhappy fellow put there by the Government to register the weather . 

 no , Kate do not want to land . the place look too sinister . she take food from the basket , and eat a little lunch , and doze . 

 in this country she be afraid . but it be her soul more than her body that know fear . she have realize , for the first time , with finality and fatality , what be the illusion she labour under . she have think that each individual have a complete self , a complete soul , an accomplished i. and now she realize as plainly as if she have turn into a new being , that this be not so . man and woman have incomplete self , make up of bit assemble together loosely and somewhat haphazard . Man be not create ready - make . man to - day be half - make , and woman be half - make . creature that exist and function with certain regularity , but which run off into a hopeless jumble of inconsequence . 

 half - make , like insect that can run fast and be so busy and suddenly grow wing , but which be only wing grub after all . a world full of half - make creature on two leg , eat food and degrade the one mystery leave to they , sex . spin a great lot of word , bury themselves inside the cocoon of word and idea that they spin round themselves , and inside the cocoon , mostly perish inert and overwhelmed . 

 half - make creature , rarely more than half - responsible and half - accountable , act in terrible swarm , like locust . 

 awful think ! and with a collective insect - like will , to avoid the responsibility of achieve any more perfected being or identity . the queer , rabid hate of be urge on into purer self . the morbid fanaticism of the non - integrate . 

 in the great seething light of the lake , with the terrible blue - rib mountain of Mexico beyond , she seem swallow by some grisly skeleton , in the cage of his death - anatomy . she be afraid , mystically , of the man crouch there in the bow with his smooth thigh and supple loin like a snake , and his black eye watch . a half - being , with a will to disintegration and death . and the tall man behind she at the tiller , he have the curious smoke - grey phosphorus eye under black lash sometimes meet among the Indians . handsome , he be , and quiet and seemingly self - contain . but with that peculiar devilish half - smile lurking under his face , the half - jeer look of a part - thing , which know its power to destroy the purer thing . 

 and yet , Kate tell herself , both these man be manly fellow . they would not molest she , unless she communicate the thought to they , and by a certain cowardliness , prompt they . their soul be nascent , there be no fixed evil in they , they could sway both way . 

 so in her soul she cry aloud to the great mystery , the high power that hover in the interstice of the hot air , rich and potent . it be as if she could lift her hand and clutch the silent , stormless potency that rove everywhere , wait . ' come then ! ' she say , draw a long slow breath , and address the silent life - breath which hang unreveale in the atmosphere , wait . 

 and as the boat run on , and her finger rustle in the warm water of the lake , she feel the fulness descend into her once more , the peace , and the power . the fulfilment fill her soul like the fulness of ripe grape . and she think to herself : ' ah , how wrong I have be , not to turn soon to the other presence , not to take the life - breath soon ! how wrong to be afraid of these two man . ' 

 she do what she have be half - afraid to do before ; she offer they the orange and sandwich still in the basket . and each of the man look at she , the smoke - grey eye look she in the eye , and the black eye look she in the eye . and the man with the smoke - grey eye , who be cunning than the other man , but also prouder , say to she with his eye : we be live ! I know your sex , and you know mine . the mystery we be glad not to meddle with . you leave I my natural honour , and I thank you for the grace . 

 in his look , so quick and proud , and in his quiet Muchas gracia ! she hear the touch of male recognition , a man glad to retain his honour , and to feel the communion of grace . perhaps it be the spanish word Gracias ! but in her soul she be think of the communion of grace . 

 with the black - eyed man it be the same . he be humbler . but as he peel his orange and drop the yellow peel on the water , she could see the stillness , the humility , and the pathos of grace in he ; something very beautiful and truly male , and very hard to find in a civilized white man . it be not of the spirit . it be of the dark , strong , unbroken blood , the flowering of the soul . 

 then she think to herself : after all , it be good to be here . it be very good to be in this boat on this lake with these two silent , semi - barbarous man . they can receive the gift of grace , and we can share it like a communion , they and I. I be very glad to be here . it be so much well than love : the love I know with Joachim . this be the fulness of the vine . 

 ' Sayula ! ' say the man in the bow , point ahead . 

 she see , away off , a place where there be green tree , where the shore be flat , and a biggish building stand out . 

 ' what be the building ? ' she ask . 

 ' the railway station . ' 

 she be suitably impressed , for it be a new - look , impose structure . 

 a little steamer be smoking , lie off from a wooden jetty in the loneliness , and black , laden boat be pole out to she , and merge back to shore . the vessel give a hoot , and slowly yet busily set off on the bosom of the water , head in a slanting line across the lake , to which the tiny high white twin - tower of Tuliapán show above the water - line , tiny and far - off , on the other side . 

 they have pass the jetty , and round the shoal where the willow grow , she could see Sayula ; white flute twin - tower of the church , obelisk shape above the pepper - tree ; beyond , a mound of a hill standing alone , dot with dry bush , distinct and Japanese - looking ; beyond this , the corrugate , blue - rib , flat - flank mountain of Mexico . 

 it look peaceful , delicate , almost japanese . as she draw near she see the beach with the washing spread on the sand ; the fleecy green willow - tree and pepper - tree , and the villa in foliage and flower , hang magenta curtain of bougainvillea , red dot of hibiscus , pink abundance of tall oleander tree ; occasional palm - tree stick out . 

 the boat be steer round a stone jetty , on which , in black letter , be paint an advertisement for motor - car tyre . there be a few seat , some deep fleecy tree grow out of the sand , a booth for sell drink , a little promenade , and white boat on a sandy beach . a few woman sit under parasol , a few bather in the water , and tree in front of the few villa deep in green or blazing scarlet blossom . 

 ' this be very good , ' think Kate . ' it be not too savage , and not over - civilized . it be not   break , but it be rather out of repair . it be in contact with the world , but the world have get a very weak grip on it . ' 

 she go to the hotel , as Don Ram n have advise she . 

 ' do you come from Orilla ? you be Mrs Leslie ? Don Ram n Carrasco send we a letter about you . ' 

 there be a house . Kate pay her boatman and shake hand with they . she be sorry to be cut off from they again . and they look at she with a touch of regret as they leave . she say to herself : 

 ' there be something rich and alive in these people . they want to be able to breathe the Great Breath . they be like child , helpless . and then they be like demon . but somewhere , I believe , they want the breath of life and the communion of the brave , more than anything . ' 

 she be surprised at herself , suddenly use this language . but her weariness and her sense of devastation have be so complete , that the other Breath in the air , and the bluish dark power in the earth have become , almost suddenly , more real to she than so - call reality . concrete , jarring , exasperate reality have melt away , and a soft world of potency stand in its place , the velvety dark flux from the earth , the delicate yet supreme life - breath in the inner air . behind the fierce sun the dark eye of a deep sun be watch , and between the bluish rib of the mountain a powerful heart be secretly beat , the heart of the earth . 

 her house be what she want ; a low , l - shape , tile building with rough red floor and deep veranda , and the other two side of the patio complete by the thick , dark little mango - forest outside the low wall . the square of the patio , within the precinct of the house and the mango - trees , be gay with oleander and hibiscus , and there be a basin of water in the seedy grass . the flower - pot along the veranda be full of flower geranium and foreign flower . at the far end of the patio the chicken be scratch under the silent motionlessness of ragged banana - tree . 

 there she have it ; her stone , cool , dark house , every room opening on to the veranda ; her deep , shady veranda , or piazza , or corridor , look out to the brilliant sun , the sparkle flower and the seed - grass , the still water and the yellow banana - tree , the dark splendour of the shadow - dense mango - tree . 

 with the house go a Mexican Juana with two thick - haired daughter and one son . this family live in a den at the back of the project bay of the dining - room . there , half screen , be the well and the toilet , and a little kitchen and a sleep - room where the family sleep on mat on the floor . there the paltry chicken paddle , and the banana - tree make a chitter as the wind come . 

 Kate have four bedroom to choose from . she choose the one whose low , bar window open on the rough , grass and cobble - stone street , close her door and window , and go to sleep , say to herself as she lie down : now I be alone . and now I have only one thing to do : not to get catch up into the world 's cog - wheel any more , and not to lose my hold on the hidden great thing . 

 she be tired with a strange weariness , feel she could make no further effort . she wake up at tea - time , but there be no tea . Juana hasten off to the hotel to buy a bit . 

 Juana be a woman of about forty , rather short , with full dark face , centreless dark eye , untidy hair , and a limping way of walk . she speak rapidly , a rather plum - in - the - mouth Spanish , add ' n ' to all her word . something of a sloven , down to her speech . 

 ' no , Niña , no hay masn ' - masn instead of mas . and call Kate , in the old mexican style , Niña , which mean child . it be the honourable title for a mistress . 

 Juana be go to be a bit of a trial . she be a widow of doubtful antecedent , a creature with passion , but not much control , strong with a certain indifference and looseness . the hotel owner assure Kate that she be honest , but that if Kate would rather find another criada , all well and good . 

 there be a bit of a battle to be fight between the two woman . Juana be obstinate and reckless ; she have not be treat very well by the world . and there be a touch of bottom - dog insolence about she . 

 but also , sudden touch of passionate warmth and the peculiar selfless generosity of the native . she would be honest out of rough defiance and indifference , so long as she be not in a state of antagonism . 

 as yet , however , she be cautiously watch her ground , with that black - eyed touch of malice and wariness to be expect . and Kate feel that the cry : niña - child ! by which she be address , hold in it a slight note of malevolent mockery . 

 but there be nothing to do but to go ahead and trust the dark - face , centreless woman . 

 the second day , Kate have the energy to cast out one suite of bent - wood and cane furniture from her salon , remove picture and little stand . 

 if there be one social instinct more dreary than all the other social instinct in the world , it be the Mexican . in the centre of Kate 's red - tile salon be two crescent : a black bent - wood cane settee flank on each side by two black bent - wood cane chair , exactly face a brown bent - wood cane settee flank on each side by two brown bent - wood cane chair . it be as if the two settee and the eight chair be occupy by the ghost of all the mexican banality ever utter , sit face one another with their knee towards one another , and their foot on the terrible piece of green - with - red - rose carpet , in the weary centre of the salon . the very sight of it be frightening . 

 Kate shatter this face - to - face symmetry , and have the two girl , Maria and Concha , assist by the ironic Juana , carry off the brown bent - wood chair and the bamboo stand into one of the spare bedroom . Juana look on cynically , and assist officiously . but when Kate have her trunk , and fish out a couple of light rug and a couple of fine shawl and a few thing to make the place human , the criada begin to exclaim : ' Qué bonita ! Qué bonita , Niña ! Mire que bonita ! ' 

 

 

 CHAPTER VII 

 the Plaza 

 

 Sayula be a little lake resort ; not for the idle rich , for Mexico have few left ; but for tradespeople from Guadalajara , and week - ender . even of these , there be few . 

 nevertheless , there be two hotel , leave over , really , from the safe quiet day of Don Porfirio , as be most of the villa . the outlying villa be shut up , some of they abandon . those in the village live in a perpetual quake of fear . there be many terror , but the two regnant be bandit and bolshevist . 

 bandit be merely man who , in the outlying village , have very often no money , no work , and no prospect , take to robbery and murder for a time - occasionally for a lifetime - as a profession . they live in their wild village until troop be send after they , when they retire into the savage mountain , or the marsh . 

 bolshevist , somehow , seem to be bear on the railway . wherever the iron rail run , and passenger be haul back and forth in railway coach , there the spirit of rootlessness , of transitoriness , of first and second class in separate compartment , of envy and malice , and of iron and demonish panting engine , seem to bring forth the logical child of materialism , the bolshevist . 

 Sayula have her little branch of railway , her one train a day . the railway do not pay , and fight with extinction . but it be enough . 

 Sayula also have that real insanity of America , the automobile . as man use to want a horse and a sword , now they want a car . as woman use to pine for a home and a box at the theatre , now it be a ' machine . ' and the poor follow the middle class . there be a perpetual rush of ' machine ' , motor - car and motor - bus - call cami nes - along the one forlorn road come to Sayula from Guadalajara . one hope , one faith , one destiny ; to ride in a cami n , to own a car . 

 there be a little bandit scare when Kate arrive in the village , but she do not pay much heed . at evening she go into the plaza , to be with the people . the plaza be a square with big tree and a disuse bandstand in the centre , a little promenade all round , and then the cobbled street where the donkey and the cami nes pass . there be a further little section of real market - place , on the north side . 

 the band play no more in Sayula , and the elegancia stroll no more on the inner pavement around the plaza , under the tree . but the pavement be still good , and the bench be still more - or - less sound . oh Don Porfirio 's day ! and now it be the peon and Indians , in their blanket and white clothe , who fill the bench and monopolize the square . true , the law persist that the peon must wear trouser in the plaza , and not the loose great floppy drawer of the field . but then the peon also want to wear trouser , instead of the drawer that be the garb of their humble labour . 

 the plaza now belong to the peon . they sit thick on the bench , or slowly stroll round in their sandal and blanket . across the cobbled road on the north side , the little booth sell soup and hot food be crowd with man after six o'clock ; it be cheap to eat out , at the end of a day 's work . the woman at home could eat tortilla , never mind the caldo , the soup or the meat mess . at the booth which sell tequila , man , woman , and boy sit on the bench with their elbow on the board . there be a mild gambling game , where the man in the centre turn the card , and the plaza ring to his voice : Cinco de Spadas ! Rey de Copas ! a large , stout , imperturbable woman , with a cigarette on her lip and danger in her lower black eye , sit on into the night , sell tequila . the sweetmeat man stand by his board and sell sweet at one centavo each . and down on the pavement , small tin torch - lamp flare upon tiny heap of mango or nauseous tropical red plum , two or three centavos the little heap , while the vendor , a woman in the full wave of her skirt , or a man with curious patient humility , squat wait for a purchaser , with that strange fatal indifference and that gentle sort of patience so puzzle to a stranger . to have thirty cent ' worth of little red plum to sell ; to pile they on the pavement in tiny pyramid , five in a pyramid ; and to wait all day and on into the night , squat on the pavement and look up from the foot to the far - off face of the passer - by and potential purchaser , this , apparently , be an occupation and a living . at night by the flare of the tin torch , blow its flame on the wind . 

 usually there would be a couple of smallish young man with guitar of different size , stand close up face one another like two fighting cock that be utter a long , endless swan - song , sing in tense subdue voice the eternal ballad , not very musical , mournful , endless , intense , audible only within close range ; keep on and on till their throat be scrap . and a few tall , dark man in red blanket stand around , listen casually , and rarely , very rarely make a contribution of one centavo . 

 in among the food - booth would be another trio , this time two guitar and a fiddle , and two of the musician blind ; the blind one sing at a high pitch , full speed , yet not very audible . the very singing seem secretive , the singer press close in , face to face , as if to keep the wild , melancholy ballad re - echo in their private breast , their back to the world . 

 and the whole village be in the plaza , it be like a camp , with the low , rapid sound of voice . rarely , very rarely , a voice rise above the deep murmur of the man , the musical ripple of the woman , the twitter of child . rarely any quick movement ; the slow promenade of man in sandal , the sandal , call huarache , make a slight cockroach shuffle on the pavement . sometimes , dart among the tree , barelegge boy go sky - larking in and out of the shadow , in and out of the quiet people . they be the irrepressible boot - black , who swarm like tiresome fly in a barefooted country . 

 at the south end of the plaza , just across from the tree and cornerwise to the hotel , be a struggle attempt at an outdoor café , with little table and chair on the pavement . here , on weekday , the few who dare flaunt their prestige would sit and drink a beer or a glass of tequila . they be mostly stranger . and the peon , sit immobile on the seat in the background , look on with basilisk eye from under the great hat . 

 but on Saturdays and Sundays there be something of a show . then the cami nes and motor - car come in lurching and hiss . and , like strange bird alight , you have slim and charming girl in organdie frock and face - powder and bobbed hair , flutter into the plaza . there they stroll , arm in arm , brilliant in red organdie and blue chiffon and white muslin and pink and mauve and tangerine frail stuff , their black hair bob out , their dark slim arm interlace , their dark face curiously macabre in the heavy make - up ; approximate to white , but the white of a clown or a corpse . 

 in a world of big , handsome peon man , these flapper flap with butterfly brightness and an incongruous shrillness , manless . the supply of fifis , the male young elegant who be suppose to equate the flapper , be small . but still , fifis there be , in white flannel trouser and white shoe , dark jacket , correct straw hat , and cane . Fifis far more ladylike than the reckless flapper ; and far more nervous , wince . but fifis none the less , gallant , smoke a cigarette with an elegant flourish , talk elegant Castilian , as near as possible , and look as if they be go to be sacrifice to some mexican god within a twelvemonth ; when they be properly plump and perfume . the sacrificial calf be fatten . 

 on Saturday , the fifis and the flapper and the motor - car people from town - only a forlorn few , after all - try to be butterfly gay , in sinister Mexico . they hire the musician with guitar and fiddle , and the jazz music begin to quaver , a little too tenderly , without enough kick . 

 and on the pavement under the tree of the alameda - under the tree of the plaza , just near the little table and chair of the café , the young couple begin to gyrate    la mode . the red and the pink and the yellow and the blue organdie frock be turn sharply with all the white flannel trouser available , and some of the white flannel trouser have smart shoe , white with black strapping or with tan brogue band . and some of the organdie frock have green leg and green foot , some have leg    la nature , and white foot . and the slim , dark arm go around the dark blue fifi shoulder - or dark blue with a white thread . and the immeasurably soft face of the male would smile with a self - conscious fatherliness at the whitened , pretty , reckless little face of the female ; soft , fatherly , sensuous smile , suggestive of a victim 's luxuriousness . 

 but they be dance on the pavement of the plaza , and on this pavement the peon be slowly stroll , or stand in group watch with black , inscrutable eye the uncanny butterfly twitching of the dancer . who know what they think ? - whether they feel any admiration and envy at all , or only just a silent , cold , dark - faced opposition ? opposition there be . 

 the young peon in their little white blouse , and the scarlet serape fold jauntily on one shoulder , stroll slowly on under their big heavy , poise hat , with a will to ignore the dancer . slowly , with a heavy , calm balance , they move irresistibly through the dance , as if the dance do not exist . and the fifis in white trouser , with organdie in their arm , steer as well they might , to avoid the heavy , relentless passage of the young peon , who go on talk to one another , smile and flash powerful white tooth , in a black , heavy sang - froid that settle like a blight even on the music . the dancer and the pass peon never touch , never jostle . in Mexico you do not run into people accidentally . but the dance break against the invisible opposition . 

 the Indians on the seat , they too watch the dancer for a while . then they turn against they the heavy negation of indifference , like a stone on the spirit . the mysterious faculty of the Indians , as they sit there , so quiet and dense , for kill off any ebullient life , for quench any light and colourful effervescence . 

 there be indeed a little native dance - hall . but it be shut apart within four wall . and the whole rhythm and meaning be different , heavy , with a touch of violence . and even there , the dancer be artisan and mechanic or railway - porter , the half - urban people . no peon at all - or practically none . 

 so , before very long , the organdie butterfly and the flannel - trouser fifis give in , succumb , crush once more beneath the stone - heavy passivity of resistance in the demonish peon . 

 the curious , radical opposition of the Indians to the thing we call the spirit . it be spirit which make the flapper flap her organdie wing like a butterfly . it be spirit which crease the white flannel trouser of the fifi and make he cut his rather pathetic dash . they try to talk the elegancie and flippancy of the modern spirit . 

 but down on it all , like a weight of obsidian , come the passive negation of the Indian . he understand soul , which be of the blood . but spirit , which be superior , and be the quality of our civilization , this , in the mass , he darkly and barbarically repudiate . not until he become an artisan or connect with machinery do the modern spirit get he . 

 and perhaps it be this ponderous repudiation of the modern spirit which make Mexico what it be . 

 but perhaps the automobile will make road even through the inaccessible soul of the Indian . 

 Kate be rather sad , see the dance swamp . she have be sit at a little table , with Juana for dueña , sip a glass of absinthe . 

 the motor - car return to town leave early , in a little group . if bandit be out , they have good keep together . even the fifis have a pistol on their hip . 

 but it be Saturday , so some of the young ' elegance ' be stay on , till the next day ; to bathe and flutter in the sun . 

 it be Saturday , so the plaza be very full , and along the cobbled street stretch from the square many torch flutter and waver upon the ground , illuminate a dark salesman and an array of straw hat , or a heap of straw mat call petate , or pyramid of orange from across the lake . 

 it be Saturday , and Sunday morning be market . so , as it be suddenly , the life in the plaza be dense and heavy with potency . the Indians have come in from all the village , and from far across the lake . and with they they bring the curious heavy potency of life which seem to hum deeply and deep when they collect together . 

 in the afternoon , with the wind from the south , the big canoas , sailing - boat with black hull and one huge sail , have come drift across the water , bring the market - produce and the native to their gathering ground . all the white speck of village on the far shore , and on the far - off slope , have send their wild quota to the throng . 

 it be Saturday , and the indian instinct for live on into the night , once they be gather together , be now arouse . the people do not go home . though market would begin at dawn , man have no thought of sleep . 

 at about nine o'clock , after the fifi dance be shatter , Kate hear a new sound , the sound of a drum , or tom - tom , and see a drift of the peon away to the dark side of the plaza , where the side market would open to - morrow . already place have be take , and little stall set up , and huge egg - shape basket big enough to hold two man be loll against the wall . 

 there be a rippling and a pulse - like thudding of the drum , strangely arrest on the night air , then the long note of a flute play a sort of wild , unemotional melody , with the drum for a syncopate rhythm . Kate , who have listen to the drum and the wild singing of the Red Indians in Arizona and New Mexico , instantly feel that timeless , primeval passion of the prehistoric race , with their intense and complicated religious significance , spread on the air . 

 she look inquiringly at Juana , and Juana 's black eye glance back at she furtively . 

 ' what be it ? ' say Kate . 

 ' Musicians , singer , ' say Juana evasively . 

 ' but it be different , ' say Kate . 

 ' yes , it be new . ' 

 ' new ? ' 

 ' yes , it have only be come for a short time . ' 

 ' where do it come from ? ' 

 ' who know ! ' say Juana , with an evasive shrug of her shoulder . 

 ' I want to hear , ' say Kate . 

 ' it be purely man , ' say Juana . 

 ' still , one can stand a little way off . ' 

 Kate move towards the dense , silent throng of man in big hat . they all have their back to she . 

 she stand on the step of one of the house , and see a little clearing at the centre of the dense throng of man , under the stone wall over which bougainvillea and plumbago flower be hang , light up by the small , brilliantly flare torch of sweet - smell wood , which a boy hold in his two hand . 

 the drum be in the centre of the clearing , the drummer standing face the crowd . he be naked from the waist up , wear snow - white cotton drawer , very full , hold round the waist by a red sash , and bind at the ankle with red cord . round his uncovered head be a red cord , with three straight scarlet feather rise from the back of his head , and on his forehead a torquoise ornament , a circle of blue with a round blue stone in the centre . the flute - player be also naked to the waist , but over his shoulder be fold a fine white serape with blue - and - dark edge , and fringe . among the crowd , man with naked shoulder be give little leaflet to the onlooker . and all the time , high and pure , the queer clay flute be repeat a savage , rather difficult melody , and the drum be give the blood - rhythm . 

 More and more man be drift in from the plaza . Kate step from her perch and go rather shyly forward . she want one of the paper . the man give she one without look at she . and she go into the light to read . it be a sort of ballad , but without rhyme , in Spanish . at the top of the leaflet be a rough print of an eagle within the ring of a serpent that have its tail in its mouth ; a curious deviation from the mexican emblem , which be an eagle stand on a nopal , a cactus with great flat leaf , and hold in its beak and claws a writhing snake . 

 this eagle stand slim upon the serpent , within the circle of the snake , that have black marking round its back , like short black ray point inward . at a little distance , the emblem suggest an eye .

 there be a dense throng of man gather now , and from the centre the ruddy glow of ocote torch rise warm and strong , and the sweet scent of the cedar - like resin be on the air . Kate could see nothing for the mass of man in big hat . 

 the flute have stop its piping , and the drum be beat a slow , regular thud , act straight on the blood . the incomprehensible hollow barking of the drum be like a spell on the mind , make the heart burst each stroke , and darken the will . 

 the man in the crowd begin to subside , sit and squat on the ground , with their hat between their knee . and now it be a little sea of dark , proud head lean a little forward above the soft , strong male shoulder . 

 near the wall be a clear circle , with the drum in the centre . the drummer with the naked torso stand tilt his drum towards he , his shoulder gleam smooth and ruddy in the flare of light . beside he stand another man hold a banner that hang from a light rod . on the blue field of the banneret be the yellow sun with a black centre , and between the four great yellow ray , four black ray emerge , so that the sun look like a wheel spinning with a dazzling motion . 

 the crowd have all sit down , the six man with naked torso , who have be give out the leaflet and order the crowd , now come back and sit down in a ring , of which the drummer , with the drum tilt between his knee as he squat on the ground , be the key . on his right hand sit the banner - bearer , on his leave the flautist . they be nine man in the ring , the boy , who sit apart watch the two ocote torch , which he have lay upon a stone support on a long cane tripod , be the tenth . 

 the night seem to have go still . the curious seed - rattle hum of voice that fill the plaza be hush . under the tree , on the pavement , people be still pass unconcerned , but they look curiously lonely , isolated figure drift in the twilight of the electric lamp , and go about some exceptional business . they seem outside the nucleus of life . 

 away on the north side , the booth be still flare , people be buy and sell . but this quarter , too , look lonely , and outside the actual reality , almost like memory . 

 when the man sit down , the woman begin to drift up shyly , and seat themselves on the ground at the outer rim , their full cotton skirt flower out around they , and their dark rebozos draw tight over their small , round , shy head , as they squat on the ground . some , too shy to come right up , linger on the near bench of the plaza . and some have go away . indeed , a good many man and woman have disappear as soon as the drum be hear . 

 so that the plaza be curiously void . there be the dense clot of people round the drum , and then the outer world , seem empty and hostile . only in the dark little street that give on to the darkness of the lake , people be stand like ghost , half light - up , the man with their serape over their face , watch erect and silent and conceal , from the shadow . 

 but Kate , stand back in the doorway , with Juana sit on the doorstep at her foot , be fascinate by the silent , half - naked ring of man in the torchlight . their head be black , their body soft and ruddy with the peculiar indian beauty that have at the same time something terrible in it . the soft , full , handsome torsos of silent man with head softly bent a little forward ; the soft , easy shoulder , that be yet so broad , and which balance upon so powerful a backbone ; shoulder droop a little , with the relaxation of slumbering , quiescent power ; the beautiful ruddy skin , gleam with a dark fineness ; the strong breast , so male and so deep , yet without the muscular hardening that belong to white man ; and the dark , closed face , close upon a darken consciousness , the black moustache and delicate beard frame the closed silence of the mouth ; all this be strangely impressive , move strange , frightening emotion in the soul . those man who sit there in their dark , physical tenderness , so still and soft , they look at the same time frightening . something dark , heavy , and reptilian in their silence and their softness . their very naked torso be clothe with a subtle shadow , a certain secret obscurity . white man sit there would have be strong - muscle and frank , with an openness in their very physique , a certain ostensible presence . but not so these man . their very nakedness only reveal the soft , heavy depth of their natural secrecy , their eternal invisibility . they do not belong to the realm of that which come forth . 

 everybody be quite still ; the expectant hush deepen to a kind of dead , night silence . the naked - shoulder man sit motionless , sink into themselves , and listen with the dark ear of the blood . the red sash go tight round their waist , the wide white trouser , starch rather stiff , be bind round the ankle with red cord , and the dark foot in the glare of the torch look almost black , in huarache that have red thong . what do they want then , in life , these man who sit so softly and without any assertion , yet whose weight be so ponderous , arrest ? 

 Kate be at once attract and repel . she be attract , almost fascinated by the strange nuclear power of the man in the circle . it be like a darkly glowing , vivid nucleus of new life . repellent the strange heaviness , the sinking of the spirit into the earth , like dark water . repellent the silent , dense opposition to the pale - face spiritual direction . 

 yet here , and here alone , it seem to she , life burn with a deep , new fire . the rest of life , as she know it , seem wan , bleached and sterile . the pallid wanness and weariness of her world ! and here , the dark ruddy figure in the glare of a torch , like the centre of the everlaste fire , surely this be a new kindling of mankind ! 

 she know it be so . yet she prefer to be on the fringe , sufficiently out of contact . she could not bear to come into actual contact . 

 the man with the banner of the sun lift his face as if he be go to speak . and yet he do not speak . he be old ; in his sparse beard be grey hair , grey hair over his thick , dark mouth . and his face have the peculiar thickness , with a few deep - score line , of the old among these people . yet his hair rise vigorous and manly from his forehead , his body be smooth and strong . only , perhaps , a little smooth , heavy , soft than the shoulder of the young man . 

 his black eye gaze sightless for some time . perhaps he be really blind ; perhaps it be a heavy abstraction , a sort of heavy memory work in he , which make his face seem sightless . 

 then he begin , in a slow , clear , far - off voice , that seem strangely to echo the vanished barking of the drum : 

 ' listen to I , man ! listen to I , woman of these man ! a long time ago , the lake start call for man , in the quiet of the night . and there be no man . the little charale be swim round the shore , look for something , and the bágari and the other big fish would jump out of the water , to look around . but there be no man . 

 ' so one of the god with hide face walk out of the water , and climb the hill ' - he point with his hand in the night towards the invisible round hill at the back of the village - ' and look about . he look up at the sun , and through the sun he see the dark sun , the same that make the sun and the world , and will swallow it again like a draught of water . 

 ' he say : be it time ? and from behind the bright sun the four dark arm of the great sun shoot out , and in the shadow man arise . they could see the four dark arm of the sun in the sky . and they start walk . 

 ' the man on the top of the hill , who be a god , look at the mountain and the flat place , and see man very thirsty , their tongue hang out . so he say to they : come ! come here ! here be my sweet water ! 

 ' they come like dog run with their tongue out , and kneel on the shore of the lake . and the man on the top of the hill hear they pant with have drunk much water . he say to they : have you drunk too much into yourself ? be your bone not dry enough ? 

 ' the man make house on the shore , and the man on the hill , who be a god , teach they to sow maize and bean , and build boat . but he say to they : no boat will save you , when the dark sun cease to hold out his dark arm abroad in the sky . 

 ' the man on the hill say : I be Quetzalcoatl , who breathe moisture on your dry mouth . I fill your breast with breath from beyond the sun . I be the wind that whirl from the heart of the earth , the little wind that whirl like snake round your foot and your leg and your thigh , lift up the head of the snake of your body , in whom be your power . when the snake of your body lift its head , beware ! it be I , Quetzalcoatl , rear up in you , rear up and reach beyond the bright day , to the sun of darkness beyond , where be your home at last . save for the dark sun at the back of the day - sun , save for the four dark arm in the heaven , you be bone , and the star be bone , and the moon an empty sea - shell on a dry beach , and the yellow sun be an empty cup , like the dry thin bone of a dead coyote 's head . so beware ! 

 ' without I you be nothing . just as I , without the sun that be back of the sun , be nothing . 

 ' when the yellow sun be high in the sky , then say : Quetzalcoatl will lift his hand and screen I from this , else I shall burn out , and the land will wither . 

 ' for , say I , in the palm of my hand be the water of life , and on the back of my hand be the shadow of death . and when man forget I , I lift the back of my hand , farewell ! farewell , and the shadow of death . 

 ' but man forget I . their bone be moist , their heart weak . when the snake of their body lift its head , they say : this be the tame snake that do as we wish . and when they could not bear the fire of the sun , they say : the sun be angry . he want to drink we up . let we give he blood of victim . 

 ' and so it be , the dark branch of shade be go from heaven , and Quetzalcoatl mourn and grow old , hold his hand before his face , to hide his face from man . 

 ' he mourn and say : let I go home . I be old , I be almost bone . bone triumph in I , my heart be a dry gourd . I be weary in Mexico . 

 ' so he cry to the Master - Sun , the dark one , of the unuttered name : I be wither white like a perish gourd - vine . I be turn to bone . I be deny of these Mexicans . I be waste and weary and old . take I away . 

 ' then the dark sun reach an arm , and lift Quetzalcoatl into the sky . and the dark sun beckon with a finger , and bring white man out of the east . and they come with a dead god on the Cross , say : lo ! this be the Son of God ! he be dead , he be bone ! Lo , your god be bleed and dead , he be bone . kneel and sorrow for he , and weep . for your tear he will give you comfort again , from the dead , and a place among the scentless rose - tree of the after - life , when you be dead . 

 ' lo ! his mother weep , and the water of the world be in her hand . she will give you drink , and heal you , and lead you to the land of God . in the land of God you shall weep no more . beyond the gate of death , when you have pass from the house of bone into the garden of white rose . 

 ' so the weeping Mother bring her Son who be dead on the Cross to Mexico , to live in the temple . and the people look up no more , say : the Mother weep . the Son of her womb be bone . let we hope for the place of the west , where the dead have peace among the scentless rose - tree , in the Paradise of God . 

 ' for the priest would say : it be beautiful beyond the grave . 

 ' and then the priest grow old , and the tear of the Mother be exhaust , and the Son on the Cross cry out to the dark sun far beyond the sun : what be this that be do to I ? be I dead for ever , and only dead ? be I always and only dead , but bone on a Cross of bone ? 

 ' so this cry be hear in the world , and beyond the star of the night , and beyond the sun of the day .
