 ' Jesus say again : be it time ? my Mother be old like a sink moon , the old bone of she can weep no more . be we perish beyond redeem ? 

 ' then the great of the great sun speak aloud from the back of the sun : I will take my Son to my bosom , I will take his mother on my lap . like a woman I will put they in my womb , like a mother I will lay they to sleep , in mercy I will dip they in the bath of forgetting and peace and renewal . 

 ' that be all . so hear now , you man , and you woman of these man . 

 ' Jesus be go home , to the Father , and Mary be go back , to sleep in the belly of the Father . and they both will recover from death , during the long long sleep . 

 ' but the Father will not leave we alone . we be not abandon . 

 ' the Father have look around , and have see the Morning Star , fearless between the rush of the oncoming yellow sun , and the backward reel of the night . so the Great one , whose name have never be speak , say : who art thou , bright watchman ? and the dawn - star answering : it be I , the Morning Star , who in Mexico be Quetzalcoatl . it be I , who look at the yellow sun from behind , have my eye on the unseen side of the moon . it be I , the star , midway between the darkness and the rolling of the sun . I , call Quetzalcoatl , wait in the strength of my day . 

 " the Father answer : it be well . it be well . and again : it be time . 

 ' thus the big word be speak behind the back of the world . the nameless say : it be time . 

 ' once more the word have be speak : it be time . 

 ' listen , man , and the woman of man : it be time . know now it be time . those that leave we be come back . those that come be leave again . say welcome , and then farewell ! 

 ' welcome ! farewell ! ' 

 the old man end with a strong , suppress cry , as if really call to the god : 

 ' bienvenido ! bienvenido ! Adi s ! Adi s ! ' 

 even Juana , seat at Kate 's foot , cry out without know what she do : 

 ' bienvenido ! bienvenido ! Adi s ! Adi s ! Adi s - n ! ' 

 on the last adi s ! she trail out to a natural human ' n. ' 

 the drum begin to beat with an insistent , intensive rhythm , and the flute , or whistle , lift its odd , far - off call voice . it be play again and again the peculiar melody Kate have hear at first . 

 then one of the man in the circle lift his voice , and begin to sing the hymn . he sing in the fashion of the old Red Indians , with intensity and restraint , sing inwardly , sing to his own soul , not outward to the world , nor yet even upward to God , as the Christians sing . but with a sort of suppress , trance intensity , sing to the inner mystery , sing not into space , but into the other dimension of man 's existence , where he find himself in the infinite room that lie inside the axis of our wheel space . space , like the world , can not but move . and like the world , there be an axis . and the axis of our worldly space , when you enter , be a vastness where even the tree come and go , and the soul be at home in its own dream , noble and unquestioned . 

 the strange , inward pulse of the drum , and the singer singing inwardly , swirl the soul back into the very centre of time , which be old than age . he begin on a high , remote note , and hold the voice at a distance , run on in subtle , run rhythm , apparently unmeasured , yet pulse underneath by the drum , and give throbbing , three - fold lilt and lurch . for a long time , no melody at all be recognizable : it be just a lurching , run , far - off crying , something like the distant faint howling of a coyote . it be really the music of the old American Indian . 

 there be no recognizable rhythm , no recognizable emotion , it be hardly music . rather a far - off , perfect cry in the night . but it go straight through to the soul , the most ancient and everlasting soul of all man , where alone can the human family assemble in immediate contact . 

 Kate know it at once , like a sort of fate . it be no good resisting . there be neither urge nor effort , nor any speciality . the sound sound in the innermost far - off place of the human core , the ever - present , where there be neither hope nor emotion , but passion sit with fold wing on the nest , and faith be a tree of shadow . 

 like fate , like doom . faith be the Tree of Life itself , inevitable , and the apple be upon we , like the apple of the eye , the apple of the chin , the apple of the heart , the apple of the breast , the apple of the belly , with its deep core , the apple of the loin , the apple of the knee , the little , side - by - side apple of the toe . what do change and evolution matter ? we be the Tree with the fruit forever upon it . and we be faith forever . Verbum sit . 

 the one singer have finish , and only the drum keep on , touch the sensitive membrane of the night subtly and knowingly . then a voice in the circle rise again on the song , and like bird fly from a tree , one after the other , the individual voice arise , till there be a strong , intense , curiously weighty soar and sweeping of male voice , like a dark flock of bird fly and dip in unison . and all the dark bird seem to have launch out of the heart , in the inner forest of the masculine chest . 

 and one by one , voice in the crowd break free , like bird launch and come in from a distance , catch by the spell . the word do not matter . any verse , any word , no word , the song remain the same : a strong , deep wind rush from the cavern of the breast , from the everlasting soul ! Kate herself be too shy and wince to sing : too blench with disillusion . but she hear the answer away back in her soul , like a far - off mocking - bird at night . and Juana be sing in spite of herself , in a croon feminine voice , make up the word unconsciously . 

 the half - naked man begin to reach for their serape : white serape , with border of blue and earth - brown bar , and dark fringe . a man rise from the crowd and go towards the lake . he come back with ocote and with faggot that a boat have bring over . and he start a little fire . after a while , another man go for fuel , and start another fire in the centre of the circle , in front of the drum . then one of the woman go off soft and bare - foot , in her full cotton skirt . and she make a little bonfire among the woman . 

 the air be bronze with the glow of flame , and sweet with smoke like incense . the song rise and fall , then die away . Rose , and die . the drum ebb on , faintly touch the dark membrane of the night . then ebb away . in the absolute silence could be hear the soundless stillness of the dark lake . 

 then the drum start again , with a new , strong pulse . one of the seat man , in his white poncho with the dark blackish - and - blue border , get up , take off his sandal as he do so , and begin softly to dance the dance step . mindless , dance heavily and with a curious bird - like sensitiveness of the foot , he begin to tread the earth with his bare sol , as if tread himself deep into the earth . alone , with a curious pendulum rhythm , lean a little forward from a powerful backbone , he trod to the drum beat , his white knee lift and lift alternately against the dark fringe of his blanket , with a queer dark splash . and another man put his huarache into the centre of the ring , near the fire , and stand up to dance . the man at the drum lift up his voice in a wild , blind song . the man be take off their ponchos . and soon , with the firelight on their breast and on their darkly abstract face , they be all afoot , with bare torso and bare foot , dance the savage bird - tread . 

 ' who sleep shall wake ! who sleep shall wake ! who tread down the path of the snake in the dust shall arrive at the place ; in the path of the dust shall arrive at the place and be dress in the skin of the snake : shall be dress in the skin of the snake of the earth , that be father of stone ; that be father of stone and the timber of earth ; of the silver and gold , of the iron , the timber of earth from the bone of the father of earth , of the snake of the world , of the heart of the world , that beat as a snake beat the dust in its motion on earth , from the heart of the world . 

 ' who slee - eep sha - all wake ! who slee - eep sha - all wake ! who sleep sha - ll wake in the way of the snake of the dust of the earth , of the stone of the earth , of the bone of the earth . ' 

 the song seem to take new wild flight , after it have sink and rustle to a last ebb . it be like wave that rise out of the invisible , and rear up into form and a fly , disappear whiteness and a rustle of extinction . and the dancer , after dance in a circle in a slow , deep absorption , each man changeless in his own place , tread the same dust with the soft churning of bare foot , slowly , slowly begin to revolve , till the circle be slowly revolve round the fire , with always the same soft , down - sink , churn tread . and the drum keep the changeless living beat , like a heart , and the song rise and soar and fall , ebb and ebb to a sort of extinction , then heave up again . 

 till the young peon could stand it no more . they put off their sandal and their hat and their blanket , and shyly , with inexpert foot that yet know the old echo of the tread , they stand behind the wheeling dancer , and dance without change place . till soon the revolving circle have a fix yet throb circle of man outside . 

 then suddenly one of the naked - shoulder dancer from the inner circle step back into the outer circle and with a slow leaning , slowly start the outer circle revolve in the reverse direction from the inner . so now there be two wheel of the dance , one within the other , and revolve in different direction . 

 they keep on and on , with the drum and the song , revolve like wheel of shadow - shape around the fire . till the fire die low , and the drum suddenly stop , and the man suddenly disperse , return to their seat again . 

 there be silence , then the low hum of voice and the sound of laughter . Kate have think , so often , that the laughter of the peon break from they in a sound almost like pain . but now the laugh come like little invisible flame , suddenly from the ember of the talk . 

 everybody be wait , wait . yet nobody move at once , when the thud of the drum strike again like a summon . they sit still talk , listen with a second consciousness . then a man arise and throw off his blanket , and throw wood on the central fire . then he walk through the seated man to where the woman cluster in the fullness of their skirt . there he wait , smile with a look of abstraction . till a girl rise and come with utmost shyness towards he , hold she rebozo tight over her lower head with her right hand , and take the hand of the man in she left . it be she who lift the motionless hand of the man in her own , shyly , with a sudden shy snatching . he laugh , and lead she through the now risen man , towards the inner fire . she go with drop head , hide her face in confusion . but side by side and loosely hold hand , they begin to tread the soft , heavy dance - step , form the first small segment of the inner , stationary circle . 

 and now all the man be stand facing outward , wait to be choose . and the woman quickly , their shawled head hide , be slip in and pick up the loose right hand of the man of their choice . the inner man with the naked shoulder be soon choose . the inner circle , of man and woman in pair , hand in hand , be close . 

 ' come , Niña , come ! ' say Juana , look up at Kate with black , gleam eye . 

 ' I be afraid ! ' say Kate . and she speak the truth . 

 one of the bare - breast man have come across the street , out of the crowd , and be stand wait , near the doorway in which Kate stand , silently , with avert face . 

 ' look ! Niña ! this master be wait for you . then come ! oh , Niña , come ! ' 

 the voice of the criada have sink to the low , crooning , almost magical appeal of the woman of the people , and her black eye glisten strangely , watch Kate 's face . Kate , almost mesmerize , take slow , reluctant step forward , towards the man who be stand with avert face . 

 ' do you mind ? ' she say in English , in great confusion . and she touch his finger with her own . 

 his hand , warm and dark and savagely suave , loosely , almost with indifference , and yet with the soft barbaric nearness , hold her finger , and he lead she to the circle . she drop her head , and long to be able to veil her face . in her white dress and green straw hat , she feel a virgin again , a young virgin . this be the quality these man have be able to give back to she . 

 shyly , awkwardly , she try to tread the dance - step . but in her shoe she feel inflexible , insulate , and the rhythm be not in she . she move in confusion . 

 but the man beside she hold her hand in the same light , soft grasp , and the slow , pulse pendulum of his body sway untrammelle . he take no notice of she . and yet he hold her finger in his soft , light touch . 

 Juana have discard her boot and stocking , and with her dark , creased face like a mask of obsidian , her eye gleam with the timeless female flame , dark and unquenchable , she be tread the step of the dance . 

 ' as the bird of the sun tread the earth at the dawn of the day like a brown hen under his foot , like a hen and the branch of her belly droop with the apple of birth , with the egg of gold , with the egg that hide the globe of the sun in the water of heaven , in the purse of the shell of earth that be white from the fire of the blood , tread the earth , and the earth will conceive like the hen ' neath the foot of the bird of the sun ; ' neath the foot of the heart , ' neath the heart 's twin foot . tread the earth , tread the earth that squat as a pullet with wing close in - ' 

 the circle begin to shift , and Kate be slowly move round between two silent and absorb man , whose arm touch her arm . and the one hold her finger softly , loosely , but with transcendent nearness . and the wild song rise again like a bird that have alight for a second , and the drum change rhythm incomprehensibly . 

 the outer wheel be all man . she seem to feel the strange dark glow of they upon her back . man , dark , collective man , non - individual . and herself woman , wheel upon the great wheel of womanhood . 

 man and woman alike dance with face lower and expressionless , abstract , go in the deep absorption of man into the great manhood , woman into the great womanhood . it be sex , but the great , not the less sex . the water over the earth wheel upon the water under the earth , like an eagle silently wheeling above its own shadow . 

 she feel her sex and her womanhood catch up and identify in the slowly revolve ocean of nascent life , the dark sky of the man lower and wheel above . she be not herself , she be go , and her own desire be go in the ocean of the great desire . as the man whose finger touch her be go in the ocean that be male , stoop over the face of the water . 

 the slow , vast , soft - touching revolution of the ocean above upon ocean below , with no vestige of rustling or foam . only the pure slide conjunction . herself go into her great self , her womanhood consummate in the great womanhood . and where her finger touch the finger of the man , the quiet spark , like the dawn - star , shin between she and the great manhood of man . 

 how strange , to be merge in desire beyond desire , to be go in the body beyond the individualism of the body , with the spark of contact linger like a morning star between she and the man , her woman 's great self , and the great self of man . even of the two man next to she . what a beautiful slow wheel of dance , two great stream stream in contact , in opposite direction . 

 she do not know the face of the man whose finger she hold . her personal eye have go blind , his face be the face of dark heaven , only the touch of his finger a star that be both her and his . 

 her foot be feel the way into the dance - step . she be begin to learn softly to loosen her weight , to loosen the uplift of all her life , and let it pour slowly , darkly , with an ebbing gush , rhythmical in soft , rhythmic gush from her foot into the dark body of the earth . erect , strong like a staff of life , yet to loosen all the sap of her strength and let it flow down into the root of the earth . 

 she have lose count of time . but the dance of itself seem to be wheel to a close , though the rhythm remain exactly the same to the end . 

 the voice finish sing , only the drum keep on . suddenly the drum give a rapid little shudder , and there be silence . and immediately the hand be loosen , the dance break up into fragment . the man give she a quick , far - off smile and be go . she would never know he by sight . but by presence she might know he . 

 the woman slip apart , clutch their rebozo tight round their shoulder . the man hide themselves in their blanket . and Kate turn to the darkness of the lake . 

 ' already you be go , Niña ? ' come Juana 's voice of mild , aloof disappointment . 

 ' I must go now , ' say Kate hurriedly . 

 and she hasten towards the dark of the lake , Juana run behind she with shoe and stocking in her hand . 

 Kate want to hurry home with her new secret , the strange secret of her great womanhood , that she could not get use to . she would have to sink into this mystery . 

 she hasten along the uneven path of the edge of the lake shore , that lie dark in shadow , though the star give enough light to show the dark bulk and mast of the sailing - canoe against the downy obscurity of the water . night , timeless , hourless night ! she would not look at her watch . she would lay her watch face down , to hide its phosphorus figure . she would not be time . 

 and as she sink into sleep , she could hear the drum again , like a pulse inside a stone beating . 

 

 

 CHAPTER VIII 

 Night in the House 

 

 over the gateway of Kate 's house be a big tree call a cuenta tree , because it drop its fruit , that be little , round , hard ball like little dark marble , perfect in shape , for the native to gather up and string for bead , cuenta , or , more particularly , for the Pater Noster bead of the rosary . at night , the little road outside be quite dark , and the dropping of the cuenta startle the silence . 

 the night , which at first have seem perfectly friendly , begin to be full of terror . Fear have rise again . a band of robber have gather in one of the outlying village on the lake , a village where the man have bad character , as be ready to turn bandit at any moment . and this gang , invisible in the daytime , consist during the day of lake fisherman and labourer on the land , at night would set off on horseback to sack any lonely , or insufficiently - protect house . 

 then the fact that a gang of bandit be out always set the isolated thief and scoundrel in action . whatever happen , it would be attribute to the bandit . and so , many an unsuspected , seemingly honest man , with the old lust in his soul , would steal out by night with his machete and perhaps a pistol , to put his finger in the pie of the darkness . 

 and again Kate feel the terror clot and thicken in the black silence of the mexican night , till the sound of a cuenta fall be terrible . she would lie and listen to the thickening darkness . a little way off would sound the long , shrill whistle of the police watch . and in a while , the police patrol , on horseback , would go clattering lightly by . but the police in most country be never present save where there be no trouble . 

 the rainy season be come , and the night - wind rise from the lake , make strange noise in the tree , and shake the many loose door of the house . the servant be away in their distant recess . and in Mexico , at night , each little distance isolate itself absolutely , like a man in a black cloak turn his back . 

 in the morning , Juana would appear from the plaza , her eye blob - like and inky , and the old , weary , monkey look of subjection to fear settle on her bronze face . a race old in subjection to fear , and unable to shake it off . she would immediately begin to pour forth to Kate , in a babbling , half - intelligent stream , some story of a house break into and a woman stab . and she would say , the owner of the hotel have send word that it be not safe for Kate to sleep alone in the house . she must go to the hotel to sleep . 

 the whole village be in that state of curious , reptile apprehension which come over dark people . a panic fear , a sense of devilment and horror thick in the night air . when blue morning come they would cheer up . but at night , like clot blood the air would begin to thicken again . 

 the fear , of course , be communicate from one person to another . Kate be sure that if Juana and her family have not be huddle in reptile terror away at the far end of the house , she herself would have be unafraid . as it be , Juana be like a terror - strike lizard . 

 there be no man about the place . Juana have two son , Jesús , who be about twenty , and Ezequiel , about seventeen . but Jesús - she pronounce it Hezoosn - run the little gasoline motor for the electric light , and he and Ezequiel sleep together on the floor of the little engine - house . so that Juana huddle with her two girl , Concha and Maria , in the den at the end of Kate 's house , and seem to sweat a rank odour of fear . 

 the village be submerge . usually the plaza keep alive till ten o'clock , with the charcoal fire burn and the ice - cream man go round with his bucket on his head , endlessly cry : Nieve ! Nieve ! and the people gossip on the street or listen to the young man with guitar . 

 now , by nine o'clock , the place be desert , curiously stony and vacuous . and the Jefe send out the order that anybody in the street after ten o'clock would be arrest . 

 Kate hurry to her house and lock herself in . it be not easy to withstand the panic fear of a black - eye , semi - barbaric people . the thing communicate itself like some drug on the air , wring the heart and paralyse the soul with a sense of evil ; black , horrible evil . 

 she would lie in her bed in the absolute dark : the electric light be cut off completely , everywhere , at ten o'clock , and primitive darkness reign . and she could feel the demonish breath of evil move on the air in wave . 

 she think of the grisly story of the country , which she have hear . and she think again of the people , outwardly so quiet , so nice , with a gentle smile . but even Humboldt have say of the Mexicans , that few people have such a gentle smile , and at the same time , such fierce eye . it be not that their eye be exactly fierce . but their blackness be inchoate , with a dagger of white light in it . and in the inchoate blackness the blood - lust might arise , out of the sediment of the uncreated past . 

 uncreated , half - create , such a people be at the mercy of old black influence that lie in a sediment at the bottom of they . while they be quiet , they be gentle and kindly , with a sort of limpid naïveté . but when anything shake they at the depth , the black cloud would arise , and they be go again in the old grisly passion of death , blood - lust , incarnate hate . a people incomplete , and at the mercy of old , upstarte lust . 

 somewhere at the bottom of their soul , she feel , be a fathomless resentment , like a raw wound . the heavy , bloody - eyed resentment of man who have never be able to win a soul for themselves , never be able to win themselves a nucleus , an individual integrity out of the chaos of passion and potency and death . they be catch in the toil of old lust and old activity as in the fold of a black serpent that strangle the heart . the heavy , evil - smell weight of an unconquered past . 

 and under this weight they live and die , not really sorry to die . clog and tangle in the element , never able to extricate themselves . blacken under a too - strong sun , surcharge with the heavy sundering electricity of the mexican air , and torment by the bubbling of volcano away below the foot . the tremendous potent element of the american continent , that give man powerful body , but which weigh the soul down and prevent its rise into birth . or , if a man arrive with a soul , the maleficent element gradually break it , gradually , till he decompose into idea and mechanistic activity , in a body full of mechanical energy , but with his blood - soul dead and putrescent . 

 so , these man , unable to overcome the element , man hold down by the serpent tangle of sun and electricity and volcanic emission , they be subject to an ever - recur , fathomless lust of resentment , a demonish hatred of life itself . then , the in - strike thud of a heavy knife , stab into a live body , this be the good . no lust of woman can equal that lust . the clutch throb of gratification as the knife strike in and the blood spurt out ! 

 it be the inevitable supreme gratification of a people entangle in the past , and unable to extricate itself . a people that have never be redeem , that have not know a Saviour . 

 for Jesus be no Saviour to the Mexicans . he be a dead god in their tomb . as a miner who be entomb underground by the collapsing of the earth in the gangway , so do whole nation become entomb under the slow subsidence of their past . unless there come some Saviour , some Redeemer to drive a new way out , to the sun . 

 but the white man bring no salvation to Mexico . on the contrary , they find themselves at last shut in the tomb along with their dead god and the conquered race . 

 which be the status quo . 

 Kate lie and think hard , in the black night . at the same time , she be listen intensely , with a clutch of horror . she could not control her heart . it seem wrench out of place , and really hurt she . she be , as she have never be before , absolute physically afraid , blood afraid . her blood be wrench in a paralysis of fear . 

 in England , in Ireland , during the war and the revolution she have know spiritual fear . the ghastly fear of the rabble ; and during the war , nation be nearly all rabble . the terror of the rabble that , mongrel - like , want to break the free spirit in individual man and woman . it be the cold , collective lust of million of people , to break the spirit in the outstanding individual . they want to break this spirit , so that they could start the great downhill rush back to old underworld level , old gold - worship and murder lust . the rabble . 

 in those day Kate have know the agony of cold social fear , as if a democracy be a huge , huge cold centipede which , if you resist it , would dig every claw into you . and the flesh would mortify around every claw . 

 that have be her bad agony of fear . and she have survive . 

 now she know the real heart - wrench of blood fear . her heart seem pull out of place , in a stretch pain . 

 she doze , and waken suddenly , at a small noise . she sit up in bed . her door on to the veranda have shutter . the door themselves be fasten , but the shutter be open for air , leave the upper space , like the window of the door , open . and against the dark grey of the night she see what look like a black cat crouch on the bottom of the panel - space . 

 ' what be that ? ' she say automatically . 

 instantly , the thing move , slide away , and she know it be the arm of a man that have be reach inside to pull the bolt of the door . she lie for a second paralyse , prepare to scream . there be no movement . so she lean and light a candle . 

 the curious panic fear be an agony to she . it paralyse she and wrench her heart out of place . she lie prostrate in the anguish of night - terror . the candle blaze duskily . there be a far - off mutter of thunder . and the night be horrible , horrible . Mexico be ghastly to she beyond description . 

 she could not relax , she could not get her heart into place . ' now , ' she think to herself , ' I be at the mercy of this thing , and I have lose myself . ' and it be a terrible feeling , to be lose , scatter , as it be , from herself in a horror of fear . 

 ' what can I do ? ' she think , summon her spirit . ' how can I help myself ? ' she know she be all alone . 

 for a long time she could do nothing . then a certain relief come to she as she think : ' I be believe in evil . I must not   believe in evil . panic and murder never start unless the lead people let slip the control . I do not   really believe in evil . I do not   believe the old Pan can wrench we back into the old , evil form of consciousness , unless we wish it . I do believe there be a great power , which will give we the great strength , while we keep the faith in it , and the spark of contact . even the man who want to break in here , I do not   think he really have the power . he be just try to be mean and wicked , but something in he would have to submit to a great faith and a great power . ' 

 so she reassure herself , till she have the courage to get up and fasten her door - shutter at the top . after which she go from room to room , to see that all be make fast . and she be thankful to realize that she be afraid of scorpion on the floor , as well as of the panic horror . 

 now she have see that the five door and the six window of her wing of communicating room be fast . she be seal inside the darkness , with her candle . to get to the other part of the house , the dining - room and kitchen , she have to go outside on the veranda . 

 she grow quieter , shut up with the dusky glow of her candle . and her heart , still wrench with the pain of fear , be think : ' Joachim say that evil be the lapsing back to old life - mode that have be surpass in we . this bring murder and lust . but the drum of Saturday night be the old rhythm , and that dance round the drum be the old savage form of expression . consciously revert to the savage . so perhaps it be evil . ' 

 but then again her instinct to believe come up . 

 ' no ! it be not a helpless , panic reversal . it be conscious , carefully choose . we must go back to pick up old thread . we must take up the old , broken impulse that will connect we with the mystery of the cosmos again , now we be at the end of our own tether . we must do it . Don Ram n be right . he must be a great man , really . I think there be no really great man any more : only great financier and great artist and so on , but no great man . he must be a great man . ' 

 she be again infinitely reassure by this thought . 

 but again , just as she have blow out the candle , vivid flare of white light spurt through all the window - crack , and thunder break in great round ball , smash down . the bolt of thunder seem to fall on her heart . she lie absolutely crush , in a kind of quiescent hysteric , torture . and the hysteric hold her listening and tense and abject , until dawn . and then she be a wreck . 

 in the morning come Juana , also look like a dead insect , with the conventional phrase : ' how have you pass the night , Niña ? ' 

 ' badly ! ' say Kate . then she tell the story of the black cat , or the man 's arm . 

 ' Mire ! ' say Juana , in a hushed voice . ' the poor innocent will be murder in her bed . no , Niña , you must go and sleep in the hotel . no , no , Niña , you can not   leave your window shutter open . no , no , impossible . see now , will you go to the hotel to sleep ? the other señora do it . ' 

 ' I do not   want to , ' say Kate . 

 ' you do not   want to , Niña ? ah ! entonce ! entonce , Niña , I will tell Ezequiel to sleep here outside your door , with his pistol . he have a pistol , and he will sleep outside your door , and you can leave your shutter open , for air in the hot night . ah , Niña , we poor woman , we need a man and a pistol . we ought not to be leave alone all the night . we be afraid , the child be afraid . and imagine it , that there be a robber try to open the bolt of your door ! imagine it to yourself ! no , Niña , we will tell Ezequiel at mid - day . ' 

 Ezequiel come stride proudly in , at mid - day . he be a wild , shy youth , very erect and proud , and half savage . his voice be break , and have a queer resonance . 

 he stand shyly while the announcement be be make to he . then he look at Kate with flash black eye , very much the man to the rescue . 

 ' yes ! yes ! ' he say . ' I will sleep here on the corridor . do not   have any fear . I shall have my pistol . ' 

 he march off , and return with the pistol , an old long - barrel affair . 

 ' it have five shot , ' he say , show the weapon . ' if you open the door in the night , you must say a word to I first . because if I see anything move , I shall fire five shot . Pst ! Pst ! ' 

 she see by the flash of his eye what satisfaction it would give he to fire five shot at something move in the night . the thought of shot be fire at he give he not the least concern . 

 ' and Niña , ' say Juana , ' if you come home late , after the light be out , you must call Ezequiel ! because if not , Brumm ! Brumm ! - and who know who will be kill ! ' 

 Ezequiel sleep on a straw mat on the brick veranda outside Kate 's door , roll up in his blanket , and with the pistol at his side . so she could leave her shutter open for air . and the first night she be keep awake once more by his fierce snoring . never have she hear such a tremendous resonant sound ! what a chest that boy must have ! it be sound from some strange , savage other world . the noise keep she awake , but there be something in it which she like . some sort of wild strength . 

 

 

 CHAPTER IX 

 Casa de las Cuentas 

 

 Kate be soon fond of the limping , untidy Juana , and of the girl . Concha be fourteen , a thick , heavy , barbaric girl with a mass of black wave hair which she be always scratch . Maria be eleven , a shy , thin bird - like thing with big eye that seem almost to absorb the light round she . 

 it be a reckless family . Juana admit a different father for Jesús , but to judge from the rest , one would have suspect a different father for each of they . there be a basic , sardonic carelessness in the face of life , in all the family . they live from day to day , a stubborn , heavy , obstinate life of indifference , careless about the past , careless about the present , careless about the future . they have even no interest in money . whatever they get they spend in a minute , and forget it again . 

 without aim or purpose , they live absolutely    terre , down on the dark , volcanic earth . they be not animal , because man and woman and their child can not be animal . it be not grant we . go , for once go , thou never canst return ! say the great urge , which drive we creatively on . when man try brutally to return to the old , previous level of evolution , he do so in the spirit of cruelty and misery . 

 so in the black eye of the family , a certain vicious fear and wonder and misery . the misery of human being who squat helpless outside their own unbuilt self , unable to win their soul out of the chaos , and indifferent to all other victory . 

 white people be become soulless too . but they have conquer the low world of metal and energy , so they whizz around in machine , circle the void of their own emptiness . 

 to Kate , there be a great pathos in her family . also a certain repulsiveness . 

 Juana and her child , once they accept their Niña as their own , be honest with intensity . point of honour , they be honest to the least little plum in the fruit bowl . and almost intensely eager to serve . 

 themselves indifferent to their surrounding , they would live in squalor . the earth be the great garbage - bowl . everything discard be fling on the earth and they do not care . almost they like to live in a milieu of flea and old rag , bit of paper , banana skin and mango stone . here be a piece tear off my dress ! earth , take it . here be the combing of my hair ! earth , take they ! 

 but Kate could not bear it . she care . and immediately , the family be quite glad , thrill that she care . they sweep the patio with the twig broom till they sweep the very surface of the earth away . Fun ! the Niña have feeling about it . 

 she be a source of wonder and amusement to they . but she be never a class superior . she be a half - incomprehensible , half - amusing wonder - being . 

 the Niña want the aguador to bring two bote of hot water , quick , from the hot spring , to wash herself all over every morning . Fun ! Go , Maria , tell the aguador to run with the Niña 's water . 

 then they almost resent it that she shut herself off to have her bath . she be a sort of goddess to they , to provide they with fun and wonder ; but she ought always to be accessible . and a god who be forever accessible to human being have an unenviable time of it , Kate soon discover . 

 no , it be no sinecure , be a Niña . at dawn begin the scrape - scrape of the twig broom outside . Kate stay on in bed , door fasten but shutter open . flutter outside ! somebody want to sell two egg . where be the Niña ? she be sleep ! the visitor do not go . continual flutter outside . 

 the aguador ! ah , the water for the Niña 's bath ! she be sleep , she be sleep . ' no ! ' call Kate , slip into a dressing - gown and unbolt the door . in come the child with the bath - tub , in come the aguador with the two square kerosene can full of hot water . twelve centavos ! twelve centavos for the aguador ! no hay ! we have not   get twelve centavos . later ! later ! away trot the aguador , pole over his shoulder . Kate shut her door and shutter and start her bath . 

 ' Niña ? Niña ? ' 

 ' what do you want ? ' 

 ' egg boil or fried or ranchero ? which do you want ? ' 

 ' boil . ' 

 ' coffee or chocolate ? ' 

 ' Coffee . ' 

 ' or do you want tea ? ' 

 ' no , coffee . ' 

 bath proceed . 

 ' Nina ? ' 

 ' yes . ' 

 ' there be no coffee . we be go to buy some . ' 

 ' I will take tea . ' 

 ' no , Niña ! I be go . wait for I . ' 

 ' go then . ' 

 Kate come out to breakfast on the veranda . the table be set , heap with fruit and white bread and sweet bun . 

 ' good morning , Niña . how have you pass the night ? well ! ah , praise be God ! Maria , the coffee . I be go to put the egg in the water . oh , Niña , that they may not be boil hard ! - look , what foot of the Madonna ! look ! bonito ! ' 

 and Juana stoop down , fascinate to touch with her black finger Kate 's white soft foot , that be thrust in light sandal , just a thong across the foot . 

 the day have begin . Juana look upon herself as dedicate entirely to Kate . as soon as possible she shoo her girl away , to school . sometimes they go : mostly they do not . the Niña say they must go to school . listen ! listen now ! say the Niña that you must go to school ! away ! Walk ! 

 Juana would limp back and forth down the long veranda from kitchen to the breakfast table , carry away the dish one by one . then , with a great splash , she be wash up . 

 Morning ! brilliant sun pour into the patio , on the hibiscus flower and the flutter yellow and green rag of the banana - tree . bird swiftly come and go , with tropical suddenness . in the dense shadow of the mango - grove , white - clothe Indians go like ghost . the sense of fierce sun and , almost more impressive , of dark , intense shadow . a twitter of life , yet a certain heavy weight of silence . a dazzle flicker and brilliance of light , yet the feeling of weight . 

 Kate would sit alone , rock on her veranda , pretend to sew . silently appear an old man with one egg hold up mysteriously , like some symbol . would the patrona buy it for five centavos ? La Juana only give four centavos . all right . where be Juana ? 

 Juana appear from the plaza with more purchase . the egg ! the four centavos ! the account of the spending . entonce ! entonce ! Luego ! Luego ! ah , Niña , no tengo memoria ! Juana could not read nor write . she scuffle off to the market with her peso , buy endless little thing at one or two centavos each , every morning . and every morning there be a reckoning up . ah ! ah ! where be we ? I have no memory . well then - ah - yes - I buy ocote for three centavos ! how much ? how much , Niña ? how much be it now ? 

 it be a game which thrill Juana to the marrow , reckon up the centavos to get it just right . if she be a centavo short in the change , she be paralyse . time after time she would reappear . there be a centavo short , Niña ! ah , how stupid I be ! but I will give you one of mine ! 

 ' do not   bother , ' say Kate . ' do not   think of it any more . ' 

 ' but yes . but yes ! ' and away she limp in distraction . 

 till an hour later , loud cry from the far end of the house . Juana wave a scrap of greenery . 

 ' Mire ! Niña ! compré perejil a un centavo - I buy parsley for one cent . be it right ? ' 

 ' it be right , ' say Kate . 

 and life could proceed once more . 

 there be two kitchen , the one next the dining - room , belong to Kate , and the narrow little shed under the banana - tree , belong to the servant . from her veranda Kate look away down to Juana 's kitchen shed . it have a black window - hole . 

 clap ! clap ! clap ! clap ! why , I think Concha be at school ! say Kate to herself . 

 no ! - there , in the darkness of the window - hole , be Concha 's swarthy face and mane , peer out like some animal from a cave , as she make the tortilla . Tortillas be flat pancake of maize dough , bake dry on a flat earthenware plate over the fire . and the making consist of clap a bit of new dough from the palm of one hand to the other , till the tortilla be of the requisite thinness , roundness , and so - call lightness . 

 clap ! clap ! clap ! clap ! clap ! clap ! clap ! it be as inevitable as the tick of some spider , the sound of Concha make tortillas in the heat of the morning , peer out of her dark window - hole . and some time after mid - day , the smoke would be come out of the window - hole ; Concha be throw the raw tortilla on the big earthen plate over the slow wood fire . 

 then Ezequiel might or might not stride in , very much the man , serape poise over one shoulder and big straw hat jauntily curl , to eat the mid - day tortilla . if he have work in the field at any distance , he would not appear till nightfall . if he appear , he sit on the doorstep and the woman serve he his tortillas and fetch he his drink of water as if he be a king , boy though he might be . and his rough , break voice be hear in quiet command . 

 Command be the word . though he be quiet and gentle , and very conscientious , there be calm , kingly command in his voice when he speak to his mother or sister . the old male prerogative . somehow , it make Kate want to ridicule he . 

 come her own meal : one of her trial . hot , rather greasy soup . inevitable hot , greasy , rather peppery rice . inevitable meat in hot , thick , rather greasy sauce . boil calabacita or egg - plant , salad , perhaps some dulce make with milk - and the big basket of fruit . Overhead , the blaze tropical sun of late May . 

 Afternoon , and great heat . Juana set off with the girl and the dish . they would do the washing up in the lake . squat on the stone , they would dabble the plate one by one , the spoon and the fork one by one in the filmy water of the lake , then put they in the sun to dry . after which Juana might wash a couple of towel in the lake and the girl might bathe . saunter the day away - saunter the day away . 

 Jesús , the eld son , a queer , heavy , greasy fellow , usually appear in the afternoon , to water the garden . but he eat his meal at the hotel , and really live there , have his home there . not that he have any home , any more than a zopilote have a home . but he run the planta , and do odd job about the hotel , and work every day in the year till half - past ten at night , earn twenty - two peso , eleven dollar , a month . he wear a black shirt , and his thick , massive black hair drop over his low brow . very near to an animal . and though , to order , he wear a black Fascisti shirt , he have the queer , animal jeering of the socialist , an instinct for pull thing down . 

 his mother and he have a funny little intimacy of quiet and indifferent mutual taunting of one another . he would give she some money if she be in a strait . and there be a thin little thread of blood - bondage between they . apart from that , complete indifference . 

 Ezequiel be a fine type . he be slender and so erect that he almost curved backwards . he be very shy , farouche . Proud also , and more responsible to his family . he would not go to work in an hotel . no . he be a worker in the field , and he be proud of it . a man 's work . no equivocal sort of half - service for he . 

 though he be just a hire labourer , yet work on the land he never feel he be work for a master . it be the land he work for . somewhere inside himself he feel that the land be his , and he belong in a measure to it . perhaps a lingering feeling of tribal , communal land - ownership and service . 

 when there be work , he be due to earn a peso a day . there be often no work : and often only seventy - five centavos a day for wage . when the land be dry , he would try to get work on the road , though this he do not like . but he earn his peso a day . 

 often , there be no work . often , for day , sometimes for week , he would have to hang about , nothing to do , nothing to do . only , when the Socialist Government have begin give the peasant bit of land , divide up the big hacienda , Ezequiel have be allot a little piece outside the village . he would go and gather the stone together there , and prepare to build a little hut . and he would break the earth with a hoe , his only implement , as far as possible . but he have no blood connection with this square allotment of unnatural earth , and he could not get himself into relation with it . he be fitful and diffident about it . there be no incentive , no urge . 

 on workday he would come stride in about six o'clock , shyly greet Kate as he pass . he be a gentleman in his barbarism . then , away in the far recess , he would rapidly fold tortilla after tortilla , sit on the floor with his back to the wall , rapidly eat the leathery thing that taste of mortar , because the maize be first boil with lime to loosen the husk , and accept another little pile , serve on a leaf , from the cook , Concha . Juana , cook for the Niña , would no long condescend to cook for her own family . and sometimes there be a mess of meat and chile for Ezequiel to scoop up out of the earthenware casserole , with his tortilla . and sometimes there be not . but always , he eat with a certain blind , rapid indifference , that also seem to be mexican . they seem to eat even with a certain hostile reluctance , and have a strange indifference to what or when they eat . 

 his supper finish , as a rule he be off again like a shot , to the plaza , to be among man . and the woman would sit desultorily about , on the ground . sometimes Kate would come in at nine o'clock to an empty place - Ezequiel in the plaza , Juana and Maria disappear somewhere or other , and Choncha lie asleep like a heap of rag on the gravel of the patio . when Kate call she , she would raise her head , stupefied and hopeless ; then get up like a dog and crawl away to the gate . the strange stupor of boredom and hopelessness that be always sink upon they would make Kate 's heart stand still with dread . 

 the peculiar indifference to everything , even to one another . Juana wash a cotton shirt and a pair of cotton trouser for each of her son , once a week , and there her maternal effort end . she see hardly anything of they , and be often completely unaware of what Ezequiel be do , where he be work , or at what . he have just go off to work , no more . 

 yet again , sometimes she have hot , fierce pang of maternal protectiveness , when the boy be unjustly treat , as he often be . and if she think he be ill , a black sort of fatalistic fear come over she . but Kate have to rouse she into get some simple medicine . 

 like animal , yet not at all like animal . for animal be complete in their isolation and their insouciance . with they it be not indifference . it be completeness in themselves . but with the family there be always a kind of bleeding of incompleteness , a terrible stupor of boredom settle down . 

 the two girl could not be apart : they must always be run after one another . yet Concha continually tease the big - eye , naïve simpleton of a Maria . and Maria be always in tear . or the two be suddenly throw stone at one another . but with no real aim to hit . and Juana be abuse they with sudden vehemence , that flicker in a minute to complete indifference again . 

 Queer , the savage ferocity with which the girl would suddenly be throw stone at one another . but queerer still , they always aim just to miss , Kate notice the same in the savage attack the boy make on one another , on the beach ; hurl large stone with intense , terrible ferocity . but almost always , aim with a curious cast in the eye , just to miss . 

 but sometimes not . sometimes hit with a sharp cut . and then the wound one would drop right down , with a howl , as if dead . and the other boy would edge away , in a silent kind of dread . and the wounded boy would be prostrate , not really much hurt , but as if he be kill . 

 then , maybe , suddenly he would be up , with a convulsion of murder in his face , pursue his adversary with a stone . and the adversary would abjectly flee . 

 always the same thing among the young : a ceaseless , endless taunting and tormenting . the same as among the Red Indians . but the Pueblo Indians rarely lapse from speech into violence . the mexican boy almost always . and almost always , one boy in murderous rage , pursue his taunter till he have hurt he : then an abject collapse of the one hurt . then , usually , a revival of the one hurt , the murderous frenzy transfer to he , and the first attacker flee abjectly , in terror . one or the other always abject . 

 they be a strange puzzle to Kate . she feel something must be do . she herself be inspire to help . so she have the two girl for an hour a day , teach they to read , to sew , to draw . Maria want to learn to read : that she do want . for the rest , they begin well . but soon , the regularity and the slight insistence of Kate on their attention make they take again that peculiar invisible jeer tone , something peculiar to the American Continent . a quiet , invisible , malevolent mockery , a desire to wound . they would press upon she , trespass upon her privacy , and with a queer effrontery , do all they could to walk over she . with their ugly little will , try to pull her will down . 

 ' no , do not   lean on I , Concha . stand on your own foot . ' 

 the slight grin of malevolence on Concha 's face , as she stand on her own foot . then : 

 ' do you have lice in your hair , Niña ? ' 

 the question ask with a peculiar , subtle , indian insolence . 

 ' no , ' say Kate , suddenly angry . ' and now go ! go ! go away from I ! do not   come near I . ' 

 they slunk out , abject . so much for educate they . 

 Kate have visitor from Guadalajara - great excitement . but while the visitor be drink tea with Kate on the veranda , at the other side of the patio , full in view , Juana , Concha , Maria and Felipa , a cousin of about sixteen , squat on the gravel with their splendid black hair down their back , display themselves as they hunt in each other 's hair for lice . they want to be full in view . and they be it . they want the basic fact of lice to be thrust under the nose of those white people . 

 Kate stride down the veranda . 

 ' if you must pick lice , ' she say in a shake voice to Juana , shake with anger , ' pick they there , in your own place , where you can not   be see . ' 

 one instant , Juana 's black inchoate eye gleam with a malevolent ridicule , meet Kate 's . the next instant , humble and abject , the four with their black hair down their back slunk into the recess out of sight . 

 but it please Juana that she have be able to make Kate 's eye blaze with anger . it please she . she feel a certain low power in herself . true , she be a little afraid of that anger . but that be what she want . she would have no use for a Niña of whom she be not a bit afraid . and she want to be able to provoke that anger , of which she feel a certain abject twinge of fear . 

 ah the dark race ! Kate 's own Irish be near enough for she to have glimpse some of the mystery . the dark race belong to a bygone cycle of humanity . they be leave behind in a gulf out of which they have never be able to climb . and on to the particular white man 's level they never will be able to climb . they can only follow as servant . 

 while the white man keep the impetus of his own proud , onward march , the dark race will yield and serve , perforce . but let the white man once have a misgiving about his own leadership , and the dark race will at once attack he , to pull he down into the old gulfs . to engulf he again . 

 which be what be happen . for the white man , let he bluster as he may , be hollow with misgive about his own supremacy . 

 full speed ahead , then , for the débâcle . 

 but once Kate have be rouse to a passion of revulsion from these lice - picking , down - drag people , they change again , and serve she with a certain true wistfulness that could not but touch she . Juana care really about nothing . but just that last thread of relationship that connect she with Kate and the upper world of daylight and fresh air , she do not   want to break . no , no , she do not   want finally to drive her Niña away . no , no , the only one thing she do want , ultimately , be to serve her Niña . 

 but at the same time , she cherish a deep malevolent grudge against rich people , white people , superior people . perhaps the white man have finally betray his own leadership . who know ! but it be a thing of the brave , on - marching soul , and perhaps this have be betray already by the white man . so that the dark be rise upon he . 

 Juana would come to Kate , tell her story from the past . and the sinister mocking film would be on her black eye , and her lined copper face would take on its reptile mask as she would continue : ' usted sabe , Niña , los gringo , los gringuito llevan todo - you know , Niña , the gringo and the gringuito take away everything . . . ' 

 the gringo be the Americans . but Kate herself be include by Juana in the gringuito : the white foreigner . the woman be make another slide , insolent attack . 

 ' it be possible , ' say Kate coldly . ' but tell I what I take away from Mexico . ' 

 ' no , Niña , no ! ' the subtle smile of satisfaction lurk under the bronze tarnish of Juana 's face . she have be able to get at the other woman , touch the raw . ' I do not   speak of you , Niña ! ' but there be too much protest in it . 

 almost , they want to drive she away : to insult she and drag she down and make she want to go away . they could not   help it . like the Irish , they could cut off their nose to spite their face . 

 the backward race ! 

 at the same time there be a true pathos about they . Ezequiel have work for a man for two month , build a house , when he be a boy of fourteen , in order to get a serape . at the end of the two month , the man have put he off , and he have not get the serape : have never get it . a bitter disappointment . 

 but , then , Kate be not responsible for that . and Juana seem almost to make she so . 

 a people without the energy of get on , how could they fail to be hopelessly exploit . they have be hopelessly and cruelly exploit , for century . and their backbone be lock in malevolent resistance . 

 ' but , ' as Kate say to herself , ' I do not   want to exploit they . not a bit . on the contrary , I be willing to give more than I get . but that nasty insinuate insultingness be not fair in the game . I never insult they . I be so careful not to hurt they . and then they deliberately make these centipede attack on I , and be pleased when I be hurt . ' 

 but she know her own Irish at the game . so she be able to put Juana and the girl away from she , and isolate herself from they . once they be put away , their malevolence subside and they remember what Kate want . while she stay amiable , they forget . they forget to sweep the patio , they forget to keep themselves clean . only when they be shove back , into isolation , do they remember again . 

 the boy , Ezequiel , seem to she to have more honour than the woman . he never make these insidious attack . 

 and when her house be clean and quiet and the air seem clean again , the soul renew , her old fondness for the family come back . their curious flitting , come and go , like bird : the busy clap - clap - clapping of tortilla , the excited scrunching of tomato and chile on the metate , as Juana prepare sauce . the noise of the bucket in the well . Jesús , come to water the garden . 

 the game , the game of it all ! everything they do must be fun , or they could not do it . they could not abstract themselves to a routine . never . everything must be fun , must be variable , must be a bit of an adventure . it be confusion , but after all , a live confusion , not a dead , dreary thing . Kate remember her english servant in the english kitchen : so mechanical and somehow inhuman . well , this be the other extreme . 

 here there be no discipline nor method at all . although Juana and her brat really want to do the thing Kate wish they must do they their own way . sometimes Kate feel distract : after all , the mechanical line be so much easy to follow . but as far as possible , she let the family be . she have to get use , for example , to the vagary of her dining - table : a little round table that always stand on the veranda . at breakfast time it would be discreetly set under the planta by the salon ; for dinner , at one o'clock , it would have travel way down the veranda ; for tea it might be under a little tree on the grass . and then Juana would decide that the Niña must take supper , two egg , ranchero , in the dining - room itself , isolate at the corner of the long dining - table mean for fourteen people . 

 the same with the dish . why they should , after wash up in the big bowl in the kitchen for several day , suddenly struggle way down to the lake with the unwashed pot in a basket on Concha 's shoulder , Kate never know . except for the fun of the thing . 

 child ! but , then , not at all child . none of the wonder insouciance of childhood . something dark and cognisant in their soul all the time : some heavy weight of resistance . they work in fit and start , and could be very industrious ; then come day when they lay about on the ground like pig . at time they be merry , seat round on the ground in group , like arabian night , and laugh away . then suddenly resist even merriment in themselves , relapse into the numb gloom . when they be busily work , suddenly , for no reason , throw away the tool , as if resent have give themselves . careless in their moral , always change their love , the man at least resist all the time any real giving of themselves . they do not   want the thing they be pursue . it be the woman who draw they on . and a young man and a girl go down the road from the lake in the dark , teasing and poke each other in excitement , would startle Kate because of their unusualness - the man and woman never walk their sex abroad , as white people do . and the sudden , sexual laugh of the man , so strange a sound of pain and desire , obstinate reluctance , and helpless passion , a noise as if something tear in his breast , be a sound to remember . 

 Kate feel her household a burden . in a sense , they be like parasite , they want to live on her life , and pull she down , pull she down . again , they be so generous with she , so good and gentle , she feel they be wonderful . and then once more she come up against that unconscious , heavy , reptilian indifference in they , indifference and resistance . 

 her servant be the clue to all the native life , for she . the man always together , erect , handsome , balance their great hat on the top of their head and sitting , stand , crouch with a snake - like impassivity . the woman together separately , soft , and as if hide , wrap tight in their dark rebozos . man and woman seem always to be turn their back on one another , as if they do not   want to see one another . no flirting , no courting . only an occasional quick , dark look , the signal of a weapon - like desire , give and take . 

 the woman seem , on the whole , softly callous and determined to go their own way : to change man if they wish . and the man seem not to care very profoundly . but it be the woman who want the man . 

 the native woman , with their long black hair stream down their full , ruddy back , would bathe at one end of the beach , usually wear their chemise , or a little skirt . the man take absolutely no notice . they do not   even look the other way . it be the woman bath , that be all . as if it be , like the charale swimming , just a natural part of the lake life . the man just leave that part of the lake to the woman . and the woman sit in the shallow of the lake , isolate in themselves like moor - fowl , pour water over their head and over their ruddy arm from a gourd scoop . 

 the quiet , unobtrusive , but by no mean down - trodden woman of the peon class . they go their own way , envelop in their rebozos as in their own darkness . they hurry nimbly along , their full cotton skirt swing , chirping and quick like bird . or they sit in the lake with long hair streaming , pour water over themselves : again like bird . or they pass with a curious slow inevitability up the lake - shore , with a heavy red jar of water perch on one shoulder , one arm over the head , hold the rim of the jar . they have to carry all water from the lake to their house . there be no town supply . or , especially on Sunday afternoon , they sit in their doorway de - louse one another . the most resplendent belle , with magnificent black wavy hair , be most thoroughly de - loused . it be as if it be a meritorious public act . 

 the man be the obvious figure . they assert themselves on the air . they be the dominant . usually they be in loose group , talk quietly , or silent : always stand or sit apart , rarely touch one another . often a single man would stand alone at a street corner in his serape , motionless for hour , like some powerful spectre . or a man would lie on the beach as if he have be cast up dead from the water . impassive , motionless , they would sit side by side on the bench of the plaza , not exchange a word . each one isolate in his own fate , his eye black and quick like a snake 's , and as blank . 

 it seem to Kate that the high thing this country might produce would be some powerful relationship of man to man . marriage itself would always be a casual thing . though the man seem very gentle and protective to the little child . then they forget they . 

 but sex itself be a powerful , potent thing , not to be play with or parade . the one mystery . and a mystery great than the individual . the individual hardly count . 

 it be strange to Kate to see the indian hut on the shore , little hole build of straw or corn - stalk , with half - naked child squat on the naked earth floor , and a lousy woman - squalor around , a litter of rag and bone , and a sharp smell of human excrement . the people have no nose . and stand silent and erect not far from the hole of the doorway , the man , handsome and impassive . how could it be , that such a fine - look human male should be so absolutely indifferent , content with such paltry squalor ? 

 but there he be , unconscious . he seem to have life and passion in he . and she know he be strong . no man in the world can carry heavy load on their back , for long distance , than these Indians . she have see an indian trotting down a street with a piano on his back : hold it , also , by a band round his forehead . from his forehead , and on his spine he carry it , trot along . the woman carry with a band round the breast . 

 so there be strength . and apparently , there be passionate life . but no energy . nowhere in Mexico be there any sign of energy . this be , as it be , switch off . 

 even the new artisan class , though it imitate the artisan class of the United States , have no real energy . there be workman 's club . the workman dress up and parade a good girl on their arm . but somehow it seem what it be , only a weak imitation . 

 Kate 's family be increase , without she expect it . one day there arrive from Ocotlan a beautiful ox - eyed girl of about fifteen , wrap in her black cotton rebozo , and somewhat towny in her Madonna - meekness : Maria del Carmen . with she , Julio , a straight and fierce young man of twenty - two . they have just be marry , and have come to Sayula for a visit . Julio be Juana 's cousin . 

 might they sleep in the patio with herself and the girl , be Juana 's request . they would stay only two day . 

 Kate be amazed . Maria del Carmen must have have some spanish blood , her beauty be touch with Spain . she seem even refined and superior . yet she be to sleep out on the ground like a dog , with her young husband . and he , so erect and proud - look , possess nothing in the world but an old serape . 

 ' there be three spare bedroom , ' say Kate . ' they may sleep in one of those . ' 

 the bed be single bed . would they need more blanket ? she ask Juana . 

 no ! they would manage with the one serape of Julio 's . 

 the new family have arrive . Julio be a bricklayer . that be to say , he work build the adobe wall of the little house . he belong to Sayula , and have come back for a visit . 

 the visit continue . Julio would come stride in at midday and at evening ; he be look for work . Maria del Carmen , in her one black dress , would squat on the floor and pat tortillas . she be allow to cook they in Juana 's kitchen hole . and she talk and laugh with the girl . at night , when Julio be home , he would lie on the ground with his back to the wall , impassive , while Maria del Carmen fondle his thick black hair . 

 they be in love . but even now , he be not yield to his love . 

 she want to go back to Ocotlan , where she be at home , and more a señorita than here in Sayula . but he refuse . there be no money : the young ménage live on about five american cent a day . 

 Kate be sewing . Maria del Carmen , who do not   even know how to put a chemise together , watch with great eye . Kate teach she , and buy a length of cotton material . Maria del Carmen be sew herself a dress ! 

 Julio have get work at a peso a day . the visit continue . Kate think Julio be not   very nice with Maria del Carmen : his quiet voice be so overbearing in command when he speak to she . and Maria del Carmen , who be a bit towny , do not take it well . she brood a little . 

 the visit stretch into week . and now Juana be get a bit tired of her relative . 

 but Julio have get a bit of money . he have rent a little one - room adobe house , at one peso fifty per week . Maria del Carmen be go to move into her own home . 

 Kate see the new outfit get together . it consist of one straw mat , three cooking - plate of earthenware , five bit of native crockery , two wooden spoon , one knife and Julio 's old blanket . that be all . but Maria del Carmen be move in . 

 Kate present she with a large old eiderdown , whose silk be rather worn , a couple of bowl , and a few more bit of crockery . Maria del Carmen be set up . good ! good ! oh good ! Kate hear her voice down the patio . I have get a coverlet ! I have get a coverlet ! 

 in the rainy season , the night can be very cold , owe to evaporation . then the native lie through the small hour like lizard , numb and prostrate with cold . they be lie on the damp earth on a thin straw mat , with a corner of an old blanket to cover they . and the same terrible inertia make they endure it , without try to make any change . they could carry in corn husk or dry banana leaf for a bed . they could even cover themselves with banana leaf . 

 but no ! on a thin mat on damp cold earth they lie and tremble with cold , night after night , night after night , night after night . 

 but Maria del Carmen be a bit towny . oh good ! oh good ! I have   get a coverlet ! 

 

 

 CHAPTER X 

 Don Ram n and Doña Carlota 

 

 Kate have be in Sayula ten day before she have any sign from Don Ram n. she have be out in a boat on the lake , and have see his house , round the bend of the western point . it be a reddish - and - yellow two - storey house with a little stone basin for the boat , and a mango grove between it and the lake . among the tree , away from the lake , be the black adobe hut , two row , of the peon . 

 the hacienda have once be a large one . but it have be irrigate from the hill , and the revolution have break all the aqueduct . only a small supply of water be available . then Don Ram n have have enemy in the Government . so that a good deal of his land be take away to be divide among the peon . now , he have only some three hundred acre . the two hundred acre along the lake - shore be mostly lose to he . he work a few acre of fruit land round the house , and in a tiny valley just in the hill he raise sugar - cane . on the patch of the mountain slope little patch of maize be to be see . 

 but Doña Carlota have money . she be from Torreon and draw still a good income from the mine . 

 a mozo come with a note from Don Ram n : might he bring his wife to call on Kate ? 

 Doña Carlota be a thin , gentle , wide - eyed woman , with a slightly startled expression , and soft , brownish hair . she be pure European in extraction , of a spanish father and french mother : very different from the usual stout , over - powder , ox - like mexican matron . her face be pale , fade , and without any make - up at all . her thin , eager figure have something english about it , but her strange , wide brown eye be not english . she speak only Spanish - or French . but her Spanish be so slow and distinct and slightly plaintive , that Kate understand she at once . 

 the two woman understand one another quickly , but be a little nervous of one another . Doña Carlota be delicate and sensitive like a Chihuahua dog , and with the same slightly prominent eye . Kate feel she have rarely meet a woman with such a dog - like finesse of gentleness . and the two woman talk . ram n , large and muted , keep himself in reserve . it be as if the two woman rush together to unite against his silence and his powerful , different significance . 

 Kate know at once that Doña Carlota love he , but with a love that be now nearly all will . she have worship he , and she have have to leave off worship he . she have have to question he . and she would never now cease from question . 

 so he sit apart , a little constrain , his handsome head hang a little , and his dark , sensitive hand dangle between his thigh . 

 ' I have such a wonderful time ! ' Kate say suddenly to he . ' I dance a dance round the drum with the Men of Quetzalcoatl . ' 

 ' I hear , ' he say , with a rather stiff smile . 

 Doña Carlota understand English , though she would not speak it . 

 ' you dance with the man of Quetzalcoatl ! ' she say in Spanish , in a pained voice . ' but , Señora , why do you do such a thing ? oh why ? ' 

 ' I be fascinated , ' say Kate . 

 ' no , you must not be fascinate . no ! no ! it be not good . I tell you . I be so sorry my husband interest himself in this thing . I be so sorry . ' 

 Juana be bring a bottle of vermouth : all that Kate have to offer her visitor , in the morning . 

 ' you go to see your boy in the United States ? ' say Kate to Doña Carlota . ' how be they ? ' 

 ' oh , well , thank you . they be well ; that is , the young be very delicate . ' 

 ' you do not   bring he home ? ' 

 ' no ! no ! I think they be well at school . here - here - there be so many thing to trouble they . no ! but they will come home next month , for the vacation . ' 

 ' how nice ! ' say Kate . ' then I shall see they . they will be here , will not   they ? - on the lake ? ' 

 ' well ! - I be not sure . perhaps for a little while . you see I be so busy in Mexico with my Cuna . ' 

 ' what be a Cuna ? ' say Kate ; she only know it be the Spanish for cradle . 

 it turn out to be a foundling ' home , run by a few obscure carmelite sister . and Doña Carlota be the director . Kate gather that Don Ram n 's wife be an intense , almost exalt Catholic . she exalt herself in the Church , and in her work for the Cuna . 

 ' there be so many child bear in Mexico , ' say Doña Carlota , ' and so many die . if only we could save they , and equip they for life . we do a little , all we can . ' 

 it seem the waste , unwanted baby could be deliver in at the door of the Cuna , like parcel . the mother have only to knock , and hand in the little live bundle . 

 ' it save so many mother from neglect their baby , and let they die , ' say Doña Carlota . ' then we do what we can . if the mother do not   leave a name , I name the child . very often I do . the mother just hand over a little naked thing , sometimes without a name or a rag to cover it . and we never ask . ' 

 the child be not all keep in the home . only a small number . of the other , some decent indian woman be pay a small sum to take the child into her home . every month she must come with the little one to the Cuna , to receive her wage . the Indians be so very rarely unkind to child . Careless , yes . but rarely , rarely unkind . 

 in former day , Doña Carlota say , nearly every well - bear lady in Mexico would receive one or more of these foundling into her home , and have it bring up with the family . it be the loose , patriarchal generosity innate in the bosom of the Spanish - Mexicans . but now , few child be adopt . instead , they be teach as far as possible to be carpenter or gardener , or house - servant , or , among the girl , dressmaker , even school - teacher . 

 Kate listen with uneasy interest . she feel there be so much real human feeling in this mexican charity : she be almost rebuke . perhaps what Doña Carlota be do be the good that could be do , in this half - wild , helpless country . at the same time , it be such a forlorn hope , it make one 's heart sink . 

 and Doña Carlota , confident as she be in her good work , still have just a bit the look of a victim ; a gentle , sensitive , slightly startled victim . as if some secret enemy drain her blood . 

 Don Ram n sit there impassive , listen without heeding ; solid and unmove against the charitable quiver of his wife 's emotion . he let she do as she would . but against her work and against her flow he be in silent , heavy , unchanging opposition . she know this , and tremble in her nervous eagerness , as she talk to Kate about the Cuna , and win Kate 's sympathy . till it seem to she that there be something cruel in Don Ram n 's passive , mask poise . an impassive male cruelty , changeless as a stone idol . 

 ' now will not   you come and spend the day with I while I be here with Don Ram n ? ' say Doña Carlota . ' the house be very poor and rough . it be no long what it use to be . but it be your house if you will come . ' 

 Kate accept , and say she would prefer to walk out . it be only four mile , and surely she would be safe , with Juana . 

 ' I will send a man to come with you , ' say Don Ram n. ' it might not be quite safe . ' 

 ' where be General Viedma ? ' ask Kate . 

 ' we shall try to get he out when you come , ' reply Doña Carlota . ' I be so very fond of Don Cipriano , I have know he for many year , and he be the godfather of my young son . but now he be in command of the Guadalajara division , he be not very often able to come out . ' 

 ' I wonder why he be a general ? ' say Kate . ' he seem to I too human . ' 

 ' oh , but he be very human too . but he be a general ; yes , yes , he want to be in command of the soldier . and I tell you , he be very strong . he have great power with his regiment . they believe in he , oh , they believe in he . he have that power , you know , that some of the high type of Indians have , to make many other want to follow they and fight for they . you know ? Don Cipriano be like that . you can never change he . but I think a woman might be wonderful for he . he have live so without any woman in his life . he will not   care about they . ' 

 ' what do he care about ? ' ask Kate . 

 ' ah ! ' Doña Carlota start as if sting . then she glance quickly , involuntarily at her husband , as she add : ' I do not   know . really , I do not   know . ' 

 ' the Men of Quetzalcoatl , ' say Don Ram n heavily , with a little smile . 

 but Doña Carlota seem to be able to take all the ease and the banter out of he . he seem stiff and a bit stupid . 

 ' ah , there ! there ! there you have it ! the Men of Quetzalcoatl - that be a nice thing for he to care about ! a nice thing , I say , ' flutter Doña Carlota , in her gentle , fragile , scold way . and it be evident to Kate that she adore both the man , and tremble in opposition to their wrongness , and would never give in to they . 

 to ram n it be a terrible burden , his wife 's quivering , absolute , blind opposition , take in conjunction with her helpless adoration . 

 a man - servant appear at nine o'clock one morning , to accompany Kate to the hacienda , which be call Jamiltepec . he have a basket , and have be shop in the market . an elderly man , with grey in his moustache , he have bright young eye and seem full of energy . his bare foot in the huarache be almost black with exposure , but his clothe be brilliantly white . 

 Kate be glad to be walk . the one depress thing about life in the village be that one could not walk out into the country . there be always the liability to be hold up or attack . and she have walk already , as far as possible , in every direction , in the neighbourhood of the village , accompany usually by Ezequiel . now she be begin to feel a prisoner . 

 she be glad , then , to be set off . the morning be clear and hot , the pale brown lake quite still , like a phantom . People be move on the beach , in the distance tiny , like dot of white : white dot of man follow the faint dust of donkey . she wonder often why humanity be like speck in the mexican landscape ; just speck of life . 

 they pass from the lake shore to the rough , dusty road go west , between the steep slope of the hill and the bit of flat by the lake . for almost a mile there be villa , most of they shut up fast , some of they smash , with broken wall and smash window . only flower bloom in mass above the rubble . 

 in the empty place be flimsy straw hut of the native , haphazard , as if blow there . by the road under the hill be black - grey adobe hut , like box , and fowl run about , and brown pig or grey pig spot with black careered and grunt , and half - naked child , dark orange - brown , trot or lie flat on their face in the road , their little naked posterior hunch up , fast asleep . already asleep again .
