 the house be many of they be re - thatched , or the tile roof be be patch by man who assume a great air of importance at have undertake such a task . they be pretend to hurry , too , because the real rain might begin any day . and in the little stony level by the lake , the land be be scratch - plough by a pair of oxen and a lump of pointed wood . 

 but this part of the road Kate know . she know the fine villa on the knoll , with its tuft of palm , and the lay - out avenue that be lay out , indeed , as the dead be , to crumble back again . she be glad to be past the villa , where the road come down to the lake again , under big shady tree that have twist , wriggly bean . on the left be the water , the colour of turtledove , lap the pale fawn stone . at a water - hole of a stream in the beach , a cluster of woman be busily wash clothe . in the shallow of the lake itself two woman sit bath , their black hair hang dense and wet . a little far along a man be wad slowly , stop to throw his round net skilfully upon the water , then slowly stoop and gather it in , pick out the tiny , glittery fish call charale . strangely silent and remote everything , in the gleam morning , as if it be some distant period of time . 

 a little breeze be come from the lake , but the deep dust underfoot be hot . on the right the hill rise precipitous , baked and yellowish , give back the sun and the intense dryness , and exhale the faint , desiccated , peculiar smell of Mexico , that smell as if the earth have sweat itself dry . 

 all the time string of donkey trot laden through the dust , their driver stalk erect and rapid behind , watch with eye like black hole , but always answer Kate 's salute with a respectful Adi s ! and Juana echo her laconic Adi sn ! she be limp , and she think it horrible of Kate to walk four mile , when they might have struggle out in an old hire motor - car , or go in a boat , or even ride donkey - back . 

 but to go on foot ! Kate could hear all her criada 's feeling in the drawled , sardonic Adi sn ! but the man behind strode bravely and call cheerfully . his pistol be prominent in his belt . 

 a bluff of yellow rock come jut at the road . the road wound round it , and into a piece of flat open country . there be field of dry stone , and hedge of dusty thorn and cactus . to the left the bright green of the willow by the lake - shore . to the right the hill swerve inland , to meet the sheer , fluted side of dry mountain . away ahead , the hill curve back at the shore , and a queer little crack or niche show . this crack in the hill lead from Don Ram n 's shore - property to the little valley where he grow the sugar - cane . and where the hill approach the lake again there be a dark clustering of mango - tree , and the red upper storey of the hacienda house . 

 ' there it be ! ' cry the man behind . ' Jamiltepec , Señorita . ' La hacienda de Don Ram n ! ' 

 and his eye shine as he say the name . he be a proud peon , and he really seem happy . 

 ' look ! how far ! ' cry Juana . 

 ' another time , ' say Kate , ' I shall come alone , or with Ezequiel . ' 

 ' no , Niña ! do not   say so . only my foot hurt this morning . ' 

 ' yes . well not to bring you . ' 

 ' no , Niña ! I like to come , very much ! ' 

 the tall windmill fan for draw up water from the lake be spin gaily . a little valley come down from the niche in the hill , and at the bottom a little water run . towards the lake , where this valley flatten out , be a grove of banana - plant , screen a little from the lake breeze by a vivid row of willow - tree . and on the top of the slope , where the road run into the shade of mango - trees , be the two row of adobe hut , like a village , set a little back from the road . 

 woman be come up between the tree , on the patch from the lake , with jar of water on their shoulder ; child be play around the door , squat with little naked posterior in deep dust ; and here and there a goat be tether . man in soil white clothe be lounge , with fold arm and one leg cross in front of the other , against the corner of a house , or crouch under the wall . not by any mean dolce far niente . they seem to be wait , eternally wait for something . 

 ' that way , Señorita ! ' call the man with the basket , run to her side and indicate the smoother road slop down between some big tree , towards the white gate of the hacienda . ' we be here ! ' 

 always he speak with pleased delight , as if the place be a wonder - place to he . 

 the big door of the zaguán , the entrance , stand open , and in the shade of the entrance - way a couple of little soldier be seat . across the clear , straw - litter space in front of the gate two peon be trot , each with a big bunch of banana on his head . the soldier say something , and the two peon halt in their trotting , and slowly turn under their yellow - green load , to look back at Kate and Juana and the man Martin , approach down the road . then they turn again and trot into the courtyard , barefoot . 

 the soldier stand up . Martin , trot at Kate 's side again , usher she into the arched entrance , where the ox - wagon rumble through have wear deep rut . Juana come behind , make a humble noise . 

 Kate find herself in a big , barren yard , that seem empty . there be high wall on the three side , with shed and stable . the fourth side , face , be the house , with heavily - bar window look on to the courtyard , but with no door . instead , there be another zaguán , or passage with closed door pierce the house . 

 Martin trot ahead to knock on the closed door . Kate stand look round at the big yard . in a shed in one corner , four half - naked man be pack bunch of banana . a man in the shade be saw pole , and two man in the sun be unload tile from a donkey . in a corner be a bullock - wagon , and a pair of big black - and - white oxen stand with head press down , wait . 

 the big door open , and Kate enter the second zaguán . it be a wide entrance way , with stair go up on one side , and Kate linger to look through the open iron gate in front of she , down a formal garden hem in with huge mango - tree , to the lake , with its little artificial harbour where two boat be moor . the lake seem to give off a great light , between the dark wall of mango . 

 at the back of the new - comer the servant woman close the big door on to the yard , then wave Kate to the stair . 

 ' pass this way , Señorita . ' 

 a bell tinkle above . Kate climb the stone stair . and there above she be Doña Carlota , in white muslin and with white shoe and stocking , her face look curiously yellow and fade by contrast . her soft brown hair be low over her ear , and she hold out her thin brownish arm with queer effusiveness . 

 ' so you have come ! and you have walk , walk all the way ? oh , imagine walk in so much sun and dust ! come , come in and rest . ' 

 she take Kate 's hand and lead she across the open terrace at the top of the stair . 

 ' it be beautiful here , ' say Kate . 

 she stand on the terrace , look out past the mango - tree at the lake . a distant sailing - canoe be go down the breeze , on the pallid , unreal water . away across rise the bluish , grooved mountain , with the white speck of a village : far away in the morning it seem , in another world , in another life , in another mode of time . 

 ' what be that village ? ' Kate ask . 

 ' that one ? that one there ? it be San Ildefonso , ' say Doña Carlota , in her flutter eagerness . 

 ' but it be beautiful here ! ' Kate repeat . 

 ' Hermoso - sí ! Sí , bonito ! ' quaver the other woman uneasily , always answer in Spanish . 

 the house , reddish and yellow in colour , have two short wing towards the lake . the terrace , with green plant on the terrace wall , go round the three side , the roof above support by big square pillar that rise from the ground . down below , the pillar make a sort of cloister around the three side , and in the little stone court be a pool of water . beyond , the rather neglect formal garden with strong sun and deep mango - shade . 

 ' come , you will need to rest ! ' say Doña Carlota . 

 ' I would like to change my shoe , ' say Kate . 

 she be show into a high , simple , rather bare bedroom with red - tile floor . there she change into the shoe and stocking Juana have carry , and rest a little . 

 as she lay rest , she hear the dull thud - thud of the tom - tom drum , but , save the crowing of a cock in the distance , no other sound on the bright , yet curiously hollow mexican morning . and the drum , thud with its dull , black insistence , make she uneasy . it sound like something come over the horizon . 

 she rise , and go into the long , high salon where Doña Carlota be sit talk to a man in black . the salon , with its three window - door open on to the terrace , its worn , red floor tile with old square brick , its high wall colour - wash a faint green , and the many - beam ceiling whitewash ; and with its bareness of furniture ; seem like part of the out - of - door , like some garden - arbour put for shade . the sense , which house have in hot climate , of be just three wall wherein one linger for a moment , then go away again . 

 as Kate enter the room , the man in black rise and shake hand with Doña Carlota , bow very low and deferential . then with a deferential sideways sort of bow to Kate , he vanish out of door . 

 ' come ! ' say Doña Carlota to Kate . ' be you sure now you be rest ? ' and she pull forward one of the cane rock - chair that have poise itself in the room , en route to nowhere . 

 ' perfectly ! ' say Kate . ' how still it seem here ! except for the drum . perhaps it be the drum that make it seem so still . though I always think the lake make a sort of silence . ' 

 ' ah , the drum ! ' cry Doña Carlota , lift her hand with a gesture of nervous , spend exasperation . ' I can not hear it . no , I can not , I can not bear to hear it . ' 

 and she rock herself in a sudden access of agitation . 

 ' it do hit one rather below the belt , ' say Kate . ' what be it ? ' 

 ' ah , do not ask I ! it be my husband . ' 

 she make a gesture of despair , and rock herself almost into unconsciousness . 

 ' be Don Ram n drum ? ' 

 ' drum ? ' Doña Carlota seem to start . ' no ! oh no ! he be not drum , himself . he bring down two Indians from the north to do that . ' 

 ' do he ! ' say Kate , non - committal . 

 but Doña Carlota be rock in a sort of semi - consciousness . then she seem to pull herself together . 

 ' I must talk to somebody , I must ! ' she say , suddenly straighten herself in her chair , her face creamy and crease , her soft brown hair sag over her ear , her brown eye oddly desperate . ' may I talk to you ? ' 

 ' do ! ' say Kate , rather uneasy . 

 ' you know what Ram n be do ? ' she say , look at Kate almost furtively , suspiciously . 

 ' do he want to bring back the old god ? ' say Kate vaguely . 

 ' ah ! ' cry Doña Carlota , again with that desperate , fly jerk of her hand . ' as if it be possible ! as if it be possible ! the old god ! imagine it , Señora ! the old god ! why , what be they ? nothing but dead illusion . and ugly , repulsive illusion ! ah ! I always think my husband such a clever man , so superior to I ! ah , it be terrible to have to change one 's idea ! this be such nonsense . how dare he ! how dare he take such nonsense seriously ! how do he dare ! ' 

 ' do he believe in it himself ? ' ask Kate . 

 ' himself ? but , Señora - ' and Doña Carlota give a pitiful , pity smile of contempt . ' how could he ! as if it be possible . after all , he be an educate man ! how could he believe in such nonsense ! ' 

 ' then why do he do it ? ' 

 ' why ? why ? ' there be a tone of unspeakable weariness in Doña Carlota 's voice . ' I wish I know . I think he have go insane , as Mexicans do . insane like Francisco Villa , the bandit . ' 

 Kate think of the pug - face notorious Pancho Villa in wonder , unable to connect he with Don Ram n. 

 ' all the Mexicans , as soon as they rise above themselves , go that way , ' say Doña Carlota . ' their pride get the well of they . and then they understand nothing , nothing but their own foolish will , their will to be very , very important . it be just the male vanity . do not   you think , Señora , that the beginning and the end of a man be his vanity ? do not   you think it be just against this danger that Christ come , to teach man a proper humility ? to teach they the sin of pride . but that be why they hate Christ so much , and his teaching . first and last , they want their own vanity . ' 

 Kate have often think so herself . her own final conclusion about man be that they be the vanity of vanity , nothing but vanity . they must be flatter and make to feel great : nothing else . 

 ' and now , my husband want to go to the other extreme of Jesus . he want to exalt pride and vanity high than God . ah , it be terrible , terrible ! and foolish like a little boy ! ah , what be a man but a little boy who need a nurse and a mother ! ah , Señora , I can not   bear it . ' 

 Doña Carlota cover her face with her hand , as if swoon . 

 ' but there be something wonderful , too , about Don Ram n , ' say Kate coaxingly : though at the moment she hat he . 

 ' wonderful ! ah yes , he have gift . he have great gift ! but what be gift to a man who pervert they ! ' 

 ' tell I what you think he really want , ' say Kate . 

 ' power ! just power ! just foolish , wicked power . as if there have not be enough horrible , wicked power let loose in this country . but he - he - want to be beyond they all . he - he - he want to be worship . to be worship ! to be worship ! a God ! he , whom I have   hold , I have   hold in my arm ! he be a child , as all man be child . and now he want - to be worship - ! ' she go off into a shrill , wild laughter , cover her face with her hand , and laugh shrilly , her laughter punctuate by hollow , ghastly sob . 

 Kate sit in absolute dismay , wait for the other woman to recover herself . she feel cold against these hysteric , and exert all her heavy female will to stop they . 

 ' after all , ' she say , when Doña Carlota become quiet , her face in her hand , ' it be not   your fault . we can not   be responsible , even for our husband . I know that , since my husband die , and I could not   prevent he die . and then - then I learn that no matter how you love another person , you can not   really do anything , you be helpless when it come to the last thing . you have to leave they to themselves , when they want to die : or when they want to do thing that seem foolish , so , so foolish , to a woman . ' 

 Doña Carlota look up at the other woman . 

 ' you love your husband very much - and he die ? ' she say softly . 

 ' I do love he . and I shall never , never love another man . I could not . I have   lose the power . ' 

 ' and why do he die ? ' 

 ' ah , even that be really his own fault . he break his own soul and spirit , in those irish politic . I know it be wrong . what do Ireland matter , what do nationalism and all that rubbish matter , really ! and revolution ! they be so , so stupid and vieux jeu . ah ! it would have be so much well if Joachim have be content to live his life in peace , with I . it could be so jolly , so lovely . and I try and try and try with he . but it be no good . he want to kill himself with that beastly irish business , and I try in vain to prevent he . ' 

 Doña Carlota star slowly at Kate . 

 ' as a woman must try to prevent a man , when he be go wrong , ' she say . ' as I try to prevent Ram n. as he will get himself kill , as surely as they all do , down to Francisco Villa . and when they be dead , what good be it all ? ' 

 ' when they be dead , ' say Kate , ' then you know it be no good . ' 

 ' you do ! oh , Señora , if you think you can help I with Ram n , do help I , do ! for it mean the death either of I or he . and I shall die , though he be wrong . unless he get kill . ' 

 ' tell I what he want to do , ' say Kate . ' what do he think he want to do , anyhow ? - like my husband think he want to make a free Ireland and a great irish people . but I know all the time , the Irish be not   a great people any more , and you can not   make they free . they be only good at destroy - just mere stupid destroying . how can you make a people free , if they be not   free ? if something inside they compel they to go on destroy ! ' 

 ' I know ! I know ! and that be Ram n. he want to destroy even Jesus and the Blessed Virgin , for this people . imagine it ! to destroy Jesus and the blessed Virgin ! the last thing they have   get ! ' 

 ' but what do he say himself , that he want to do ? ' 

 ' he say he want to make a new connection between the people and God . he say himself , God be always God . but man lose his connection with God . and then he can never recover it again , unless some new Saviour come to give he his new connection . and every new connection be different from the last , though God be always God . and now , Ram n say , the people have lose God . and the Saviour can not lead they to he any more . there must be a new Saviour with a new vision . but ah , Señora , that be not true for I . God be love , and if Ram n would only submit to love , he would know that he have find God . but he be perverse . ah , if we could be together , quietly loving , and enjoy the beautiful world , and wait in the love of God ! ah , Señora , why , why , why can not   he see it ? oh , why can not   he see it ! instead of do all these - ' 

 the tear come to Doña Carlota 's eye , and spill over her cheek . Kate also be in tear , mop her face . 

 ' it be no good ! ' she say , sob . ' I know it be no good , no matter what we do . they do not   want to be happy and peaceful . they want this strife and these other false , horrible connection . it be no good whatever we do ! that be what be so bitter , so bitter ! ' 

 the two woman sit in their bent - wood rocking - chair and just sob . and as they sob , they hear a step come along the terrace , the faint swish of the sandal of the people . 

 it be Don Ram n , draw unconsciously by the emotional disturbance of the two woman . 

 Doña Carlota hastily dab her eye , and her sniffing nose , Kate blow her nose like a trumpet , and Don Ram n stand in the doorway . 

 he be dress in white , dazzle , in the costume of the peon , the white blouse jacket and the white , wide pantaloon trouser . but the white be linen , slightly starch , and brilliant , almost unnatural in its whiteness . from under his blouse , in front , hang the end of a narrow woollen sash , white , with blue and black bar , and a fringe of scarlet . and on his naked foot be the plait huarache , of blue and black strip of leather , with thick , red - dye sol . his loose trouser be bind round the ankle with blue , red , and black woollen braid . 

 Kate glance at he as he stand in the sun , so dazzingly white , that his black hair and dark face look like a hole in the atmosphere . he come forward , the end of his sash swing against his thigh , his sandal slightly swish . 

 ' I be pleased to see you , ' he say , shake hand with Kate . ' how do you come ? ' 

 he drop into a chair , and sit quite still . the two woman hang their head , hide their face . the presence of the man seem to put their emotion out of joint . he ignore all the sign of their discomfort , overlook it with a powerful will . there be a certain strength in his presence . they all cheer up a bit . 

 ' you do not   know my husband have become one of the people - a real peon - a Señor Peon , like Count Tolstoy become a Señor Moujik ? ' say Doña Carlota , with an attempt at raillery . 

 ' anyway it suit he , ' say Kate . 

 ' there ! ' say Don Ram n. ' give the devil his due . ' 

 but there be something unyielding , unbend about he . he laugh and speak to the woman only from a surface self . underneath , powerful and inscrutable , he make no connection with they . 

 so it be at lunch . there be a flit conversation , with interval of silence . it be evident that Ram n be think in another world , in the silence . and the ponderous stillness of his will , work in another sphere , make the woman feel overshadowed . 

 ' the Señora be like I , Ram n , ' say Doña Carlota . ' she can not bear the sound of that drum . must it play any more this afternoon ? ' 

 there be a moment 's pause , before he answer : 

 ' after four o'clock only . ' 

 ' must we have that noise to - day ? ' Carlota persist . 

 ' why not to - day like other day ! ' he say . but a certain darkness be on his brow , and it be evident he want to leave the presence of the two woman . 

 ' because the Señora be here : and I be here : and we neither of we like it . and to - morrow the Señora will not be here , and I shall be go back to Mexico . so why not spare we to - day ! surely you can show we this consideration . ' 

 Ram n look at she , and then at Kate . there be anger in his eye . and Kate could almost feel , in his powerful chest , the big heart swell with a suffocation of anger . both woman keep mum . but it please they , anyhow , that they could make he angry . 

 ' why not row with Mrs Leslie on the lake ! ' he say , with quiet control . 

 but under his dark brow be a level , indignant anger . 

 ' we may not want to , ' say Carlota . 

 then he do what Kate have not know anyone to do before . he withdraw his consciousness away from they as they all three sit at table , leave the two woman , as it be , seat outside a closed door , with nothing more happen . Kate feel for the time startle and forlorn , then a slow anger burn in her warm ivory cheek . 

 ' oh , yes , ' she say . ' I can start home before then . ' 

 ' no ! no ! ' say Doña Carlota , with a spanish wail . ' do not   leave I . stay with I till evening , and help I to amuse Don Cipriano . he be come to supper . ' 

 

 

 CHAPTER XI 

 Lords of the Day and Night 

 

 when lunch be over , Ram n go to his room , to sleep for an hour . it be a hot , still afternoon . cloud be stand erect and splendid , at the west end of the lake , like messenger . Ram n go into his room and close the window - door and the shutter , till it be quite dark , save for yellow pencil of light that stand like substance on the darkness , from the crack of the shutter . 

 he take off his clothe , and in the darkness thrust his clenched fist upwards above his head , in a terrible tension of stretch , upright prayer . in his eye be only darkness , and slowly the darkness revolve in his brain , too , till he be mindless . only a powerful will stretch itself and quiver from his spine in an immense tension of prayer . stretch the invisible bow of the body in the darkness with inhuman tension , erect , till the arrow of the soul , mindless , shoot to the mark , and the prayer reach its goal . 

 then , suddenly , the clenched and quiver arm drop , the body relax into softness . the man have reach his strength again . he have break the cord of the world , and be free in the other strength . 

 softly , delicately , take great care not to think , not to remember , not to disturb the poisonous snake of mental consciousness , he pick up a thin , fine blanket , wrap it round he , and lie down on the pile of mat on the floor . in an instant he be asleep . 

 he sleep in complete oblivion for about an hour . then suddenly he open his eye wide . he see the velvety darkness , and the pencil of light go frail . the sun have move . listen , there seem not a sound in the world : there be no world . 

 then he begin to hear . he hear the faint rumble of an ox - wagon : then leave in a wind : then a faint tap noise : then the creak of some bird call . 

 he rise and quickly dress in the dark , and throw open the door . it be mid - afternoon , with a hot wind blow , and cloud rear up dark and bronze in the west , the sun hide . but the rain would not fall yet . he take a big straw hat and balance it on his head . it have a round crest of black and white and blue feather , like an eye , or a sun , in front . he hear the low sound of woman talk . ah , the strange woman ! he have forget she . and Carlota ! Carlota be here ! he think of she for a moment , and of her curious opposition . then , before he could be angry , he lift his breast again in the black , mindless prayer , his eye go dark , and the sense of opposition leave he . 

 he go quickly , driftingly along the terrace to the stone stair that lead down to the inner entrance - way . go through to the courtyard , he see two man pack bale of banana upon donkey , under a shed . the soldier be sleep in the zaguán . through the open door , up the avenue of tree , he could see an ox - wagon slowly retreat . within the courtyard there be the sharp ringing of metal hammer on an anvil . it come from a corner where be a smithy , where a man and a boy be work . in another shed a carpenter be plan wood . 

 Don Ram n stand a moment to look around . this be his own world . his own spirit be spread over it like a soft , nourishing shadow , and the silence of his own power give it peace . 

 the man work be almost instantly aware of his presence . one after the other the dark , hot face glance up at he , and glance away again . they be man , and his presence be wonderful to they ; but they be afraid to approach he , even by star at he . they work the quick for have see he , as if it give they new life . 

 he go across to the smithy , where the boy be blow the old - fashioned bellow , and the man be hammer a piece of metal , with quick , light blow . the man work on without lift his head , as the patr n draw near . 

 ' it be the bird ? ' say Ram n , stand watch the piece of metal , now cold upon the anvil . 

 ' yes , Patr n ! it be the bird . be it right ? ' and the man look up with black , bright , wait eye . 

 the smith lift with the tong the black , flat , tongue - shape piece of metal , and Ram n look at it a long time . 

 ' I put the wing on after , ' say the smith . 

 Ram n trace with his dark , sensitive hand an imaginary line , outside the edge of the iron . three time he do it . and the movement fascinate the smith . 

 ' a little more slender - so ! ' say Ram n. 

 ' yes , Patr n ! yes ! yes ! I understand , ' say the man eagerly . 

 ' and the rest ? ' 

 ' here it be ! ' the man point to two hoop of iron , one small than the other , and to some flat disc of iron , triangular in shape . 

 ' lay they on the ground . ' 

 the man put the hoop on the ground , one within the other . then , take the triangular disc , he place they with quick , sensitive hand , so that their basis be upon the outer circle , and their apex touch the inner . there be seven . and thus they make a seven - pointed sun of the space inside . 

 ' now the bird , ' say Ram n. 

 the man quickly take the long piece of iron : it be the rudimentary form of a bird , with two foot , but , as yet without wing . he place it in the centre of the inner circle , so that the foot touch the circle and the crest of the head touch opposite . 

 ' so ! it fit , ' say the man . 

 Ram n stand look at the big iron symbol on the ground . he hear the door of the inner entrance : Kate and Carlota walk across the courtyard . 

 ' I take it away ? ' ask the workman quickly . 

 ' never mind , ' Ram n answer quietly . 

 Kate stand and star at the great wreath of iron on the ground . 

 ' what be it ? ' she ask brightly . 

 ' the bird within the sun . ' 

 ' be that a bird ? ' 

 ' when it have wing . ' 

 ' ah , yes ! when it have wing . and what be it for ? ' 

 ' for a symbol to the people . ' 

 ' it be pretty . ' 

 ' yes . ' 

 ' ram n ! ' say Doña Carlota , ' will you give I the key for the boat ? Martin will row we out . ' 

 he produce the key from under his sash . 

 ' where do you get that beautiful sash ? ' ask Kate . 

 it be the white sash with blue and brown - black bar , and with a heavy red fringe . 

 ' this ? ' he say . ' we wove it here . ' 

 ' and do you make the sandal too ? ' 

 ' yes ! they be make by Manuel . later I will show you . ' 

 ' oh , I should like to see ! - they be beautiful , do not   you think , Doña Carlota ? ' 

 ' yes ! yes ! it be true . but whether beautiful thing be wise thing , I do not   know . so much I do not   know , Señora . ay , so much ! - and you , do you know what be wise ? ' 

 ' I ? ' say Kate . ' I do not   care very much . ' 

 ' ah ! you do not   care ! - you think Ram n be wise , to wear the peasant ' clothe , and the huarache ? ' for once Doña Carlota be speak in slow English . 

 ' oh , yes ! ' cry Kate . ' he look so handsome ! - man 's clothe be so hideous , and Don Ram n look so handsome in those ! ' with the big hat poise on his head , he have a certain air of nobility and authority . 

 ' ah ! ' cry Doña Carlota , look at the other woman with intelligent , half - scared eye , and swing the key of the boat . ' shall we go to the lake ? ' 

 the two woman depart . ram n , laugh to himself , go out of the gate and across the outer yard , to where a big , barn - like building stand near the tree . he enter the barn , and give a low whistle . it be answer from the loft above , and a trap - door open . Don Ram n go up the step , and find himself in a sort of studio and carpenter 's shop . a fattish young man with curly hair , wear an artist 's blouse , and with mallet and chisel in his hand , greet he . 

 ' how be it go ? ' ask Ram n. 

 ' yes - well - ' 

 the artist be work on a head , in wood . it be large than life , conventionalize . yet under the conventional line the likeness to Ram n reveal itself . 

 ' sit for I for half an hour , ' say the sculptor . 

 Ram n sit in silence , while the other man bend over his model , work in silent concentration . and all the time , Ram n sit erect , almost motionless , with a great stillness of repose and concentration , think about nothing , but throw out the dark aura of power , in the spell of which the artist work . 

 ' that be enough , ' he say at last , quietly rise . 

 ' but give I the pose before you go , ' say the artist . 

 Ram n slowly take off his blouse - skirt , and stand with naked torso , the sash with its blue and black bar tight round his naked waist . for some moment he stand gather himself together . then suddenly , in a concentration of intense , proud prayer , he fling his right arm up above his head , and stand transfix , his left arm hang softly by his side , the finger touch his thigh . and on his face that fix , intense look of pride which be at once a prayer . 

 the artist gaze with wonder , and with an appreciation touch with fear . the other man , large and intense , with big dark eye star with intense pride , yet prayerful , beyond the natural horizon , send a thrill of dread and of joy through the artist . he bow his head as he look . 

 Don Ram n turn to he . 

 ' now you ! ' he say . 

 the artist be afraid . he seem to quail . but he meet Ram n 's eye . and instantly , that stillness of concentration come over he , like a trance . and then suddenly , out of the trance , he shoot his arm aloft , and his fat , pale face take on an expression of peace , a noble , motionless transfiguration , the blue - grey eye calm , proud , reach into the beyond , with prayer . and though he stand in his blouse , with a rather pudgy figure and curly hair , he have the perfect stillness of nobility . 

 ' it be good ! ' say Ram n , bow his head . 

 the artist suddenly change ; Ram n hold out his two hand ; the artist take they in his two hand . then he lift Ram n 's right hand and place the back of it on his brow . 

 ' Adi s ! ' say Ram n , take his blouse again . 

 ' Adi s , Señor ! ' say the artist . 

 and with a proud , white look of joy in his face , he turn again to his work . 

 Ram n visit the adobe house , its yard fence with cane and overshadow by a great mango - tree , where Manuel and his wife and child , and two assistant , be spin and weaving . two little girl be assiduously card white wool and brown wool under a cluster of banana - tree : the wife and a young maiden be spin fine , fine thread . on the line hang dye wool , red , and blue , and green . and under the shed stand Manuel and a youth , weave at two heavy hand - loom . 

 ' how be it go ? ' call Don Ram n. 

 ' Muy bien ! Muy bien ! ' answer Manuel , with that curious look of transfiguration glistening in his black eye and in the smile of his face . ' it be go well , very well , Señor ! ' 

 Ram n pause to look at the fine white serape on the loom . it have a zig - zag border of natural black wool and blue , in little diamond , and the end a complication of blackish and blue diamond - pattern . the man be just begin to do the centre - call the boca , the mouth : and he look anxiously at the design that be tack to the loom . but it be simple : the same as the iron symbol the smith be make : a snake with his tail in his mouth , the black triangle on his back be the outside of the circle : and in the middle , a blue eagle standing erect , with slim wing touch the belly of the snake with their tip , and slim foot upon the snake , within the hoop . 

 Ram n go back to the house , to the upper terrace , and round to the short wing where his room be . he put a fold serape over his shoulder , and go along the terrace . at the end of this wing , project to the lake , be a square terrace with a low , thick wall and a tile roof , and a coral - scarlet bignonia dangle from the massive pillar . the terrace , or loggia , be strew with the native palm - leaf mat , petate , and there be a drum in one corner , with the drum - stick upon it . at the far inner corner go down an enclose stone staircase , with an iron door at the bottom . 

 Ram n stand a while look out at the lake . the cloud be dissolve again , the sheet of water give off a whitish light . in the distance he could see the dancing speck of a boat , probably Martin with the two woman . 

 he take off his hat and his blouse , and stand motionless , naked to the waist . then he lift the drum - stick , and after wait a moment or two , to become still in soul , he sound the rhythmic summon , rather slow , yet with a curious urge in its strong - weak , one - two rhythm . he have get the old barbaric power into the drum . 

 for some time he stand alone , the drum , or tom - tom , lift by its thong against his leg , his right hand drumming , his face expressionless . a man enter , bareheade , run from the inner terrace . he be in the white cotton clothe , snow white , but with a dark serape fold on his shoulder , and he hold a key in his hand . he salute Ram n by put the back of his right hand in front of his eye for a moment , then he go down the stone stairway and open the iron door . 

 immediately man be come up , all dress alike , in the white cotton clothe and the huarache , each with a fold serape over his shoulder . but their sash be all blue , and their sandal blue and white . the sculptor come too , and Mirabal be there , also dress in the cotton clothe . 

 there be seven man , besides Ram n. at the top of the stair , one after another , they salute . then they take their serape , dark brown , with blue eye fill with white , along the edge , and throw they down along the wall , their hat beside they . then they take off their blouse , and fling they on their hat . 

 Ram n leave the drum , and sit down on his own serape , that be white with the blue and black bar , and the scarlet fringe . the drummer sit down and take the drum . the circle of man sit cross - legged , naked to the waist , silent . some be of a dark , ruddy coffee - brown , two be white , Ram n be of a soft creamy brown . they sit in silence for a time , only the monotonous , hypnotic sound of the drum pulsing , touch the inner air . then the drummer begin to sing , in the curious , small , inner voice , that hardly emerge from the circle , sing in the ancient falsetto of the Indians : 

 ' who sleep - shall wake ! who sleep - shall wake ! who tread down the path of the snake shall arrive at the place ; in the path of the dust shall arrive at the place and be dress in the skin of the snake - ' 

 one by one the voice of the man join in , till they be all sing in the strange , blind infallible rhythm of the ancient barbaric world . and all in the small , inward voice , as if they be sing from the old , darkest recess of the soul , not outward , but inward , the soul sing back to herself . 

 they sing for a time in the peculiar unison like a flock of bird that fly in one consciousness . and when the drum shudder for an end , they all let their voice fade out , with the same broad , clap sound in the throat . 

 there be silence . the man turn , speak to one another , laugh in a quiet way . but their daytime voice , and their daytime eye have go . 

 then Ram n 's voice be hear , and the man be suddenly silent , listen with bent head . Ram n sit with his face lift , look far away , in the pride of prayer . 

 ' there be no before and after , there be only now , ' he say , speak in a proud , but inward voice . 

 ' the great Snake coil and uncoil the plasm of his fold , and star appear , and world fade out . it be no more than the change and easing of the plasm . 

 ' I always be , say his sleep . 

 ' as a man in a deep sleep know not , but be , so be the Snake of the coil cosmo , wear its plasm . 

 ' as a man in a deep sleep have no to - morrow , no yesterday , nor to - day , but only be , so be the limpid , far - reach snake of the eternal Cosmos , now , and forever now . 

 ' now , and only now , and forever now . 

 ' but dream arise and fade in the sleep of the Snake . 

 ' and world arise as dream , and be go as dream . 

 ' and man be a dream in the sleep of the Snake . 

 ' and only the sleep that be dreamless breathe I be ! 

 ' in the dreamless now , I be . 

 ' dream arise as they must arise , and man be a dream arise . 

 ' but the dreamless plasm of the Snake be the plasm of a man , of his body , his soul , and his spirit at one . 

 ' and the perfect sleep of the Snake I be be the plasm of a man , who be whole . 

 ' when the plasm of the body , and the plasm of the soul , and the plasm of the spirit be at one , in the Snake I Am . 

 ' I be now . 

 ' be - not be a dream , and shall - be be a dream , like two separate , heavy foot . 

 ' but now , I be . 

 ' the tree put forth their leaf in their sleep , and flower emerge out of dream , into pure I Am . 

 ' the bird forget the stress of their dream , and sing aloud in the now , I be ! I be ! 

 ' for dream have wing and foot , and journey to take , and effort to make . 

 ' but the glimmering snake of the now be wingless and footless , and undivide , and perfectly coil . 

 ' it be thus the cat lie down , in the coil of now , and the cow curve round her nose to her belly , lie down . 

 ' in the foot of a dream the hare run uphill . but when he pause , the dream have pass , he have enter the timeless now , and his eye be the wide I be . 

 ' only man dream , dream , and dream , and change from dream to dream , like a man who toss on his bed . 

 ' with his eye and his mouth he dream , with his hand and his foot , with phallo and heart and belly , with body and spirit and soul , in a tempest of dream . 

 ' and rush from dream to dream , in the hope of the perfect dream . 

 ' but I , I say to you , there be no dream that be perfect , for every dream have an ache and an urge , an urge and an ache . 

 ' and nothing be perfect , save the dream pass out into the sleep , I be . 

 ' when the dream of the eye be darken , and encompass with now . 

 ' and the dream of the mouth resound in the last I Am . 

 ' and the dream of the hand be a sleep like a bird on the sea , that sleep and be lift and shift , and know not . 

 ' and the dream of the foot and the toe touch the core of the world , where the Serpent sleep . 

 ' and the dream of the phallo reach the great I know not . 

 ' and the dream of the body be the stillness of a flower in the dark . 

 ' and the dream of the soul be go in the perfume of now . 

 ' and the dream of the spirit lapse , and lay down its head , and be still with the Morning Star . 

 ' for each dream start out of now , and be accomplish in now . 

 ' in the core of the flower , the glimmering , wakeless Snake . 

 ' and what fall away be a dream , and what accrue be a dream . there be always and only now , now and I be . ' 

 there be silence in the circle of man . outside , the sound of the bullock - wagon could be hear , and from the lake , the faint knocking of oar . but the seven man sit with their head bent , in the semi - trance , listen inwardly . 

 then the drum begin softly to beat , as if of itself . and a man begin to sing , in a small voice : 

 

 the Lord of the Morning Star 
 Stood between the day and the night : 
 as a bird that lift its wing , and stand 
 with the bright wing on the right 
 and the wing of the dark on the left , 
 the Dawn Star stand into sight . 

 Lo ! I be always here ! 
 far in the hollow of space 
 I brush the wing of the day 
 and put light on your face . 
 the other wing brush the dark . 
 but I , I be always in place . 

 Yea , I be always here . I be Lord 
 in every way . and the lord among man 
 see I through the flashing of wing . 
 they see I and lose I again . 
 but lo ! I be always here 
 within ken . 

 the multitude see I not . 
 they see only the waving of wing , 
 the come and go of thing . 
 the cold and the hot . 

 but ye that perceive I between 
 the tremor of night and the day , 
 I make you the Lords of the 
 Way unseen . 

 the path between gulfs of the dark and the steep of the light ; 
 the path like a snake that be go , like the length of a fuse to ignite 
 the substance of shadow , that burst and explode into sight . 

 I be here undeparte . I sit tight 
 between wing of the endless flight , 
 at the depth of the peace and the fight . 

 Deep in the moisture of peace , 
 and far down the muzzle of the fight 
 you shall find I , who be neither increase 
 nor destruction , different quite . 

 I be far beyond 
 the horizon of love and strife . 
 like a star , like a pond 
 that wash the lord of life . 

 

 ' listen ! ' say Ram n , in the stillness . ' we will be master among man , and lord among man . but lord of man and master of man we will not be . listen ! we be lord of the night . lord of the day and night . son of the Morning Star , son of the Evening Star . man of the Morning and the Evening Star . 

 ' we be not lord of man : how can man make we lord ? nor be we master of man , for man be not worth it . 

 ' but I be the Morning and the Evening Star , and lord of the day and the night . by the power that be put in my left hand , and the power that I grasp in my right , I be lord of the two way . 

 ' and my flower on earth be the jasmine flower , and in heaven the flower Hesperus . 

 ' I will not command you , nor serve you , for the snake go crooked to his own house . 

 ' yet I will be with you , so you depart not from yourself . 

 ' there be no giving , and no taking . when the finger that give touch the finger that receive , the Morning Star shin at once , from the contact , and the jasmine gleam between the hand . and thus there be neither give nor taking , nor hand that proffer nor hand that receive , but the star between they be all , and the dark hand and the light hand be invisible on each side . the jasmine take the giving and the receiving in her cup , and the scent of the oneness be fragrant on the air . 

 ' think neither to give nor to receive , only let the jasmine flower . 

 ' let nothing spill from you in excess , let nothing be reive from you . 

 ' and reive nothing away . not even the scent from the rose , nor the juice from the pomegranate , nor the warmth from the fire . 

 ' but say to the rose : Lo ! I take you away from your tree , and your breath be in my nostril , and my breath be warm in your depth . let it be a sacrament between we . 

 ' and beware when you break the pomegranate ; it be sunset you take in your hand . say : I be come , come thou . let the Evening Star stand between we . 

 ' and when the fire burn up and the wind be cold and you spread your hand to the blaze , listen to the flame say : ah ! be it thou ? com thou to I ? Lo , I be go the long journey , down the path of the great snake . but since thou com to I , I come to thee . and where thou fallest into my hand , fall I into thine , and jasmine flower on the burn bush between we . our meeting be the burn bush , whence the jasmine flower . 

 ' reive nothing away , and let nothing be reive from you . for reiver and bereave alike break the root of the jasmine flower , and spit upon the Evening Star . 

 ' take nothing , to say : I have it ! for you can possess nothing , not even peace . 

 ' Nought be possessible , neither gold , nor land , nor love , nor life , nor peace , nor even sorrow nor death , nor yet salvation . 

 ' say of nothing : it be mine . 

 ' say only : it be with I . 

 ' for the gold that be with thee linger as a depart moon , look across space thy way , say : lo ! we be beholden of each other . lo ! for this little while , to each other thou and I be beholden . 

 ' and thy land say to thee : ah , my child of a far - off father ! come , lift I , lift I a little while , that poppy and wheat may blow on the level wind that move between my breast and thine ! then sink with I , and we will make one mound . 

 ' and listen to thy love say : Beloved ! I be mow by thy sword like mow grass , and darkness be upon I , and the tremble of the Evening Star . and to I thou art darkness and nowhere . oh thou , when thou risest up and goest thy way , speak to I , only say : the star rise between we . 

 ' and say to thy life : be I thine ? art thou mine ? be I the blue curve of day around thine uncurved night ? be my eye twilight of neither of we , where the star hang ? be my upper lip the sunset and my low lip the dawn , do the star tremble inside my mouth ? 

 ' and say to thy peace : ah ! risen , deathless star ! already the water of dawn sweep over thee , and wash I away on the flood ! 

 ' and say to thy sorrow : Axe , thou art cut I down ! 

 ' yet do a spark fly from out of thy edge and my wound ! 

 ' cut then , while I cover my face , father of the Star . 

 ' and say to thy strength : Lo , the night be foam up my foot and my loin , day be foam down from my eye and my mouth to the sea of my breast . Lo , they meet ! my belly be a flood of power , that race in down the sluice of bone at my back , and a star hang low on the flood , over a troubled dawn . 

 ' and say to thy death : be it so ! I , and my soul , we come to thee , Evening Star . flesh , go thou into the night . Spirit , farewell , ' tis thy day . leave I now . I go in last nakedness now to the nakedest Star . ' 

 

 

 CHAPTER XII 

 the First Waters 

 

 the man have rise and cover themselves , and put on their hat , and cover their eye for a second , in salute before Ram n , as they depart down the stone stair . and the iron door at the bottom have clang , the doorkeeper have return with the key , lay it on the drum , and softly , delicately depart . 

 still Ram n sit on his serape , lean his naked shoulder on the wall , and close his eye . he be tired , and in that state of extreme separateness which make it very hard to come back to the world . on the outside of his ear he could hear the noise of the hacienda , even the tinkle of tea - spoon , and the low voice of woman , and later , the low , labour sound of a motor - car struggle over the uneven road , then swirl triumphantly into the courtyard . 

 it be hard to come back to these thing . the noise of they sound on the outside of his ear , but inside they be the slow , vast , inaudible roar of the cosmo , like in a sea - shell . it be hard to have to bear the contact of commonplace daily thing , when his soul and body be naked to the cosmo . 

 he wish they would leave he the veil of his isolation awhile . but they would not : especially Carlota . she want he to be present to she : in familiar contact . 

 she be call : ' ram n ! ram n ! have you finish ? Cipriano be here . ' and even so , in her voice be fear , and an overriding temerity .

 ' you row on the lake ? ' say Ram n abstractedly , come up . 

 ' it be lovely ! ' say Kate . ' but hot when the sun come . '

 Kate see the sigh lift the soft , quiescent , cream - brown shoulder . the soft , cream - brown skin of his back , of a smooth pure sensuality , make her shudder . the broad , square , rather high shoulder , with neck and head rise steep , proudly . the full - flesh , deep - cheste , rich body of the man make she feel dizzy . in spite of herself , she could not help imagine a knife stick between those pure , male shoulder . if only to break the arrogance of their remoteness . 

 that be it . his nakedness be so aloof , far - off and intangible , in another day . so that to think of it be almost a violation , even to look at it with pry eye . Kate 's heart suddenly shrink in her breast . this be how Salome have look at John . and this be the beauty of John , that he have have ; like a pomegranate on a dark tree in the distance , naked , but not undressed ! forever still and clothe - less , and with another light about it , of a rich day than our paltry , prying , sneak - thieving day . 

 the moment Kate have imagine a knife between his shoulder her heart shrink with grief and shame , and a great stillness come over she . well to take the hush into one 's heart , and the sharp , prying beam out of one 's eye . well to lapse away from one 's own prying , assertive self , into the soft , untrespasse self , to whom nakedness be neither shame nor excitement , but clothe like a flower in its own deep , soft consciousness , beyond cheap awareness . 

 the evening breeze be blow very faintly . sailing - boat be advance through the pearly atmosphere , far off , the sun above have a golden quality . the opposite shore , twenty mile away , be distinct , and yet there seem an opalescent , spume - like haze in the air , the same quality as in the filmy water . Kate could see the white speck of the far - off church tower of Tuliapan . 

 below , in the garden below the house , be a thick grove of mango - tree . among the dark and reddish leaf of the mangos , scarlet little bird be bustle , like suddenly - open poppy - bud , and pair of yellow bird , yellow underneath as yellow butterfly , so perfectly clear , go skim past . when they settle for a moment and close their wing , they disappear , for they be grey on top . and when the cardinal bird settle , they too disappear , for the outside of their wing be brown , like a sheath . 

 ' bird in this country have all their colour below , ' say Kate . 

 Ram n turn to she suddenly .

 but at the sound of it , his wife stop as if some hand have suddenly grasp she . 

 ' Sugar ! Sugar ! ' she repeat abstractedly to herself .

 he be handsome , almost horribly handsome , with his black head poise as it be without weight , above his darken , smooth neck . a pure sensuality , with a powerful purity of its own , hostile to her sort of purity . with the blue sash round his waist , press a fold in the flesh , and the thin linen seem to gleam with the life of his hip and his thigh , he emanate a fascination almost like a narcotic , assert his pure , fine sensuality against she . the strange , soft , still sureness of he , as if he sit secure within his own dark aura . and as if this dark aura of his militate against her presence , and against the presence of his wife . he emit an effluence so powerful , that it seem to hamper her consciousness , to bind down her limb .

 Kate know now how Salome feel . she know now how John the Baptist have be , with his terrible , aloof beauty , inaccessible , yet so potent . 

 ' ah ! ' she say to herself . ' let I close my eye to he , and open only my soul . let I close my prying , see eye , and sit in dark stillness along with these two man . they have get more than I , they have a richness that I have not   get . they have get rid of that itching of the eye , and the desire that work through the eye . the itching , prurient , know , imagine eye , I be curse with it , I be hamper up in it . it be my curse of curse , the curse of Eve . the curse of Eve be upon I , my eye be like hook , my knowledge be like a fish - hook through my gill , pull I in spasmodic desire . oh , who will free I from the grappling of my eye , from the impurity of sharp sight ! daughter of Eve , of greedy vision , why do not   these man save I from the sharpness of my own eye ! ' 

 she rise and go to the edge of the terrace . yellow as daffodil underneath , two bird emerge out of their own invisibility . in the little shingle bay , with a small breakwater , where the boat be pull up and chain , two man be stand in the water , throw out a big , fine round net , catch the little silvery fish call charale , which flick out of the brownish water sometimes like splinter of glass .

 it be sunset , with a big level cloud like fur overhead , only the side of the horizon fairly clear . the sun be not visible . it have go down in a thick , rose - red fume behind the wavy ridge of the mountain . now the hill stand up bluish , all the air be a salmon - red flush , the fawn water have pinkish ripple . boy and man , bath a little way along the shore , be the colour of deep flame .

 CHAPTER XIII 

 the First Rain 

 

 Ram n and Cipriano be out by the lake . Cipriano also have change into the white clothe and sandal , and he look well than when in uniform . 

 ' I have a talk with Montes when he come to Guadalajara , ' Cipriano say to Ram n. Montes be the President of the Republic . 

 ' and what do he say ? ' 

 ' he be careful . but he do not   like his colleague . I think he feel lonely . I think he would like to know you well . ' 

 ' why ? ' 

 ' perhaps that you could give he your moral support . perhaps that you might be Secretary , and President when Montes ' term be up . ' 

 ' I like Montes , ' say Ram n. ' he be sincere and passionate . do you like he ? ' 

 ' yes ! ' say Cipriano . ' more or less . he be suspicious , and jealous for fear anyone else might want to share in his power . he have the craving of a dictator . he want to find out if I would stick to he . ' 

 ' you let he know you would ? ' 

 ' I tell he that all I care for be for you and for Mexico . '

 ' well , he be no fool . he say : " Don Ram n see the world with different eye from mine . who know which of we be right ? I want to save my country from poverty and unenlightenment , he want to save its soul . Don Ram n say , if a man have no soul , it do not   matter whether he be hungry or ignorant . well , he can go his way , and I mine . we shall never hinder one another , I believe .  ' sensible ! ' say Ram n. ' and honest in his conviction . '
