 ' yes , yes , you do . politic and all this social religion that Montes have get be like wash the outside of the egg , to make it look clean . but I , myself , I want to get inside the egg , right to the middle , to start it grow into a new bird . ay ! Cipriano ! Mexico be like an old , old egg that the bird of Time lay long ago ; and she have be sit on it for century , till it look foul in the nest of the world . but still , Cipriano , it be a good egg . it be not addle . only the spark of fire have never go into the middle of it , to start it . - Montes want to clean the nest and wash the egg . but meanwhile , the egg will go cold and die . the more you save these people from poverty and ignorance , the quick they will die : like a dirty egg that you take from under the hen - eagle , to wash it . while you wash the egg , it chill and dy . poor old Montes , all his idea be american and european . and the old Dove of Europe will never hatch the egg of dark - skin America . the United States can not   die , because it be not   alive . it be a nestful of china egg , make of pot . so they can be keep clean . - but here , Cipriano , here , let we hatch the chick before we start clean up the nest . ' 

 Cipriano hang his head . he be always test Ram n , to see if he could change he . when he find he could not , then he submit , and new little fire of joy spring up in he . but meanwhile , he have to try , and try again . 

 ' it be no good , try to mix the two thing . at this stage of affair , at least , they will not   mix . we have to shut our eye and sink down , sink away from the surface , away , like shadow , down to the bottom . like the pearl diver . but you keep bob up like a cork . ' 

 Cipriano smile subtly . he know well enough . 

 ' we have   get to open the oyster of the cosmo , and get our manhood out of it . till we have   get the pearl , we be only gnat on the surface of the ocean , ' say Ram n. 

 ' my manhood be like a devil inside I , ' say Cipriano . 

 ' it be very true , ' say Ram n. ' that be because the old oyster have he shut up , like a black pearl . you must let he walk out . ' 

 ' ram n , ' say Cipriano , ' would not   it be good to be a serpent , and be big enough to wrap one 's fold round the globe of the world , and crush it like that egg ? ' 

 Ram n look at he and laugh . 

 ' I believe we could do that , ' say Cipriano , a slow smile curl round his mouth . ' and would not   it be good ? ' 

 Ram n shake his head , laugh . 

 ' there would be one good moment , at least , ' he say . 

 ' who ask for more ! ' say Cipriano . 

 a spark flash out of Ram n 's eye too . then he check himself , and gather himself together . 

 ' what would be the good ! ' he say heavily . ' if the egg be crush , and we remain , what could we do but go howl down the empty passage of darkness ? what be the good , Cipriano ? ' 

 Ram n get up and walk away . the sun have set , the night be fall . and in his soul the great , writhe anger be alive again . Carlota provoke it into life : the two woman seem to breathe life into the black monster of his inward rage , till it begin to lash again . and Cipriano stir it up till it howl with desire . 

 ' my manhood be like a demon howl inside I , ' say Ram n to himself , in Cipriano 's word . 

 and he admit the justice of the howling , his manhood be pen up , humiliate , goad with insult inside he . and rage come over he , against Carlota , against Cipriano , against his own people , against all mankind , till he be fill with rage like the devil . 

 his people would betray he , he know that . Cipriano would betray he . give one little vulnerable chink , they would pierce he . they would leap at the place out of nowhere , like a tarantula , and bite in the poison . 

 while ever there be one little vulnerable chink . and what man can be invulnerable ? 

 he go upstairs by the outer stairway , through the iron door at the side of the house , under the heavy tree , up to his room , and sit on his bed . the night be hot , heavy , and ominously still . 

 ' the water be come , ' he hear a servant say . he shut the door of his room till it be black dark inside . then he throw aside his clothing , say : I put off the world with my clothe . and stand nude and invisible in the centre of his room he thrust his clench fist upwards , with all his might , feel he would break the wall of his chest . and his left hand hang loose , the finger softly curve downward . 

 and tense like the gush of a soundless fountain , he thrust up and reach down in the invisible dark , convulse with passion . till the black wave begin to wash over his consciousness , over his mind , wave of darkness break over his memory over his being , like an incoming tide , till at last it be full tide and he tremble , and fall to rest . invisible in the darkness , he stand soft and relaxed , star with wide eye at the dark , and feel the dark fecundity of the inner tide wash over his heart , over his belly , his mind dissolve away in the great , dark mind , which be undisturbe by thought . 

 he cover his face with his hand , and stand still , in pure unconsciousness , neither hear nor feeling nor know , like a dark sea - weed deep in the sea . with no time and no World , in the deep that be timeless and worldless . 

 then when his heart and his belly be restore , his mind begin to flicker again softly , like a soft flame flow without depart . 

 so he wipe his face with his hand , and put his serape over his head , and , silent inside an aura of pain , he go out and take the drum , carry it downstairs . 

 Martin , the man who love he , be hover in the zaguán . 

 ' ya , Patr n ? ' he say . 

 ' ya ! ' say Ram n. 

 the man run indoor , where a lamp be burn in the big , dark kitchen , and run out again with an armful of the weave straw mat . 

 ' where , Patr n ? ' he say . 

 Ram n hesitate in the centre of the courtyard , and look at the sky . 

 ' Viene el agua ? ' he say . 

 ' creo que sí , Patr n. ' 

 they go to the shed where the banana have be pack and carry away on donkey . there the man throw down the petate . Ram n arrange they . Guisleno run with cane . he be go to make light , the simple possible . three piece of thick cane , tie at the neck with a cord , stand up three - legged , waist high . in the three - pronged fork at the top he lay a piece of flat , slightly hollow lava stone . then he come run from the house with a bit of burn ocote wood . three or four bit of ocote , each bit no big than a long finger , flicker and rise in quick flame from the stone , and the courtyard dance with shadow . 

 Ram n take off his serape , fold it , and sit upon it . Guisleno light another tripod - torch . Ram n sit with his back to the wall , the fire - light dancing on his dark brow , that be sink in a sort of frown . his breast shine like gold in the flame . he take the drum and sound the summon , slow , monotonous , rather sad . in a moment two or three man come run . the drummer come , Ram n stand up and hand he the drum . he run with it to the great outer doorway , and out into the dark lane , and there sound the summon , quick , sharp . 

 Ram n put on his serape , whose scarlet fringe touch his knee , and stand motionless , with ruffle hair . round his shoulder go the woven snake , and his head be through the middle of the blue , weave bird . 

 Cipriano come from the house . he be wear a serape all scarlet and dark brown , a great scarlet sun at the centre , deep scarlet zigzag at the border , and dark brown fringe at his knee . he come and stand at Ram n 's side , glance up into Ram n 's face . but the other man 's brow be low , his eye be fix in the darkness of the shed away across the courtyard . he be look into the heart of the world ; because the face of man , and the heart of man be helpless quicksand . only in the heart of the cosmos man can look for strength . and if he can keep his soul in touch with the heart of the world , then from the heart of the world new blood will beat in strength and stillness into he , fulfil his manhood . 

 Cipriano turn his black eye to the courtyard . his soldier have draw near , in a little group . three or four man be stand in dark serape , round the fire . Cipriano stand brilliant like a cardinal bird , next to Ram n. even his sandal be bright , sealing - wax red , and his loose linen trouser be bind at the ankle with red and black band . his face look very dark and ruddy in the firelight , his little black tuft of a beard hang odd and devilish , his eye be glitter sardonically . but he catch Ram n 's hand in his small hand , and stand hold it . 

 the peon be come through the entrance - way , balance their big hat . woman be hurry barefoot , swish their full skirt , carry baby inside the dark wrap of their rebozo , child run after . they all cluster towards the flame - light , like wild animal gaze in at the circle of man in dark serape , Ram n , magnificent in his white and blue and shadow , poise his beautiful head , Cipriano at his side like a glitter cardinal bird . 

 Carlota and Kate emerge from the inner doorway of the house . but there Carlota remain , wrap in a black silk shawl , seat on a wooden bench where the soldier usually sit , look across at the ruddy flare of light , the circle of dark man , the tall beauty of her husband , the poppy - petal glitter of red , of Cipriano , the group of little , dust - colour soldier , and the solid throng of peon and woman and child , stand gaze like animal . while through the gate man still come hurrying , and from outside , the drum sound , and a high voice sing again and again : 

 

 someone will enter between the gate , 
  now , at this moment , ay ! 
 see the light on the man that wait . 
  shall you ? shall I ? 

 someone will come to the place of fire , 
  now , at this moment , ay ! 
 and hark to the word of their heart 's desire . 
  shall you ? shall I ? 

 someone will knock when the door be shut , 
  ay ! in a moment , ay ! 
 hear a voice say : I know you not ! 
  shall you ? shall I ? 

 

 there be a queer , wild yell each time on the Ay ! and like a bugle refrain : shall you ? shall I ? it make Carlota shiver . 

 Kate , wrap her yellow shawl round she , walk slowly towards the group . 

 the drum outside give a rapid shudder , and be finish . the drummer come in , the great door be shut and bar , the drummer take his place in the ring of stand man . a dead silence supervene . 

 Ram n continue to gaze from under lower brow , into space . then in a quiet , inward voice , he say : 

 ' as I take off this cover , I put away the day that be go from upon I . ' 

 he take off his serape , and stand with it over his arm . all the man in the circle do the same , till they stand with naked breast and shoulder , Cipriano very dark and strong - look , in his smallness , beside Ram n. 

 ' I put away the day that be go , ' Ram n continue , in the same still , inward voice , ' and stand with my heart uncover in the night of the god . ' 

 then he look down at the ground . 

 ' Serpent of the earth , ' he say ; ' snake that lie in the fire at the heart of the world , come ! come ! Snake of the fire of the heart of the world , coil like gold round my ankle , and rise like life around my knee , and lie your head against my thigh . come , put your head in my hand , cradle your head in my finger , snake of the deep . kiss my foot and my ankle with your mouth of gold , kiss my knee and my inner thigh , snake brand with flame and shadow , come ! and rest your head in my finger - basket ! so ! ' 

 the voice be soft and hypnotic . it die upon a stillness . and it seem as if really a mysterious presence have enter unseen from the underworld . it seem to the peon as if really they see a snake of brilliant gold and living blackness softly coil around Ram n 's ankle and knee , and rest its head in his finger , lick his palm with fork tongue . 

 he look out at the big , dilate , glitter eye of his people , and his own eye be wide and uncanny . 

 ' I tell you , ' he say , ' and I tell you truly . at the heart of this earth sleep a great serpent , in the midst of fire . those that go down in mine feel the heat and the sweat of he , they feel he move . it be the live fire of the earth , for the earth be alive . the snake of the world be huge , and the rock be his scale , tree grow between they . I tell you the earth you dig be alive as a snake that sleep . so vast a serpent you walk on , this lake lie between his fold as a drop of rain in the fold of a sleep rattlesnake . yet he none the less life . the earth be alive . 

 ' and if he die , we should all perish . only his living keep the soil sweet , that grow you maize . from the root of his scale we dig silver and gold , and the tree have root in he , as the hair of my face have root in my lip . 

 ' the earth be alive . but he be very big and we be very small , small than dust . but he be very big in his life , and sometimes he be angry . these people , small than dust , he say , they stamp on I and say I be dead . even to their ass they speak , and shout Harreh ! Burro ! but to I they speak no word . therefore I will turn against they , like a woman who lie angry with her man in bed , and eat away his spirit with her anger , turn she back to he . 

 ' that be what the earth say to we . he send sorrow into our foot , and depression into our loin . 

 ' because as an angry woman in the house can make a man heavy , take his life from he , so the earth can make we heavy , make our soul cold , and our life dreary in our foot . 

 ' speak then to the snake of the heart of the world , put oil on your finger and lower your finger for he to taste the oil of the earth , and let he send life into your foot and ankle and knee , like sap in the young maize press against the joint and make the milk of the maize bud among its hair . 

 ' from the heart of the earth man feel his manhood rise up in he , like the maize that be proud , turn its green leaf outward . be proud like the maize , and let your root go deep , deep , for the rain be here , and it be time for we to be grow in Mexico . ' 

 Ram n cease speak , the drum softly pulse . all the man of the ring be look down at the earth and softly let their left hand hang . 

 Carlota , who have not be able to hear , drift up to Kate 's side , spellbound by her husband . Kate unconsciously glance down at the earth , and secretly let her finger hang softly against her dress . but then she be afraid of what might happen to she , and she catch her hand up into her shawl . 

 suddenly the drum begin to give a very strong note , follow by a weak : a strange , exciting thud . 

 everybody look up . Ram n have fling his right arm tense into the air , and be look up at the black dark sky . the man of the ring do the same , and the naked arm be thrust aloft like so many rocket . 

 ' up ! up ! up ! ' say a wild voice . 

 ' up ! up ! ' cry the man of the ring , in a wild chorus . 

 and involuntarily the man in the crowd twitch , then shoot their arm upwards , turn their face to the dark heaven . even some of the woman boldly thrust up their naked arm , and relief enter their heart as they do so . 

 but Kate would not lift her arm . 

 there be dead silence , even the drum be silent . then the voice of Ram n be hear , speak upwards to the black sky : 

 ' your big wing be dark , Bird , you be fly low to - night . you be fly low over Mexico , we shall soon feel the fan of your wing on our face . 

 ' ay , Bird ! you fly about where you will . you fly past the star , and you perch on the sun . you fly out of sight , and be go beyond the white river of the sky . but you come back like the duck of the north , look for water and winter . 

 ' you sit in the middle of the sun , and preen your feather . you crouch in the river of star , and make the star - dust rise around you . you fly away into the deep hollow place of the sky , whence there seem no return . 

 ' you come back to we , and hover overhead , and we feel your wing fan our face - ' 

 even as he speak the wind rise , in sudden gust , and a door could be hear slam in the house , with a shivering of glass , and the tree give off a tear sound . 

 ' come then , Bird of the great sky ! ' Ram n call wildly . ' come ! oh Bird , settle a moment on my wrist , over my head , and give I power of the sky , and wisdom . oh Bird ! bird of all the wide heaven , even if you drum your feather in thunder , and drop the white snake of fire from your beak back to the earth again , where he can run in , deep down the rock again , home : even if you come as the Thunderer , come ! settle on my wrist a moment , with the clutch of the power of thunder , and arch your wing over my head , like a shadow of cloud ; and bend your breast to my brow , and bless I with the sun . bird , roam Bird of the Beyond , with thunder in your pinion and the snake of lightning in your beak , with the blue heaven in the socket of your wing and cloud in the arch of your neck , with sun in the burn feather of your breast and power in your foot , with terrible wisdom in your flight , swoop to I a moment , swoop ! ' 

 sudden gust of wind tear at the little fire of flame , till they could be hear to rustle , and the lake begin to speak in a vast hollow noise , beyond the tearing of tree . distant lightning be beat far off , over the black hill . 

 Ram n drop his arm , which have be bent over his head . the drum begin to beat . then he say : 

 ' sit down a moment , before the Bird shake water out of his wing . it will come soon . sit down . ' 

 there be a stir . man put their serape over their face , woman clutch their rebozos tight , and all sit down on the ground . only Kate and Carlota remain stand , on the outer edge . gust of wind tear at the flame , the man put their hat on the ground in front of they . 

 ' the earth be alive , and the sky be alive , ' say Ram n in his natural voice , ' and between they , we live . earth have kiss my knee , and put strength in my belly . Sky have perch on my wrist , and send power into my breast . 

 ' but as in the morning the Morning - star stand between earth and sky , a star can rise in we , and stand between the heart and the loin . 

 ' that be the manhood of man , and for woman , her womanhood . 

 ' you be not yet man . and woman , you be not yet woman . 

 ' you run about and toss about and die , and still you have not find the star of your manhood rise within you , the star of your womanhood shine out serene between your breast , woman . 

 ' I tell you , for he that wish it , the star of his manhood shall rise within he , and he shall be proud , and perfect even as the Morning - star be perfect . 

 ' and the star of a woman 's womanhood can rise at last , from between the heavy rim of the earth and the lose grey void of the sky . 

 ' but how ? how shall we do it ? how shall it be ? 

 ' how shall we man become man of the Morning Star ? and the woman the Dawn - Star Women ? 

 ' lower your finger to the caress of the Snake of the earth . 

 ' lift your wrist for a perch to the far - lie Bird . 

 ' have the courage of both , the courage of lightning and the earthquake . 

 ' and wisdom of both , the wisdom of the snake and the eagle . 

 ' and the peace of both , the peace of the serpent and the sun . 

 ' and the power of both , the power of the innermost earth and the outermost heaven . 

 ' but on your brow , Men ! the undimmed Morning Star , that neither day nor night , nor earth nor sky can swallow and put out . 

 ' and between your breast , Women ! the Dawn - Star , that can not be dim . 

 ' and your home at last be the Morning Star . neither heaven nor earth shall swallow you up at the last , but you shall pass the place beyond both , into the bright star that be lonely yet feel itself never alone . 

 ' the Morning Star be send you a messenger , a god who die in Mexico . but he sleep his sleep , and the invisible Ones wash his body with water of resurrection . so he have rise , and push the stone from the mouth of the tomb , and have stretch himself . and now he be stride across the horizon even quick than the great stone from the tomb be tumble back to the earth , to crush those that roll it up . 

 ' the Son of the Star be come back to the Sons of Men , with big , bright stride . 

 ' prepare to receive he . and wash yourself , and put oil on your hand and your foot , on your mouth and eye and ear and nostril , on your breast and navel and on the secret place of your body , that nothing of the dead day , no dust of skeleton and evil thing may pass into you and make you unclean . 

 ' do not look with the eye of yesterday , nor like yesterday listen , nor breathe , nor smell , nor taste , nor swallow food and drink . do not kiss with the mouth of yesterday , nor touch with the hand , nor walk with yesterday 's foot . and let your navel know nothing of yesterday , and go into your woman with a new body , enter the new body in she . 

 ' for yesterday 's body be dead , and carrion , the Xopilote be hover above it . 

 ' put yesterday 's body from off you , and have a new body . even as your God who be come . Quetzalcoatl be come with a new body , like a star , from the shadow of death . 

 ' yes , even as you sit upon the earth this moment , with the round of your body touch the round of the earth , say : Earth ! Earth ! you be alive as the globe of my body be alive . breathe the kiss of the inner earth upon I , even as I sit upon you . 

 ' and so , it be say . the earth be stir beneath you , the sky be rush its wing above . go home to your home , in front of the water that will fall and cut you off forever from your yesterday . 

 ' go home , and hope to be man of the Morning Star , Women of the Star of Dawn . 

 ' you be not yet man and woman - ' 

 he rise up and wave to the people to be go . and in a moment they be on their foot , scurry and hasten with the quiet mexican hurry , that seem to run low down upon the surface of the earth . 

 the black wind be all loose in the sky , tear with the thin shriek of torn fabric , in the mango - tree . man hold their big hat on their head and run with bent knee , their serape blow . woman clutch their rebozo tighter and run barefoot to the zaguán . 

 the big door be open , a soldier stand with a gun across his back , hold a hurricane lamp . and the people flee like ghost through the door , and away up the black lane like bit of paper veer away into nothingness , blow out of their line of flight . in a moment , they have all silently go . 

 Martin bar the great door . the soldier put down his lamp on the wooden bench , and he and his comrade sit huddle in their dark shawl , in a little bunch like toadstool in the dark cavern of the zaguán . already one have curl himself up on the wooden bench , wrap like a snail in his blanket , head disappear . 

 ' the water be come ! ' cry the servant excitedly , as Kate go upstairs with Doña Carlota . 

 the lake be quite black , like a great pit . the wind suddenly blow with violence , with a strange rip sound in the mango - trees , as if some membrane in the air be be rip . the white - flower oleander in the garden below lean over quite flat , their white flower ghostly , go right down to the earth , in the pale beam of the lamp - like a street lamp - that shine on the wall at the front entrance . a young palm - tree bent and spread its leaf on the ground . some invisible juggernaut car roll in the dark over the outside world . 

 away across the lake , south - west , lightning blaze and run down the sky like some portentous writing . and soft , velvety thunder break inwardly , strangely . 

 ' it frighten I ! ' cry Doña Carlota , put her hand over her eye and hasten into a far corner of the bare salon . 

 Cipriano and Kate stand on the terrace , watch the coloured flower in the pot shake and fly to bit , disappear up into the void of darkness . Kate clutch her shawl . but the wind suddenly get under Cipriano 's blanket , and lift it straight up into the air , then drop it in a scarlet flare over his head . Kate watch his deep , strong indian chest lift as his arm quickly fight to free his head . how dark he be , and how primitively physical , beautiful , and deep - breast , with soft , full flesh ! but all , as it be , for himself . nothing that come forth from he to meet with one outside . all oblivious of the outside , all for himself . 

 ' ah ! the water ! ' he cry , hold down his serape . 

 the first great drop be fly darkly at the flower , like arrow . Kate stand back into the doorway of the salon . a pure blaze of lightning slip three - fold above the black hill , seem to stand a moment , then slip back into the dark . 

 Down come the rain with a smash , as if some great vessel have break . with it , come a waft of icy air . and all the time , first in one part of the sky , then in another , in quick succession the blue lightning , very blue , break out of heaven and light up the air for a blue , breathless moment , loom tree and ghost of a garden , then be go , while thunder drop and explode continually . 

 Kate watch the dropping mass of water in wonder . already , in the blue moment of lightning , she see the garden below a pond , the walk be rush river . it be cold . she turn indoor . 

 a servant be go round the room with a lantern , to look if scorpion be come out . he find one scuttle across the floor of Kate 's room , and one fall from the ceiling beam on to Carlota 's bed . 

 they sit in the salon in rock - chair , Carlota and Kate , and rock , smell the good wetness , breathe the good , chill air . Kate have already forget what really chill air be like . she wrap she shawl tighter round she . 

 ' ah , yes , you feel cold ! you must take care in the night now . sometimes in the rainy season the night be very cold . you must be ready with an extra blanket . and the servant , poor thing , they just lie and shudder , and they get up in the morning like corps . - but the sun soon warm they again , and they seem to think they must bear what come . so they complain sometimes , but still they do not   provide . ' 

 the wind have go , suddenly . Kate be uneasy , uneasy , with the smell of water , almost of ice , in her nostril , and her blood still hot and dark . she get up and go again to the terrace . Cipriano be still stand there , motionless and inscrutable , like a monument , in his red and dark serape . 

 the rain be abate . down below in the garden two barefoote woman - servant be run through the water , in the faint light of the zaguán lamp , run across the garden and put olla and square gasoline can under the arch spout of water that seethe down from the roof , then dart away while they fill , then struggle in with the frothy vessel . it would save make trip to the lake , for water . 

 ' what do you think of we ? ' Cipriano say to she . 

 ' it be strange to I , ' she reply , wonder and a little awed by the night . 

 ' good , no ? ' he say , in an exultant tone . 

 ' a little scar , ' she reply , with a slight laugh . 

 ' when you be use to it , ' he say , ' it seem natural , no ? it seem natural so - as it be . and when you go to a country like England , where all be so safe and ready - make , then you miss it . you keep say to yourself : " what be I miss ? what be it that be not here ? " ' 

 he seem to be gloat in his native darkness . it be curious , that though he speak such good English , it seem always foreign to she , more foreign than Doña Carlota 's Spanish . 

 ' I can not   understand that people want to have everything , all life , no ? - so safe and ready - make as in England and America . it be good to be awake . on the qui vive , no ? ' 

 ' perhaps , ' she say . 

 ' so I like it , ' he say , ' when Ram n tell the people the earth be alive , and the sky have a big bird in it , that you do not   see . I think it be true . certainly ! and it be good to know it , because then one be on the qui vive , no ? ' 

 ' but it be tiring to be always on the qui vive , ' she say . 

 ' why ? why tiring ? no , I think , on the contrary , it be refreshing . - ah , you should marry , and live in Mexico . at last , I be sure , you would like it . you would keep wake up more and more to it . ' 

 ' or else go more and more deaden , ' she say . ' that be how most foreigner go , it seem to I . ' 

 ' why deaden ? ' he say to she . ' I do not   understand . why deaden ? here you have a country where night be night , and rain come down and you know it . and you have a people with whom you must be on the qui vive all the time , all the time . and that be very good , no ? you do not   go sleepy . like a pear ! do not   you say a pear go sleepy , no ? - cuando se echa a perder ? ' 

 ' yes ! ' she say . 

 ' and here you have also ram n. how do Ram n seem to you ? ' 

 ' I do not   know . I do not   want to say anything . but I do think he be almost too much : too far . - and I do not   think he be mexican . ' 

 ' why not ? why not mexican ? he be mexican . ' 

 ' not as you be . ' 

 ' how not as I be ? he be mexican . ' 

 ' he seem to I to belong to the old , old Europe , ' she say . 

 ' and he seem to I to belong to the old , old Mexico - and also to the new , ' he add quickly . 

 ' but you do not   believe in he . ' 

 ' how ? ' 

 ' you - yourself . you do not   believe in he . you think it be like everything else , a sort of game . everything be a sort of game , a put - up job , to you Mexicans . you do not   really believe , in anything . ' 

 ' how not believe ? I not believe in Ram n ? - well , perhaps not , in that way of kneeling before he and spread out my arm and shed tear on his foot . but I - I believe in he , too . not in your way , but in mine . I tell you why . because he have the power to compel I . if he have not   the power to compel I , how should I believe ? ' 

 ' it be a queer sort of belief that be compel , ' she say . 

 ' how else should one believe , except by be compel ? I like Ram n for that , that he can compel I . when I grow up , and my godfather could not compel I to believe , I be very unhappy . it make I very unhappy . - but Ram n compel I , and that be very good . it make I very happy , when I know I can not   escape . it would make you happy too . ' 

 ' to know I could not escape from Don Ram n ? ' she say ironically . 

 ' yes , that also . and to know you could not escape from Mexico . and even from such a man as I . ' 

 she pause in the dark before she answer , sardonically : 

 ' I do not   think it would make I happy to feel I could not   escape from Mexico . no , I feel , unless I be sure I could get out any day , I could not   bear to be here . ' 

 in her mind she think : and perhaps Ram n be the only one I could not   quite escape from , because he really touch I somewhere inside . but from you , you little Cipriano , I should have no need even to escape , because I could not be catch by you . 

 ' ah ! ' he say quickly . ' you think so . but then you do not   know . you can only think with american thought , it be natural . from your education , you have only american thought , U.S.A. thought , to think with . nearly all woman be like that : even mexican woman of the spanish - mexican class . they be all think nothing but u.s.a. thought , because those be the one that go with the way they dress their hair . and so it be with you . you think like a modern woman , because you belong to the anglo - saxon or teutonic world , and dress your hair in a certain way , and have money , and be altogether free . - but you only think like this because you have have these thought put in your head , just as in Mexico you spend centavos and peso , because that be the mexican money you have put in your pocket . it be what they give you at the bank . - so when you say you be free , you be not free . you be compel all the time to be think U.S.A. thought - compel , I must say . you have not as much choice as a slave . as the peon must eat tortilla , tortillas , tortillas , because there be nothing else , you must think these u.s.a. thought , about be a woman and be free . every day you must eat those tortilla , tortillas . - till you do not   know how you would like something else . '

 ' other thought , other feeling . - you be afraid of such a man as I , because you think I should not treat you    l'américaine . you be quite right . I should not treat you as an american woman must be treat . why should I ? I do not   wish to . it do not   seem good to I . ' 

 ' you would treat a woman like a real old Mexican , would you ? keep her ignorant , and shut she up ? ' say Kate sarcastically . 

 ' I could not keep she ignorant if she do not start ignorant . but what more I have to teach she would not   be in the american style of teaching . ' 

 ' what then ? ' 

 ' Quién sabe ! ça reste    voir . ' 

 ' et continuera    y rester , ' say Kate , laugh . 

 

 

 CHAPTER XIV 

 Home to Sayula 

 

 the morning come perfectly blue , with a freshness in the air and a blue luminousness over the tree and the distant mountain , and bird so bright , absolutely like new - open bud spark in the air .

 to ram n , Carlota be still , at time , a torture . she seem to have the power still to lacerate he , inside his bowel . not in his mind or spirit , but in his old emotional , passional self : right in the middle of his belly , to tear he and make he feel he bleed inwardly . 

 because he have love she , he have care for she : for the affectionate , passionate , whimsical , sometimes elfish creature she have be . he have make much of she , and spoil she , for many year . 

 but all the while , gradually , his nature be change inside he . not that he cease to care for she , or want other woman . that she could have understand . but inside he be a slow , blind imperative , urge he to cast his emotional and spiritual and mental self into the slow furnace , and smell they into a new , whole being . 

 but he have Carlota to reckon with . she love he , and that , to she , be the outstanding factor . she love he , emotionally . and spiritually , she love mankind . and mentally , she be sure she be quite right .

 and she feel she be rob , cheat . why could not   he go on be gentle , good , and loving , and try to make the whole world more gentle , good , and loving ?

 the emotion of love , and the great emotion of liberty for mankind seem to go hard and congeal upon he , like the shell on a chrysalis . it be the old caterpillar stage of Christianity evolve into something else . 

 but Carlota feel this be all she have , this emotion of love , for her husband , her child , for her people , for the animal and bird and tree of the world . it be she all , her Christ , and her blessed Virgin . how could she let it go ? 

 so she continue to love he , and to love the world , steadily , pathetically , obstinately , and devilishly . she pray for he , and she engage in work of charity .

 her winsomeness and her elfishness depart from she , she begin to wither , she grow tense . and she blame he , and pray for he . even as the spontaneous mystery die in she , the will harden , till she be nothing but a will : a lost will .

 they be the child of his old body . his new body have no child : would probably never have any . 

 ' but remember , ' he say to she , with southern logic , ' you do not love , save with your will . I do not   like the love you have for your god : it be an assertion of your own will . I do not   like the love you have for I : it be the same . I do not   like the love you have for your child . if ever I see in they a spark of desire to be save from it , I shall do my good to save they . meanwhile have your love , have your will . but you know I dislike it . I dislike your insistence . I dislike your monopoly of one feeling , I dislike your charity work . I disapprove of the whole trend of your life . you be weaken and vitiate the boy . you do not love they , you be only put your love will over they . one day they will turn and hate you for it . remember I have say this to you . '

 Life have do its work on one more human being , quench the spontaneous life and leave only the will . kill the god in the woman , or the goddess , and leave only charity , with a will . 

 ' Carlota , ' he have say to she , ' how happy you would be if you could wear deep , deep mourning for I . - I shall not give you this happiness . ' 

 she give he a strange look from her hazel - brown eye .

 ' yes . '

 the victim , the inevitable victim , and the inevitable victimizer .

 he could not see that the bird be a real living creature with a life of its own . this , his race have never see . with black eye they star out on an elemental world , where the element be monstrous and cruel , as the sun be monstrous , and the cold , crush black water of the rain be monstrous , and the dry , dry , cruel earth . 

 and among the monstrosity of the element flicker and tower other presence : terrible uncouth thing call gringo , white people , and dress up monster of rich people , with power like god , but uncouth , demonish god . and uncouth thing like bird that could fly and snake that could crawl and fish that could swim and bite . an uncouth , monstrous universe of monster big and little , in which man hold his own by sheer resistance and guardedness , never , never go forth from his own darkness . 

 and sometimes , it be good to have revenge on the monster that flutter and strode . the monster big and the monster little . even the monster of that bird , which have its own monstrous bird - nature . on this the mite could wreck the long human vengeance , and for once be master . 

 blind to the creature as a soft , struggle thing find its own fluttering way through life . see only another monster of the outer void . 

 walk forever through a menace of monster , blind to the sympathy in thing , hold one 's own , and not give in , nor go forth . hence the lift chest and the prance walk . hence the stiff , insentient spine , the rich physique , and the heavy , dreary nature , heavy like the dark - grey mud - brick , with a terrible obstinate ponderosity and a dry sort of gloom . 

 

 

 CHAPTER XV 

 the Written Hymns of Quetzalcoatl 

 

 the electric light in Sayula be as inconstant as everything else . it would come on at half - past six in the evening , and it might bravely burn till ten at night , when the village go dark with a click . but usually it do no such thing . often it refuse to sputter into being till seven , or half - past , or even eight o'clock . but its bad trick be that of pop out just in the middle of supper , or just when you be write a letter . all of a sudden , the black mexican night come down on you with a thud . and then everybody run blindly for match and candle , with a calling of frightened voice . why be they always frightened ? then the electric light , like a wound thing , would try to revive , and a red glow would burn in the bulb , sinister . all hold their breath - be it come or not ? sometimes it expire for good , sometimes it get its breath back and shine , rather dully , but well than nothing . 

 once the rainy season have set in , it be hopeless . night after night it collapse . and Kate would sit with her weary , flutter candle , while blue lightning reveal the dark shape of thing in the patio . and half - see people go swiftly down to Juana 's end of the patio , secretly . 

 on such a night Kate sit on her veranda face the deepness of the black night . a candle shone in her desert salon . now and again she see the oleander and the papaya in the patio garden , by the blue gleam of lightning that fall with a noiseless splash into the pitch darkness . there be a distant noise of thunder , several storm prowl round like hungry jaguar , above the lake . 

 and several time the gate click , and crunch step come along the gravel , someone pass on the gravel walk , salute she , go down to Juana 's quarter , where the dull light of a float oil - wick shone through the grated window - hole . then there be a low , monotonous sound of a voice , recite or read . and as the wind blow and the lightning alight again like a blue bird among the plant , there would come the sharp noise of the round cuenta fall from the cuenta - tree . 

 Kate be uneasy and a bit forlorn . she feel something be happen down in the servant ' corner , something secret in the dark . and she be strand in her isolation on her terrace . 

 but , after all , it be her house , and she have a right to know what her own people be up to . she rise from her rock - chair and walk down the veranda and round the dining - room bay . the dining - room , which have its own two door on the patio , be already lock up . 

 in the far corner beyond the well she see a group sit on the ground , outside the doorway of Juana 's kitchen - hole . out of this little kitchen - shed shine the light of the float - wick lamp , and a voice be slowly intone , all the face be look into the dim light , the woman dark - hooded in rebozos , the man with their hat on , their serape over their shoulder . 

 when they hear Kate 's footstep , the face look her way , and a voice murmur in warning . Juana struggle to her foot . 

 ' it be the Niña ! ' she say . ' come , then , Niña , you poor innocent all alone in the evening . ' 

 the man in the group rise to their foot - she recognize the young Ezequiel , take his hat off to she . and there be Maria del Carmen , the bride . and inside the little shed , with the wick lamp on the floor , be Julio , the bridegroom of a few week ago . Concha and little Maria be there , and a couple of stranger . 

 ' I could hear the voice - ' say Kate . ' I do not   know it be you , Julio . how do you do ? - and I wonder so much what it be . ' 

 there be a moment 's dead silence . then Juana plunge in . 

 ' yes , Niña ! come ! it be very nice that you come . Concha , the chair for the Niña ! ' 

 Concha get up rather unwillingly , and fetch the little low chair which form Juana 's sole article of furniture , save the one bed . 

 ' I do not   disturb you ? ' say Kate . 

 ' no , Niña , you be a friend of Don Ram n , verdad ? ' 

 ' yes , ' say Kate . 

 ' and we - we be read the Hymns . ' 

 ' yes ? ' say Kate . 

 ' the Hymns of Quetzalcoatl , ' say Ezequiel , in his bark young voice , with sudden bravado . 

 ' do go on ! may I listen ! ' 

 ' you hear ! the Niña want to listen . Read , Julio , read ! read then . ' 

 they all sit down once more on the ground , and Julio sit down by the lamp , but he hang his head , hide his face in the shadow of his big hat . 

 ' entonce ! - read then , ' say Juana . 

 ' he be afraid , ' murmur Maria del Carmen , lay her hand on the young man 's knee . ' however , read , Julio ! because the Niña want to hear . ' 

 and after a moment 's struggle , Julio say in a muffled voice : 

 ' do I begin from the beginning . ' 

 ' yes , from the beginning ! read ! ' say Juana . 

 the young man take a sheet of paper , like an advertisement leaflet , from under his blanket . at the top it have the Quetzalcoatl symbol , call the Eye , the ring with the bird - shape standing in the middle . 

 he begin to read in a rather muffle voice : 

 ' I be Quetzalcoatl with the dark face , who live in Mexico in other day . 

 ' till there come a stranger from over the sea , and his face be white , and he speak with strange word . he show his hand and his foot , that in both there be hole . and he say : " my name be Jesus , and they call I Christ . man crucify I on a Cross till I die . but I rise up out of the place where they put I , and I go up to heaven to my Father . now my Father have tell I to come to Mexico . " 

 ' Quetzalcoatl say : you alone ? 

 ' Jesus say : my mother be here . she shed many tear for I , see I crucify . so she will hold the Sons of Mexico on her lap , and soothe they when they suffer , and when the woman of Mexico weep , she will take they on her bosom and comfort they . and when she cry to the Father for her people , he will make everything well . 

 ' Quetzatlcoatl say : that be well . and brother with the name Jesus , what will you do in Mexico ? 

 ' Jesus say : I will bring peace into Mexico . and on the naked I will put clothe , and food between the lip of the hungry , and gift in all man 's hand , and peace and love in their heart . 

 ' Quetzalcoatl say : it be very good . I be old . I could not do so much . I must go now . farewell , people of Mexico . Farewell , strange brother call Jesus . Farewell , woman call Mary . it be time for I to go . 

 ' so Quetzalcoatl look at his people ; and he embrace Jesus , the Son of Heaven ; and he embrace Maria , the Blessed Virgin , the Holy Mother of Jesus , and he turn away . slowly he go . but in his ear be the sound of the tearing down of his temple in Mexico . nevertheless he go on slowly , be old , and weary with much living . he climb the steep of the mountain , and over the white snow of the volcano . as he go , behind he rise a cry of people die , and a flame of place burn . he say to himself : surely those be mexican cry ! yet I must not hear , for Jesus have come to the land , and he will wipe the tear from all eye , and his Mother will make they all glad . 

 ' he also say : surely that be Mexico burn . but I must not look , for all man will be brother , now Jesus have come to the land , and the woman will sit by the blue skirt of Mary , smile with peace and with love . 

 ' so the old god reach the top of the mountain , and look up into the blue of heaven . and through a door in the blue wall he see a great darkness , and star and a moon shin . and beyond the darkness he see one great star , like a bright gateway . 

 ' then fire rise from the volcano around the old Quetzalcoatl , in wing and glitter feather . and with the wing of fire and the glitter of spark Quetzalcoatl fly up , up , like a waft fire , like a glitter bird , up , into the space , and away to the white step of heaven , that lead to the blue wall , where be the door to the dark . so he enter in and be go . 

 ' night fall , and Quetzalcoatl be go , and man in the world see only a star travel back into heaven , depart under the low branch of darkness . 

 ' then man in Mexico say : Quetzalcoatl have go . even his star have depart . we must listen to this Jesus , who speak in a foreign tongue . 

 ' so they learn a new speech from the priest that come from upon the great water to the east . and they become Christians . ' 

 Julio , who have become absorb , end abruptly , as the tale of the leaflet be end . 

 ' it be beautiful , ' say Kate . 

 ' and it be true ! ' cry the sceptical Juana . 

 ' it seem to I true , ' say Kate . 

 ' Señora ! ' yell Concha . ' be it true that heaven be up there , and you come down step like cloud to the edge of the sky , like the step from the mole into the lake ? be it true that El Señor come and stand on the step and look down at we like we look down into the lake to see the charale ? ' 

 Concha shove up her fierce swarthy face , and shake her mass of hair , glare at Kate , wait for an answer . 

 ' I do not   know everything , ' laugh Kate . ' but it seem to I true . ' 

 ' she believe it , ' say Concha , turn her face to her mother . 

 ' and be it true , ' ask Juana , ' that El Señor , El Cristo del Mundo , be a gringo , and that he come from your country , with his Holy Mother ? ' 

 ' not from my country , but from a country near . ' 

 ' listen ! ' exclaim Juana , awestruck . ' El Señor be a gringuito , and his Holy Mother be a gringuita . yes , one really know . look ! look at the foot of the Niña ! pure foot the Santísima ! look ! ' Kate be barefoot , wear sandal with a simple strap across the foot . Juana touch one of the Niña 's white foot , fascinated . ' foot of the Santísima . and she , the Holy Mary , be a gringuita . she come over the sea , like you , Niña ? ' 

 ' yes , she come over the sea ! ' 

 ' ah ! you know it ? ' 

 ' yes . we know that . ' 

 ' think of it ! the Santísima be a gringuita , and she come over the Sea like the Niña , from the country of the Niña ! ' Juana speak in a wicked wonder , horrified , delight , mock . 

 ' and the Lord be a Gringuito - pure Gringuito ? ' bark Concha . 

 ' and Niña - it be the gringo who kill El Señor ? it be not   the Mexicans ? it be those other gringo who put he on the Cross ? ' 

 ' yes ! ' say Kate . ' it be not   the Mexicans . ' 

 ' the gringo ? ' 

 ' yes , the gringo . ' 

 ' and he himself be a Gringo ? ' 

 ' yes ! ' say Kate , not know what else to say . 

 ' look ! ' say Juana , in her hush , awed , malevolent voice . ' he be a Gringo , and the gringo put he on the Cross . ' 

 ' but a long time ago , ' say Kate hastily . 

 ' a long time ago , say the Niña , ' echo Juana , in her awed voice . 

 there be a moment of silence . the dark face of the girl and man seat on the ground be turn up to Kate , watch she fixedly , in the half light , count every word . in the outer air , thunder mutter in different place . 

 ' and now , Niña , ' come the cool , clear voice of Maria del Carmen , ' El Señor be go back again to his Father , and our Quetzalcoatl be come back to we ? ' 

 ' and the Santísima be leave we ? ' put in the hurried voice of Juana . ' think of it ! the Santísima be leave we , and this Quetzalcoatl be come ! he have no mother , he ! ' 

 ' perhaps he have a wife , ' say Kate . 

 ' Quién sabe ! ' murmur Juana . 

 ' they say , ' say the bold Concha , ' that in Paradise he have grow young . ' 

 ' who ? ' ask Juana . 

 ' I do not   know how they call he , ' mutter Concha , ashame to say the word . 

 ' Quetzalcoatl ! ' say Ezequiel , in his bark strong young voice . ' yes , he be young . he be a god in the flower of life , and finely build . ' 

 ' they say so ! they say so ! ' murmur Juana . ' think of it ! ' 

 ' here it say so ! ' cry Ezequiel . ' here it be write . in the second Hymn . ' 

 ' read it then , Julio . ' 

 and Julio , now nothing loth , take out a second paper . 

 ' I , Quetzalcoatl , of Mexico , I travel the long journey . 

 ' beyond the blue outer wall of heaven , beyond the bright place of the Sun , across the plain of darkness where the star spread out like tree , like tree and bush , far away to the heart of all the world , low down like the Morning Star . 

 ' and at the heart of all the world those be wait whose face I could not see . and in voice like bee they murmur among themselves : this be Quetzalcoatl whose hair be white with fan the fire of life . he come alone , and slowly . 

 ' then with hand I could not see , they take my hand , and in their arm that I could not see , at last I die . 

 ' but when I be dead , and bone , they cast not my bone away , they do not give I up to the four wind , nor to the six . no , not even to the wind that blow down to the middle of earth , nor to he that blow upward like a finger pointing , do they give I . 

 ' he be dead , they say , but unrelinquished . 

 ' so they take the oil of the darkness , and lay it on my brow and my eye , they put it in my ear and nostril and my mouth , they put it on the two - fold silence of my breast , and on my sunken navel , and on my secret place , before and behind : and in the palm of my hand , and on the mound of my knee , and under the tread of my foot . 

 ' lastly , they anoint all my head with the oil that come out of the darkness . they they say : he be seal up . lay he away . 

 ' so they lay I in the fountain that bubble darkly at the heart of the world , far , far behind the sun , and there lie I , Quetzalcoatl , in warm oblivion . 

 ' I sleep the great sleep , and dream not . 

 ' till a voice be call : Quetzalcoatl ! 

 ' I say : who be that ? 

 ' no one answer , but the voice say : Quetzalcoatl ! 

 ' I say : where art thou ? 

 ' so ! he say . I be neither here nor there . I be thyself . get up . 

 ' now all be very heavy upon I , like a tomb - stone of darkness . 

 ' I say : be I not old ? how shall I roll this stone away ? 

 ' how art thou old , when I be new man ? I will roll away the stone . sit up ! 

 ' I sit up , and the stone go roll , crash down the gulfs of space . 

 ' I say to myself : I be new man . I be young than the young and old than the old . Lo ! I be unfold on the stem of time like a flower , I be at the midst of the flower of my manhood . neither do I ache with desire , to tear , to burst the bud ; neither do I yearn away like a seed that float into heaven . the cup of my flowering be unfold , in its middle the star float balanced with array . my stem be in the air , my root be in all the dark , the sun be no more than a cupful within I . 

 ' Lo ! I be neither young nor old , I be the flower unfold , I be new . 

 ' so I rise and stretch my limb and look around . the sun be below I in a daze of heat , like a hot humming - bird hover at mid - day over the world . and his beak be long and very sharp , he be like a dragon . 

 ' and a faint star be hesitate wearily , wait to pass . 

 ' I call aloud , say : " who be that ? " 

 

 my name be Jesus , I be Mary 's son . 
 I be come home . 
 my mother the Moon be dark . 

 Brother , Quetzalcoatl , 
 hold back the wild hot sun . 
 bind he with shadow while I pass . 
 let I come home . 

 

 ' I catch the sun and hold he , and in my shade the faint star slip past , go slowly into the dark reach beyond the burning of the sun . then on the slope of silence he sit down and take off his sandal , and I put they on . 

 ' " how do they wear the wing of love , Jesus , the mexican people ? " 

 ' " the soul of the mexican people be heavy for the wing of love , they have swallow the stone of despair . " 

 ' " where be your Lady Mother in the mantle of blue , she with comfort in her lap ? " 

 ' " her mantle fade in the dust of the world , she be weary without sleep , for the voice of people cry night and day , and the knife of the mexican people be sharp than the pinion of love , and their stubbornness be strong than hope . Lo ! the fountain of tear dry up in the eye of the old , and the lap of the aged be comfortless , they look for rest . Quetzalcoatl , Sir , my mother go even before I , to her still white bed in the moon . " 

 ' " she be go , and thou art go , Jesus , the Crucified . then what of Mexico ? " 

 ' " the image stand in their church , Oh Quetzalcoatl , they do not   know that I and my Mother have depart . they be angry soul , Brother , my Lord ! they vent their anger . they break my church , they steal my strength , they wither the lip of the Virgin . they drive we away , and we creep away like a totter old man and a woman , tearless and bend double with age . so we flee while they be not look . and we seek but rest , to forget forever the child of man who have swallow the stone of despair . " 

 ' then say I : it be good , pass on . I , Quetzalcoatl , will go down . sleep thou the sleep without dream . farewell at the cross - road , Brother Jesus . 

 ' he say : oh , Quetzalcoatl ! they have forget thee . the feathered snake ! the serpent - silent bird ! they be ask for none of thee . 

 ' I say : go thy way , for the dust of earth be in thy eye and on thy lip . for I the serpent of middle - earth sleep in my loin and my belly , the bird of the outer air perch on my brow and sweep her bill across my breast . but I , I be lord of two way . I be master of up and down . I be as a man who be a new man , with new limb and life , and the light of the Morning Star in his eye . Lo ! I be I ! the lord of both way . Thou wert lord of the one way . now it lead thee to the sleep . farewell ! 

 ' so Jesus go on towards the sleep . and Mary the Mother of Sorrows lie down on the bed of the white moon , weary beyond any more tear . 

 ' and I , I be on the threshold . I be step across the border . I be Quetzalcoatl , lord of both way , star between day and the dark . ' 

 there be silence as the young man finish read . 

 

 

 CHAPTER XVI 

 Cipriano and Kate 

 

 on Saturday afternoon the big black canoe with their large square sail come slowly approach out of the thin haze across the lake , from the west , from Tlapaltepec , with big straw hat and with blanket and earthenware stuff , from Ixtlahuacan and Jaramay and Las Zemas with mat and timber and charcoal and orange , from Tuliapan and Cuxcueco and San Cristobal with boatload of dark - green , globular water - melon , and pile of red tomato , mango , vegetable , orange : and boat - load of brick and tile , burn red , but rather friable ; then more charcoal , more wood , from the stark dry mountain over the lake . 

 Kate nearly always go out about five o'clock , on Saturdays , to see the boat , flat - bottom , drift up to the shallow shore , and begin to unload in the glow of the evening . it please she to see the man run along the plank with the dark - green melon , and pile they in a mound on the rough sand , melon dark - green like creature with pale belly . to see the tomato all pour out into a shallow place in the lake , bob about while the woman wash they , a bob scarlet upon the water . 

 the long , heavy brick be pile in heap along the scrap of demolish breakwater , and little gang of ass come trot down the rough beach , to be laden , press their little foot in the gravelly sand , and flop their ear . 

 the cargadore be busy at the charcoal boat , carry out the rough sack . 

 ' do you want charcoal , Niña ? ' shout a grimy cargador , who have carry the trunk from the station on his back . 

 ' at how much ? ' 

 ' twenty - five real the two sack . ' 

 ' I pay twenty real . ' 

 ' at twenty real then , Señorita . but you give I two real for the transport ? ' 

 ' the owner pay the transport , ' say Kate . ' but I will give you twenty centavos . ' 

 away go the man , trotting barelegge , barefoot , over the stony ground , with two large sack of charcoal on his shoulder . the man carry huge weight , without seem ever to think they be heavy . almost as if they like to feel a huge weight crush on their iron spine , and to be able to resist it . 

 basket of spring guavas , basket of sweet lemon call lima , basket of tiny green and yellow lemon , big as walnut ; orange - red and greenish mango , orange , carrot , cactus fruit in great abundance , a few knobbly potato , flat , pearl - white onion , little calabazita and speckle green calabazita like frog , camote cook and raw - she love to watch the basket trot up the beach past the church . 

 then , rather late as a rule , big red pot , bulge red olla for water - jar , earthenware casserole and earthenware jug with cream and black scratch pattern in glaze , bowl , big flat earthenware disc for cook tortillas - much earthenware . 

 on the west shore , man be run up the beach wear twelve enormous hat at once , like a trotting pagoda . man trot with finely weave huarache and rough strip sandal . and man with a few dark serape , with gaudy rose - pink pattern , in a pile on their shoulder . 

 it be fascinating . but at the same time , there be a heavy , almost sullen feeling on the air . these people come to market to a sort of battle . they come , not for the joy of selling , but for the sullen contest with those who want what they have get . the strange , black resentment always present . 

 by the time the church bell clang for sunset , the market have already begin . on all the pavement round the plaza squat the Indians with their ware , pyramid of green watermelon , array of rough earthenware , hat in pile , pair of sandal side by side , a great array of fruit , a spread of collar - stud and knick - knack , call novedade , little tray with sweet . and people arrive all the time out of the wild country , with laden ass . 

 yet never a shout , hardly a voice to be hear . none of the animation and the frank wild clamour of a Mediterranean market . always the heavy friction of the will ; always , always , grind upon the spirit , like the grey black grind of lava - rock . 

 when dark fall , the vendor light their tin torch - lamp , and the flame waver and stream as the dark - face man squat on the ground in their white clothe and big hat , wait to sell . they never ask you to buy . they never show their ware . they do not   even look at you . it be as if their static resentment and indifference would hardly let they sell at all . 

 Kate sometimes feel the market cheerful and easy . but more often she feel an unutterable weight slowly , invisibly sink on her spirit . and she want to run . she want , above all , the comfort of Don Ram n and the Hymns of Quetzalcoatl . this seem to she the only escape from a world go ghastly . 

 there be talk of revolution again , so the market be uneasy and grind the black grit into the spirit . foreign - look soldier be about , with loop hat , and knife and pistol , and savage northern face : tall , rather thin figure . they would loiter about in pair , talk in a strange northern speech , and seem more alien even than Kate herself . 

 the food - stall be brilliantly light . row of man sit at the plank board , drink soup and eat hot food with their finger . the milkman ride in on horseback , his two big can of milk sling before he , and he make his way slowly through the people to the food - stall . there , still sit unmove on horseback , he deliver bowl of milk from the can in front of he , and then , on horseback like a monument , take his supper , his bowl of soup , and his plate of tamale , or of mince , fiery meat spread on tortilla . the peon drift slowly round . guitar be sound , half - secretly . a motor - car work its way in from the city , choke with people , girl , young man , city papa , child , in a pile . 

 the rich press of life , above the flare of torch upon the ground ! the throng of white - clad , big - hatted man circulate slowly , the woman with dark rebozos slip silently . dark tree overhead . the doorway of the hotel bright with electricity . girl in organdie frock , white , cherry - red , blue , from the city . group of singer sing inwardly . and all the noise subdue , suppress . 

 the sense of strange , heavy suppression , the dead black power of negation in the soul of the peon . it be almost pitiful to see the pretty , pretty slim girl from Guadalajara go round and round , their naked arm link together , so light in their gauzy , scarlet , white , blue , orange dress , look for someone to look at they , to take note of they . and the peon man only emit from their soul the black vapour of negation , that perhaps be hate . they seem , the native , to have the power of blight the air with their black , rock - bottom resistance . 

 Kate almost weep over the slim , eager girl , pretty as rather papery flower , eager for attention , but thrust away , victimize . 

 suddenly there be a shot . the market - place be on its foot in a moment , scatter , pour away into the street and the shop . another shot ! Kate , from where she stand , see across the rapidly - empty plaza a man sit back on one of the bench , fire a pistol into the air . he be a lout from the city , and he be half drunk . the people know what it be . yet any moment he might lower the pistol and start fire at random . everybody hurry silently , melt away , leave the plaza void . 

 two more shot , pap - pap ! still into the air . and at the same moment a little officer in uniform dart out of the dark street where the military station be , and where now the big hat be pile on the ground ; he rush straight to the drunkard , who be spread his leg and wave the pistol : and before you could breathe , slap ! and again slap ! he have slap the pistol - firer first on one side of the face , then on the other , with slap that resound almost like shot . and in the same breath he seize the arm that hold the pistol and wrest the weapon away . 

 two of the strange soldier instantly rush up and seize the man by the arm . the officer speak two word , they salute and march off their prisoner . 

 instantly the crowd be ebb back into the plaza , unconcerned . Kate sit on a bench with her heart beat . she see the prisoner pass under a lamp , streak of blood on his cheek . and Juana , who have flee , now come scuttle back and take Kate 's hand , say : 

 ' look ! Niña ! it be the General ! ' 

 she rise startled to her foot . the officer be salute she . 

 ' Don Cipriano ! ' she say . 

 ' the same ! ' he reply . ' do that drunken fellow frighten you ? ' 

 ' not much ! only startle I . I do not   feel any evil intention behind it . ' 

 ' no , only drunk . ' 

 ' but I shall go home now . ' 

 ' shall I walk with you ? ' 

 ' would you care to ? ' 

 he take his place at her side , and they turn down by the church , to the lake shore . there be a moon above the mountain and the air be come fresh , not too strong , from the west . from the Pacific . little light be burn ruddy by the boat at the water 's edge , some outside , and some inside , under the roof - tilt of the boat 's little inward shed . woman be prepare a mouthful of food . 

 ' but the night be beautiful , ' say Kate , breathe deep . 

 ' with the moon clip away just a little , ' he say . 

 Juana be follow close on her heel : and behind , two soldier in slouch hat . 

 ' do the soldier escort you ? ' she say . 

 ' I suppose so , ' say he . 

 ' but the moon , ' she say , ' be not   lovely and friendly as it be in England or Italy . ' 

 ' it be the same planet , ' he reply . 

 ' but the moonshine in America be not   the same . it do not   make one feel glad as it do in Europe . one feel it would like to hurt one . ' 

 he be silent for some moment . then he say : 

 ' perhaps there be in you something European , which hurt our Mexican Moon . ' 

 ' but I come in good faith . ' 

 ' european good faith . perhaps it be not the same as Mexican . ' 

 Kate be silent , almost stunned . 

 ' Fancy your mexican moon object to I ! ' she laugh ironically . 

 ' fancy your objecting to our mexican moon ! ' say he . 

 ' I be not , ' say she . 

 they come to the corner of Kate 's road . at the corner be a group of tree , and under the tree , behind the hedge , several reed hut . Kate often laugh at the donkey look over the dry - stone low wall , and at the black sheep with curved horn , tie to a bitten tree , and at the lad , naked but for a bit of a shirt , flee into the corner under the thorn screen . 

 Kate and Cipriano sit on the veranda of the House of the Cuentas . she offer he vermouth , but he refuse . 

 they be still . there come the faint pip!-pip ! from the little electric plant just up the road , which Jesús tend . then a cock from beyond the banana crow powerfully and hoarsely . 

 ' but how absurd ! ' say Kate . ' cock do not   crow at this hour . ' 

 ' only in Mexico , ' laugh Cipriano . 

 ' yes ! only here ! ' 

 ' he think your moon be the sun , no ? ' he say , tease she . 

 the cock crow powerfully , again and again . 

 ' this be very nice , your house , your patio , ' say Cipriano . 

 but Kate be silent . 

 ' or do not   you like it ? ' he say . 

 ' you see , ' she answer , ' I have nothing to do ! the servant will not   let I do anything . if I sweep my room , they stand and say Qué Niña ! Qué Niña ! as if I be stand on my head for their benefit . I sew , though I have   no interest in sewing . - what be it , for a life ? ' 

 ' and you read ! ' he say , glance at the magazine and book . 

 ' ah , it be all such stupid , lifeless stuff , in the book and paper , ' she say . 

 there be a silence . after which he say :
