 QUETZALCOATL look down ON MEXICO 

 

 Jesus have go far up the dark slope , when he look back . 
 Quetzalcoatl , my brother ! he call . send I my image , 
 and the image of my mother , and the image of my saint . 
 send I they by the swift way , the way of the spark , 
 that I may hold they like memory in my arm when I go to sleep . 

 and Quetzalcoatl call back : I will do it . 

 then he laugh , see the sun dart fiercely at he . 
 he put up his hand , and hold back the sun with his shadow . 
 so he pass the yellow one , who lash like a dragon in vain . 
 and have pass the yellow one , he see the earth beneath . 
 and he see Mexico lie like a dark woman with white breast - tip . 

 wonder he step nearer , and look at she , 
 at her train , at her railway and her automobile , 
 at her city of stone and her hut of straw , 
 and he say : surely this look very curious ! 

 he sit within the hollow of a cloud , and see the man that work in the field , with foreign overseer . 
 he see the man that be blind , reel with aguardiente . 
 he see the woman that be not clean . 
 he see the heart of they all , that be black , and heavy , with a stone of anger at the bottom . 

 surely , he say , this be a curious people I have find ! 

 so lean forward on his cloud , he say to himself : 
 I will call to they . 
 hold ! hold ! Mexicanos ! glance away a moment towards I . 
 just turn your eye this way , Mexicanos ! 

 they turn not at all , they glance not one his way . 

 Holalá ! Mexicanos ! Holalá ! 

 they have go stone deaf ! he say . 

 so he blow down on they , to blow his breath in their face . 
 but in the weight of their stupefaction , none of they know . 

 Holalá ! what a pretty people ! 
 all go stupefy ! 

 a fall star be run like a white dog over a plain . 
 he whistle to it loudly , twice , till it fall to his hand . 
 in his hand it lie and go dark . 
 it be the Stone of Change . 

 this be the stone of change ! he say . 

 so he toss it awhile in his hand , and play with it . 
 then suddenly he spy the old lake , and he throw it in . 
 it fall in . 
 and two man look up . 

 Holalá ! he say . Mexicanos ! 
 be there two of you awake ? 
 so he laugh , and one hear he laugh . 

 why be you laugh ? ask the first man of Quetzalcoatl . 

 I hear the voice of my First Man ask I why I be laugh ? Holalá , Mexicanos ! it be funny ! 
 to see they so glum and so lumpish ! 

 hey ! First Man of my name ! Hark here ! 
 here be my sign . 
 get a place ready for I . 

 send Jesus his image back , Mary and the saint and all . 
 wash yourself , and rub oil in your skin . 
 on the seventh day , let every man wash himself , and put oil on his skin ; let every woman . 
 let he have no animal walk on his body , nor through the shadow of his hair . say the same to the woman . 
 tell they they all be fool , that I be laugh at they . 
 the first thing I do when I see they , be to laugh at the sight of such fool . 
 such lump , such frog with stone in their belly . 
 tell they they be like frog with stone in their belly , can not   hop ! 
 tell they they must get the stone out of their belly , 
 get rid of their heaviness , 
 their lumpishness , 
 or I will smother they all . 

 I will shake the earth , and swallow they up , with their city . 
 I will send fire and ash upon they , and smother they all . 
 I will turn their blood like sour milk rotten with thunder , 
 they will bleed rotten blood , in pestilence . 
 even their bone shall crumble . 

 tell they so , First Man of my name . 

 for the sun and the moon be alive , and watch with gleam eye . 
 and the earth be alive , and ready to shake off his flea . 
 and the star be ready with stone to throw in the face of man . 
 and the air that blow good breath in the nostril of people and beast 
 be ready to blow bad breath upon they , to perish they all . 

 the star and the earth and the sun and the moon and the wind 
 be about to dance the war dance round you , man ! 
 when I say the word , they will start . 
 for sun and star and earth and the very rain be weary 
 of toss and roll the substance of life to your lip . 
 they be say to one another : let we make an end 
 of those ill - smell tribe of man , these frog that can not   jump , 
 these cock that can not   crow 
 these pig that can not   grunt 
 this flesh that smell 
 these word that be all flat 
 these money vermin . 
 these white man , and red man , and yellow man , and brown man , and black man 
 that be neither white , nor red , nor yellow , nor brown , nor black 
 but everyone of they dirtyish . 
 let we have a spring cleaning in the world . 
 for man upon the body of the earth be like lice , 
 devour the earth into sore . 
 this be what star and sun and earth and moon and wind and rain 
 be discuss with one another ; they be make ready to start . 
 so tell the man I be come to , 
 to make themselves clean , inside and out . 
 to roll the grave - stone off their soul , from the cave of their belly , 
 to prepare to be man . 

 or else prepare for the other thing . 

 

 Kate read this long leaflet again and again , and a swift darkness like a whirlwind seem to envelop the morning . she drink her coffee on the veranda , and the heavy papayas in their grouping seem to be ooze like great drop from the invisible spouting of the fountain of non - human life . she seem to see the great sprouting and urging of the cosmo , move into weird life . and man only like green - fly clustering on the tender tip , an aberration there . so monstrous the rolling and unfolding of the life of the cosmo , as if even iron could grow like lichen deep in the earth , and cease grow , and prepare to perish . iron and stone render up their life , when the hour come . and man be less than the green - fly suck the stem of the bush , so long as they live by business and bread alone . parasite on the face of the earth . 

 she stray to the shore . the lake be blue in the morning light , the opposite mountain pale and dry and rib like mountain in the desert . only at their foot , next the lake , the dark strip of tree and white speck of village . 

 near she against the light five cow stand with their nose to the water , drinking . woman be kneel on the stone , fill red jar . on fork stick stick up on the foreshore , frail fishing - net be hang out , dry , and on the net a small bird sit face the sun ; he be red as a drop of new blood , from the artery of the air . 

 from the straw hut under the tree , her urchin of the mud - chick be scuttle towards she , clutch something in his fist . he open his hand to she , and on the palm lie three of the tiny cooking - pot , the ollita which the native have throw into the water long ago , to the god . 

 ' muy chiquita ! ' he say , in his brisk way , a little , fight tradesman ; ' do you buy they ? ' 

 ' I have no money . to - morrow ! ' say Kate . 

 ' to - morrow ! ' he say , like a pistol shot . 

 ' to - morrow . ' 

 he have forgive she , but she have not forgive he . 

 somebody in the fresh Sunday morning be sing rather beautifully , let the sound , as it be , produce itself . 

 a boy be prowl with a sling , prowl like a cat , to get the little bird . the red bird like a drop of new blood twitter upon the almost invisible fish - net , then in a flash be go . the boy prowl under the delicate green of the willow - tree , stumble over the great root in the sand . 

 along the edge of the water fly four dark bird , their neck push out , skim silent near the silent surface of the lake , in a jagged level rush . 

 Kate know these morning by the lake . they hypnotize she almost like death . scarlet bird like drop of blood , in very green willow - tree . the aguador trot to her house with a pole over his shoulder , and two heavy square gasoline can , one at each end of the pole , fill with hot water . he have be to the hot spring for her daily supply . now barefoot , with one bare leg , the young man trot softly beneath the load , his dark , handsome face sink beneath the shadow of the big hat , as he trot in a silence , mindlessness that be like death . 

 dark head out on the water in little group , like black water - fowl bobbing . be they bird ? be they head ? be this human life , or something intermediate , that lift its orange , wet , glisten shoulder a little out of the lake , beneath the dark head ? 

 she know so well what the day would be . slowly the sun thickening and intensify in the air overhead . and slowly the electricity clotting invisibly as afternoon approach . the beach in the blind heat , strew with refuse , smell of refuse and the urine of creature . 

 everything go vague in the immense sunshine , as the air invisibly thicken , and Kate could feel the electricity press like hot iron on the back of her head . it stupefy she like morphine . meanwhile the cloud rise like white tree from behind the mountain , as the afternoon swoon in silence , rise and spread black branch , quickly , in the sky , from which the lightning stab like bird . 

 and in the midst of the siesta stupor , the sudden round bolt of thunder , and the crash and the chill of rain . 

 tea - time , and evening coming . the last sailing - boat make to depart , wait for the wind . the wind be from the west , the boat go east and south have go , their sail be lapse far away on the lake . but the boat towards the west be wait , wait , while the water rattle under their black flat keel . 

 the big boat from Tlapaltepec , bring many people from the west , wait on into the night . she be anchor a few yard out , and in the early night her passenger come down the dark beach , weary of the day , to go on board . they cluster in a group at the edge of the flap water . 

 the big , wide , flat - bottom canoe , with her wooden awning and her one straight mast , lie black , a few yard out , in the dark night . a lamp be burn under the wooden roof ; one look in , from the shore . and this be home for the passenger . 

 a short man with trouser roll up come to carry the people on board . the man stand with their back to he , leg apart . he suddenly dive at they , duck his head between the fork of their leg and rise , with a man on his shoulder . so he wad out through the water to the black boat , and heave his live load on board . 

 for a woman , he crouch down before she , and she sit on one of his shoulder . he clasp her leg with his right arm , she clasp his dark head . so he carry she to the ship , as if she be nothing . 

 soon the boat be full of people . they sit on the mat on the floor , with their back to the side of the vessel , basket hang from the pent roof , sway as the vessel sway . man spread their serape and curl up to sleep . the light of the lantern light they up , as they sit and lie and sleep , or talk in murmur . 

 a little woman come up out of the darkness ; then suddenly run back again . she have forget something . but the vessel would not sail without she , for the wind would not change yet . 

 the tall mast stand high , the great sail lie in fold along the roof , ready . under the roof , the lantern sway , the people sleep and stretch . probably they would not sail till midnight . then down the lake to Tlapaltepec , with its reed at the end of the lake , and its dead , dead plaza , its dead dry house of black adobe , its ruin street , its strange , bury silence , like Pompeii . 

 Kate know it . so strange and deathlike , it frighten she , and mystify she . 

 but to - day ! to - day she would not loiter by the shore all morning . she must go to Jamiltepec in a motor - boat , to see Ram n. to talk to he even about marry Cipriano . 

 ah , how could she marry Cipriano , and give her body to this death ? take the weight of this darkness on her breast , the heaviness of this strange gloom ? die before die , and pass away whilst still beneath the sun ? 

 ah no ! well to escape to the white man 's land . 

 but she go to arrange with Alonso for the motor - boat . 

 

 

 CHAPTER XVII 

 Fourth Hymn and the Bishop 

 

 the President of the Republic , as a new broom , have be sweep perhaps a little too clean for the common liking , so there be a ' rebellion . ' it be not a very large one . but it mean , of course , banditry , robbery , and cow village . 

 Ram n be determined to keep free from the taint of politic . but already the Church , and with the Church the Knights of Cortés and a certain ' black ' faction , be prepare against he . the priest begin to denounce he from the pulpit - but not very loudly - as an ambitious Anti - Christ . with Cipriano beside he , however , and with Cipriano the army of the west , he have not much to fear . 

 but it be possible Cipriano would have to march away in defence of the Government . 

 ' above all thing , ' say Ram n , ' I do not   want to acquire a political smell . I do not   want to be push in the direction of any party . unless I can stand uncontaminated , I have well abandon everything . but the Church will push I over to the socialists - and the socialist will betray I on the first opportunity . it be not myself . it be the new spirit . the sure way to kill it - and it can be kill , like any other live thing - be to get it connect with any political party . ' 

 ' why do not   you see the Bishop ? ' say Cipriano . ' I will see he too . be I to be chief of the division in the west for nothing ? ' 

 ' yes , ' say Ram n slowly , ' I will see Jimenez . I have think of it . yes , I intend to use every mean in my power . - Montes will stand for we , because he hat the Church and hat any hint of dictation from outside . he see the possibility of a " national " church . though myself , I do not   care about national church . only one have to speak the language of one 's own people . you know the priest be forbid the people to read the Hymns ? ' 

 ' what do that matter ? ' say Cipriano . ' these people be nothing if not perverse , nowadays . they will read they all the more . ' 

 ' maybe ! - I shall take no notice . I will let my new legend , as they call it , grow while the earth be moist . but we have to keep our eye very close on all the little bunch of " interest " . ' 

 ' ram n ! ' say Cipriano . ' if you can turn Mexico entirely into a Quetzalcoatl country , what then ? ' 

 ' I shall be First Man of Quetzalcoatl - I know no more . ' 

 ' you will not   trouble about the rest of the world ? ' 

 Ram n smile . already he see in Cipriano 's eye the gleam of a Holy War . 

 ' I would like , ' he say , smile , ' to be one of the Initiates of the Earth . one of the Initiators . every country its own Saviour , Cipriano : or every people its own saviour . and the First Men of every people , form a Natural Aristocracy of the World . one must have aristocrat , that we know . but natural one , not artificial . and in some way the world must be organically unite : the world of man . but in the concrete , not in the abstract . league and Covenants and International Programmes . ah ! Cipriano ! it be like an international pestilence . the leaf of one great tree can not   hang on the bough of another great tree . the race of the earth be like tree ; in the end they neither mix nor mingle . they stand out of each other 's way , like tree . or else they crowd on one another , and their root grapple , and it be the fight to the death . - only from the flower there be commingle . and the flower of every race be the natural aristocrat of that race . and the spirit of the world can fly from flower to flower , like a humming - bird , and slowly fertilize the great tree in their blossom . only the Natural Aristocrats can rise above their nation ; and even then they do not rise beyond their race . only the Natural Aristocrats of the World can be international , or cosmopolitan , or cosmic . it have always be so . the people be no more capable of it than the leaf of the mango - tree be capable of attach themselves to the pine . - so if I want Mexicans to learn the name of Quetzalcoatl , it be because I want they to speak with the tongue of their own blood . I wish the teutonic world would once more think in term of Thor and Wotan , and the tree Igdrasil . and I wish the druidic world would see , honestly , that in the mistletoe be their mystery , and that they themselves be the Tuatha De Danaan , alive , but submerge . and a new Hermes should come back to the Mediterranean , and a new Ashtaroth to Tunis ; and Mithras again to Persia , and Brahma unbroken to India , and the old of dragon to China . then I , Cipriano , I , First Man of Quetzalcoatl , with you , First Man of Huitzilopochtli , and perhaps your wife , First Woman of Itzpapalotl , could we not meet , with sure soul , the other great aristocrat of the world , the First Man of Wotan and the First Woman of Freya , First Lord of Hermes , and the Lady of Astarte , the Best - bear of Brahma , and the Son of the Greatest Dragon ? I tell you , Cipriano , then the earth might rejoice , when the First Lords of the West meet the First Lords of South and East , in the Valley of the Soul . ah , the earth have Valleys of the Soul , that be not city of commerce and industry . and the mystery be one mystery , but man must see it differently . the hibiscus and the thistle and the gentian all flower on the Tree of Life , but in the world they be far apart ; and must be . and I be hibiscus and you be a yucca flower , and your Caterina be a wild daffodil , and my Carlota be a white pansy . only four of we , yet we make a curious bunch . so it be . the man and woman of the earth be not manufacture good , to be interchangeable . but the Tree of Life be one tree , as we know when our soul open in the last blossoming . we can not   change ourselves , and we do not   want to . but when our soul open out in the final blossoming , then as blossom we share one mystery with all blossom , beyond the knowledge of any leaf and stem and root : something transcendent . 

 ' but it do not   matter . at the present time I have to fight my way in Mexico , and you have to fight your . so let we go and do it . ' 

 he go away to his workshop and his man who be labour under his direction , while Cipriano sit down to his correspondence and his military planning . 

 they be both interrupt by the thudding of a motor - boat enter the little bay . it be Kate , escort by the black - scarve Juana . 

 Ram n , in his white clothe , with the blue - and - black figured sash and the big hat with the turquoise - inlay Eye of Quetzalcoatl , go down to meet she . she be in white , too , with a green hat and the shawl of pale yellow silk . 

 ' I be so glad to come again , ' she say , hold out her hand to he . ' Jamiltepec have become a sort of Mecca to I , my inside yearn for it . ' 

 ' then why do not   you come oftener ? I wish you would come . ' 

 ' I be afraid of intrude . ' 

 ' no ! you could help if you would . ' 

 ' oh ! ' she say . ' I be so frightened , and so sceptical of big undertaking . I think it be because , at the very bottom of I , I dislike the mass of people - anywhere . I be afraid I rather despise people ; I do not   want they to touch I , and I do not   want to touch they . - so how could I pretend to join any - any - any sort of Salvation Army ? - which be a horrid way of put it . ' 

 Don Ram n laugh . 

 ' I do myself , ' he say . ' I det and despise mass of people . but these be my own people . ' 

 ' I , ever since I be a child , since I can remember . - they say of I , when I be a little girl of four , and my parent be have a big dinner - party , they have the nurse bring I in to say good night to all the people they have there dress up and eat and drink . and I suppose they all say nice thing to I , as they do . I only answer : you be all monkey ! it be a great success ! - but I feel it even as a child , and I feel it now . People be all monkey to I , perform in different way . ' 

 ' even the people near you ? ' 

 Kate hesitate . then she confess , rather unwillingly : 

 ' yes ! I be afraid so . both my husband - even Joachim - they seem , somehow , so obstinate in their little stupidity - rather like monkey . I feel a terrible revulsion from Joachim when he be dead . I think : what peak monkey be that , that I have be lose my blood about . - do you think it be rather awful ? ' 

 ' I do ! but then I think we all feel like that , at moment . or we would if we dare . it be only one of our moment . ' 

 ' sometimes , ' say she , ' I think that be my permanent feeling towards people . I like the world , the sky and the earth and the great mystery beyond . but people - yes , they be all monkey to I . ' 

 he could see that , at the bottom of her soul , it be true . 

 ' Puros monos ! ' he say to himself in Spanish . ' Y lo que hacen , pura monerías . ' 

 ' pure monkey ! and the thing they do , sheer monkeydom ! ' then he add : ' yet you have child ! ' 

 ' yes ! yes ! ' she say , struggle with herself . ' my first husband 's child . ' 

 ' and they ? - monos y no más ? ' 

 ' no ! ' she say , frown and look angry with herself . ' only partly . ' 

 ' it be bad , ' he say , shake his head . ' but then ! ' he add . - ' what be my own child to I , but little monkey ? and their mother - and their mother - ah , no ! Señora Caterina ! it be no good . one must be able to disentangle oneself from person , from people . if I go to a rose - bush , to be intimate with it , it be a nasty thing that hurt I . one must disentangle oneself from person and personality , and see people as one see the tree in the landscape . People in some way dominate you . in some way , humanity dominate your consciousness . so you must hate people and humanity , and you want to escape . but there be only one way of escape : to turn beyond they , to the great life . ' 

 ' but I do ! ' cry Kate . ' I do nothing else . when I be with Joachim absolutely alone in a cottage , do all the work myself , and know nobody at all , just live , and feel the great thing all the time ; then I be free , I be happy . ' 

 ' but he ? ' say Ram n. ' was he free and happy ? ' 

 ' he be really . but that be where the monkeyishness come in . he would not   let himself be content . he insist on have people and a cause , just to torture himself with . ' 

 ' then why do not   you live in your cottage quite alone , and without he ? ' he say . ' why do you travel and see people ? ' 

 she be silent , very angry . she know she could not live quite alone . the vacuity crush she . she need a man there , to stop the gap , and to keep she balanced . but even when she have he , in her heart of heart she despise he , as she despise the dog and the cat . between herself and humanity there be the bond of subtle , helpless antagonism . 

 she be naturally quite free - handed and she leave people their liberty . servant would get attach to she , and casual people all like and admire she . she have a strong life - flow of her own , and a certain assertive joie de vivre . 

 but underneath it all be the unconquerable dislike , almost disgust of people . More than hate , it be disgust . whoever it be , wherever it be , however it be , after a little while this disgust overcome she . her mother , her father , her sister , her first husband , even her child whom she love , and Joachim , for whom she have feel such passionate love , even these , be near she , fill she with a certain disgust and repulsion after a little while , and she long to fle they down the great and final oubliette . 

 but there be no great and final oubliette : or at least , it be never final , until one have fling oneself down . 

 so it be with Kate . till she fling herself down the last dark oubliette of death , she would never escape from her deep , her bottomless disgust with human being . brief contact be all right , thrill even . but close contact , or long contact , be short and long revulsion of violent disgust . 

 she and Ram n have sit down on a bench under the white - flower oleander of the garden downstairs . his face be impassive and still . in the stillness , with a certain pain and nausea , he realize the state she be in , and realize that his own state , as regard personal people , be the same . mere personal contact , mere human contact fill he , too , with disgust . Carlota disgust he . Kate herself disgust he . sometimes , Cipriano disgust he . 

 but this be because , or when , he meet they on a merely human , personal plane . to do so be disaster : it fill he with disgust of they and loathing of himself . 

 he have to meet they on another plane , where the contact be different ; intangible , remote , and without intimacy . his soul be concerned elsewhere . so that the quick of he need not be bind to anybody . the quick of a man must turn to God alone : in some way or other . 

 with Cipriano he be most sure . Cipriano and he , even when they embrace each other with passion , when they meet after an absence , embrace in the recognition of each other 's eternal and abide loneliness ; like the Morning Star . 

 but woman would not have this . they want intimacy - and intimacy mean disgust . Carlota want to be eternally and closely identify with Ram n , consequently she hat he and hat everything which she think draw he away from this eternal close identification with herself . it be just a horror and he know it . 

 man and woman should know that they can not , absolutely , meet on earth . in the close kiss , the dear touch , there be the small gulf which be none the less complete because it be so narrow , so nearly non - existent . they must bow and submit in reverence , to the gulf . even though I eat the body and drink the blood of Christ , Christ be Christ and I be I , and the gulf be impassable . though a woman be dearer to a man than his own life , yet he be he and she be she , and the gulf can never close up . any attempt to close it be a violation , and the crime against the Holy Ghost . 

 that which we get from the beyond , we get it alone . the final I I be , come from the farth off , from the Morning Star . the rest be assemble . all that of I which be assemble from the mighty cosmos can meet and touch all that be assemble in the beloved . but this be never the quick . never can be . 

 if we would meet in the quick , we must give up the assemble self , the daily I , and , put off ourselves one after the other , meet unconscious in the Morning Star . Body , soul , and spirit can be transfigure into the Morning Star . but without transfiguration we shall never get there . we shall gnash at the leash . 

 Ram n know what it be to gnash at his leash . he have gnash himself almost to piece , before he have find the way to pass out in himself , in the quick of himself , to the Quick of all be and existence , which he call the Morning Star , since man must give all thing name . to pass in the quick of himself , with transfiguration , to the Morning Star , and there , there alone meet his fellow man . 

 he know what it be to fail even now , and to keep on fail . with Carlota he fail absolutely . she claim he and he restrain himself in resistance . even his very naked breast , when Carlota be there , be self - conscious and assertively naked . but then that be because she claim it as her property . 

 when man meet at the quick of all thing , they be neither naked nor clothe ; in the transfiguration they be just complete , they be not see in part . the final perfect strength have also the power of innocence . 

 sit on the seat beside Kate , Ram n be sad with the sense of heaviness and inadequacy . his third Hymn be angry and bitter . Carlota almost embitter his soul . in Mexico , turbulent fellow have catch at his idea and burlesque it . they have invade one of the church of the city , throw out the sacred image , and hang in their place the grotesque papi - mâché Judas figure , which the Mexicans explode at Easter time . this of course make a scandal . and Cipriano , whenever he be away on his own for some time , slip back into the inevitable Mexican General , fascinate by the opportunity for further his own personal ambition and impose his own personal will . then come Kate , with this centre of sheer repudiation deep in the middle of she , the will to explode the world . 

 he feel his spirit sink again , his limb go like lead . there be only one thing that a man really want to do , all his life ; and that be , to find his way to his God , his Morning Star , and be alone there . then afterwards , in the Morning Star , salute his fellow man , and enjoy the woman who have come the long way with he . 

 but to find the way , far , far along , to the bright Quick of all thing , this be difficult , and require all a man 's strength and courage , for himself . if he break a trail alone , it be terrible . but if every hand pull at he , to stay he in the human place ; if the hand of love drag at his entrail and the hand of hate seize he by the hair , it become almost impossible . 

 this be how Ram n feel at the moment : - I be attempt the impossible . I have well either go and take my pleasure of life while it last , hopeless of the pleasure which be beyond all pleasure . or else I have well go into the desert and take my way all alone , to the Star where at last I have my wholeness , holiness . the way of the anchorite and the man who go into the wilderness to pray . for surely my soul be crave for her consummation , and I be weary of the thing man call life . live , I want to depart to where I be . 

 yet , he say to himself , the woman that be with I in the Morning Star , how glad I should be of she ! and the man that be with I there , what a delight his presence would be ! surely the Morning Star be a meeting - ground for we , for the joy ! 

 sit side by side on the bench , Ram n and Kate forget one another , she think back on the past , with the long disgust of it all , he think on into his future , and try to revive his heavy spirit . 

 in the silence , Cipriano come out on to the balcony above , look around . he almost start as he see the two figure seat on the bench below , under the white oleander tree , mile apart , world apart , in their silence . 

 Ram n hear the step , and glance up . 

 ' we be come up ! ' he call , rise and look round at Kate . ' shall we go upstairs ? will you drink something cool , tepache , or squeeze orange ? there be no ice . ' 

 ' I would like orange juice and water , ' she say . 

 he call to his servant and give the order . 

 Cipriano be in the white pantaloon and blouse , like Ram n. but his sash be scarlet , with black curve , something like the marking on a snake . 

 ' I hear you come . I think perhaps you have go away again , ' he say , look at she with a certain black reproachfulness : an odd , hesitate wistfulness of the barbarian , who feel himself at a loss . then also a certain resentment . 

 ' not yet , ' she say . 

 Ram n laugh , and fling himself into a chair . 

 ' the Señora Caterina think we be all monkey , but perhaps this particular monkey - show be the most amusing after all , ' he say . ' so she will see a little more of it . ' 

 Cipriano , a real Indian , be offend in his pride , and the little black imperial on his chin seem to become portentous . 

 ' that be rather an unfair way of put it ! ' laugh Kate . 

 the black eye of Cipriano glance at she in hostility . he think she be laugh at he . and so , at the depth of her female soul , she be . she be jeer at he inwardly . which no man can stand , least of all a dark - skin man . 

 ' no ! ' she say . ' there be something else beside that . ' 

 ' ah ! ' say Ram n. ' take care ! a little mercy be a dangerous thing . ' 

 ' no ! not mercy ! ' she say , flush . ' why be you be horrid to I ? ' 

 ' monkey always end by be horrid to the spectator , ' say Ram n. 

 she look up at he , and catch the flash of anger in his eye . 

 ' I come , ' she say , ' to hear about the mexican pantheon . I be even give to understand I might be admit . ' 

 ' ah , that be good ! ' laugh Ram n. ' a rare speciman of the female monkey have be add to the Ram n menagerie ! I be sure you would be a good draw . there have be some pretty goddess , I assure you , in the aztec pantheon . ' 

 ' how horrid ! ' she say . 

 ' come ! come ! ' he cry . ' let we keep to the bedrock of thing , Señora mía . we be all monkey . mono somos . - ihr seid alle Affen ! out of the mouth of babe and suckling be it speak , as Carlota say . you see that little male monkey , Cipriano . he have the monkey 's idea of marry you . say the word . marriage be a monkey 's game . say the word . he will let you go when you have   have enough ; and he be have enough . he be a general and a very great jefe . he can make you monkey - queen of monkey - Mexico , if it please you . and what should monkey do , but amuse themselves ! Vamos ! Embobémonos ! shall I be priest ? Vamos ! Vamos ! ' 

 he rise with sudden volcanic violence , and rush away . 

 Cipriano look at Kate in wonder . she have go pale . 

 ' what have you be say to he ? ' he ask . 

 ' nothing ! ' she say , rise . ' I would well go now . ' 

 Juana be collect ; and Alonso and Kate set off back down the lake . she sit with a certain obstinate offendedness under the awning of the boat . the sun be terrifically hot , and the water blind she . she put on black spectacle , in which she look a monster . 

 ' Mucho calor , Niña ! Mucho calor ! ' Juana be repeat behind she . the criada have evidently imbibe tepache . 

 on the pale - brown water little tuft of water - hyacinth be vaguely sailing , hold up the hand of a leaf for a sail . everywhere the lake be dot with these sailing tuft . the heavy rain have wash in flood down the Lerma river into the lake , wash the acre of lirio loose from the marshy end of the water , thirty mile away , and slowly set they travel over all the expanse of the inland sea , till the shore begin to be pile , and the far - off Santiago river , which flow out of the lake , be choke . 

 that day Ram n write his Fourth Hymn . 

 

 what QUETZALCOATL see in MEXICO 

 

 who be these strange face in Mexico ? 
 paleface , yellowface , blackface ? these be no Mexicans ! 
 where do they come from , and why ? 

 Lord of the Two Ways , these be the foreigner . 
 they come out of nowhere . 
 sometimes they come to tell we thing , 
 mostly they be the greedy one . 

 what then do they want ? 

 they want gold , they want silver from the mountain , 
 and oil , much oil from the coast . 
 they take sugar from the tall tube of the cane , 
 wheat from the high land , and maize ; 
 Coffee from the bush in the hot land , even the juicy rubber . 
 they put up tall chimney that smoke , 
 and in the big house they keep their machine , that talk 
 and work iron elbow up and down , 
 and hold myriad thread from their claw ! 
 Wonderful be the machine of the greedy one ! 

 and you , Mexicans and peon , what do you do ? 

 we work with their machine , we work in their field , 
 they give we peso make of mexican silver . 
 they be the clever one . 

 do you love they then ? 

 we love they not , and never . 
 their face be ugly , yet they make wonderful thing . 
 and their will be like their machine of iron . 
 what can we do ? 

 I see dark thing rush across the country . 

 Yea , Lord ! even train and camione and automobile . 

 train and camione , automobile and aeroplane . 
 how nice ! say the peon , to go rush in a train ! 
 how nice , to get in the camion , and for twenty centavos , to be go ! 
 how nice , in the great city , where all thing rush , and huge light flare bright , to wander and do nothing ! 
 how nice to sit in the cine , where the picture of all the world dance before the eye ! 
 how nice if we could take all these thing away from the foreigner , and possess they ! 
 take back our land and silver and oil , take the train and the factory and the automobile 
 and play with they all the time ! 
 how nice ! 

 oh , fool ! mexican and peon ! 
 who be you , to be master of machine which you can not make ? 
 which you can only break ! 
 those that can make be master of these machine . 
 not you , poor boob . 

 how have these paleface , yellowface cross the water of the world ? 
 oh , fool ! mexican and peon , with muddy heart ! 
 do they do it by squat on their ham ? 
 you do nothing but squat on your ham , and stare with vacant eye , and drink fire - water , and quarrel and stab . 
 and then run like surly dog at the bidding of paleface master . 

 oh , dog and fool , Mexicans and peon ! 
 Watery - hearted , with wishy - washy knee . 
 Sulky in spirit , and inert . 
 what be you good for , but to be slave , and rot away ? 

 you be not worth a god ! 
 Lo ! the universe tangle its great dragon , 
 the dragon in the cosmo be stir with anger again . 
 the dragon of the disappointed dead , that sleep in the snow - white north 
 be lash his tail in his sleep ; the wind howl , the cold rock round . 
 the spirit of the cold dead whistle in the ear of the world . 
 prepare for doom . 

 for I tell you , there be no dead dead , not even your dead . 
 there be dead that sleep in the wave of the Morning Star , with freshen limb . 
 there be dead that weep in bitter rain . 
 there be dead that cluster in the frozen north , shudder and chatter among the ice 
 and howl with hate . 
 there be dead that creep through the burn bowel of the earth , 
 stir the fire to acid of bitterness . 
 there be dead that sit under the tree , watch with ash - grey eye for their victim . 
 there be dead that attack the sun like swarm of black fly , to suck his life . 
 there be dead that stand upon you , when you go in to your woman , 
 and they dart to her womb , they fight for the chance to be bear , they struggle at the gate you have open , 
 they gnash when it close , and hate the one that get in to be bear again , 
 child of the live dead , the dead that live and be not refresh . 
 I tell you , sorrow upon you ; you shall all die . 
 and be dead , you shall not be refresh . 
 there be no dead dead . 
 be dead , you shall rove like dog with broken haunch 
 seek the offal and garbage of life , in the invisible lane of the air . 

 the dead that have master fire live on , salamander , in fire . 
 the dead of the water - lord rock and glimmer in the sea . 
 the dead of the steel machine go up in motion , away ! 
 the dead of electric master be electricity itself . 

 but the dead of those who have master nothing , nothing at all , 
 crawl like masterless dog in the back street of the air , 
 creep for the garbage of life , and bite with venomous mouth . 

 those that have master the force of the world , die into the force , they have home in death . 
 but you ! what have you master , among the dragon host of the cosmo ? 
 there be dragon of sun and ice , dragon of the moon and the earth , dragon of salty water , dragon of thunder ; 
 there be the spangled dragon of the star at large . 
 and far at the centre , with one unblinking eye , the dragon of the Morning Star . 

 Conquer ! say the Morning Star . pass the dragon , and pass on to I . 
 for I be sweet , I be the last and the good , the pool of new life . 
 but lo ! you inert one , I will set the dragon upon you . 
 they shall crunch your bone . 
 and even then they shall spit you out , as break - haunche dog , 
 you shall have nowhere to die into . 

 Lo ! in the back street of the air , dead one be crawl like cur ! 
 Lo ! I release the dragon ! the great white one of the north , 
 he of the disappointed dead , he be lash and turn round . 
 he be breathe cold corruption upon you , you shall bleed in your chest . 

 I be go to speak to the dragon of the inner fire , 
 he who housel the dead of the gun , 
 to withdraw his warmth from your foot , so your foot turn cold with death . 

 I be about to tell the dragon of the water to turn round on you 
 and spew out corrosion into your stream , on your rain . 

 and I wait for the final day , when the dragon of thunder , wake under the spider - web net 
 which you have   throw upon he , shall suddenly shake with rage , 
 and dart his electric needle into your bone , and curdle your blood like milk with electric venom . 

 wait ! only wait ! little by little it all shall come upon you . 

 

 Ram n put on his black city clothe , and a black hat , and go himself with this hymn to the printer in the city . the sign of Quetzalcoatl he have print in black and red , and the sign of the dragon , at the end , in green and black and red . and the sheet be fold . 

 six soldier of Cipriano 's command take the bundle of hymn by train ; one to the capital , one to Puebla and Jalapa , one to Tampico and Monterrey , one to Torreon and Chihuahua , one to Sinaloa and Sonora , and one to the mine in Pachucha , Guanajuato , and the central region . each soldier take only a hundred sheet . but in every town there be a recognized reader of the Hymns ; or two , or three , or four , or even ten reader in one city . and reader who go round to the village . 

 because there be a strange , submerge desire in the people for thing beyond the world . they be weary of event , and weary of news and the newspaper , weary even of the thing that be teach in education . Weary be the spirit of man with man 's importunity . of all thing human , and humanly invent , we have have enough , they seem to say . and though they take not much active notice of the Hymns , they crave for they , as man crave for alcohol , as a relief from the weariness and ennui of mankind 's man - make world . 

 everywhere , in all the town and village , at night - time the little flame would be see flickering , a cluster of people be see , sometimes stand , sometimes sit upon the ground , listen to the slow voice of some Reader . 

 more rarely , in some small , out - of - the - way plaza , would sound the sinister thud of the tom - tom , beat out of the hollow of the age . and there would be two man with white serape with the blue edge . then the singing of the Songs of Quetzalcoatl , and perhaps the slow round dance , with the ancient rhythm of the foot on the earth , belong to aboriginal America . 

 for the old dance of the Aztecs and the Zapotees , of all the submerge indian race , be base upon the old , sink bird - step of the Red Indians of the north . it be in the blood of the people ; they can not quite forget it . it come back to they , with a sense of fear , and joy , and relief . 

 of themselves , they dare not revive the old motion , nor stir the blood in the old way . the spell of the past be too terrible . but in the Songs and the Hymns of Quetzalcoatl there speak a new voice , the voice of a master and authority . and though they be slow to trust , the slow and the most untrusting , they seize upon the new - old thrill , with a certain fear , and joy , and relief . 

 the Men of Quetzalcoatl avoid the great market - place and centre of activity . they take their stand in the little side place . on the rim of a fountain a man in a dark blanket with blue border , or with the sign of Quetzalcoatl in his hat , would sit down and begin to read aloud . it be enough . the people linger to listen . he would read to the end , then say : ' I have finish this reading of the Fourth Hymn of Quetzalcoatl . now I will begin again . ' 

 in this way , by a sort of far - away note in the voice , and by the slow monotony of repetition , the thing would drift darkly into the consciousness of the listener . 

 already in the beginning there have be the scandal of the Judases . Holy Week , in Mexico City , be , to all appearance , the great week of Judas . everywhere you see man carry home in triumph the great , gaudily - varnish doll of papi - mâché . they be all man - doll , more or less life - like grotesque . most frequently it be a fat mexican - spanish hacendado , landowner and big farmer , who be represent with his tight trouser , stick - out belly , and huge upturned moustache . the old - fashioned patr n. some of the figure be like Punch , some be like harlequin . but they all have rosy face and the white man 's get - up . you never see the dark - face image of a native - blooded Mexican ; always a stiff , haughty grotesque of a white man . 

 and all these be Judases . Judas be the fun of the fair , the victim , the big man of Holy Week , just as the Skeleton , and the skeleton on horseback , be the idol of the first week in November , the day of the dead and of all the saint . 

 on Easter Saturday the Judases be hang from the balcony , the string be light , and at length , bang ! shriek of joy , Judas have explode into nothingness , from a big cracker in the middle of he ! - all the town be pop with Judases . 

 there be the scandal of the Holy Images throw out of one of the church in Mexico City , and these judas put in their place . the Church begin to move . 

 but then the Church in Mexico have to move gingerly ; it be not popular , and its claw be cut . the priest may not ring the church bell for more than three minute . neither priest nor monk may wear any habit in the street , beyond the hideous black vest and white collar of the protestant clergy . so that the priest show himself as little as possible in the street , and practically never in the chief street and the chief plazas . 

 nevertheless , he still have influence . procession in the street be forbid , but not sermon from the pulpit , nor advice from the confessional . Montes , the President , have no love for the Church , and be meditate the expulsion of all foreign priest . the Archbishop himself be an italian . but he be also a fighter . 

 he give order to all the priest , to forbid the people from listen to anything concern with Quetzalcoatl , to destroy any hymn - sheet that might fall into their hand , and to prevent as far as possible the Hymns from be read , and the Songs from be sing , in the parish . 

 but Montes have give order to the police and the military to afford such protection to the Men of Quetzalcoatl as be accord to any other law - abide citizen . 

 Mexico be not Mexico for nothing , however , and already blood have be shed on both side . this Ram n particularly want to avoid , as he feel that violent death be not so easily wipe out of the air and out of the soul of man , as spilt blood be wash off the pavement . 

 therefore , when he be in the City , he ask the Bishop of the West if he would consent to an interview with himself and Don Cipriano , and would he name the place . the Bishop - who be an old friend and adviser of Carlota , and who know Ram n well enough - reply that he would be pleased to see Don Ram n and the Señor General the next day , if they would be so good as to come to his house . 

 the Bishop no long occupy the great episcopal palace . this be turn into the post - office building . but he have a large house not far from the Cathedral , which have be present by the faithful . 

 Ram n and Cipriano find the thin old man in a dusty , uninteresting library , wait . he wear a simple black cassock , not too clean , with purple button . he receive Ram n , who be in a black town suit , and Cipriano , who be in uniform , with an affable manner and suspicious look . but he play at be the lively , genial old bird . 

 ' ah , Don Ram n , it be long since I see you ! how go it , eh ? well , well ? that be good ! that be very good ! ' and he pat Ram n on the sleeve like a fussy old uncle . ' ah , my General , much honour , much honour ! welcome to this poor house of your . it be the house of your Honour ! to serve you ! gentleman ! will not   you take a seat ? ' 

 they all sit down , in the dusty , dreary room , in the old leather chair . the Bishop nervously look at his thin old hand , at the fine , but rather dull amethyst ring he wear . 

 ' good ! señore ! ' he say , glance up with his little black eye . ' at your service ! entirely at the service of your Honours . ' 

 ' Doña Carlota be in the city , Father . you have see she ? ' say Ram n. 

 ' yes , son of mine , ' say the Bishop . 

 ' then you know the late news about I . she tell you everything . ' 

 ' somewhat ! somewhat ! she speak somewhat of you , the poor little thing . thank to God she have her son with she . they be safely back in their native country , in good health . ' 

 ' do you see they ? ' 

 ' yes ! yes ! two of my dear child ! very sympathetic , very intelligent , like their father ; and , like he , promise to be of very handsome presence . yes ! yes ! smoke if you will , my General . do not   hesitate . ' 

 Cipriano light a cigarette . from old association , he be nervous , albeit amuse . 

 ' you know all about what I want to do , Father ? ' say Ram n. 

 ' I do not   know all , son of mine , but I know enough . I would not   want to hear more . eh ! ' he sigh . ' it be very sad . ' 

 ' not so very sad , Father , if we do not   make it sad . why make a sad thing out of it , Father ? we be in Mexico for the most part Indians . they can not understand the high Christianity , Father , and the Church know it . Christianity be a religion of the spirit , and must need be understand if it be to have any effect . the Indians can not understand it , any more than the rabbit of the hill . ' 

 ' very good ! very good ! Son of mine ! but we can convey it to they . the rabbit of the hill be in the hand of God . ' 

 ' no , Father , it be impossible . and without a religion that will connect they with the universe , they will all perish . only religion will serve ; not socialism , nor education , nor anything . ' 

 ' thou speak well , ' say the Bishop . 

 ' the rabbit of the hill may be in the hand of God , Father . but they be at the mercy of man . the same with Mexico . the people sink heavy and heavy into inertia , and the Church can not help they , because the Church do not possess the key - word to the mexican soul . ' 

 ' do not   the mexican soul know the Voice of God ? ' say the Bishop . 

 ' your own child may know your voice , Father . but if you go out to speak to the bird on the lake , or the deer among the mountain , will they know your voice ? will they wait and listen ? ' 

 ' who know ? it be say they wait to listen to the Holy Francisco of Assisi . ' 

 ' now , Father , we must speak to the Mexicans in their own language , and give they the clue - word to their own soul . I shall say Quetzalcoatl . if I be wrong , let I perish . but I be not wrong . ' 

 the Bishop fidget rather restlessly . he do not   want to hear all this . and he do not want to answer . he be impotent anyhow . 

 ' your Church be the Catholic Church , Father ? ' 

 ' surely ! ' say the Bishop . 

 ' and Catholic Church mean the Church of All , the Universal Church ? ' 

 ' surely , son of mine . ' 

 ' then why not let it be really catholic ? why call it catholic , when it be not only just one among many church , but be even hostile to all the rest of the church ? Father , why not let the Catholic Church become really the Universal Church ? ' 

 ' it be the Universal Church of Christ , my son . ' 

 ' why not let it be the Universal Church of Mohammed as well ; since ultimately , God be one God , but the people speak vary language , and each need its own prophet to speak with its own tongue . the Universal Church of Christ , and Mohammed , and Buddha , and Quetzalcoatl , and all the other - that would be a Catholic Church , Father . ' 

 ' you speak of thing beyond I , ' say the Bishop , turn his ring . 

 ' not beyond any man , ' say Don Ram n. ' a Catholic Church be a church of all the religion , a home on earth for all the prophet and the Christs , a big tree under which every man who acknowledge the great life of the soul can sit and be refresh . be not   that the Catholic Church , Father ? ' 

 ' alas , my son , I know the Apostolic Church of Christ in Rome , of which I be a humble servant . I do not understand these clever thing you be say to I . ' 

 ' I be ask you for peace , Father . I be not one who hat the Church of Christ , the Roman Catholic Church . but in Mexico I think it have no place . when my heart be not bitter , I be grateful forever to Christ , the Son of God . the affair of the Judases grieve I more than it do you , and the affair of bloodshed be far bitter to I . ' 

 ' I be no innovator , my son , to provoke bloodshed . ' 

 ' listen ! I be go to remove the holy image from the church at Sayula , with reverence , and with reverence burn they upon the lake . then I shall put the image of Quetzalcoatl in the church at Sayula . ' 

 the Bishop look up furtively . for some moment he say nothing . but his silence be furtive , cornered . 

 ' would you dare do that , Don Ram n ? ' he say . 

 ' yes ! and I shall not be prevent . General Viedma be with I . ' 

 the Bishop glance sideways at Cipriano . 

 ' certainly , ' say Cipriano . 

 ' nevertheless it be illegal , ' say the Bishop , with acid bitterness . 

 ' what be illegal in Mexico ? ' say Ram n. ' what be weak be illegal . I will not be weak , my Lord . ' 

 ' lucky you ! ' say the Bishop , lift his shoulder . 

 there be a break of silence . 

 ' no ! ' say Ram n. ' I come to ask you for peace . tell the Archbishop what I say . let he tell the Cardinals and the Pope that the time have come for a Catholic Church of the Earth , the Catholic Church of all the Sons of Men . the Saviours be more than one , and let we pray they will still be increase . but God be one God , and the Saviours be the Sons of the one God . let the Tree of the Church spread its branch over all the earth , and shelter the prophet in its shade , as they sit and speak their knowledge of the beyond . ' 

 ' be you one of these prophet , Don Ram n ? ' 

 ' I surely be , Father . and I would speak about Quetzalcoatl in Mexico , and build his Church here . ' 

 ' Nay ! you would invade the church of Christ and the Blessed Virgin , I hear you say . ' 

 ' you know my intention . but I do not want to quarrel with the Church of Rome , nor have bloodshe and enmity , Father . can you not understand I ? should there not be peace between the man who strive down their different way to the God - Mystery ? ' 

 ' once more desecrate the altar ! bring in strange idol . burn the image of our Lord and our Lady , and ask for peace ? ' say the poor Bishop , who helplessly long to be leave alone . 

 ' all that , Father , ' say Ram n. 

 ' Son , what can I answer ? you be a good man smite with the madness of pride . Don Cipriano be one more mexican general . I be the poor old Bishop of this diocese , faithful servant of the Holy Church , humble child of the Holy Father in Rome . what can I do ? what can I answer ? take I out to the cemetery and shoot I at once , general ! ' 

 ' I do not   want to , ' say Cipriano . 

 ' it will end like that , ' say the Bishop . 

 ' but why ? ' cry Don Ram n. ' be there no sense in what I say ? can not you understand ? ' 

 ' my son , my understanding go no far than my faith , my duty , will allow . I be not a clever man , I live by faith and my duty to my sacred office . understand that I do not understand . ' 

 ' good - day , Father ! ' say Ram n , suddenly rise . 

 ' go with God , my son , ' say the Bishop , rise and lift his finger . 

 ' Adi s , Señor ! ' say Cipriano , click his spur , and put his hand on his sword as he turn to the door . 

 ' Adi s , Señor General , ' say the Bishop , dart after they his eye of old malice , which they could feel in their back . 

 ' he will say nothing , ' say Cipriano , as he and Ram n go down the step . ' the old jesuit , he only want to keep his job and his power , and prevent the heart 's beating . I know they . all they treasure , even more than their money , be their centipede power over the frightened people ; especially over the woman . ' 

 ' I do not   know you hat they , ' laugh Ram n. 

 ' waste no more breath on they , my dear one , ' say Cipriano . ' go forward , you can walk over break snake such as those . ' 

 as they go on foot past the post - office square , where the modern scribe at little table under the arch sit tap out letter on their typewriter for the poor and illiterate , who wait with their few centavos to have their message turn into florid Castilian , Ram n and Cipriano meet with an almost startled respect . 

 ' why talk to the Bishop ? - he do not   exist any more . I hear his Knights of Cortés have a big dinner the other evening , and it be say - I do not   believe it - that they drink oath in blood to have my life and your . but I think the oath of the Catholic Dames would frighten I more . why , if a man stop to unfasten his trouser to make water , the Knights of Cortés run for their life , think the pistol be point at they . do not   think about they , man ! do not   try to conciliate they . they will only puff up and become insolent , think you be afraid of they . six soldier will trample down all that dirt , ' say the General . 

 it be the city , and the spirit of the city . 

 Cipriano have a suite in the big Palace on the Plaza de Armas . 

 ' if I marry , ' he say , as they pass into the stone patio , where soldier stand at attention , ' I shall take a house in the colony , to be more private . ' 

 Cipriano in town be amusing . he seem to exude pride and arrogant authority as he walk about . but his black eye , glance above his fine nose and that little goat beard , be not to be laugh at . they seem to get everything , in the stab of a glance . a demoniacal little fellow . 

 

 

 CHAPTER xviii 

 Auto da Fe 

 

 Ram n see Carlota and his boy in the city , but it be a rather fruitless meeting . the eld boy be just uncomfortable in the presence of his father , but the young Cyprian , who be delicate and very intelligent , have a rather lofty air of displeasure with his parent . 

 ' do you know what they sing , papa ? ' he say . 

 ' not all the thing they sing , ' say Ram n. 

 ' they sing - ' the boy hesitate . then , in his clear young voice , he pip up , to the tune of La Cucaracha : 

 

 ' Don Ram n do not   drink , do not   smoke . 
 Doña Carlota wish he would . 
 he be go to wear the sky - blue cloak 
 that he be steal from the Mother of God . ' 

 

 ' no , I be not , ' say Ram n , smile . ' mine be get a snake and a bird in the middle , and black zigzag and a red fringe . you would well come and see it . ' 

 ' no , papa ! I do not   want to . ' 

 ' why not ? ' 

 ' I do not   want to be mix up in this affair . it make we all look ridiculous . '

 ' I mean good people do not . decent people . ' 

 ' now you will have to confess again , for call your father indecent . - terrible child ! ' 

 the child flush , and tear rise to his eye . there be silence for a while .
