 ' yes ! ' say the eld boy , slowly . ' I want to come and bathe in the lake , and have a boat . but - they say it be impossible . ' 

 ' why ? ' 

 ' they say you make yourself a peon , in your clothe . ' - the boy be shy . 

 ' they be very nice clothe , you know . Nicer than those little breech of your . ' 

 ' they say , also , that you pretend to be the aztec god Quetzalcoatl . ' 

 ' not at all . I only pretend that the aztec god Quetzalcoatl be come back to the Mexicans . ' 

 ' but , papa , it be not true . ' 

 ' how do you know ? ' 

 ' because it be impossible . ' 

 ' why ? ' 

 ' there never be any Quetzalcoatl , except idol . ' 

 ' be there any Jesus , except image ? ' 

 ' yes , papa . ' 

 ' where ? ' 

 ' in heaven . ' 

 ' then in heaven there be also Quetzalcoatl . and what be in heaven be capable of come back to earth . do not   you believe I ? ' 

 ' I can not . ' 

 ' then go on unbelieve , ' say the father , laugh at they and rise to leave they . 

 ' it be very bad that they sing song about you , and put mama in ; like about Pancho Villa , ' say the young boy . ' it hurt I very much . ' 

 ' rub it with Vapour - rub , my pet , ' say Ram n. ' rub it with Vapour - rub , where it hurt you . ' 

 ' what a real bad man you be , papa ! ' 

 ' what a real good child be you , my son ! be not   that so ? ' 

 ' I do not   know , papa . I only know you be bad . ' 

 ' oh ! oh ! be that all they teach thee at thy american school ? ' 

 ' next term , ' say Ciprianito , ' I want to change my name . I do not   want to be call Carrasco any more . when thou art in the newspaper , they will laugh at we . ' 

 ' oh ! oh ! I be laugh at thee now , little frog ! what name wilt thou choose , then ? Espina , perhaps . Thou know Carrasco be a wild bush , on the moor in Spain , where we come from . wilt thou be the little thorn on the bush ? call thyself Espina , thou art a sprig of the old tree . entonce , adi s ! Señor Espina Espinita ! ' 

 ' Adi s ! ' say the boy abruptly , flush with rage . 

 Ram n take a motor - car to Sayula , for there be a make road . but already the rain be wash it away . the car lurch and bump in the great gap . in one place a cami n lie on its back , where it have overturn . 

 on the flat desert there be already small smear of water , and the pink cosmo flower , and the yellow , be just sprout their tuft of bud . the hill in the distance be go opaque , as leaf come out on the invisible tree and bush . the earth be come to life . 

 Ram n call in Sayula at Kate 's house . she be out , but the wild Concha come scour across the beach , to fetch she . - ' there be Don Ram n ! there be Don Ram n ! ' 

 Kate hurry home , with sand in her shoe . 

 she think Ram n look tired , and , in his black suit , sinister . 

 ' I do not   expect you , ' she say . 

 ' I be on my way back from town . ' 

 he sit very still , with that angry look on his creamy dark face , and he keep push back his black moustache from his closed , angry lip . 

 ' do you see anybody in town ? ' she ask . 

 ' I see Don Cipriano - and Doña Carlota , and my boy ! ' 

 ' oh , how nice for you ! be they quite well ? ' 

 ' in excellent health , I believe . ' 

 she laugh suddenly . 

 ' you be still cross , ' she say . ' be it about the monkey still ? ' 

 ' Señora , ' he say , lean forward , so that his black hair drop a little on his brow , ' in monkeydom I do not   know who be prince . but in the kingdom of fool , I believe it be I. ' 

 ' why ? ' she say . 

 and as he do not answer , she add : 

 ' it must be a comfort to be a prince , even of fool . ' 

 he look dagger at she , then burst into a laugh . 

 ' oh , Señora mía ! what ail we man , when we be always want to be good ? ' 

 ' be you repent of it ? ' she laugh . 

 ' yes ! ' he say . ' I be a prince of fool ! why have I start this Quetzalcoatl business ? why ? pray tell I why . ' 

 ' I suppose you want to . ' 

 he ponder for a time , push up his moustache . 

 ' perhaps it be well to be a monkey than a fool . I object to be call a monkey , nevertheless . Carlota be a monkey , no more ; and my two boy be prize young monkey in sailor suit . and I be a fool . yet what be the difference between a fool and a monkey ? ' 

 ' Quién sabe ? ' say Kate . 

 ' one want to be good , and the other be sure he be good . so I make a fool of myself . they be sure they be always good , so that make monkey of they . oh , if only the world would blow up like a bomb ! ' 

 ' it will not ! ' say Kate . 

 ' true enough . - ah , well ! ' 

 he draw himself erect , pull himself together . 

 ' do you think , Señora Caterina , you might marry our mutual general ? ' Ram n have put himself aside again . 

 ' i - I do not   know ! ' stammer Kate . ' I hardly think so . ' 

 ' he be not sympathetic to you at all ? ' 

 ' yes , he be . he be alive , and there be even a certain fascination about he . - but one should not   try marry a man of another race , do you think , even if he be more sympathetic ? ' 

 ' ah ! ' sigh Ram n. ' it be no good generalizing . it be no good marry anybody , unless there will be a real fusion somewhere . ' 

 ' and I feel there would not , ' say Kate . ' I feel he just want something of I ; and perhaps I just want something of he . but he would never meet I . he would never come forward himself , to meet I . he would come to take something from I and I should have to let he . and I do not   want merely that . I want a man who will come half - way , just half - way , to meet I . ' 

 Don Ram n ponder , and shake his head . 

 ' you be right , ' he say . ' yet , in these matter , one never know what be half - way , nor where it be . a woman who just want to be take , and then to cling on , be a parasite . and a man who want just to take , without give , be a creature of prey . ' 

 ' and I be afraid Don Cipriano might be that , ' say Kate . 

 ' possibly , ' say Ram n. ' he be not so with I . but perhaps he would be , if we do not meet - perhaps it be our half - way - in some physical belief that be at the very middle of we , and which we recognize in one another . do not   you think there might be that between you and he ? ' 

 ' I doubt if he would feel it necessary , with a woman . a woman would not   be important enough . ' 

 Ram n be silent . 

 ' perhaps ! ' he say . ' with a woman , a man always want to let himself go . and it be precisely with a woman that he should never let himself go . it be precisely with a woman that he should never let himself go , but stick to his innermost belief , and meet she just there . because when the innermost belief coincide in they both , if it be physical , there , and then , and nowhere else , they can meet . and it be no good unless there be a meeting . it be no good a man ravish a woman , and it be absolutely no good a woman ravish a man . it be a sin , that be . there be such a thing as sin , and that be the centre of it . man and woman keep on ravish one another . Absurd as it may sound , it be not I who would ravish Carlota . it be she who would ravish I . strange and absurd and a little shameful , it be true . - let oneself go , be either ravish or be ravish . oh , if we could only abide by our own soul , and meet in the abide place . - Señora , I have not a very great respect for myself . woman and I have fail with one another , and it be a bad failure to have in the middle of oneself . ' 

 Kate look at he in wonder , with a little fear . why be he confess to she ? be he go to love she ? she almost suspend her breathing . he look at she with a sort of sorrow on his brow , and in his dark eye , anger , vexation , wisdom , and a dull pain . 

 ' I be sorry , ' he go on , ' that Carlota and I be as we be with one another . who be I , even to talk about Quetzalcoatl , when my heart be hollow with anger against the woman I have marry and the child she bear I ? - we never meet in our soul , she and I. at first I love she , and she want I to ravish she . then after a while a man become uneasy . he can not   keep on want to ravish a woman , the same woman . he have revulsion . then she love I , and she want to ravish I . and I like it for a time . but she have revulsion too . the eld boy be really my boy , when I ravish she . and the young be her boy , when she ravish I . see how miserable it be ! and now we can never meet ; she turn to she crucify Jesus , and I to my uncrucified and uncrucifiable Quetzalcoatl , who at least can not be ravish . ' 

 ' and I be sure you will not   make he a ravisher , ' she say . 

 ' who know ? if I err , it will be on that side . but you know , Señora , Quetzalcoatl be to I only the symbol of the good a man may be , in the next day . the universe be a nest of dragon , with a perfectly unfathomable life - mystery at the centre of it . if I call the mystery the Morning Star , surely it do not   matter ! a man 's blood can not   beat in the abstract . and man be a creature who win his own creation inch by inch from the nest of the cosmic dragon . or else he lose it little by little , and go to piece . now we be all lose it , in the ravishing and ravish disintegration . we must pull ourselves together , hard , both man and woman , or we be all lose . - we must pull ourselves together , hard . ' 

 ' but be you a man who need a woman in his life ? ' she say . 

 ' I be a man who yearn for the sensual fulfilment of my soul , Señora , ' he say . ' I be a man who have no belief in abnegation of the blood desire . I be a man who be always on the verge of take wife and concubine to live with I , so deep be my desire for that fulfilment . except that now I know that be useless - not momentarily useless , but in the long run - my ravish a woman with hot desire . no matter how much she be in love with I and desire I to ravish she . it be no good , and the very inside of I know it be no good . wine , woman , and song - all that - all that game be up . our inside will not   really have it any more . yet it be hard to pull ourselves together . ' 

 ' so that you really want a woman to be with you ? ' say Kate . 

 ' ah , Señora ! if I could trust myself ; and trust she ! I be no long a young man , who can afford to make mistake . I be forty - two year old , and I be make my last - and perhaps in truth , my first great effort as a man . I hope I may perish before I make a big mistake . ' 

 ' why should you make a mistake ? you need not ? ' 

 ' I ? it be very easy for I to make a mistake . very easy , on the one hand , for I to become arrogant and a ravisher . and very easy , on the other hand , for I to deny myself , and make a sort of sacrifice of my life . which be be ravish . easy to let myself , in a certain sense , be ravish . I do it to a small degree even yesterday , with the Bishop of Guadalajara . and it be bad . if I have to end my life in a mistake , Señora , I have rather end it in be a ravisher , than in be ravish . as a hot ravisher , I can still slash and cut at the disease of the other thing , the horrible pandering and the desire man have to be ravish , the hateful , ignoble desire they have . ' 

 ' but why do not   you do as you say , stick by the innermost soul that be in you , and meet a woman there , meet she , as you say , where your two soul coincide in their deep desire ? not always that horrible unbalance that you call ravish . ' 

 ' why do not   I ? but which woman can I meet in the body , without that slow degradation of ravish , or be ravish , set in ? if I marry a spanish woman or a dark Mexican , she will give herself up to I to be ravish . if I marry a woman of the anglo - Saxon or any blonde northern stock , she will want to ravish I , with the will of all the ancient white demon . those that want to be ravish be parasite on the soul , and one have revulsion . those that want to ravish a man be vampire . and between the two , there be nothing . ' 

 ' surely there be some really good woman ? ' 

 ' well , show I they . they be all potential Carlotas or - or - yes , Caterinas . I be sure you ravish your Joachim till he die . no doubt he want it ; even more than you want it . it be not just sex . it lie in the will . victim and victimizer . the upper class , crave to be victim to the low class ; or else craving to make victim of the low class . the politician , crave to make one people victim to another . the Church , with its evil will for turn the people into humble , writhe thing that shall crave to be victimize , to be ravish - I tell you , the earth be a place of shame . ' 

 ' but if you want to be different , ' say Kate , ' surely a few other people do - really . ' 

 ' it may be , ' he say , become calm . ' it may be . I wish I keep myself together well . I must keep myself together , keep myself within the middle place , where I be still . my Morning Star . now I be ashamed of have talk like this to you , Señora Caterina . ' 

 ' why ? ' she cry . and for the first time , the flush of hurt and humiliation come into her face . 

 he see it at once , and put his hand on hers for a moment . 

 ' no , ' he say . ' I be not ashamed . I be relieve . ' 

 she flush deeply at his touch , and be silent . he rise hastily , to leave , crave to be alone again with his own soul . 

 ' on Sunday , ' he say , ' will you come into the plaza , in the morning , when the drum sound ? will you come ? ' 

 ' what for ? ' she say . 

 ' well ! come , and you will see . ' 

 he be go in a flash . 

 there be many soldier in the village . when she go to the post - office , she see the man in their cotton uniform lie about in the entrance to the military station . there must have be fifty or more , little man , not the tall soldier in slouch hat . these be little , quick , compact man , like Cipriano , and they talk in a strange indian language , very subdued . they be very rarely see in the street . they keep out of sight . 

 but at night everyone be request to be indoor by ten o'clock , and through the darkness Kate hear the patrol of horse - soldier rid round . 

 there be an air of excitement and mystery in the place . the parish priest , a rather overbearing , fat man of fifty or so , have preach a famous Saturday evening sermon against Ram n and Quetzalcoatl , forbid the heathen name to be mention , threaten with all the penalty any parishioner who read the Hymns , or even listen . 

 so , of course , he be attack when he leave the church , and have to be rescue by soldier who be in the doorway . they march he safely home . but his criada , the old woman who serve he , be tell by more woman than one that the next time the padre open his mouth against Quetzalcoatl , he would have a few inch of machete in his fat gut . 

 so his reverence stay at home , and a curate officiate . 

 practically all the people who come over the lake in boat on Saturdays go to mass in Sayula church . the great door stand open all the day . man as they pass to and fro to the lake , take off their big hat , with a curious cringing gesture , as they go by the gateway of the church . all day long , scatter people be kneel in the aisle or among the bench , the man kneel erect , their big hat down by their knee , their curious tall - shaped indian head with the thick black hair also erect ; only the kneeling leg , close together , humble . the woman hood themselves in their dark rebozos and spread their elbow as they kneel at a bench , in a slack sort of voluptuousness . 

 on Saturday night , a great ruddy flickering of many candle - point , away down the dark cavern of the church ; and a clustering of dark man 's head , a shuffling of woman , a come and go of man arrive from the lake , of man depart to the market . a hush , not exactly of worship , but of a certain voluptuous admiration of the loftiness and glitter , a sensual , almost victimize self - abandon to the god of death , the Crucified streak with blood , or to the pretty white woman in a blue mantle , with her little doll 's face under her crown , Mary , the doll of doll , Niña of Niñas . 

 it be not worship . it be a sort of numbness and let the soul sink uncontrolle . and it be a luxury , after all the week of unwashed dullness in their squalid village of straw hut . but it irritate Kate . 

 the man get up and tiptoe away in their sandal , cross themselves front and back , on the navel and on the back of the head , with holy water . and their black eye shine with a loose , sensuous look . instead of have gather themselves together and become graver , strong , more collected and deep in their own integrity , they emerge only the more loose and sloppy and uncontrolle . 

 oh , if there be one thing man need to learn , but the Mexican Indians especially , it be to collect each man his own soul together deep inside he , and to abide by it . the Church , instead of help man to this , push they more and more into a soft , emotional helplessness , with the unpleasant sensuous gratification of feel themselves victim , victimize , victimize , but at the same time with the lurk sardonic consciousness that in the end a victim be strong than the victimizer . in the end , the victim pull down their victimizer , like a pack of hyena on an unwary lion . they know it . Cursed be the falsely meek , for they be inherit the earth . 

 on Sunday morning there be early mass at sunrise , another mass at seven o'clock , another at nine , another at eleven . then there be a little band of violin and ' cellos , play old - fashioned dance music ; there be , especially early in the morning , a solid mass of peon and woman , kneel on the floor ; and a flapping of dusky candle , a smell of the exhaust air of candle , a heavy , rolling fume of incense , and the heavy choir of man 's voice , solid , powerful , impressive , from the gallery . 

 and the people go away in sensuous looseness , which soon turn , in the market , to hate , the old , unfathomable hate which lie at the bottom of the indian heart , and which always rise black and turbid when they have sway awhile in sensuous gratification . 

 the church inside be a dead interior , like all mexican church , even the gorgeous Puebla cathedral . the interior of almost any mexican church give the impression of cynical barrenness , cynical meaninglessness , an empty , cynical , mock shell . the italian church be build much in the same style , and yet in they linger a shadow and stillness of old , mysterious holiness . the hush . 

 but not in Mexico . the church outside be impressive . inside , and it be curious to define it , they be blatant ; void of sound and yet with no hush , simple , and yet completely vulgar , barren , sterile . more barren than a bank or a schoolroom or an empty concert - hall , less mysterious than any of these . you get a sense of plaster , of mortar , of whitewash , of smeared blue - wash or grey - wash ; and of gilt lay on and ready to peel off . even in the most gorgeous church , the gilt be hatefully gild , never golden . nothing be soft nor mellow . 

 so the interior of Sayula church ; and Kate have often be in . the white exterior be charming , and so valuable in the landscape , with the twin white pagoda - tower peer out of the green willow - tree . but inside , it seem nothing but whitewash , stencil over with grey scroll - work decoration . the window be high , and many , let in the light as into a schoolroom . Jesus , streak with blood , be in one of the transept , and the Virgin , a doll in faded satin , stand startle inside a glass case . there be rag flower and paper flower , coarse lace and silver that look like tin . 

 nevertheless , it be quite clean , and very much frequent . 

 the Month of Mary have go by , the blue and white paper ribbon be all take down , the palm - tree in pot be all remove from the aisle , the little girl in white dress and little crown of flower no long come with posy in their hand , at evening . curious , the old gentle ceremonial of Europe , how trashy they seem in Mexico , just a cheap sort of charade . 

 the day of Corpus Christi come , with high mass and the church full to the door with kneeling peon , from dawn till noon . then a feeble little procession of child within the church , because the law forbid religious procession outside . but all , somehow , for nothing . just so that the people could call it a fiesta , and so have an excuse to be more slack , more sloshy and uncontrolle than ever . the one mexican desire ; to let themselves go in sloppy inertia . 

 and this be the all - in - all of the religion . instead of do as it should , collect the soul into its own strength and integrity , the religious day leave it all the more decomposed and degenerate . 

 however , the week pass , the crowd in the church seem the same as ever . but the crowd in the church one hour be the crowd of Quetzalcoatl the next hour . just a sensation . 

 till the more socialistic Readers mingle a little anti - clerical bitterness in their reading . and all the peon begin to say : be El Señor a gringo , and the Santísima , be she nothing but a gringuita ? 

 this provoke retaliation on the part of the priest , first mere admonition , then at last the loud denunciation and threat of that sermon . which mean war . 

 everybody wait for Saturday . Saturday come , and the church remain shut . Saturday night , the church be dark and closed . Sunday , the church be silent and the door blank fasten . 

 something like consternation spread through the market host . they have nowhere to go ! - but among the consternation be a pique curiosity . perhaps something exciting be go to happen . 

 thing have happen before . in the revolution , many of the church in Mexico have be use for stable and for barrack . and church be turn into school , and concert hall , and cinematograph theatre . the convent and the monastery be most of they barrack for the rag - tag - and - bobtail soldier . the world change , be bind to change . 

 the second Saturday of the closed church be , as it happen , a big market . much fruit and stuff have come up the lake , from the south from far distance , even from Colima . there be man with lacquer wooden bowl , and woman with glaze pottery . and as usual , man crouch in guard over twenty centavos worth of nauseous tropical plum , or chile , or mango , in tiny pyramid along the roadway . 

 a crowded market , with the much and the little of the Indians . and the church door shut and lock , the church bell silent , even the clock stop . true , the clock be always stop . but not with such a final arrest . 

 no mass , no confession , no little orgy of incense and slack emotion ! the low rumble of murmur tone , the quick , apprehensive glance around . vendor by the causeway squat tight , as if to make themselves dense and small , squat down on their haunch with their knee up to their shoulder , like the aztec idol . and soldier in two and three sprinkle everywhere . and señora and Señoritas , in their black gauze scarf or mantilla , trip to the church for mass and shrill round the gateway of the church , all a bubble and a froth of chatter ; though they have know quite well the church be shut . 

 but it be Sunday morning , and something be due to happen . 

 at about half - past ten , a boat appear , and man in snow - white clothe get out , one carry a drum . they march quickly through the people , under the old tree on the sand , across to the church . they pass through the break iron gate into the stone courtyard in front of the church . 

 at the church door , which be still shut , they take off their blouse , and stand in a ring , with dark naked shoulder and the blue - and - black sash of Quetzalcoatl round their waist . 

 the drum begin to beat , with a powerful , pound note , as the man stand bare - headed and bare - breasted in a circle outside the church door ; a strange ring of lustrous , bluey - black head and dark shoulder , above the snowy - white pantaloon . monotonously the drum beat , on and on . then the little clay flute with the husky sound wheeze a clear melody . 

 the whole market press densely towards the gateway of the church . but there , soldier stand guard . and on the inside of the stone yard in front of the church , soldier quietly guard the low wall , let nobody mount . so that outside , under the old willow- and pepper - tree , in the hot morning sun , the dense crowd stand gaze at the church door . they be mostly man in big hat ; but some townsman be there , and some woman , and Kate with a parasol line with dark blue . a close , silent , tense throng under the spangled shade , press round the trunk of the palm - tree , climb on the root of the pepper - tree . and behind be the camione and the motorcar draw up . 

 the drum shudder and go still , and the earthen flute be silent . the lake could be hear lapping , and a clink of glass and a sound of chauffeur ' voice at the little cantina - booth . for the rest , the silent breathing of the crowd . - soldier be quickly distribute a few leaflet among the crowd . a strong , far - carry male voice begin to sing to the softened thud of the drum . 

 

 JESUS ' FAREWELL 

 Farewell , Farewell , Despedida ! 
 the last of my day be go . 
 to - morrow Jesus and Holy Mary 
 will be bone . 

 it be a long , long way 
 from Mexico to the Pool of Heaven . 
 look back the last time , Mary Mother , 
 let we call the eleven . 

 James , and John , and Mark , 
 Felipe and San Cristobal , 
 all my saint , and Anna , Teresa , 
 Guadalupe whose face be oval . 

 come then , now , it be finish for all of we . 
 let we all be go . 
 follow I now up the ladder of spark . 
 every one . 

 Joaquin , Francis , and Anthony 
 and many - name Maria , 
 Purísima , Refugio , and Soledad 
 Follow here . 

 Ho ! all my saint and my Virgins 
 troop out of your shrine , 
 after your master , the Crucified ; 
 bring all your sign . 

 run up the flame , and with foot on the spark 
 troop into the sky . 
 once more follow the Master , 
 back again now , on high . 

 Farewell , let all be forget 
 in Mexico . 
 to the pool of peace and forget in heaven 
 we go . 

 

 while this be sing , another boat have arrive , and soldier make way through the crowd for Ram n , in his white serape with the blue edge and scarlet fringe , and a young priest of the church in a black cassock , and six man in dark serape with the blue border of Quetzalcoatl . this strange procession march through the crowd and through the gateway of the yard . 

 as they approach , the ring of man round the drum open , and spread into a crescent . Ram n stand tall behind the drum , the six man in dark serape divide and go to the wing of the crescent , the young , slim priest in a black cassock stand alone , in front of the crescent , face the crowd . 

 he lift his hand ; Ram n take off his hat ; all the man in the crowd take off their hat . 

 the priest turn , meet Ram n at the centre of the crescent , and , across the drum , hand he the key of the church . then the priest wait . 

 Ram n unlock the church door and fling they open . the man in front of the crowd kneel down suddenly , see the church dark like a cavern , but a trembling blaze of many candle , away , seemingly far down the mysterious darkness , shudder with dark , ripple flame , like the Presence of the burn bush . 

 the crowd sway and rustle , and subside , kneeling . only here and there a labourer , a chauffeur or a railway man stand erect . 

 the priest raise his hand a little high , re - turn towards the people . 

 ' my child , ' he say ; and as he speak the lake seem to rustle ; ' God the Almighty have call home his Son , and the Holy Mother of the Son . their day be over in Mexico . they go back to the Father . 

 

 Jesus , the Son of God , bid you farewell . 
 Mary , the Mother of God , bid you farewell . 
 for the last time they bless you , as they leave you . 
 Answer Adi s ! 
 say Adi s ! my child . ' 

 

 the man in the circle say a deep Adi s ! and from the soldier , and from the kneeling crowd , a ragged , muttered , strange repeating of Adi s ! again and again , like a sort of storm . 

 suddenly , in a blast , down the darkness of the church into which the kneeling people be star , the burn bush of candle be go , there be only darkness . across the sunshine , light here and there by a frail light of a taper , be a cave of darkness . 

 man in the crowd exclaim and groan . 

 then the drum softly touch , and two man in the crescent begin to sing , in magnificent , terrible voice , the Farewell Hymn again . they be man whom Ram n , or his follower , have find in low drinking - dens in Mexico City , man with train and amazing voice , the powerful mexican tenor that seem to tear the earth open . man whom the ' time ' have reduce to sing in low city dive . and now they sing with all the terrible desperation that be in they , the hopeless , demonish recklessness . 

 when they finish , the priest again lift his hand , and give the benediction ; add in a quiet voice : 

 ' and now , with all the saint , let I go , saith Jesus . for I go back to my Father which be in heaven , and I lead my Mother in my right hand , home to peace . ' 

 he turn and go into the church . Ram n follow . then slowly , all the man of the crescent . Overhead the church bell ring a little while , on the deathly silence . it cease . 

 and in a moment , from the depth of the church sound a drum , with a remote , fearsome thud , and a slow monotony . 

 the priest , in his white vestment with rich lace , appear in the doorway of the church , bear a tall crucifix . he hesitate , then come into the sun . the kneeling people clasp their hand . 

 candle in the dark church be cluster towards the door , lonely flame . Don Ram n come out of the dark , naked to the waist , his serape over one shoulder , bear the front pole of the great bi whereon lie , within a glass case , the lifelike , terrible dead Christ of Holy Week . a tall , dark man , naked to the waist , hold the other end of the pole on his shoulder . the crowd moan and cross themselves . the lifelike Dead Christ seem really dead , as he pass the gate . as he enter the crowd , kneel man and woman lift sightless face and fling their arm wide apart , and so remain , arm rigid and outflung , in an unspeakable ecstasy of fear , supplication , acknowledgement of death . 

 after the bi of the Dead Christ , a slow procession of man naked to the waist , carry litter after litter . first the terrible scourged Christ , with naked body strip like a tiger with blood . then the image of the Saviour of the Sacred Heart , the well - know figure from the side altar , with long hair and outstretche hand . then the image of Jesus of Nazareth , with a crown of thorn . 

 then the Virgin with the blue mantle and lace , and the golden crown . the woman begin to moan as she emerge rather trashily into the blaze sunlight . behind she , in the church , the candle be one by one go out . 

 then come brown Saint Anthony of Padua , with a child in his arm . then Saint Francis , look strangely at a cross in his hand . then Saint Anna . and last , Saint Joaquin . and as he emerge , the last candle in the dark church go out , there be only open door upon a darkness . 

 the image on the shoulder of the brown - skin man ride rather childishly out through the blaze sun , into the shadow of tree . the drum follow last , slowly thud . on the glass case of the big Dead Christ the sun flash with startling flash , as the powerful man carry it turn towards the water . the crowd murmur and sway on its knee . woman cry : Purísima ! Purísima ! do not   leave we ! and some man ejaculate in strangle anguish , over and over again : Señor ! Señor ! Señor ! 

 but the strange procession make its way slowly under the tree , to the coarse sand , and descend again into the great light towards the lake . there be a little breeze under a blaze of sun . fold serape on naked , soft shoulder swing unevenly , the image rock and totter a little . but onwards to the edge of the water go the tall crucifix , then the flash glass box . and after , come Jesus in a red silk robe , flutter , then a wooden Jesus all paint and streak , then Jesus in white with a purple mantle that blow like a kerchief , Mary in lace that flutter upon stiff white and blue satin . but the Saints be only paint ; paint wood . 

 the slim , lace - smock priest stagger down the sand under the heavy crucifix , which have a white Christ Crucified stretch aloft , face the lake . by the little wall be a large black canoa , sailing boat , with a broad plank gangway up to her stern . two bare - legged , white - clothe man walk by the slim priest , whose white sleeve blow like flag as he slowly climb the gangway to the ship . man help he on board , and he walk away to the prow , where at length he stand the big crucifix , with the Christ still face outward . 

 the ship be open , without deck or hatch , but with fix table for the image . slowly Ram n ascend and descend into the boat , the great glass case be lay down on its rest , the two man could wipe their wet brow and their hot , black hair . Ram n put on his blanket and his hat , against the sun . the boat heave very slightly . the wind be from the west . the lake be pale and unreal , sun - blinded . 

 one after another the image rise over the stern of the boat , against the sky , then descend into the vessel , to be set down on their rest , where they rise above the black side of the canoa , in view of the throng on the shore . 

 it be a strange and tawdry collection of image . and yet , each image have a certain pathos of its own , and a certain touch of horror , as they be group together for their last ride , upon the trestle - support , within the vessel . by each image stand the bearer , in hat and serape , keep a steady hand on the pole . 

 there be a little line of soldier on the shore , and three motor - boat with soldier wait by the big canoa . the shore be cover with a mass of people . many row - boat come row inquisitively round , like fish . but none come too near . 

 Bare - legged sailor begin to pole the ship from the shore . they lean heavily on the pole , and walk along the rim of the vessel . slowly she begin to move upon the water , in the shallow . slowly she be leave the shore , and the throng . 

 two other sailor swiftly begin to hoist the huge , square white sail . quickly , yet heavily it rise in the air , and take the wind . it have the great sign of Quetzalcoatl , the circle blue snake and the blue eagle upon a yellow field , at the centre , like a great eye . 

 the wind come from the west , but the boat be steer south - east , for the little Island of the Scorpions , which rise like a small dim hummock from the haze of the lake . so the sail reach out , and the great eye seem to be glance back , at the village with the green willow and the empty white church , the throng on the shore . 

 Motor - boat circle the huge , slow canoe , small boat like insect follow and range round at a distance , never come too close . the run water cluck and speak , the man by the image steady the pole with one hand , their hat with the other , the great eye on the sail ever look back at the land , the sweep of the white canvas sweep low above the glass case of death , the Christ cake with gore , the image in their flutter mantle . 

 on the shore , the people wander away , or sit on the sand wait and watch in a sort of dumb patience that be half indifference . the canoe grow small , more inconspicuous , lapse into the light , the little boat circle around it like mere dot . the lake tire the eye with its light . 

 away under the tree , in a half silence , a half vacancy , a woman buy a dark water - melon , smash it open on a stone , and give the big pinky fragment to her child . in silence , man sprinkle salt on the thick slice of cucumber sell by the woman under the tree . in silence they wander into the church , past the soldier on guard at the door . 

 the church be absolutely dark , save for the light that enter the doorway , and absolutely bare ; wall , floor , altar , transept , all stark bare and empty . the people wander away again , in silence . 

 it be noon , and a hot day . the canoa slowly range to the small hummock of the island amid the water , where live one family of Indians - fisher , with a few goat and one dry little place where they grow a few bean and head of maize . for the rest , the island be all dry rock and thorny bush , and scorpion . 

 the vessel be pole round to the one rocky bay . slowly she draw near the island . the motor - boat and the little boat hurry ahead . already brown , naked man be bath among the rock . 

 the great sail sank , the canoa edge up to the rocky shore , man spring from she into the water , the image be lower and slowly carry on to the rock . there they wait for the bearer . 

 slowly the procession go again up the bank of the dishevel island , past the couple of hut , where a red cock be crow among the litter , and over to rock , beyond the bush , on the far side . 

 the side face Sayula be all rock , naked and painful to tread on . in a rocky hollow at the water 's edge , tall stone have be put up on end , with iron bar across the top , like a grill . underneath , a pile of faggot ready ; and at the side , a pile of faggot . 

 the image , the glass box of the great Dead Christ , be lay on the iron bar of the grill , in a pathetic cluster all together . the crucifix be lean against they . it be noon , the heat and the light be fierce and erect . but already down the lake cloud be push up fantastically . 

 beyond the water , beyond the glare , the village look like a mirage , with its tree and village and white church tower . 

 man who have come in boat crowd on the rock of the little amphitheatre . in silence , Ram n kindle shred of cane and ocote , with a burning - glass . little hasty flame like young snake arise in the solid sunlight , with vapour of smoke . he set fire to the carefully - arrange pyramid of faggot beneath the grill - table of the image . 

 there be a crackling , and a puffing of whitish smoke , the sweet scent of ocote , and orange - red tongue of half - substantial flame be leap up in the hot white air . hot breath blow suddenly , sudden flame gush up , and the ocote , full of sweet resin , begin to roar . the glass of the great box emit strange , painful yelp as it splinter and fall tinkle . between the iron bar , brownish flame push up among the image , which at once go black . the little vestment of silk and satin wither in a moment to blackness , the cake wound of paint bubble black . 

 the young priest take off his linen vestment , his stole , and his chasuble , and with flushed face fling they in the flame . then he strip off his black cassock , and emerge in the white cotton of the man of Quetzalcoatl , his white drawer roll up to the knee . he throw his cassock in the fire . someone hand he a big hat , and a white serape with blue end . 

 there be a smell of burn paint , and wool , and ocote . the fire rush in a dusky mass upon the blacken , flickering image , till nothing be to be see but a confused bush of smoke and brown - red flame , puthering , reeking , roar . the flaming crucifix slip aside , and fall . a man seize it and push it into the fire , under the image . man in a sort of ecstasy throw on more of the heavy , resinous wood , that almost explode into flame . rock crack and explode like gun . everybody draw back from that roaring tree of flame , which rise ever higher and high , its dark smoke and its spark unfold into heaven . 

 one of the support stone burst with a bang , bar of iron and blazing stump of image tumble in a confused roar . the glass case have disappear , but ribbon of iron wave , then curl over red , into the torrent of the sudden fire . strange rod of iron appear out of nowhere , protrude from solid red coal . 

 and soon , all that be leave be a fierce glow of red coal of wood , with a medley of half - fuse iron . 

 Ram n stand aside and watch in silence , his dark brow quite expressionless . 

 then , when only the last bluish flame flicker out of a tumble of red fire , from the eminence above rocket begin to shoot into the air with a swish , explode high in the sightless hot blue , with a glimmer of bluish shower , and of gold . 

 the people from the shore have see the tree of smoke with its trunk of flame . now they hear the heavy firing of the rocket , they look again , exclaim , half in dismay , half in the joyful lust of destruction : 

 ' Señor ! Señor ! La Purísima ! La Santísima ! ' 

 the flame and the smoke and the rocket melt as if by miracle , into nothingness , leave the hot air unblemishe . the coal of fire be shovel and drop down a steep hole . 

 as the canoa sail back , the side of the lake , through filmy air , look brownish and changeless . a cloud be rise in the south - west , from behind the dry , silent mountain , like a vast white tail , like the vast white fleecy tail of some squirrel , that have just dive out of sight behind the mountain . this wild white tail fleece up and up , to the zenith , straight at the sun . and as the canoa spread her sail to tack back , already a delicate film of shadow be over the chalk - white lake . 

 only on the low end of the isle of Scorpions , hot air still quiver . 

 Ram n return in one of the motor - boat . slowly the sky be cloud for the thunder and the rain . the canoa , unable to make her way across , be sail for Tuliapan . the little boat hurry in silence . 

 they land before the wind rise . Ram n go and lock the door of the church . 

 the crowd scatter in the wind , rebozos wave wildly , leaf tear , dust racing . Sayula be empty of God , and , at heart , they be glad . 

 

 

 CHAPTER XIX 

 the Attack on Jamiltepec 

 

 suddenly , nearly all the soldier disappear from the village , there be a ' rebellion ' in Colima . a train have be hold up , people kill . and somebody , Generals Fulano and Tulano , have ' pronounce ' against the government . 

 stir in the air , everybody enjoy those periodical shiver of fear ! but for these shiver , everything much the same as usual . the church remain shut up , and dumb . the clock do not   go . Time suddenly fall off , the day walk naked and timeless , in the old , uncounted manner of the past . the strange , old , uncounted , unregistered , unreckone day of the ancient heathen world . 

 Kate feel a bit like a mermaid try to swim in a wrong element . she be sweep away in some silent tide , to the old , antediluvian silence , where thing move without contact . she move and exist without contact . even the striking of the hour have cease . as a drown person see nothing but the water , so Kate see nothing but the face of the timeless water . 

 so , of course , she clutch at her straw . she could not   bear it . she order an old , rickety Ford car , to take her bumping out to Jamiltepec , over the ruinous road in the afternoon . 

 the country have go strange and void , as it do when these ' rebellion ' start . as if the life - spirit be suck away , and only some empty , anti - life void remain in the wicked hollow countryside . though it be not far to Jamiltepec , once outside the village , the chauffeur and his little attendant lad begin to get frightened , and to go frog - like with fear . 

 there be something truly mysterious about the mexican quality of fear . as if man and woman collapse and lie wriggle on the ground like broken reptile , unable to rise . Kate use all her will , against this cringing nonsense . 

 they arrive without ado at Jamiltepec . the place seem quiet , but normal . an oxen wagon stand empty in the courtyard . there be no soldier on guard . they have all be withdraw , against the rebellion . but several peon be move round , in a desultory fashion . the day be a fiesta , when not much work be do . in the house of the peon , the woman be pat tortilla , and prepare hot chile sauce , grind away on the metate . a fiesta ! only the windmill that pump up water from the lake be spin quickly , with a little noise . 

 Kate drive into the yard in silence , and two mozo with gun and belt of cartridge come to talk in low tone to the chauffeur . 

 ' be Doña Carlota here ? ' ask Kate . 

 ' no , Señora . the patrona be not here . ' 

 ' Don Ram n ? ' 

 ' Sí , Señora ! Está . ' 

 even as she hesitate , rather nervous , Ram n come out of the inner doorway of the courtyard , in his dazzle white clothe . 

 ' I come to see you , ' say Kate . ' I do not   know if you would rather I have not . but I can go back in the motor - car . ' 

 ' no , ' he say . ' I be glad . I be feel deserted , I do not   know why . let we go upstairs . ' 

 ' Patr n ! ' say the chauffeur , in a low voice . ' must I stay ? ' 

 Ram n say a few word to he . the chauffeur be uneasy , and do not   want to stay . he say he have to be back in Sayula at such and such a time . excuse , anyhow . but it be evident he want to get away . 

 ' then well let he go , ' say Ram n to Kate . ' you do not mind go home in the boat ? ' 

 ' I do not   want to give you trouble . ' 

 ' it be least trouble to let this fellow go , and you can leave by boat just whenever you wish to . so we shall all be more free . ' 

 Kate pay the chauffeur , and the Ford start rattle . after rattle a while , it move in a curve round the courtyard , and lurch through the zaguán , disappear as fast as possible . 

 Ram n speak to his two mozo with the gun . they go to the outer doorway , obediently . 

 ' why do you have to have armed man ? ' she say . 

 ' oh , they be afraid of bandit , ' he say . ' whenever there be a rebellion anywhere , everybody be afraid of bandit . so of course that call bandit into life . ' 

 ' but where do they come from ? ' say Kate , as they pass into the inner doorway . 

 ' from the village , ' he say , close the heavy door of that entrance behind he , and put the heavy iron bar across , from wall to wall . 

 the inner archway be now a little prison , for the strong iron gate at the lake end of the passage be shut fast . she look through , at the little round pond . it have some blue water - lily on it . beyond , the pallid lake seem almost like a ghost , in the glare of the sun . 

 a servant be send to the kitchen quarter , Ram n and Kate climb the stone stair to the upper terrace . how lonely , stonily lonesome and forlorn the hacienda could feel ! the very stone wall could give off emptiness , loneliness , negation . 

 ' but which village do the bandit come from ? ' she insist . 

 ' any of they . mostly , they say , from San Pablo or from Ahuajijic . ' 

 ' quite near ! ' she cry . 

 ' or from Sayula , ' he add . ' any of the ordinary man in big hat you see around the plaza may possibly be bandit , when banditry pay , as a profession , and be not   punish with any particular severity . ' 

 ' it be hard to believe ! ' she say . 

 ' it be so obvious ! ' he say , drop into one of the rock - chair opposite she , and smile across the onyx table . 

 ' I suppose it be ! ' she say . 

 he clap his hand , and his mozo Martin come up . Ram n order something , in a low , subdued tone . the man reply in an even low , more subdue tone . then the master and man nod at one another , and the man depart , his huarache swish a little on the terrace . 

 Ram n have fall into the low , crush sort of voice so common in the country , as if everyone be afraid to speak aloud , so they murmur guardedly . this be unusual , and Kate notice it in he with displeasure . she sit look past the thick mango - trees , whose fruit be change colour like something gradually grow hot , to the ruffled , pale - brown lake . the mountain of the opposite shore be very dark . above they lie a heavy , but distant black cloud , out of which lightning flap suddenly and uneasily . 

 ' where be Don Cipriano ? ' she ask . 

 ' Don Cipriano be very much General Viedma at the moment , ' he reply . ' chase rebel in the State of Colima . ' 

 ' will they be very hard to chase ? ' 

 ' probably not . anyhow Cipriano will enjoy chase they . he be Zapotee , and most of his man be Zapotecans , from the hill . they love chase man who be not . ' 

 ' I wonder why he be not   there on Sunday when you carry away the image , ' she say . ' I think it be an awfully brave thing to do . ' 

 ' do you ? ' he laugh . ' it be not . it be never half so brave to carry something off , and destroy it , as to set a new pulse beating . ' 

 ' but you have to destroy those old thing , first . ' 

 ' those frowsty image - why , yes . but it be no good until you have   get something else move , from the inside . ' 

 ' and have you ? ' 

 ' I think I have . do not   you ? ' 

 ' yes , ' she say , a little doubtful . 

 ' I think I have , ' he say . ' I feel there be a new thing move inside I . ' he be laugh at she , for her hesitation . ' why do not   you come and join we ? ' he add . 

 ' how ? ' she say . ' by be marry off to Don Cipriano ? ' 

 ' not necessarily . not necessarily . not necessarily by be marry to anybody . ' 

 ' what be you go to do next ? ' she say . 

 ' I ? I be go to re - open the church , for Quetzalcoatl to come in . but I do not   like lonely god . there should be several of they , I think , for they to be happy together . ' 

 ' do one need god ? ' she say . 

 ' why yes . one need manifestation , it seem to I . ' 

 Kate sit in unwilling silence . 

 ' one need goddesse too . that be also a dilemma , ' he add , with a laugh . 

 ' how I would hate , ' say Kate , ' to have to be a goddess for people . ' 

 ' for the monkey ? ' he say , smile . 

 ' yes ! of course . ' 

 at that moment , he sit erect , listen . there have be a shot , which Kate have hear , but which she have hardly notice ; to her ear , it might have be a motor - car back - firing , or even a motor - boat . 

 suddenly , a sharp little volley of shot . 

 Ram n rise swiftly , swift as a great cat , and slam to the iron door at the top of the stairway , shoot the bar . 

 ' will not   you go into that room ? ' he say to she , point to a dark doorway . ' you will be all right there . just stay a few minute till I come back . ' 

 as he speak , there come a shriek from the courtyard at the back , and a man 's death - voice yell Patr n ! 

 Ram n 's eye dilate with terrible anger , the anger of death . his face go pale and strange , as he look at she without see she , the black flame fill his eye . he have draw a long - barrel steel revolver from his hip . 

 still without see she , he stride rapidly , soft and catlike , along the terrace , and leap up the end staircase on to the roof . the soft , eternal passion of anger in his limb . 

 Kate stand in the doorway of the room , transfix . the light of day seem to have darken before her face . 

 ' Holá ! you there ! ' she hear his voice from the roof , in such anger it be almost a laugh , from far away . 

 for answer , a confused noise from the courtyard , and several shot . the slow , steady answer of shot ! 

 she start as a rush hiss break on the air . in terror she wait . then she see it be a rocket burst with a sound like a gun , high over the lake , and emit a shower of red ball of light . a signal from Ram n ! 

 unable to go into the dark room , Kate wait as if smite to death . then something stir deep in she , she fly along the terrace and up the step to the roof . she realize that she do not   mind die so long as she die with that man . not alone . 

 the roof be glare with sunshine . it be flat , but its different level be uneven . she run straight out into the light , towards the parapet wall , and have nearly come in sight of the gateway of the courtyard below , when something give a slight smack , and bit of plaster fly in her face and her hair . she turn and flee back like a bee to the stairway . 

 the stair come up in a corner , where there be a little sort of stone turret , square , with stone seat . she sink on one of these seat , look down in terror at the turn of the stair . it be a narrow little stone stairway , between the solid stone wall . 

 she be almost paralysed with shock and with fear . yet something within she be calm . lean and look out across calm sunshine of the level roof , she could not believe in death . 

 she see the white figure and the dark head of Ram n within one of the small square turret across the roof . the little tower be open , and hardly high than his head . he be stand in a corner , look sideways down a loop - hole , perfectly motionless . Snap ! go his revolver , deliberately . there be a muffled cry below , and a sudden volley of shot . 

 Ram n stand away from the loop - hole and take off his white blouse , so that it should not betray he . above his sash be a belt of cartridge . in the shadow of the turret , his body look curiously dark , rise from the white of his trouser . again he take his stand quietly at the side of the long , narrow , slant aperture . he lift his revolver carefully , and the shot , one , two , three , slow and deliberate , startle her nerve . and again there be a volley of shot from below , and bit of stone and plaster smoking against the sky . then again , silence , long silence . Kate press her hand against her body , as she sit . 

 the cloud have shift , the sun shone yellowish . in the heavy light , the mountain beyond the parapet show a fleece of young green , smoky and beautiful . 

 all be silent . ram n in the shadow do not move , press himself against the wall , and look down . he command , she know , the big inner door . 

 suddenly , however , he shift . with his revolver in his hand he stoop and run , like some terrible cat , the sun gleam on his naked back as he crouch under the shelter of the thick parapet wall , run along the roof to the correspond front turret . 

 this turret be roofless , and it be near to Kate , as she sit spellbound , in a sort of eternity , on the stone seat at the head of the stair , watch Ram n. he press himself against the wall , and lift his revolver to the slit . and again , one , two , three , four , five , the shot explode deliberately . some voice below yell Ay - ee ! ay - ee ! ay - ee ! in yelps of animal pain . a voice be hear shout command . Ram n kneel on one knee , re - load his revolver . then he strike a match , and again Kate almost start out of her skin , as a rocket rush ferociously up into the sky , explode like a gun , and let fall the ball of red flame that linger as if loth to die away , in the high , remote air .

 CHAPTER XX 

 marriage by Quetzalcoatl 

 

 Kate hide in her own house , numb . she could not bear to talk to people . she could not bear even Juana 's bubble discourse . the common thread that bind she to humanity seem to have snap . the little human thing do not   interest she any more . her eye seem to have go dark , and blind to individual . they be all just individual , like leaf in the dark , make a noise . and she be alone under the tree . 

 the egg - woman want six centavos for an egg . 

 ' and I say to she - I say to she - we buy they at five centavos ! ' Juana go on . 

 ' yes ! ' say Kate . she do not   care whether they be buy at five or fifty , or not buy at all . 

 she do not   care , she do not   care , she do not   care . she do not   even care about life any more . there be no escape her own complete indifference . she feel indifferent to everything in the whole world , almost she feel indifferent to death . 

 ' Niña ! Niña ! here be the man with the sandal ! look ! look how nicely he have make they for you , Niña ! look what Mexican huarache the Niña be go to wear ! ' 

 she try they on . the man charge she too much . she look at he with her remote , indifferent eye . but she know , in the world one must live , so she pay he less than he ask , though more than he really would have accept . 

 she sit down again in her rock - chair in the shade of the room . only to be alone ! only that no one should speak to she . only that no one should come near she ! because in reality her soul and spirit be go , depart into the middle of some desert , and the effort of reach across to people to effect an apparent meeting , or contact , be almost more than she could bear . 

 never have she be so alone , and so inert , and so utterly without desire ; plunge in a wan indifference , like death . never have she pass her day so blindly , so unknowingly , in stretch of nothingness . 

 sometimes , to get away from her household , she sit under a tree by the lake . and there , without know it , she let the sun scorch her foot and burn her face inflame . Juana make a great outcry over she . the foot blister and swell , her face be red and painful . but it all seem to happen merely to her shell . and she be wearily , wanly indifferent . 

 only at the very centre of she sometimes a little flame rise , and she know that what she want be for her soul to live . the life of day and fact and happening be dead on she , and she be like a corpse . but away inside she a little light be burn , the light of her innermost soul . sometimes it sink and seem extinct . then it be there again . 

 Ram n have light it . and once it be light the world go hollow and dead , all the world - activity be empty weariness to she . her soul ! her frail , innermost soul ! she want to live its life , not her own life . 

 the time would come again when she would see Ram n and Cipriano , and the soul that be gutter would kindle again in she , and feel strong . meanwhile she only feel weak , weak , weak , weak as the dying . she feel that afternoon of bloodshed have blow all their soul into the twilight of death , for the time . but they would come back . they would come back . nothing to do but to submit , and wait . wait , with a soul almost dead , and hand and heart of uttermost inert heaviness , indifference . 

 Ram n have lose much blood . and she , too , in other way , have be drain of the blood of the body . she feel bloodless and powerless . 

 but wait , wait , wait , the new blood would come . 

 one day Cipriano come . she be rock in her salon , in a cotton housedress , and her face red and rather swollen . she see he , in uniform , pass by the window . he stand in the doorway on the terrace , a dark , grave , small , handsome man . 

 ' do come in , ' she say with effort . 

 her eyelid feel burn . he look at she with his full black eye , that always have in they so many thing she do not understand . she feel she could not look back at he . 

 ' have you chase all your rebel ? ' she say . 

 ' for the present , ' he reply . 

 he seem to be watch , watch for something . 

 ' and you do not   get hurt ? ' 

 ' no , I do not   get hurt . ' 

 she look away out of the door , have nothing to say in the world . 

 ' I go to Jamiltepec yesterday evening , ' he say . 

 ' how be Don Ram n ? ' 

 ' yes , he be well . ' 

 ' quite well ? ' 

 ' no . not quite well . but he walk a little . ' 

 ' wonderful how people heal . ' 

 ' yes . we die very easily . but we also come quickly back to life . ' 

 ' and you ? do you fight the rebel , or do not   they want to fight ? ' 

 ' yes , they want to . we fight once or twice ; not very much . ' 

 ' man kill ? ' 

 ' yes ! some ! not many , no ? perhaps a hundred . we can never tell , no ? maybe two hundred . ' 

 he wave his hand vaguely . 

 ' but you have the bad rebellion at Jamiltepec , no ? ' he say suddenly , with heavy indian gravity , gloom suddenly settle down . 

 ' it do not   last long , but it be rather awful while it do . ' 

 ' rather awful , no ? - if I have know ! I say to Ram n , will not   you keep the soldier ? - the guard , no ? he say they be not necessary . but here - you never know , no ? ' 

 ' Niña ! ' cry Juana , from the terrace . ' Niña ! Don Antonio say he be come to see you . ' 

 ' tell he to come to - morrow . '

 ' the bedroom the girl use to have be that one , on the terrace not far from where the stair go up to the roof . the bedroom have a lattice window , high up , look out on the tree . there be a big laurel de India grow outside . it appear the girl climb on a table and knock the iron lattice of the window loose , while she be live here , and that Guillermo , by take a jump from the bough - a very risky thing , but then he be one of that sort - could land on the window - sill and pull himself into the room .

 ' Martin , my man , who be wait on the other stair , ready if they try to blow out the iron door , hear the smash of the window and rush round just as the second bandit - the one you shoot - be crouch on the window - sill to jump down into the room . the window be quite small , and high up .
