 these girl stand by their wheel , spinning , stand beside the run wheel , which they set go with one hand , while with the other hand they keep a long , miraculous thread of white wool - yarn dancing at the very tip of the rapidly - spin spool - needle , the filmy roll of the card wool just touch the point of the spool , and at once run out into a long , pure thread of white , which wound itself on to the spool , and another piece of card wool be attach . one of the girl , a beautiful oval - face one , who smile shyly at Kate , be very clever . it be almost miraculous the way she touch the spool and draw out the thread of wool almost as fine as sew cotton . 

 at the other end of the corridor , under the black shed , be two loom , and two man weave . they treddle at the wooden tread - loom , first with one foot and then the other , absorb and silent , in the shadow of the black mud wall . one man be weave a brilliant scarlet serape , very fine , and of the beautiful cochineal red . it be difficult work . from the pure scarlet centre zigzag of black and white be run in a sort of whorl , away to the edge , that be pure black . wonderful to see the man , with small bobbin of fine red and white yarn , and black , weave a bit of the ground , weave the zigzag of black up to it , and , up to that , the zigzag of white , with deft , dark finger , quickly adjust his set needle , quick as lightning thread his pattern , then bring down the beam heavily to press it tight . the serape be weave on a black warp , long fine thread of black , like a harp . but beautiful beyond word the perfect , delicate scarlet weaving in . 

 ' for whom be that ? ' say Kate to Cipriano . ' for you ? ' 

 ' yes , ' he say . ' for I ! ' 

 the other weaver be weave a plain white serape with blue and natural - black end , throw the spool of yarn from side to side , between the white harp - string , press down each thread of his woof heavily , with the wooden bar , then treddle to change the long , fine thread of the warp . 

 in the shadow of the mud shed , the pure colour of the lustrous wool look mystical , the cardinal scarlet , the pure , silky white , the lovely blue , and the black , gleam in the shadow of the blackish wall . 

 the fat man with the one eye bring serape , and two boy open they one by one . there be a new one , white , with close flower of blue on black stalk , and with green leaf , form the border , and at the boca , the mouth , where the head go through , a whole lot of little , rainbow - colour flower , in a coil blue circle . 

 ' I love that ! ' say Kate . ' what be that for ? ' 

 ' it be one of Ram n 's ; they be Quetzalcoatl 's colour , the blue and white and natural black . but this one be for the day of the opening of the flower , when he bring in the goddess who will come , ' say Cipriano . 

 Kate be silent with fear . 

 there be two scarlet serape with a diamond at the centre , all black , and a border - pattern of black diamond . 

 ' be these your ? ' 

 ' well , they be for the messenger of Huitzilopochtli . those be my colour : scarlet and black . but I myself have white as well , just as Ram n have a fringe of my scarlet . ' 

 ' do not   it make you afraid ? ' she say to he , look at he rather blench . 

 ' how make I afraid ? ' 

 ' to do this . to be the living Huitzilopochtli , ' she say . 

 ' I be the live Huitzilopochtli , ' he say . ' when Ram n dare to be the live Quetzalcoatl , I dare to be the live Huitzilopochtli . I be he . - be I not ? ' 

 Kate look at he , at his dark face with the little hanging tuft of beard , the arched brow , the slightly slanting black eye . in the round , fierce gaze of his eye there be a certain silence , like tenderness , for she . but beyond that , an inhuman assurance , which look far , far beyond she , in the darkness . 

 and she hide her face from he , murmur : 

 ' I know you be . ' 

 ' and on the day of flower , ' he say , ' you , too , shall come , in a green dress they shall weave you , with blue flower at the seam , and on your head the new moon of flower . ' 

 she hide her face , afraid . 

 ' come and look at the wool , ' he say , lead she across the patio to the shade where , on a line , the yarn hang in dripping tress of colour , scarlet and blue and yellow and green and brown . 

 ' see ! ' he say . ' you shall have a dress of green , that leave the arm bare , and a white under - dress with blue flower . ' 

 the green be a strong apple - green colour . 

 two woman under the shed be crouch over big earthenware vessel , which sit over a fire which burn slowly in a hole dig in the ground . they be watch the steaming water . one take dry , yellow - brown flower , and fling they in her water as if she be a witch brewing decoction . she watch as the flower rise , watch as they turn softly in the boiling water . then she throw in a little white powder . 

 ' and on the day of flower you , too , will come . ah ! if Ram n be the centre of a new world , a world of new flower shall spring up round he , and push the old world back . I call you the First Flower . ' 

 they leave the courtyard . the soldier have bring the black arab stallion for Cipriano , and for she the donkey , on which she could perch sideways , like a peasant woman . so they go through the hot , deserted silence of the mud - brick town , down the lane of deep , dark - grey dust , under vivid green tree that be burst into flower , again to the silent shore of the lake - end , where the delicate fishing - net be hang in long line and blow in the wind , loop after loop stride above the shingle and blow delicately in the wind , as away on the low place the green maize be blow , and the fleecy willow shake like soft green feather hang down . 

 the lake stretch pale and unreal into nowhere ; the motor - boat ride near in , the black canoas stand motionless a little far out . two woman , tiny as bird , be kneel on the water 's edge , washing . 

 Kate jump from her donkey on to the shingle . 

 ' why not ride through the water to the boat ? ' say Cipriano . 

 she look at the boat , and thought of the donkey stumble and splash . 

 ' no , ' she say . ' I will wade again . ' 

 he ride his black Arab to the water . it sniff , and enter with delicate foot into the warm shallow . then , a little way in , it stand and suddenly start paw the water , as a horse paw the ground , in the oddest manner possible , very rapidly strike the water with its fore - foot , so that little wave splash up over its black leg and belly . 

 but this splash Cipriano too . he lift the rein and touch the creature with his spur . it jump , and go half - stumble , half - dance through the water , prettily , with a splashing noise . Cipriano quiet it , and it wad gingerly on through the shallow of the vast lake , bend its black head down to look , to look in a sort of fascination at the stony bottom , sway its black tail as it move its glossy , raven haunch gingerly . 

 then again it stand still , and suddenly , with a rapid beating of its fore - paw , send the water hollowly splash up , till its black belly glisten wet like a black serpent , and its leg be shiny wet pillar . and again Cipriano lift its head and touch it with the spur , so the delicate creature dance in a churn of water . 

 ' oh , it look so pretty ! it look so pretty when it paw the water ! ' cry Kate from the shore . ' why do it do it ? ' 

 Cipriano turn in the saddle and look back at she with the sudden , gay indian laugh . 

 ' it like to be wet - who know ? ' he say . 

 a soldier hurry wad through the water and take the horse 's bridle . Cipriano dismount neatly from the stirrup , with a little backward leap into the boat , a real savage horseman . the barefoot soldier leap into the saddle , and turn the horse to shore . but the black horse , male and wilful , insist on stop to paw the water and splash himself , with a naïve , wilful sort of delight . 

 ' look ! look ! ' cry Kate . ' it be so pretty . ' 

 but the soldier be perch in the saddle , draw up his leg like a monkey , and shout at the horse . it would wet its fine harness . 

 he ride the arab slanting through the water , to where an old woman , sit in her own silence and almost invisible before , be squat in the water with brown bare shoulder emerge , ladle water from a half gourd - shell over her matted grey head . the horse splash and dance , the old woman rise with her rag of chemise clinging to she , scold in a quiet voice and bend forward with her calabash cup ; the soldier laugh , the black horse joyfully and excitedly paw the water and make it splash high up , the soldier shout again . - but the soldier know he could make Cipriano responsible for the splashing . 

 Kate wad slowly to the boat , and step in . the water be warm , but the wind be blow with strong , electric heaviness . Kate quickly dry her foot and leg on her handkerchief , and pull on her biscuit - colour silk stocking and brown shoe . 

 she sit look back , at the lake - end , the desert of shingle , the blowing , gauzy net , and , beyond they , the black land with green maize standing , a further fleecy green of tree , and the broken lane lead deep into the row of old tree , where the soldier from Jaramay be now rid away on the black horse and the donkey . on the right there be a ranch , too ; a long , low black building and a cluster of black hut with tile roof , empty garden with reed fence , clump of banana and willow - tree . all in the changeless , heavy light of the afternoon , the long lake reach into invisibility , between its unreal mountain . 

 ' it be beautiful here ! ' say Kate . ' one could almost live here . ' 

 ' Ram n say he will make the lake the centre of a new world , ' say Cipriano . ' we will be the god of the lake . ' 

 ' I be afraid I be just a woman , ' say Kate . 

 his black eye come round at she swiftly . 

 ' what do it mean , just a woman ? ' he say , quickly , sternly . 

 she hang her head . what do it mean ? what indeed do it mean ? just a woman ! she let her soul sink again into the lovely elusiveness where everything be possible , even that oneself be elusive among the god . 

 the motor - boat , with wave slap behind , be run quickly along the brownish pale water . the soldier , who be in the front , for balance , crouch on the floor with the glaze , stupefied mask - face of the people when they be sleepy . and soon they be a heap in the bottom of the boat , two little heap lie in contact . 

 Cipriano sit behind she , his tunic remove , spread his white - sleeve arm on the back of his seat . the cartridge - belt be heavy on his hip . his face be completely expressionless , star ahead . the wind blow his black hair on his forehead , and blow his little beard . he meet her eye with a far - off , remote smile , far , far down his black eye . but it be a wonderful recognition of she . 

 the boatman in the stern sit tall and straight , watch with pale eye of shallow , superficial consciousness . the great hat make his face dark , the chin - ribbon fall black against his cheek . feel her look at he , he glance at she as if she be not there . 

 turn , she push her cushion on to the floor and slide down . Cipriano get up , in the running , heaving boat , and pull she another seat - cushion . she lay , cover her face with her shawl , while the motor chug rapidly , the awning rattle with sudden wind , the hurrying wave rise behind , give the boat a slap and throw she forward , send spray sometimes , in the heat and silence of the lake . 

 Kate lose her consciousness , under her yellow shawl , in the silence of man . 

 she wake to the sudden stopping of the engine , and sit up . they be near shore ; the white tower of San Pablo among near tree . the boatman , wide - eye , be bend over the engine , abandon the tiller . the wave push the boat slowly round . 

 ' what be it ? ' say Cipriano . 

 ' More gasoline , Excellency ! ' say the boatman . 

 the soldier wake and sit up . 

 the breeze have die . 

 ' the water be come , ' say Cipriano . 

 ' the rain ? ' say Kate . 

 ' yes - ' and he point with his fine black finger , which be pale on the inside , to where black cloud be rush up behind the mountain , and in another place far off , great heavy bank be rise with strange suddenness . the air seem to be knit together overhead . lightning flash in various place , muffle thunder speak far away . 

 still the boat drift . there be a smell of gasoline . the man potter with the engine . the motor start again , only to stop again in a moment . 

 the man roll up his trouser , and , to Kate 's amazement , step into the lake , though they be a mile from the shore . the water be not up to his knee . they be on a bank . he slowly push the boat before he , wad in the silence . 

 ' how deep be the lake far in ? ' ask Kate . 

 ' there , Señorita , where the bird with the white breast be swim , it be eight and a half metre , ' he say , point as he wad . 

 ' we must make haste , ' say Cipriano . 

 ' yes , Excellency ! ' 

 the man step in again , with his long , handsome brown leg . the motor splutter . they be under way , run fast . a new chill wind be spring up . 

 but they round a bend , and see ahead the flat promontory with the dark mango - tree , and the pale yellow upper story of the hacienda house of Jamiltepec rise above the tree . palm - tree stand motionless , the bougainvillea hang in heavy sheet of magenta colour . Kate could see hut of peon among the tree , and woman washing , kneel on stone at the lake side where the stream run in , and a big plantation of banana just above . 

 a cool wind be spin round in the heaven . black cloud be fill up . Ram n come walk slowly down to the little harbour as they land . 

 ' the water be come , ' he say in Spanish . 

 ' we be in time , ' say Cipriano . 

 Ram n look they both in the face , and know . Kate , in her new elusiveness , laugh softly . 

 ' there be another flower open in the garden of Quetzalcoatl , ' say Cipriano in Spanish . 

 ' under the red canna of Huitzilopochtli , ' say Ram n. 

 ' yes , there , Señor , ' say Cipriano . ' Pero una florecita tan zarca ! Y abri en mi sombra , amigo . ' 

 ' Seis hombre de la alta fortuna . ' 

 ' Verdad ! ' 

 it be about five in the afternoon . the wind hiss in the leaf , and suddenly the rain be stream down in a white smoke of power . the ground be a solid white smoke of water , the lake be go . 

 ' you will have to stay here to - night , ' say Cipriano to Kate in Spanish , in the soft , lap indian voice . 

 ' but the rain will leave off , ' she say . 

 ' you will have to stay here , ' he repeat , in the same spanish phrase , in a curious voice like a breath of wind . 

 Kate look at Ram n , blushing . he look back at she , she think , very remote , as if look at she from far , far away . 

 ' the bride of Huitzilopochtli , ' he say , with a faint smile . 

 ' Thou , Quetzalcoatl , thou wilt have to marry we , ' say Cipriano . 

 ' do you wish it ? ' say Ram n. 

 ' yes ! ' she say . ' I want you to marry we , only you . ' 

 ' when the sun go down , ' say Ram n. 

 and he go away to his room . Cipriano show Kate to her room , then leave she and go to Ram n. 

 the cool water continue to come down , rush with a smoke of speed down from heaven . 

 as the twilight come through the unceasing rain , a woman - servant bring Kate a sleeveless dress or chemise of white linen , scallop at the bottom and embroider with stiff blue flower upside - down on the black stalk , with two stiff green leaf . in the centre of the flower be the tiny Bird of Quetzalcoatl . 

 ' the patr n ask that you put this on ! ' say the woman , bring also a lamp and a little note . 

 the note be from Ram n , say in Spanish : ' take the dress of the bride of Huitzilopochtli , and put it on , and take off everything but this . leave no thread nor thing that can touch you from the past . the past be finish . it be the new twilight . ' 

 Kate do not quite know how to put on the slip , for it have no sleeve nor arm - hole , but be just a straight slip with a run string . then she remember the old indian way , and tie the string over her left shoulder ; rather , slip the tie string over her left shoulder , leave her arm and part of her right breast bare , the slip gather full over her breast . and she sigh . for it be but a shirt with flower upturned at the bottom . 

 Ram n , barefoot , in his white clothe , come for she and take she in silence downstairs into the garden . the zaguán be dark , the rain fall steadily in the twilight , but be abate . all be dark twilight . 

 Ram n take off his blouse and throw it on the stair . then with naked breast he lead she into the garden , into the massive rain . Cipriano come forward , barefoot , with naked breast , bareheade , in the floppy white pantaloon . 

 they stand barefoot on the earth , that still throw back a white smoke of water . the rain drench they in a moment . 

 ' barefoot on the live earth , with face to the live rain , ' say Ram n in Spanish , quietly ; ' at twilight , between the night and the day ; man , and woman , in presence of the unfading star , meet to be perfect in one another . lift your face , Caterina , and say : this man be my rain from heaven . ' 

 Kate lift her face and shut her eye in the downpour . 

 ' this man be my rain from heaven , ' she say . 

 ' this woman be the earth to I - say that , Cipriano , ' say Ram n , kneel on one knee and lay his hand flat on the earth . 

 Cipriano kneel and lay his hand on the earth . 

 ' this woman be the earth to I , ' he say . 

 ' i , woman , kiss the foot and the heel of this man , for I will be strength to he , throughout the long twilight of the Morning Star . ' 

 Kate kneel and kiss the foot and heel of Cipriano , and say she say . 

 ' i , man , kiss the brow and the breast of this woman , for I will be her peace and her increase , through the long twilight of the Morning Star . ' 

 Cipriano kiss she , and say his say . 

 then Ram n put Cipriano 's hand over the rain - wet eye of Kate , and Kate 's hand over the rain - wet eye of Cipriano . 

 ' I , a woman , beneath the darkness of this cover hand , pray to this man to meet I in the heart of the night , and never deny I , ' say Kate . ' but let it be an abide place between we , for ever . ' 

 ' I , a man , beneath the darkness of this cover hand , pray to this woman to receive I in the heart of the night , in the abide place that be between we for ever . ' 

 ' man shall betray a woman , and woman shall betray a man , ' say Ram n , ' and it shall be forgive they , each of they . but if they have meet as earth and rain , between day and night , in the hour of the Star ; if the man have meet the woman with his body and the star of his hope , and the woman have meet the man with her body and the star of her yearning , so that a meeting have come to pass , and an abide place for the two where they be as one star , then shall neither of they betray the abide place where the meeting live like an unsetting star . for if either betray the abide place of the two , it shall not be forgive , neither by day nor by night nor in the twilight of the star . ' 

 the rain be leave off , the night be dark . 

 ' go and bathe in the warm water , which be peace between we all . and put oil on your body , which be the stillness of the Morning Star . anoint even the sol of your foot , and the root of your hair . ' 

 Kate go up to her room and find a big earthenware bath with steaming water , and big towel . also , in a beautiful little bowl , oil , and a soft bit of white wool . 

 she bath her rain - wet body in the warm water , dry and anoint herself with the clear oil , that be clear as water . it be soft , and have a faint perfume , and be grateful to the skin . she rub all her body , even among her hair and under her foot , till she glow softly . 

 then she put on another of the slip with the invert blue flower that have be lay on the bed for she , and over that a dress of green , hand - weave wool , make of two piece join openly together down the side , show a bit of the white , full under - dress , and fasten on the left shoulder . there be a stiff flower , blue , on a black stem , with two black leaf , embroider at the bottom , at each side . and her white slip show a bit at the breast , and hang below the green skirt , show the blue flower . 

 it be strange and primitive , but beautiful . she push her foot into the plait green huarache . but she want a belt . she tie a piece of ribbon round her waist . 

 a mozo tap to say supper be ready . 

 laugh rather shyly , she go along to the salon . 

 Ram n and Cipriano be both wait , in silence , in their white clothe . Cipriano have his red serape loosely throw over his shoulder . 

 ' so ! ' say Cipriano , come forward . ' the bride of Huitzilopochtli , like a green morning . but Huitzilopochtli will put on your sash , and you will put on his shoe , so that he shall never leave you , and you shall be always in his spell . ' 

 Cipriano tie round her waist a narrow woollen sash of white wool , with white , terrace tower upon a red and black ground . and she stoop and put on his small , dark foot the huarache of weave red strip of leather , with a black cross on the toe . 

 ' one more little gift , ' say Ram n. 

 he make Kate put over Cipriano 's head a blue cord bear a little symbol of Quetzalcoatl , the snake in silver and the bird in blue turquoise . Cipriano put over her head the same symbol , but in gold , with a bird in black dull jet , and hang on a red cord . 

 ' there ! ' say Ram n. ' that be the symbol of Quetzalcoatl , the Morning Star . remember the marriage be the meeting - ground , and the meeting - ground be the star . if there be no star , no meeting - ground , no true come together of man with the woman , into a wholeness , there be no marriage . and if there be no marriage , there be nothing but an agitation . if there be no honourable meeting of man with woman and woman with man , there be no good thing come to pass . but if the meeting come to pass , then whosoever betray the abide place , which be the meeting - ground , which be that which live like a star between day and night , between the dark of woman and the dawn of man , between man 's night and woman 's morning , shall never be forgive , neither here nor in the hereafter . for man be frail and woman be frail , and none can draw the line down which another shall walk . but the star that be between two people and be their meeting - ground shall not be betray . 

 ' and the star that be between three people , and be their meeting - ground , shall not be betray . 

 ' and the star that be between all man and all woman , and between all the child of man , shall not be betray . 

 ' Whosoever betray another man , betray a man like himself , a fragment . for if there be no star between a man and a man , or even a man and a wife , there be nothing . but whosoever betray the star that be between he and another man , betray all , and all be lose to the traitor . 

 ' where there be no star and no abide place , nothing be , so nothing can be lose . ' 

 

 

 CHAPTER XXI 

 the opening of the Church 

 

 Kate go back to her house in Sayula , and Cipriano go back to his command in the city . 

 ' will you not come with I ? ' he say . ' shall we not make a civil marriage , and live in the same house together ? ' 

 ' no , ' she say . ' I be married to you by Quetzalcoatl , no other . I will be your wife in the world of Quetzalcoatl , no other . and if the star have rise between we , we will watch it . ' 

 conflicting feeling play in his dark eye . he could not bear even to be the least bit thwart . then the strong , rather distant look come back . 

 ' it be very good , ' he say . ' it be the good . ' 

 and he go away without look back . 

 Kate return to her house , to her servant and her rock - chair . inside herself she keep very still and almost thoughtless , take no count of time . what be go to unfold must unfold of itself . 

 she no long fear the night , when she be shut alone in her darkness . but she fear the day a little . she shrink so mortally from contact . 

 she open her bedroom window one morning , and look down to the lake . the sun have come , and queer blotty shadow be on the hill beyond the water . way down at the water 's edge a woman be pour water from a calabash bowl over a statuesque pig , dip rapidly and assiduously . the little group be see in silhouette against the pale , dun lake . 

 but impossible to stand at her open window look on the little lane . an old man suddenly appear from nowhere , offer she a leaf full of tiny fish , charale , like splinter of glass , for ten centavos , and a girl be unfold three egg from the ragged corner of her rebozo , thrust they imploringly forward to Kate . an old woman be shamble up with a sad story , Kate know . she flee from her window and the importunity . 

 at the same instant the sound that always make her heart stand still wake on the invisible air . it be the sound of drum , of tom - tom rapidly beat . the same sound she have hear in the distance , in the tropical dusk of Ceylon , from the temple at sunset . the sound she have hear from the edge of the forest in the north , when the Red Indians be dance by the fire . the sound that wake dark , ancient echo in the heart of every man , the thud of the primeval world . 

 two drum be violently throb against one another . then gradually they be slow down , in a peculiar uneven rhythm , till at last there be only leave one slow , continual , monotonous note , like a great drop of darkness fall heavily , continually , drip in the bright morning . 

 the re - evoked past be frightening , and if it be re - evoke to overwhelm the present , it be fiendish . Kate feel a real terror of the sound of a tom - tom . it seem to beat straight on her solar plexus , to make she sick . 

 she go to her window . across the lane rise a tall garden - wall of adobe brick , and above that , the sun on the top of the orange - tree , deep gold . beyond the orange garden rise three tall , handsome , shaggy palm - tree , side by side on slim stem . and from the very top of the two outer palm rise the twin tip of the church tower . she have notice it so often ; the two ironwork greek cross seem to stand on the mop of the palm . 

 now in an instant she see the glitter of the symbol of Quetzalcoatl in the place where the cross have be ; two circular sun , with the dark bird at the centre . the gold of the sun - or the serpent - flash new in the light of the sun , the bird lift its wing dark in outline within the circle . 

 then again the two drum be speed up , beat against one another with the peculiar uneven savage rhythm , which at first seem no rhythm , and then seem to contain a summon almost sinister in its power , act on the helpless blood direct . Kate feel her hand flutter on her wrist , in fear . almost , too , she could hear the heart of Cipriano beating ; her husband in Quetzalcoatl . 

 ' listen , Niña ! listen , Niña ! ' come Juana 's frightened voice from the veranda . 

 Kate go to the veranda . Ezequiel have roll up his mattress and be hitch up his pant . it be Sunday morning , when he sometimes lie on after sunrise . his thick black hair stand up , his dark face be blank with sleep , but in his quiet aloofness and his slightly bow head Kate could see the secret satisfaction he take in the barbarous sound of the drum . 

 ' it come from the Church ! ' say Juana . 

 Kate catch the other woman 's black , reptilian eye unexpectedly . usually , she forget that Juana be dark , and different . for day she would not realize it . till suddenly she meet that black , void look with the glint in it , and she start inwardly , involuntarily ask herself : ' do she hate I ? ' 

 or be it only the unspeakable difference in blood ? 

 now , in the dark glitter which Juana show she for one moment , Kate read fear , and triumph , and a slow , savage nonchalant defiance . something very inhuman . 

 ' what do it mean ? ' Kate say to she . 

 ' it mean , Niña , that they will not   ring the bell any more . they have take the bell away , and they beat the drum in the church . listen ! listen ! ' 

 the drum be shudder rapidly again . 

 Kate and Juana go across to the open window . 

 ' look ! Niña ! the Eye of the other one ! no more cross on the church . it be the Eye of the other one . look ! how it shin ! how nice ! ' 

 ' it mean , ' say Ezequiel 's break young voice , which be just turn deep , ' that it be the church of Quetzalcoatl . now it be the temple of Quetzalcoatl ; our own God . ' 

 he be evidently a staunch Man of Quetzalcoatl . 

 ' think of it ! ' murmur Juana , in an awed voice . she seem like a heap of darkness low at Kate 's side . 

 then again she glance up , and the eye of the two woman meet for a moment . 

 ' see the Niña 's eye of the sun ! ' cry Juana , lay her hand on Kate 's arm . Kate 's eye be a sort of hazel , change , grey - gold , flicker at the moment with wonder , and a touch of fear and dismay . Juana sound triumphant . 

 a man in a white serape , with the blue and black border , suddenly appear at the window , lift his hat , on which be the sign of Quetzalcoatl , and push a little card through the window . 

 the card say : come to the church when you hear the one big drum ; about seven o'clock . - it be sign with the sign of Quetzalcoatl . 

 ' very well ! ' say Kate . ' I will come . ' 

 it be a quarter to seven already . outside the room be the noise of Juana sweep the veranda . Kate put on a white dress and a yellow hat , and a long string of pale - colour topaz that glimmer with yellow and mauve . 

 the earth be all damp with rain , the leaf be all fresh and tropical thick , yet many old leaf be on the ground , beat down . 

 ' Niña ! you be go out already ! wait ! wait ! the coffee . Concha ! quick ! ' 

 there be a running of bare foot , the child bring cup and plate and sweet bun and sugar , the mother hastily limp with the coffee . Ezequiel come stride along the walk , lift his hat . he go down to the servant ' quarter . 

 ' Ezequiel say - ! ' Juana come cry . when suddenly a soft , slack thud seem to make a hole in the air , leave a gap behind it . Thud ! - Thud ! - Thud ! - rather slowly . it be the big drum , irresistible . 

 Kate rise at once from her coffee . 

 ' I be go to the church , ' she say . 

 ' yes , Niña - Ezequiel say - I be come , Niña - ' 

 and Juana scuttle away , to get her black rebozo . 

 the man in the white serape with the blue and black end be wait by the gate . he lift his hat , and walk behind Kate and Juana . 

 ' he be follow we ! ' whisper Juana . 

 Kate draw her yellow shawl around her shoulder . 

 it be Sunday morning , sailing - boat line the water 's edge , with their black hull . but the beach be empty . as the great drum let fall its slow , bellowing note , the last people be run towards the church . 

 in front of the church be a great throng of native , the man with their dark serape , or their red blanket over their shoulder ; the night of rain be cold ; and their hat in their hand . the high , dark indian head ! - Women in blue rebozos be press along . the big drum slowly , slackly explode its note from the church - tower . Kate have her heart in her mouth . 

 in the middle of the crowd , a double row of man in the scarlet serape of Huitzilopochtli with the black diamond on the shoulder , stand with rifle , hold open a lane through the crowd . 

 ' pass ! ' say her guard to she . and Kate enter the lane of scarlet and black serape , go slow and daze between watchful black eye of the man . her guard follow she . but Juana have be turn back . 

 Kate look at her foot , and stumble . then she look up . 

 in the gateway of the yard before the church stand a brilliant figure in a serape whose zig - zag whorl of scarlet , white , and black run curve , dazzle , to the black shoulder ; above which be the face of Cipriano , calm , superb , with the little black beard and the arch brow . he lift his hand to she in salute . 

 behind he , stretch from the gateway to the closed door of the church , be a double row of the guard of Quetzalcoatl , in their blanket with the blue and black border . 

 ' what shall I do ? ' say Kate . 

 ' stand here with I a moment , ' say Cipriano , in the gateway .

 the big drum overhead cease , and suddenly the little drum break like a shower of hail on the air , and as suddenly cease .

 ' but the Sons of God come and go . 
 they come from beyond the Morning Star ;

 ' those that follow I , must cross the mountain of the sky ,

 ' I be the live Quetzalcoatl , ' come the solemn , impassive voice of Ram n. 

 

 ' I be the Son of the Morning Star , and child of the deep . 
 no man know my Father , and I know he not . 
 my Father be deep within the deep , whence he send I forth . 
 he send the eagle of silence down on wide wing 
 to lean over my head and my neck and my breast 
 and fill they strong with strength of wing . 
 he send the serpent of power up my foot and my loin 
 so that strength well up in I like water in hot spring . 
 but midmost shin as the Morning Star midmost shin 
 between night and day , my Soul - star in one , 
 which be my Father whom I know not . 
 I tell you , the day should not turn into glory , 
 and the night should not turn deep , 
 save for the morning and evening star , upon which they turn . 
 night turn upon I , and Day , who be the star between . 
 between your breast and belly be a star . 
 if it be not there 
 you be empty gourd - shell fill with dust and wind . 
 when you walk , the star walk with you , between your breast and your belly . 
 when you sleep , it softly shin . 
 when you speak true and true , it be bright on your lip and your tooth . 
 when you lift your hand in courage and bravery , its glow be clear in your palm . 
 when you turn to your wife as brave man turn to their woman 
 the Morning Star and the Evening Star shine together . 
 for man be the Morning Star . 
 and woman be the Star of Evening . 
 I tell you , you be not man alone . 
 the star of the beyond be within you . 
 but have you see a dead man , how his star have go out of he ? 
 so the star will go out of you , even as a woman will leave a man if his warmth never warm she . 
 should you say : I have no star ; I be no star . 
 so it will leave you , and you will hang like a gourd on the vine of life 
 with nothing but rind : 
 wait for the rat of the dark to come and gnaw your inside . 
 do you hear the rat of the darkness gnaw at your inside ? 
 till you be as empty as rat - gnaw pomegranate hang hollow on the Tree of Life ? 
 if the star shine , they dare not , they could not . 
 if you be man with the Morning Star . 
 if the star shine within you 
 no rat of the dark dare gnaw you . 
 but I be Quetzalcoatl , of the Morning Star . 
 I be the live Quetzalcoatl . 
 and you be man who should be man of the Morning Star . 
 see you be not rat - gnaw gourd . 
 I be Quetzalcoatl of the eagle and the snake . 
 the earth and air . 
 of the Morning Star . 
 I be Lord of the Two Ways - ' 

 

 the drum begin to beat , the man of Quetzalcoatl suddenly take off their serape , and Ram n do the same . they be now man naked to the waist . the eight man from the altar - step file up to the altar where the fire burn , and one by one kindle tall green candle , which burn with a clear light . they range themselves on either side the chancel , hold the light high , so that the wooden face of the image glow as if alive , and the eye of silver and jet flash most curiously . 

 ' a man shall take the wine of his spirit and the blood of his heart , the oil of his belly and the seed of his loin , and offer they first to the Morning Star , ' say Ram n , in a loud voice , turn to the people . 

 four man come to he . one put a blue crown with the bird on his brow , one put a red belt round his breast , another put a yellow belt around his middle , and the last fasten a white belt round his loin . then the first one press a small glass bowl to Ram n 's brow , and in the bowl be white liquid like bright water . the next touch a bowl to the breast , and the red shake in the bowl . at the navel the man touch a bowl with yellow fluid , and at the loin a bowl with something dark . they hold they all to the light . 

 then one by one they pour they into a silver mixing - bowl that Ram n hold between his hand . 

 ' for save the unknown God pour his Spirit over my head and fire into my heart , and send his power like a fountain of oil into my belly , and his lightning like a hot spring into my loin , I be not . I be nothing . I be a dead gourd .

 ' Fourfold be man . but the star be one star . and one man be but one star . '

 ' I be the Living Quetzalcoatl .

 all thing that lift in the lift of live between earth and sky , know I .

 ' you be glad ! you be glad ! ' say Cipriano in anger , angry with the very ghost of the woman , talk to the ghost . ' you be glad because you never pour the wine of your body into the mixing - bowl ! yet in your day you have drink the wine of his body and be soothe with his oil . you be glad you keep yours back ? you be glad you keep back the wine of your body and the secret oil of your soul ? that you give only the water of your charity ? I tell you the water of charity , the hiss water of the spirit , be bitter at last in the mouth and in the breast and in the belly ; it put out the fire . you would have put out the fire , Doña Carlota . - but you can not . you shall not . you have be charitable and compassionless to the man you call your own . so you have put out your own fire . ' 

 ' who be talk ? ' say the ghost of Carlota . 

 ' i , Cipriano Viedma , be talk . ' 

 ' the oil and the wine ! the oil and the wine and the bread ! they be the sacrament ! they be the body and the blessing of God ! where be the priest ? I want the sacrament . where be the priest ? I want to confess , and take the sacrament , and have the peace of God , ' say the ghost of Carlota . 

 ' the priest be come . - but you can take no sacrament , unless you give it . the oil and the wine and the bread ! they be not for the priest to give . they be to be pour into the mixing - bowl , which Ram n call the cup of the star . if you pour neither oil nor wine into the mixing - bowl , from the mixing - bowl you can not drink . so you have no sacrament . '

 Doña Carlota have relapse into unconsciousness ; even her ghost refuse to hear . Cipriano fling his sinisterly - flame serape over his shoulder and his face , over his nose , till only his black , glitter eye be visible as he blow out of the room . 

 Kate sit by the window , and laugh a little . the primeval woman inside she laugh to herself , for she have know all the time about the two thief on the Cross with Jesus ; the bullying , maraud thief of the male in his own right , and the much more subtle , cold , sly , charitable thief of the woman in her own right , forever chant her beggar 's whine about the love of God and the God of pity . 

 but Kate , too , be a modern woman and a woman in her own right . so she sit on with Carlota . and when the doctor come , she accept the obsequiousness of the man as part of her right . and when the priest come , she accept the obsequiousness from he , just the same , as part of her woman 's right . these two minister of love , what be they for , but to be obsequious to she ? as for herself , she could hardly be call a thief , and a sneak - thief of the world 's virility , when these man come force their obsequiousness upon she , whine to she to take it and relieve they of the responsibility of their own manhood . no , if woman be thief , it be only because man want to be thieve from . if woman thieve the world 's virility it be only because man want to have it thieve , since for man to be responsible for their own manhood seem to be the last thing man want . 

 so Kate sit on in the room of the die Carlota , smile a little cynically . outside she hear the roll of the tom - tom and the deep chanting of the man of Quetzalcoatl . beyond , under the tree , in the smooth , clear space before the church , she see the half - naked man dance in a circle , to the drum ; the round dance . then later , dance a religious dance of the return of Quetzalcoatl . it be the old , barefoote , absorb dancing of the Indians , the dance of downward - sink absorption . it be the dance of these people , too , just the same : the dance of the Aztecs and Zapotees and the huichole , just the same in essence , indigenous to America ; the curious , silent , absorb dance of the softly - beat foot and ankle , the body come down softly , but with deep weight , upon powerful knee and ankle , to the tread of the earth , as when a male bird tread the hen . and woman softly step in unison . 

 and Kate , listen to the drum , and the full - throate singing , and watch the rich , soft body in the dance , think to herself a little sceptically : yes ! for these it be easy . but all the white man , of the dominant race , what be they do at this moment ? 

 in the afternoon there be a great dance of the welcome of Quetzalcoatl . Kate could only see a little of it , in front of the church . 

 the drum beat vigorously all the time , the dance wound strangely to the water 's edge . Kate hear afterwards that the procession of woman with basket on their head , fill with bread and fruit all wrap in leaf , go down to the shore and load the boat . then dancer and all get into the boat and canoas , and row to the island . 

 they make a feast on the island , and learn the dance of the welcome of Quetzalcoatl , which they would dance every year on that day . and they learn the Song of the welcome of Quetzalcoatl ; which later on Cipriano bring to Kate , as she sit in that dim room with the unconscious woman , who make small , terrible , mechanical noise . 

 the doctor come hastening , and the priest come after a while . neither could do anything . they come in the afternoon again , and Kate walk out and wander on the half - desert beach , look at the flock of boat draw near the island , and feel that life be a more terrible issue even than death . one could die and have do . but living be never do , it could never be finish , and the responsibility could never be shift . 

 she go back again to the sick - room , and with the aid of a woman she undress poor Carlota and put a nightdress on she . another doctor come from the city . but the sick woman be die . and Kate be alone with she again . 

 the man , where be they ? 

 the business of living ? be they really go about the great business of living , abandon she here to this business of die ? 

 it be nightfall before she hear the drum return . and again that deep , full , almost martial singing of man , savage and remote , to the sound of the drum . perhaps after all , life would conquer again , and man would be man , so that woman could be woman . till man be man indeed , woman have no hope to be woman . she know that fatally enough .

 ' the doctor think she may come round . '

 ' see ! ' he say . ' this be what they be sing . '

 strange ! the people have open heart at last . they have roll the stone of their heaviness away , a new world have begin . Kate be frightened . it be dusk . she lay her hand on Cipriano 's knee , lose . and he lean and put his dark hand against her cheek , breathe silently .
