 she could almost feel her soul appeal to Cipriano for this sacrament . 

 they sit side by side in darkness , as the night fall , and he hold his hand loosely on her . outside , the people be still sing . some be dance round the drum . on the church - tower , where the bell have be , there be fire flicker , and white form of man , the noise of a heavy drum , then again , the chant . in the yard before the church door a fire be blaze , and man of Huitzilopochtli stand watch two of their man , naked save for a breech - cloth and the scarlet feather on their head , dance the old spear - dance , whooping challenge in the firelight . 

 Ram n come in , in his white clothe . he pull off his big hat , and stand look down at Carlota . she no long make noise , and her eye be turn up horribly , show the white . Ram n close his eye a moment , and turn away , say nothing . he come to the window , where Cipriano still sit in his impenetrable but live silence , that satisfy where all speech have fail , hold Kate 's hand loosely . nor do he let go her hand . 

 Ram n look out , at the fire in the church tower , the fire before the church door , the little fire on the beach by the lake ; and the figure of man in white , the figure of woman in dark rebozos , with full white skirt , the two naked dancer , the standing crowd , the occasional scarlet serape of Huitzilopochtli , the white and blue of Quetzalcoatl , the creep away of a motor - car , the running of boy , the man cluster round the drum , to sing . 

 ' it be life , ' he say , ' which be the mystery . death be hardly mysterious in comparison . ' 

 there be a knocking . the doctor have come again , and a sister to nurse the die woman . softly the sister pace round the room and bent over her charge . 

 Cipriano and Kate go away in a boat over the dark lake , away from all the fire and the noise into the deep darkness of the lake beyond , to Jamiltepec . Kate feel she want to be cover with deep and living darkness , the deep where Cipriano could lay she . 

 

 put sleep as black as beauty in the secret of my belly . 
 Put star - oil over I . 

 

 and Cipriano , as he sit in the boat with she , feel the inward sun rise darkly in he , diffuse through he ; and feel the mysterious flower of her woman 's femaleness slowly open to he , as a sea - anemone open deep under the sea , with infinite soft fleshliness . the hardness of self - will be go , and the soft anemone of her deep blossom for he of itself , far down under the tide . 

 Ram n remain behind in the hotel , in the impenetrable sanctuary of his own stillness . Carlota remain unconscious . there be a consultation of doctor ; to no effect . she die at dawn , before her boy could arrive from Mexico ; as a canoa be put off from the shore with a little breeze , and the passenger be sing the Song of Welcome to Quetzalcoatl , unexpectedly , upon the pale water . 

 

 

 CHAPTER XXII 

 the Living Huitzilopochtli 

 

 they bury Doña Carlota in Sayula , and Kate , though a woman , go also to the funeral . Don Ram n follow the coffin , in his white clothe and big hat with the Quetzalcoatl sign . his boy go with he ; and there be many stranger , man , in black . 

 the boy look odd young shoot , in their black suit with short breech and bare knee . they be both round - face and creamy brown in complexion , both have a touch of fairness . the elder , Pedro , be more like Don Ram n ; but his hair be soft , more fluffy than his father 's , with a hint of brown . he be sulky and awkward , and keep his head duck . the young boy , Cyprian , have the fluffy , upstande brown hair and the startled , hazel eye of his mother . 

 they have come in a motor - car with their aunt , from Guadalajara , and be return straight to town . in her will , the mother have name guardian in place of the father , state that the father would consent . and her considerable fortune she have leave in trust for the boy . but the father be one of the trustee . 

 Ram n sit in his room in the hotel , overlook the lake , and his two boy sit on the cane settee opposite he . 

 ' what do you want to do , my son ? ' say Ram n. ' to go back with your Aunt Margarita , and return to school in the United States ? ' 

 the boy remain a while in sulky silence . 

 ' yes ! ' say Cyprian at last , his brown hair seem to fluff up with indignation . ' that be what our mother wish we to do . so , of course , we shall do it . ' 

 ' very well ! ' say Ram n quietly . ' but remember I be your father , and my door , and my arm , and my heart will always be open to you , when you come . ' 

 the eld boy shuffle with his foot , and mutter , without look up : 

 ' we can not come , papa ! ' 

 ' why not , child ? ' 

 the boy look up at he with brown eye as challenging as his own . 

 ' you , papa , you call yourself the Living Quetzalcoatl ? ' 

 ' yes . ' 

 ' but , papa , our father be call Ram n Carrasco . ' 

 ' it be also true , ' say Ram n , smile . 

 ' we , ' say Pedro , rather heavily , ' be not the child of the Living Quetzalcoatl , papa . we be Carrasco y de Lara . ' 

 ' good name both , ' say Ram n. 

 ' never , ' say the young Cyprian , his eye flash , ' never can we love you , papa . you be our enemy . you kill our mother . ' 

 ' no , no ! ' say Ram n. ' that you must not say . your mother seek her own death . ' 

 ' Mama love you much , much , much ! ' cry Cyprian , the tear rise to his eye . ' always she love you and pray for you - ' he begin to cry . 

 ' and I , my son ? ' say Ram n. 

 ' you hat she and kill she ! oh , mama ! Mama ! oh , mama ! I want my mother ! ' he weep . 

 ' come to I , little one ! ' say Ram n softly , hold out his hand . 

 ' no ! ' cry Cyprian , stamp his foot and flash his eye through his tear . ' no ! no ! ' 

 the eld boy hang his head and be cry too . Ram n have the little , perplex frown of pain on his brow . he look from side to side , as if for some issue . then he gather himself together . 

 ' listen , my son , ' he say . ' you also will be man ; it will not be long . while you be little boy , you be neither man nor woman . but soon , the change will come , and you will have to be man . and then you will know that a man must be a man . when his soul tell he to do a thing , he must do it . when you be man , you must listen carefully to your own soul , and be sure to be true . be true to your own soul ; there be nothing else for a man to do . ' 

 ' Je m'en fiche de ton âme , mon père ! ' say Cyprian , with one of his flash into French . it be a language he often speak with his mother . 

 ' that you may , my boy , ' say Ram n. ' but I may not . ' 

 ' papa ! ' put in the eld boy . ' be your soul different from mama 's soul ? ' 

 ' who know ? ' say Ram n. ' I understand it differently . ' 

 ' because mama always pray for your soul . ' 

 ' and I , in my way , pray for her , child . if her soul come back to I , I will take it into my heart . ' 

 ' Mama 's soul , ' say Cyprian , ' will go straight into Paradise . ' 

 ' who know , child ! perhaps the Paradise for the soul of the dead be the heart of the living . ' 

 ' I do not   understand what you say . ' 

 ' it be possible , ' say Ram n , ' that even now the only Paradise for the soul of your mother be in my heart . ' 

 the two boy star at he with open eye . 

 ' never will I believe that , ' say Cyprian . 

 ' or it may be in thy heart , ' say Ram n. ' Hast thou a place in thy heart for the soul of thy mother ? ' 

 the young Cyprian star with bewildered hazel eye . 

 ' the soul of my mother go direct to Paradise , because she be a saint , ' he assert flatly . 

 ' which Paradise , my son ? ' 

 ' the only one . where God be . ' 

 ' and where be that ? ' 

 there be a pause . 

 ' in the sky , ' say Cyprian , stubbornly . 

 ' it be very far and very empty . but I believe , my son , that the heart of live man be the very middle of the sky . and there God be ; and Paradise ; inside the heart of live man and woman . and there the soul of the dead come to rest , there , at the very centre , where the blood turn and return ; that be where the dead sleep well . ' 

 there be a very blank pause . 

 ' and wilt thou go on say thou art the Living Quetzalcoatl ? ' say Cyprian . 

 ' surely ! and when you be a little old , perhaps you will come to I and say it too . ' 

 ' never ! Thou hast kill our mother , and we shall hate thee . when we be man we ought to kill thee . ' 

 ' Nay , that be bombast , child ! why wilt thou listen only to servant and priest and people of that sort ? be they not thy inferior , since thou art my son , and thy mother 's son ? why dost thou take the talk of servant and inferior into thy mouth ? Hast thou no room for the speech of brave man ? thou wilt not kill I , neither will thy brother . for I would not allow you , even if you wish it . and you do not wish it . talk no more of this empty lackey - talk to I , Cyprian , for I will not hear it . art thou already a little lackey , or a priest ? come , thou art vulgar . thou art a little vulgarian . we have well speak English ; or thy French . Castilian be too good a language to turn into this currish talk . ' 

 Ram n rise and go to the window to look out at the lake . the drum on the church be sound for midday , when every man should glance at the sun , and stand silent with a little prayer . 

 

 ' the sun have climb the hill , the day be on the downward slope . 
 between the morning and the afternoon , stand I here with my soul , and lift it up . 
 my soul be heavy with sunshine , and steep with strength . 
 the sunbeam have fill I like a honeycomb , 
 it be the moment of fulness , 
 and the top of the morning . ' 

 

 Ram n turn and repeat the mid - day verse to his boy . they listen in confused silence . 

 ' come ! ' he say . ' why be you confused ? if I talk to you about your new boot , or ten peso , you would not be confuse . but if I speak of the sun and your own soul fill from the sun like honeycomb , you sulk . you have well go back to your school in America , to learn to be business man . you have well say to everybody : oh , no ! we have no father ! our mother die , but we never have a father . we be child of an immaculate conception , so we should make excellent business man . ' 

 ' I shall be a priest , ' say Cyprian . 

 ' and I a doctor , ' say Pedro . 

 ' very good ! very good ! shall - be be far from am , and tomorrow be another day . come to I when your heart tell you to come . you be my little boy , whatever you say , and I shall stroke your hair and laugh at you . come ! come here ! ' 

 he look at they , and they dare not refuse to obey , his power be so much great than theirs . 

 he take his eld son in his arm and stroke his head . 

 ' there ! ' he say . ' thou art my eld son , and I be thy father , who call himself the Living Quetzalcoatl . when they say : " be it thy father who call himself the Living Quetzalcoatl ? " - say to they : " yes , he be my father . " and when they ask you what you think of such a father , say : " I be young , and I do not understand he yet . but I do not judge my father without understand he . " Wilt thou say that , my boy , Pedro , my son ? ' and Ram n stroke the boy 's hair with the gentleness and tenderness which fill the child with a sort of awe . 

 ' yes , papa ! I will say that , ' say the boy , relieve . 

 ' it be well , ' say Ram n , lay his hand on the child 's head for a moment , like a blessing . 

 then he turn to the young son . 

 ' come then , ' he say , ' and let I stroke thy upstande hair . ' 

 ' if I love thee , I can not love mama ! ' say Cyprian . 

 ' Nay , be thy heart so narrow ? love not at all , if it make thee petty . ' 

 ' but I do not want to come to thee , papa . ' 

 ' then stay away , my son , and come when thou dost want it . ' 

 ' I do not think thou lov I , papa . ' 

 ' Nay , when thou art an obstinate monkey , I love thee not . but when thy real manhood come upon thee , and thou art brave and daring , rather than rash and impudent , then thou wilt be lovable . how can I love thee if thou art not lovable ? ' 

 ' Mama always love I . ' 

 ' she call thee her own . I do not call thee mine own . thou art thyself . when thou art lovable , I can love thee . when thou art rash and impudent , nay , I can not . the mill will not spin when the wind do not blow . ' 

 the boy go away . Ram n watch they as they stand in their black clothe and bare knee upon the jetty , and his heart yearn over they . 

 ' ah , the poor little devil ! ' he say to himself . and then : 

 ' but I can do no more than keep my soul like a castle for they , to be a stronghold to they when they need it - if ever they do . ' 

 these day Kate often sit by the lake shore , in the early light of the morning . between the rain , the day come very clear , she could see every wrinkle in the great hill opposite , and the fold , or pass , through which a river come , away at Tuliapan , be so vivid to she she feel she have walk it . the red bird look as if rain have freshen even their poppy - bud , and in the morning frog be whir . 

 but the world be somehow different ; all different . no jingle of bell from the church , no striking of the clock . the clock be take away . 

 and instead , the drum . at dawn , the heavy drum roll its sound on the air . then the sound of the Dawn - Verse chant from the tower , in a strong man 's voice : 

 

 ' the dark be divide , the sun be come past the wall . 
 Day be at hand . 
 lift your hand , say Farewell ! say welcome ! 
 then be silent . 
 let the darkness leave you , let the light come into you , 
 man in the twilight . ' 

 

 the voice and the great drum cease . and in the dawn the man who have rise stand silent , with arm uplifted , in the moment of change , the woman cover their face and bent their head . all be changeless still for the moment of change . 

 then the light drum rattle swiftly , as the first sparkle of the bright sun flash in sheer light from the crest of the great hill . the day have begin . People of the world move on their way . 

 at about nine o'clock the light drum rattle quickly , and the voice in the tower cry : 

 ' half - way ! half - way up the slope of the morning ! ' 

 there be the heavy drum at noon , the light drum again at about three o'clock , with the cry : 

 ' half - way ! half - way down the slope of afternoon . ' 

 and at sunset again , the great drum rolling , and the voice cry : 

 

 ' leave off ! leave off ! leave off ! 
 lift your hand , say Farewell ! say welcome ! 
 Man in the twilight . 
 the sun be in the outer porch , cry to he : thank ! oh , Thanks ! 
 then be silent . 
 you belong to the night . ' 

 

 and again in the sunset everywhere man stand with lift face and hand , and woman cover their face and stand with bow head ; all be changeless still for the moment of change . 

 then the light drum suddenly beat , and people move on into the night . 

 the world be different , different . the drum seem to leave the air soft and vulnerable , as if it be alive . above all , no clang of metal on metal , during the moment of change . 

 

 ' Metal for resistance . 
 drum for the beat heart . 
 the heart cease not . ' 

 

 this be one of Ram n 's little verse . 

 strange , the change that be take place in the world . always the air have a soft , more velvety silence , it seem alive . and there be no hour . Dawn and noon and sunset , mid - morning , or the up - slope middle , and mid - afternoon , or the down - slope middle , this be the day , with the watch of the night . they begin to call the four watch of the day the watch of the rabbit , the watch of the hawk , the watch of the turkey - buzzard and the watch of the deer . and the four quarter of the night be the watch of the frog , the watch of the fire - fly , the watch of the fish , the watch of the squirrel . 

 ' I shall come for you , ' write Cipriano to she , ' when the deer be thrust his last foot towards the forest . ' 

 that mean , she know , in the last quarter of the hour of the deer ; something after five o'clock . 

 it be as if , from Ram n and Cipriano , from Jamiltepec and the lake region , a new world be unfold , unroll , as softly and subtly as twilight fall and remove the clutter of day . it be a soft , twilit newness slowly spread and penetrate the world , even into the city . now , even in the city the blue serape of Quetzalcoatl be see , and the drum be hear at the hour , cast a strange mesh of twilight over the clash of bell and the clash of traffic . even in the capital the big drum roll again , and man , even man in city clothe , would stand still with uplifted face and arm upstretche , listen for the noon - verse , which they know in their heart , and try not to hear the clash of metal . 

 

 ' Metal for resistance . 
 drum for the beat heart . ' 

 

 but it be a world of metal , and a world of resistance . Cipriano , strangely powerful with the soldier , in spite of the hatred he arouse in other official , be for meet metal with metal . for get Montes to declare : the Religion of Quetzalcoatl be the religion of Mexico , official and declare . - then back up the declaration with the army . 

 but no ! no ! say Ram n. let it spread of itself . and wait awhile , till you can be declare the living Huitzilopochtli , and your man can have the red and black blanket , with the snake - curve . then perhaps we can have the open wedding with Caterina , and she will be a mother among the god . 

 all the time , Ram n try as far as possible to avoid arouse resistance and hate . he write open letter to the clergy , say : 

 ' who be I , that I should be enemy of the one Church ? I be catholic of catholic . I would have one Church of all the world , with Rome for the Central City , if Rome wish . 

 ' but different people must have different saviour , as they have different speech and different colour . the final mystery be one mystery . but the manifestation be many . 

 ' God must come to Mexico in a blanket and in huarache , else he be no God of the Mexicans , they can not know he . naked , all man be but man . but the touch , the look , the word that go from one naked man to another be the mystery of living . we live by manifestation . 

 ' and man be fragile , and fragment , and strangely group in their fragmentariness . the invisible God have do it to we , darken some face and whitened other , and group we in group , even as the zopilote be a bird , and the parrot of the hot land be a bird , and the little oriole be a bird . but the angel of the zopilote must be a zopilote , and the angel of the parrot a parrot . and to one , the dead carcase will ever smell good ; to the other , the fruit . 

 ' priest who will come to I do not forsake either faith or God . they change their manner of speech and vestment , as the peon call with one cry to the oxen , and with another cry to the mule . each respond to its own call in its own way - ' 

 to the socialist and agitator he write : 

 ' what do you want ? would you make all man as you be ? and when every peon in Mexico wear an american suit of clothe and shiny black shoe , and look for life in the newspaper and for his manhood to the government , will you be satisfied ? do the government , then , give you your manhood , that you expect it to give it to these other ? 

 ' it be time to forget . it be time to put away the grudge and the pity . no man be ever the well for be pity , and every man be the bad for a grudge . 

 ' we can do nothing with life , except live it . 

 ' let we seek life where it be to be find . and , have find it , life will solve the problem . but every time we deny the live life , in order to solve a problem , we cause ten problem to spring up where be one before . solve the problem of the people , we lose the people in a poisonous forest of problem . 

 ' life make , and mould , and change the problem . the problem will always be there , and will always be different . so nothing can be solve , even by life and living , for life dissolve and resolve , solve it leave alone . 

 ' therefore we turn to life ; and from the clock to the sun and from metal to membrane . 

 ' this way we hope the problem will dissolve , since it can never be solve . when man seek life first , they will not seek land nor gold . the land will lie on the lap of the god , where man lie . and if the old communal system come back , and the village and the land be one , it will be very good . for truly , no man can possess land . 

 ' but when we be deep in a bog , it be no use attempt to gallop . we can only wade out with toil . and in our haste to have a child , it be no good tear the babe from the womb . 

 ' seek life , and life will bring the change . 

 ' seek life itself , even pause at dawn and at sunset , and life will come back into we and prompt we through the transition . 

 ' Lay forcible hand on nothing , only be ready to resist , if forcible hand should be lay on you . for the new shoot of life be tender , and well ten death than that they should be tear or trample down by the bully of the world . when it come to fight for the tender shoot of life , fight as the jaguar fight for her young , as the she - bear for her cub . 

 ' that which be life be vulnerable , only metal be invulnerable . fight for the vulnerable unfolding of life . but for that , fight never to yield . ' 

 Cipriano , too , be always speak to his soldier , always with the same cry : 

 ' we be man ! we be fighter ! 

 ' but what can we do ? 

 ' shall we march to simple death ? 

 ' no ! no ! we must march to life . 

 ' the gringo be here . we have let they come . we must let they stay , for we can not drive they out . with gun and sword and bayonet we can never drive they out , for they have a thousand where we have one . and if they come in peace , let they stay in peace . 

 ' but we have not lose Mexico yet . we have not lose each other . 

 ' we be the blood of America . we be the blood of Montezuma . 

 ' what be my hand for ? be it to turn the handle of a machine alone ? 

 ' my hand be to salute the God of Mexicans , beyond the sky . 

 ' my hand be to touch the hand of a brave man . 

 ' my hand be to hold a gun . 

 ' my hand be to make the corn grow out of the ground . 

 ' what be my knee for ? 

 ' my knee be to hold I proud and erect . 

 ' my knee be for march on my way . 

 ' my knee be the knee of a man . 

 ' our god be Quetzalcoatl of the blue sky , and Huitzilopochtli red at the gate , watch . 

 ' our god hate a kneeling man . they shout Ho ! erect ! 

 ' then what can we do ? 

 ' wait ! 

 ' I be a man , naked inside my clothe as you be . 

 ' be I a big man ? be I a tall and powerful man , from Tlascala , for example . 

 ' I be not . I be little . I be from the south . I be small - 

 ' yet be I not your general ? 

 ' why ? 

 ' why be I a general , and you only soldier ? 

 ' I will tell you . 

 ' I find the other strength . 

 ' there be two strength ; the strength which be the strength of oxen and mule and iron , of machine and gun , and of man who can not get the second strength . 

 ' then there be the second strength . it be the strength you want . and you can get it , whether you be small or big . it be the strength that come from behind the sun . and you can get it ; you can get it here ! ' - he strike his breast - ' and here ! ' - he strike his belly - ' and here ! ' - he strike his loin . ' the strength that come from back of the sun . ' 

 when Cipriano be rouse , his eye flash , and it be as if dark feather , like pinion , be start out of he , out of his shoulder and back , as if these dark pinion clash and flash like a rouse eagle . his man seem to see he , as by second sight , with the demonish clashing and dashing of wing , like an old god . and they murmur , their eye flash : 

 ' it be Cipriano ! it be he ! we be Ciprianistos , we be his child . ' 

 ' we be man ! we be man ! ' cry Cipriano . 

 ' but listen . there be two kind of man . there be man with the second strength , and man without it . 

 ' when the first gringo come , we lose our second strength . and the padre teach we : submit ! submit ! 

 ' the gringo have get the second strength ! 

 ' how ? 

 ' like cunning one , they steal it on the sly . they keep very still , like a tarantula in his hole . then when neither sun nor moon nor star know he be there , Biff ! - the tarantula spring across , and bit , and leave the poison and suck the secret . 

 ' so they get the secret of the air and the water , and they get the secret out of the earth . so the metal be theirs , and they make gun and machine and ship , and they make train and telegram and radio . 

 ' why ? why do they make all these thing ? how could they do it ? 

 ' because , by cunne , they have get the secret of the second strength , which come from behind the sun . 

 ' and we have to be slave , because we have only get the first strength , we have lose the second strength . 

 ' now we be get it back . we have find our way again to the secret sun behind the sun . there sit Quetzalcoatl , and at last Don Ram n find he . there sit the red Huitzilopochtli , and I have find he . for I have find the second strength . 

 ' when he come , all you who strive shall find the second strength . 

 ' and when you have it , where will you feel it ? 

 ' not here ! ' - and he strike his forehead . ' not where the cunning gringo have it , in the head , and in their book . not we . we be man , we be not spider . 

 ' we shall have it here ! ' - he strike his breast - ' and here ! ' - he strike his belly - ' and here ! ' - he strike his loin . 

 ' be we man ? can we not get the second strength ? can we not ? have we lose it forever ? 

 ' I say no ! Quetzalcoatl be among we . I have find the red Huitzilopochtli . the second strength ! 

 ' when you walk or sit , when you work or lie down , when you eat or sleep , think of the second strength , that you must have it . 

 ' be very quiet . it be shy as a bird in a dark tree . 

 ' be very clean , clean in your body and your clothe . it be like a star , that will not shine in dirt . 

 ' be very brave , and do not drink till you be drunk , nor soil yourself with bad woman , nor steal . because a drunken man have lose his second strength , and a man lose his strength in bad woman , and a thief be a coward , and the red Huitzilopochtli hat a coward . 

 ' try ! try for the second strength . when we have it , the other will lose it . ' 

 Cipriano struggle hard with his army . the curse of any army be the have nothing to do . Cipriano make all his man cook and wash for themselves , clean and paint the barrack , make a great garden to grow vegetable , and plant tree wherever there be water . and he himself take a passionate interest in what they do . a dirty tunic , a sore foot , a badly - make huarache do not escape he . but even when they cook their meal he go among they . 

 ' give I something to eat , ' he would say . ' give I an enchilada ! ' 

 then he praise the cooking , or say it be bad . 

 like all savage , they like do small thing . and , like most Mexicans , once they be a little sure of what they be do , they love do it well . 

 Cipriano be determined to get some discipline into they . Discipline be what Mexico need , and what the whole world need . but it be the discipline from the inside that matter . the machine discipline , from the outside , break down . 

 he have the wild Indians from the north beat their drum in the barrack - yard , and start the old dance again . the dance , the dance which have meaning , be a deep discipline in itself . the old Indians of the north still have the secret of animistic dancing . they dance to gain power ; power over the live force or potency of the earth . and these dance need intense dark concentration , and immense endurance . 

 Cipriano encourage the dance more than anything . he learn they himself , with curious passion . the shield and spear dance , the knife dance , the dance of ambush , and the surprise dance , he learn they in the savage village of the north , and he dance they in the barrack - yard , by the bonfire , at night , when the great door be shut . 

 then , naked save for a black breech - cloth , his body smear with oil and red earth - powder , he would face some heavy naked indian and with shield and spear dance the dance of the two warrior , champion in the midst of the dense ring of soldier . and the silent , rhythmic concentration of this duel in subtlety and rapidity keep the foot softly beat with the drum , the naked body suave and subtle , circle with suave , primitive stealth , then crouch and leap like a panther , with the spear poise , to a clash of shield , part again with the crowing yell of defiance and exultance . 

 in this dance , no one be more suave and sudden than Cipriano . he could swerve along the ground with bent , naked back , as invisible as a lynx , circle round his opponent , his foot beat and his suave body subtly lilt to the drum . then in a flash he be in the air , his spear point down at the collarbone of his enemy and glide over his shoulder , as the opponent swerve under , and the war - yell resound . the soldier in the deep circle watch , fascinated , utter the old low cry . 

 and as the dance go on , Cipriano feel his strength increase and surge inside he . when all his limb be glisten with sweat , and his spirit be at last satisfy , he be at once tired and surcharge with extraordinary power . then he would throw his scarlet and dark serape around he , and motion other man to fight , give his spear and shield to another officer or soldier , go himself to sit down on the ground and watch , by the firelight . and then he feel his limb and his whole body immense with power , he feel the black mystery of power go out of he over all his soldier . and he sit there imperturbable , in silence , hold all those black - eyed man in the splendour of his own , silent self . his own dark consciousness seem to radiate through their flesh and their bone ; they be conscious , not through themselves but through he . and as a man 's instinct be to shield his own head , so that instinct be to shield Cipriano , for he be the most precious part of themselves to they . it be in he they be supreme . they get their splendour from his power and their great consciousness be his consciousness diffuse they . 

 ' I be not of myself , ' he would say to they . ' I be of the red Huitzilopochtli and the power from behind the sun . and you be not of yourself . of yourself you be nothing . you be of I , my man . ' 

 he encourage they to dance naked , with the breech - cloth , to rub themselves with the red earth - powder , over the oil . 

 ' this be the oil of the star . rub it well into your limb and you will be strong as the starry sky . this be the red blood of volcano . rub yourself with it , you will have the power of the fire of the volcano , from the centre of the earth . ' 

 he encourage they to dance the silent , concentrated dance to the drum , to dance for hour , gather power and strength . 

 ' if you know how to tread the dance , you can tread deeply and deeply , till you touch the middle of the earth with your foot . and when you touch the middle of the earth , you will have such power in your belly and your breast , no man will be able to overcome you . get the second strength . get it , get it out of the earth , get it from behind the sun . get the second strength . ' 

 he make long , rapid march across the wild mexican country , and through the mountain , move light and swift . he like to have his man camp in the open , with no tent : but the watch set , and the star overhead . he pursue the bandit with swift movement . he strip his captive , and tie they up . but if it seem a brave man , he would swear he in . if it seem to he a knave , a treacherous cur , he stab he to the heart , say : 

 ' I be the red Huitzilopochtli , of the knife . ' 

 already he have get his own small , pick body of man out of the ignominious drab uniform , dress in white with the scarlet sash and the scarlet ankle cord , and carry the good , red and black serape . and his man must be clean . on the march they would stop by some river , with the order for every man to strip and wash , and wash his clothing . then the man , dark and ruddy , move about naked , while the white clothing of strong white cotton dry on the earth . they move on again , glitter with the peculiar whiteness of cotton clothe in Mexico , gun at their back , serape and small pack on their back , wear the heavy straw hat with the scarlet crown on their head . 

 ' they must move ! ' he say to his officer . ' they must learn again to move swiftly and untiringly , with the old power . they must not lie about . in the sleep hour , let they sleep . in the waking , let they work , or march , or drill , or dance . ' 

 he divide his regiment up into little company of a hundred each , with a centurion and a sergeant in command . each company of a hundred must learn to act in perfect unison , freely and flexibly . ' perfect your hundred , ' Cipriano insist , ' and I will perfect your thousand and your ten of thousand . ' 

 ' listen ! ' he say . ' for we , no trench and cannon warfare . my man be no cannon - fodder , nor trench - dung . where cannon be , we move away . our hundred break up , and we attack where the cannon be not . that we be swift , that we be silent , that we have no burden , and that the second strength be in we : that be all . we intend to put up no battle - front , but to attack at our own moment , and at a thousand point . ' 

 and always he reiterate : 

 ' if you can get the power from the heart of the earth , and the power from behind the sun ; if you can summon the power of the red Huitzilopochtli into you , nobody can conquer you . get the second strength . ' 

 Ram n be press Cipriano now openly to assume the living Huitzilopochtli . 

 ' come ! ' he say . ' it be time you let General Viedma be swallow up in the red Huitzilopochtli . do not   you think ? ' 

 ' if I know what it mean , ' say Cipriano . 

 they be sit on the mat in Ram n 's room , in the heat before the rain come , towards the end of the rainy season . 

 ' stand up ! ' say Ram n. 

 Cipriano stand up at once , with that soft , startling alertness in his movement . 

 Ram n come quickly to he , place one of his hand over Cipriano 's eye , close they . Ram n stand behind Cipriano , who remain motionless in the warm dark , his consciousness reel in strange concentric wave , towards a centre where it suddenly plunge into the bottomless deep , like sleep . 

 ' Cipriano ? ' - the voice sound so far off . 

 ' yes . ' 

 ' be it dark ? ' 

 ' it be dark . ' 

 ' be it alive ? be the darkness alive ? ' 

 ' surely it be alive . ' 

 ' who live ? ' 

 ' i. ' 

 ' where ? ' 

 ' I know not . in the live darkness . ' 

 Ram n then bind Cipriano 's eye and head with a strip of black fur . then again , with a warm , soft pressure , he press one naked hand over Cipriano 's naked breast , and one between his shoulder . Cipriano stand in profound darkness , erect and silent . 

 ' Cipriano ? ' 

 ' yes . ' 

 ' be it dark in your heart ? ' 

 ' it be come dark . ' 

 Ram n feel the thud of the man 's heart slowly slacken . in Cipriano , another circle of darkness have start slowly to revolve , from his heart . it swing in widen round , like a great sleep . 

 ' be it dark ? ' 

 ' it be dark . ' 

 ' who live ? ' 

 ' I. ' 

 Ram n bind Cipriano 's arm at his side , with a belt of fur round the breast . then he put his one hand over the navel , his other hand in the small of the other man 's back , press with slow , warm , powerful pressure . 

 ' Cipriano ? ' 

 ' yes . ' 

 the voice and the answer go far and far away . 

 ' be it dark ? ' 

 ' no , my Lord . ' 

 Ram n knelt and press his arm close round Cipriano 's waist , press his black head against his side . and Cipriano begin to feel as if his mind , his head be melt away in the darkness ; like a pearl in black wine , the other circle of sleep begin to swing , vast . and he be a man without a head , move like a dark wind over the face of the dark water . 

 ' be it perfect ? ' 

 ' it be perfect . ' 

 ' who live ? ' 

 ' who - ! ' 

 Cipriano no long know . 

 Ram n bind he fast round the middle , then , press his head against the hip , fold the arm round Cipriano 's loin , close with his hand the secret place . 

 ' Cipriano ? ' 

 ' yes . ' 

 ' be it all dark ? ' 

 but Cipriano could not answer . the last circle be sweeping round , and the breath upon the water be sink into the water , there be no more utterance . Ram n kneel with press head and arm and hand , for some moment still . then he bind the loin , bind the wrist to the hip . 

 Cipriano stand rigid and motionless . Ram n clasp the two knee with his hand , till they be warm , and he feel they dark and asleep like two live stone , or two egg . then swiftly he bind they together , and grasp the ankle , as one might grasp the base of a young tree , as it emerge from the earth . crouch on the earth , he grip they in an intense grip , rest his head on the foot . the moment pass , and both man be unconscious . 

 then Ram n bind the ankle , lift Cipriano suddenly , with a sleep - move softness , lay he on the skin of a big mountain - lion , which be spread upon the blanket , throw over he the red and black serape of Huitzilopochtli , and lie down at his foot , hold Cipriano 's foot to his own abdomen . 

 and both man pass into perfect unconsciousness , Cipriano within the womb of undisturbed creation , Ram n in the death sleep . 

 how long they be both dark , they never know . it be twilight . Ram n be suddenly arouse by the jerking of Cipriano 's foot . he sit up , and take the blanket off Cipriano 's face . 

 ' be it night ? ' say Cipriano . 

 ' almost night , ' say Ram n. 

 Silence follow , while Ram n unfasten the bond , begin at the foot . before he unbound the eye , he close the window , so the room be almost dark . then he unfasten the last binding , and Cipriano sit up , look , then suddenly cover his eye . 

 ' make it quite dark ! ' he say . 

 Ram n close the shutter , and the room be complete night . then he return and sit on the mat by Cipriano . Cipriano be asleep again . after a while , Ram n leave he . 

 he do not see he again till dawn . then Ram n find he go down to the lake , to swim . the two man swam together , while the sun rise . with the rain , the lake be colder . they go to the house to rub oil in their limb . 

 Cipriano look at Ram n with black eye which seem to be look at all space . 

 ' I go far , ' he say . 

 ' to where there be no beyond ? ' say Ram n. 

 ' yes , there . ' 

 and in a moment or two , Cipriano be wrap in his blanket again , and asleep . 

 he do not wake till the afternoon . then he eat , and take a boat , and row down the lake to Kate . he find she at home . she be surprised to see he , in his white clothe and with his serape of Huitzilopochtli . 

 ' I be go to be the living Huitzilopochtli , ' he say . 

 ' be you ? when ? do it feel queer ? ' - Kate be afraid of his eye ; they seem inhuman . 

 ' on Thursday . the day of Huitzilopochtli be to be Thursday . will not   you sit beside I , and be wife of I when I be a god ? ' 

 ' but do you feel you be a god ? ' she ask , querulous . 

 he turn his eye on she strangely . 

 ' I have be , ' he say . ' and I have come back . but I belong there , where I go . ' 

 ' where ? ' 

 ' where there be no beyond , and the darkness sink into the water , and wake and sleeping be one thing . ' 

 ' no , ' say Kate , afraid . ' I never understand mystical thing . they make I uneasy . ' 

 ' be it mystical when I come in to you ? ' 

 ' no , ' say Kate . ' surely , that be physical . ' 

 ' so be the other , only far . will not   you be the bride of Huitzilopochtli ? ' he ask again . 

 ' not so soon , ' say Kate . 

 ' not so soon ! ' he re - echo . 

 there be a pause . 

 ' will you come back with I to Jamiltepec now ? ' he ask . 

 ' not now , ' she say . 

 ' why not now ? ' 

 ' oh , I do not   know . - you treat I as if I have no life of my own , ' she say . ' but I have . ' 

 ' a life of your own ? who give it you ? where do you get it ? ' 

 ' I do not   know . but I have get it . and I must live it . I can not   be just swallow up . ' 

 ' why , Malintzi ? ' he say , give she a name . ' why can not   you ? ' 

 ' be just swallow up ? ' she say . ' well , I just can not . ' 

 ' I be the live Huitzilopochtli , ' he say . ' and I be swallow up . I think , so could you be , malintzi . ' 

 ' no ! not quite ! ' she say . 

 ' not quite ! not quite ! not now ! not just now ! how often you say not , to - day ! - I must go back to Ram n. ' 

 ' yes . go back to he . you only care about he , and your live Quetzalcoatl and your living Huitzilopochtli . - I be only a woman . ' 

 ' no , Malintzi , you be more . you be more than Kate , you be malintzi . ' 

 ' I be not ! I be only Kate , and I be only a woman . I mistrust all that other stuff . ' 

 ' I be more than just a man , Malintzi . - do not   you see that ? ' 

 ' no ! ' say Kate . ' I do not   see it . why should you be more than just a man ? ' 

 ' because I be the live Huitzilopochtli . do not   I tell you ? you have   get dust in your mouth to - day , Malintzi . ' 

 he go away , leave she rock in anger on her terrace , in love again with her old self , and hostile to the new thing . she be think of London and Paris and New York , and all the people there . 

 ' oh ! ' she cry to herself , stifle . ' for heaven 's sake let I get out of this , and back to simple human people . I loathe the very sound of Quetzalcoatl and Huitzilopochtli . I would die rather than be mix up in it any more . horrible , really , both Ram n and Cipriano . and they want to put it over I , with their high - fly bunk , and their Malintzi . Malintzi ! I be Kate Forrester , really . I be neither Kate Leslie nor Kate Tylor . I be sick of these man put name over I . I be bear Kate Forrester , and I shall die Kate Forrester . I want to go home . Loathsome , really , to be call Malintzi . - I have   have it put over I . ' 

 

 

 CHAPTER XXIII 

 Huitzilopochtli 's Night 

 

 they have the Huitzilopochtli ceremony at night , in the wide yard in front of the church . the guard of Huitzilopochtli , in serape of black , red , and yellow stripe , strip like tiger or wasp , stand hold torch of blaze ocote . a tall bonfire be build , but unkindle , in the centre of the yard . 

 in the tower where the bell have be , fire be blaze and the heavy drum of Huitzilopochtli go roll its deep , sinister note . it have be sound all the while since the sun go down . 

 the crowd gather under the tree , outside the gate in front of the church . the church door be close . 

 there be a bang of four firework cannon explode simultaneously , then four rocket shoot up into the sky , lean in the four direction , and explode in shower of red , green , white , and yellow . 

 the church door open , and Cipriano appear , in his brilliant serape of Huitzilopochtli , and with three green parrot feather erect on his brow . he be carry a torch . he stoop and light the big bonfire , then pluck out four blaze brand and toss they to four of his man , who stand wait , naked save for their black breech - cloth . the man catch the brand as they fly , and run in the four direction , to kindle the four bonfire that wait , one in each corner of the yard . 

 the guard have take off their blanket and blouse , and be naked to the red sash . the light drum begin to beat for the dance , and the dance begin , the half - naked man throw their blaze torch whirl in the air , catch they as they come down , dance all the while . Cipriano , in the centre , throw up brand after brand from the fire . 

 now that he be strip of his blanket , his body be see paint in horizontal bar of red and black , while from his mouth go a thin green line , and from his eye a band of yellow . 

 the five fire , build hollow of little tower of ocote faggot , send pure flame in a rush up to the dark sky , illuminate the dancing man , who sing in deep voice as they dance . 

 the fire rush rapidly upwards in flame . the drum beat without cease . and the man of Huitzilopochtli dance on , like demon . meanwhile the crowd sit in the old indian silence , their black eye glitter in the firelight . and gradually the fire begin to die down , the white facade of the church , that have dance also to the yellow flame , begin to go bluish above , merge into the night , rose - colour below , behind the dark shape that dance to the sink fire . 

 suddenly the dance cease , the man throw their serape around they , and sit down . little ocote fire upon the cane tripod flicker here and there , in a silence that last for some minute . then the drum sound , and a man begin to sing , in a clear , defiant voice , the First Song of Huitzilopochtli : 

 

 ' I be Huitzilopochtli , 
 the Red Huitzilopochtli , 
 the blood - red . 

 I be Huitzilopochtli , 
 Yellow of the sun , 
 Sun in the blood . 

 I be Huitzilopochtli , 
 White of the bone , 
 bone in the blood . 

 I be Huitzilopochtli , 
 with a blade of grass between my tooth . 

 I be Huitzilopochtli , sit in the dark . 
 with my redness stain the body of the dark . 

 I watch by the fire . 
 I wait behind man . 

 in the stillness of my night 
 the cactus sharpen his thorn . 
 the grass feel with his root for the other sun . 

 Deeper than the root of the mango tree 
 down in the centre of the earth 
 be the yellow , serpent - yellow shining of my sun . 

 oh , beware of he ! 
 oh , beware of I ! 
 who run athwart my serpent - flame 
 get bite and must die . 

 I be the sleeping and wake 
 of the anger of the manhood of man . 
 I be the leaping and quaking 
 of fire bent back again . ' 

 

 the song come to an end . there be a pause . then all the man of Huitzilopochtli take it up again , change the ' I ' into ' he . ' 

 

 ' he be Huitzilopochtli , 
 the Red Huitzilopochtli , 
 the blood - red . 

 he be Huitzilopochtli , 
 Yellow of the sun , 
 Sun in the blood . 

 he be Huitzilopochtli , 
 White of the bone , 
 bone in the blood . 

 he be Huitzilopochtli , 
 with a blade of green grass between his tooth . 

 he be Huitzilopochtli , sit in the dark , 
 with his redness stain the body of the night . 

 he be watch by the fire . 
 wait behind man . 

 in the stillness of his night 
 cactus sharpen their thorn . 
 Grass feel downwards with his root . 

 Deeper than the root of the mango tree 
 down in the centre of the earth 
 Shines the yellow , serpent - yellow shining of the sun . 

 oh , man , take care , take care ! 
 take care of he and it . 
 nor run aslant his ray . 
 who be bite , die . 

 he be Huitzilopochtli , sleep or wake 
 Serpent in the belly of man . 
 Huitzilopochtli , leaping and quake 
 Fire of the passion of man . ' 

 

 the big fire have all die down . only the little flame on the tripod light up the scene with a ruddy glow . the guard withdraw to the outer wall of the yard , hold bayonet erect . the big drum be go alone , slowly . 

 the yard be now a clear space , with the glow red heap of the bonfire , and the ocote flame flap . and now be see a platform erect against the white wall of the church . 

 in the silence the big door of the church open , and Cipriano come out , in his bright serape , hold in his hand a bunch of black leaf , or feather , and with a tuft of scarlet feather , black - tip , rise from the back of his head . he mount the platform and stand face the crowd , the light of a torch on his face and on the brilliant feather that rise like flame from the back of his head . 

 after he come a strange procession : a peon in floppy white clothe , lead prisoner between two of the guard of Huitzilopochtli : who wear their serape with red and black and yellow and white and green stripe : then another peon prisoner : then another : in all , five , the fifth one tall , limping , and with a red cross paint on the breast of his white jacket . last of all come a woman - prisoner , likewise between two guard , her hair flow loose , over a red tunic . 

 they mount the platform . the peon , prisoner , be place in a row , their guard behind they . the limping peon be apart , with his two guard behind he : the woman again be apart , her two guard behind she . 

 the big drum cease , and a bugle ring out , a long , loud triumphant note , repeat three time . then the kettle - drum , or the small tom - tom like kettle - drum , rattle fierce as hail . 

 Cipriano lift his hand , and there be silence . 

 out of the silence he begin to speak , in his short , martial sentence : 

 

 ' man that be man be more than a man . 
 no man be man till he be more than a man . 
 till the power be in he 
 which be not his own . 

 the power be in I from behind the sun , 
 and from middle earth . 
 I be Huitzilopochtli . 
 I be dark as the sunless under - earth , 
 and yellow as the fire that consume , 
 and white as bone , 
 and red as blood . 

 but I touch the hand of Quetzalcoatl . 
 and between our finger rise a blade of green grass . 
 I touch the hand of Quetzalcoatl . 
 Lo ! I be lord of the watch of the night 
 and the dream of the night rise from I like a red feather . 

 I be the watcher , and master of the dream . 
 in the dream of the night I see the grey dog prowl . 
 prowl to devour the dream . 

 in the night the soul of a coward creep out of he 
 like a grey dog whose mouth be foul with rabie , 
 creep among the sleeping and the dreaming , who be lap in my dark , 
 and in whom the dream sit up like a rabbit , lift long ear tip with night , 
 on the dream - slope browsing like a deer in the dusk . 

 in the night I see the grey dog creep , out of the sleep man 
 who be coward , who be liar , who be traitor , who have no dream 
 that prick their ear like a rabbit , or browse in the dark like deer , 
 but whose dream be dog , grey dog with yellow mouth . 
 from the liar , from the thief , from the false and treacherous and mean 
 I see the grey dog creep out , where my deer be browse in the dark . 
 then I take my knife , and throw it upon the grey dog . 
 and lo ! it stick between the rib of a man ! 
 the house of the grey dog ! 

 beware ! beware ! 
 of the man and the woman who walk among you . 
 you know not how many be house of grey dog . 
 man that seem harmless , woman with fair word , 
 maybe they kennel the grey dog . ' 

 

 the drum begin to beat and the singer begin to sing , clear and pure : 

 

 the song of the GREY DOG 

 

 ' when you sleep and know it not 
 the grey dog creep among you . 
 in your sleep , you twist , your soul hurt you . 
 the grey dog be chew your entrail . 

 then call on Huitzilopochtli : 
 the grey dog catch I at the cross - road 
 as I go down the road of sleep 
 and cross the road of the uneasy . 

 the grey dog leap at my entrail . 
 Huitzilopochtli , call he off . 
 Lo ! the Great one answer . track he down ! 
 kill he in his unclean house . 

 down the road of the uneasy 
 you track the grey dog home 
 to his house in the heart of a traitor , 
 a thief , a murderer of dream . 

 and you kill he there with one stroke , 
 Crying : Huitzilopochtli , be this well do ? 
 that your sleep be not as a cemetery 
 where dog creep unclean . ' 

 

 the song cease , and there be silence . then Cipriano beckon to the man to bring forward the peon with the black cross paint on his front and back . he limp forward . 

 Cipriano : ' what man be that , limp ? ' 

 guard : ' it be Guillermo , overseer of Don Ram n , who betray Don Ram n , his master . ' 

 Cipriano : ' why do he limp ? ' 

 guard : ' he fall from the window on to the rock . ' 

 Cipriano : ' what make he wish to betray his master ? ' 

 guard : ' his heart be a grey dog , and a woman , a grey bitch , entice he forth . ' 

 Cipriano : ' what woman entice the grey dog forth ? ' 

 the guard come forward with the woman . 

 guard : ' this woman , Maraca , my Lord , with the grey bitch heart . ' 

 Cipriano : ' be it she , indeed ? ' 

 guard : ' it be she . ' 

 Cipriano : ' the grey dog , and the grey bitch , we kill , for their mouth be yellow with poison , be it well , man of Huitzilopochtli ? ' 

 guard : ' it be very well , my Lord . ' 

 the guard strip the peon Guillermo of his white clothe , leave he naked , in a grey loin - cloth , with a grey - white cross paint on his naked breast . the woman , too , have a grey - white cross paint on her body . she stand in a short petticoat of grey wool . 

 Cipriano : ' the grey dog and the grey bitch shall run no more about the world . we will bury their body in quick - lime , till their soul be eat , and their body , and nothing be leave . for lime be the thirsty bone that swallow even a soul and be not slake . - bind they with the grey cord , put ash on their head . ' 

 the guard quickly obey . the prisoner , ash - grey , gaze with black , glitter eye , make not a sound . a guard stand behind each of they . Cipriano give a sign , and quick as lightne the guard have get the throat of the two victim in a grey cloth , and with a sharp jerk have break their neck , lift they backwards in one movement . the grey cloth they tie hard and tight round the throat , lay the twitch body on the floor . 

 Cipriano turn to the crowd : 

 

 ' the Lords of Life be the Masters of Death . 
 Blue be the breath of Quetzalcoatl . 
 Red be Huitzilopochtli 's blood . 
 but the grey dog belong to the ash of the world . 
 the Lords of Life be the Masters of Death . 
 Dead be the grey dog . 
 living be the Lords of Life . 
 Blue be the deep sky and the deep water . 
 Red be the blood and the fire . 
 Yellow be the flame . 
 the bone be white and alive . 
 the hair of night be dark over our face . 
 but the grey dog be among the ash . 
 the Lords of Life be the Masters of Death . ' 

 

 then he turn once more , to the other , imprison peon . 

 Cipriano : ' who be these four ? ' 

 guard : ' four who come to kill Don Ram n. ' 

 Cipriano : ' four man , against one man ? ' 

 guard : ' they be more than four , my Lord . ' 

 Cipriano : ' when many man come against one , what be the name of the many ? ' 

 guard : ' coward , my Lord . ' 

 Cipriano : ' coward it be . they be less than man . man that be less than man be not good enough for the light of the sun . if man that be man will live , man that be less than man must be put away , lest they multiply too much . man that be more than man have the judgment of man that be less than man . shall they die ? ' 

 guard : ' they shall surely die , my Lord . ' 

 Cipriano : ' yet my hand have touch the hand of Quetzalcoatl , and among the black leaf one spring green , with the colour of Malintzi . ' 

 an attendant come and lift Cipriano 's serape over his head , leave his body bare to the waist . the guard likewise take off their serape . 

 Cipriano lift up his fist , in which he hold a little tuft of black feather , or leaf . 

 then he say slowly : 

 

 Huitzilopochtli give the black blade of death . 
 take it bravely . 
 take death bravely . 
 go bravely across the border , admit your mistake . 

 determine to go on and on , till you enter the Morning Star . 
 Quetzalcoatl will show you the way . 
 Malintzi of the green dress will open the door . 

 in the fountain you will lie down . 
 if you reach the fountain , and lie down 
 and the fountain cover your face , forever , 
 you will have depart forever from your mistake . 

 and the man that be more than a man in you 
 will wake at last from the clean forgetting 
 and stand up , and look about he , 
 ready again for the business of be a man . 

 but Huitzilopochtli touch the hand of Quetzalcoatl 
 and one green leaf spring among the black . 
 the green leaf of Malintzi 
 who pardon once , and no more . 

 

 Cipriano turn to the four peon . he hold out his fist with the four black twig , to the first . this first one , a little man , peer at the leaf curiously . 

 ' there be no green one , ' he say sceptically . 

 ' good ! ' say Cipriano . ' then receive a black . ' 

 and he hand he a black leaf . 

 ' I know it , ' say the man , and he throw the leaf away with contempt and defiance . 

 the second man draw a black leaf . he stand gaze at it , as if fascinated , turn it round . 

 the third man draw a leaf whose low half be green . 

 ' see ! ' say Cipriano . ' the green leaf of Malintzi ! ' 

 and he hand the last black leaf to the last man . 

 ' have I get to die ? ' say the last man . 

 ' yes . ' 

 ' I do not   want to die , Patr n. ' 

 ' you play with death , and it have spring upon you . ' 

 the eye of the three man be blindfold with black cloth , their blouse and pantaloon be take away . Cipriano take a bright , thin dagger . 

 ' the Lords of Life be Masters of death , ' he say in a loud , clear voice . 

 and swift as lightning he stab the blindfolded man to the heart , with three swift , heavy stab . then he lift the red dagger and throw it down . 

 ' the Lords of Life be Masters of death , ' he repeat . 

 the guard lift the bleed body one by one , and carry they into the church . there remain only the one prisoner , with the green leaf . 

 ' put the green leaf of Malintzi between his brow ; for Malintzi pardon once , and no more , ' say Cipriano . 

 ' yes , my Lord ! ' reply the guard . 

 and they lead the man away into the church . 

 Cipriano follow , the last of his guard after he . 

 in a few minute the drum begin to beat and man come slowly stream into the church . woman be not admit . all the interior be hang with red and black banner . at the side of the chancel be a new idol : a heavy , seat figure of Huitzilopochtli , do in black lava stone . and round he burn twelve red candle . the idol hold the bunch of black strip , or leaf , in his hand . and at his foot lie the five dead body . 

 the fire on the altar be flicker high , to the dark statue of Quetzalcoatl . on his little throne Ram n sit , wear his blue and white colour of Quetzalcoatl . there be another corresponding throne next he , but it be empty . six of the guard of Quetzalcoatl stand by Ram n : but Huitzilopochtli 's side of the chancel be empty save for the dead . 

 the hard drum of Huitzilopochtli be beat incessantly outside , with a noise like madness . inside be the soft roll of the drum of Quetzalcoatl . and the man from the crowd outside throng slowly in , between the guard of Quetzalcoatl . 

 a flute sound the summon to close the door . the drum of Quetzalcoatl cease , and from the tower be hear again the wild bugle of Huitzilopochtli . 

 then down the centre of the church , in silence , barefoot , come the procession of Huitzilopochtli , naked save for the black loin - cloth and the paint , and the scarlet feather of the head - dress . Cipriano have his face paint with a white jaw , a thin band of green stretch from his mouth , a band of black across his nose , yellow from his eye , and scarlet on his brow . one green feather rise from his forehead , and behind his head a beautiful head - dress of scarlet feather . a band of red be paint round his breast , yellow round his middle . the rest be ash - grey . 

 after he come his guard , their face red , black , and white , their body paint as Cipriano 's , and a scarlet feather rise from the back of their head . the hard , dry drum of Huitzilopochtli beat monotonously . 

 as the Living Huitzilopochtli come near the altar step , the Living Quetzalcoatl rise and come to meet he . the two salute , each cover his eye with his left hand for a moment , then touch finger with the right hand . 

 Cipriano stand before the statue of Huitzilopochtli , dip his hand in a stone bowl , and give the loud cry or whoop of Huitzilopochtli , lift up his red hand . his guard utter the loud cry , and quickly file past , each man dip his hand and raise his wet , red fist . the hard drum of Huitzilopochtli rattle like madness in the church , then fall suddenly silent . 

 Ram n : ' why be your hand red , Huitzilopochtli , my brother ? ' 

 Cipriano : ' it be the blood of the treacherous , Oh Quetzalcoatl . ' 

 Ram n : ' what have they betray ? ' 

 Cipriano : ' the yellow sun and the heart of darkness ; the heart of man , and the bud of woman . while they live , the Morning Star could not be see . ' 

 Ram n : ' and be they verily dead ? ' 

 Cipriano : ' verily dead , my Lord . ' 

 Ram n : ' their blood be shed ? ' 

 Cipriano : ' yes , my Lord , save that the grey dog shed no blood . two die the bloodless death of the grey dog , three die in blood . ' 

 Ram n : ' give I the blood of the three , my brother Huitzilopochtli , to sprinkle the fire . ' 

 Cipriano bring the stone bowl , and the little bunch of black leaf from Huitzilopochtli 's idol . ram n slowly , gently , sprinkle a little blood on the fire , with the black leaf . 

 Ram n : ' darkness , drink the blood of expiation . Sun , swallow up the blood of expiation . rise , Morning Star , between the divide sea . ' 

 he give back the bowl and the leaf to Huitzilopochtli , who place they by the black idol . 

 Ram n : ' Thou who didst take the life of the three , Huitzilopochtli , my brother , what wilt thou do with the soul ? ' 

 Cipriano : ' even give they to thee , my Lord , Quetzalcoatl , my Lord of the Morning Star . ' 

 Ram n : ' yea , give they to I and I will wrap they in my breath and send they the long journey , to the sleep and the far awakening . ' 

 Cipriano : ' my Lord be lord of two way . ' 

 the naked , paint guard of Huitzilopochtli come and carry the dead body of the three stab man , carry they on red bier , and lay they at the foot of the Quetzalcoatl statue . 

 Ram n : ' so , there be a long way to go , past the sun to the gate of the Morning Star . and if the sun be angry he strike swifter than a jaguar , and the whirr of the wind be like an angry eagle , and the upper water strike in wrath like silver - colour snake . ah , three soul , make peace now with the sun and wind and water , and go in courage , with the breath of Quetzalcoatl around you like a cloak . fear not and shrink not and fail not ; but come to the end of the long journey , and let the fountain cover your face . so shall all at length be make new . ' 

 when he have speak to the dead , Ram n take incense and throw it on the fire , so cloud of blue smoke arise . then with a censer he swing the blue smoke over the dead . then he unfold three blue cloth and cover the dead . then the guard of Quetzalcoatl lift the bier , and the flute of Quetzalcoatl sound . 

 ' salute the Morning Star ! ' cry Ram n , turn to the light beyond the statue of Quetzalcoatl , and throw up his right arm in the Quetzalcoatl prayer . every man turn to the light and throw up his arm in the passion . and the silence of the Morning Star fill the church . 

 the drum of Quetzalcoatl sound : the guard slowly move away with the three blue - wrap dead . 

 then come the voice of the Living Huitzilopochtli : 

 ' upon the dead grey dog the face of Quetzalcoatl can not look . upon the corps of grey dog rise no Morning Star . but the fire of corps shall consume they . ' 

 there be a sharp rattle of the dry drum of Huitzilopochtli . Ram n remain with his back to the church , his arm upraise to the Morning Star . and the guard of Huitzilopochtli lift the strangled body , lay they on bier , cover they with grey cloth , and bear they away . 

 the bugle of Huitzilopochtli sound . 

 Cipriano : ' the dead be on their way . Quetzalcoatl help they on the long journey . - but the grey dog sleep within the quick - lime , in the slow corpse - fire . - it be finish . ' 

 Ram n drop his arm and turn to the church . all man drop their hand . the soft drum of Quetzalcoatl sound , mingle with the hard drum of Huitzilopochtli . then both guard begin to sing together :
