 CHAPTER XXIV 

 Malintzi 

 

 when the woman be shut out of the church , Kate go home gloomy and uneasy . the execution shock and depress she . she know that Ram n and Cipriano do deliberately what they do : they believe in their deed , they act with all their conscience . and as man , probably they be right . 

 but they seem nothing but man . when Cipriano say : man that be man be more than a man , he seem to be drive the male significance to its utmost , and beyond , with a sort of demonism . it seem to she all terrible will , the exertion of pure , awful will . 

 and deep in her soul come a revulsion against this manifestation of pure will . it be fascinating also . there be something dark and lustrous and fascinating to she in Cipriano , and in Ram n. the black , relentless power , even passion of the will in man ! the strange , sombre , lustrous beauty of it ! she know herself under the spell . 

 at the same time , as be so often the case with any spell , it do not bind she completely . she be spellbound , but not utterly acquiescent . in one corner of her soul be revulsion and a touch of nausea . 

 Ram n and Cipriano no doubt be right for themselves , for their people and country . but for herself , ultimately , ultimately she belong elsewhere . not to this terrible , natural will which seem to beat its wing in the very air of the american continent . always will , will , will , without remorse or relent . this be America to she : all the Americas . sheer will ! 

 the will of God ! she begin to understand that once fearsome phrase . at the centre of all thing , a dark , momentous will send out its terrific ray and vibration , like some vast octopus . and at the other end of the vibration , man , create man , erect in the dark potency , answer Will with will , like god or demon . 

 it be wonderful too . but where be woman , in this terrible interchange of will ? truly only a subservient , instrumental thing : the soft stone on which the man sharpen the knife of his relentless volition : the soft lode - stone to magnetize his blade of steel and keep all its molecule alive in the electric flow . 

 ah , yes , it be wonderful . it be , as Ram n say , a manifestation , a manifestation of the Godhead . but to the Godhead as a sheer and awful will she could not respond . 

 Joachim , let himself be bleed to death for people who would profit nothing by his sacrifice , he be the other extreme . the black and magnificent pride of will which come out of the volcanic earth of Mexico have be unknown to he . he be one of the white , self - sacrifice god . hence her bitterness . and hence , naturally , the spell of beauty and lustrous satisfaction which Cipriano could cast over she . she be in love with he , when he be with she ; in his arm , she be quite go in his spell . she be the deep , slumbrous lodestone which set all his bone glitter with the energy of relentless pride . and she herself derive a great gratification in the embrace , a sense of passive , downward - sink power , profound . 

 yet she could not be purely this , this thing of sheer reciprocity . surely , though her woman 's nature be reciprocal to his male , surely it be more than that ! surely he and she be not two potent and reciprocal current between which the Morning Star flash like a spark out of nowhere . surely this be not it ? surely she have one tiny Morning Star inside she , which be herself , her own very soul and star - self ! 

 but he would never admit this . the tiny star of her very self he would never see . to he she be but the answer to his call , the sheath for his blade , the cloud to his lightning , the earth to his rain , the fuel to his fire . 

 alone , she be nothing . only as the pure female corresponding to his pure male , do she signify . 

 as an isolated individual , she have little or no significance . as a woman on her own , she be repulsive , and even evil , to he . she be not real till she be reciprocal . 

 to a great extent this be true , and she know it . to a great extent , the same be true of he , and without she to give he the power , he too would not achieve his own manhood and meaning . with she or without she , he would be beyond ordinary man , because the power be in he . but fail she , he would never make his ultimate achievement , he would never be whole . he would be chiefly an instrument . 

 he know this too : though perhaps not well enough . he would strive to keep she , to have she , for his own fulfilment . he would not let she go . 

 but that little star of her own single self , would he ever recognize that ? Nay , do he even recognize any single star of his own being ? do he not conceive of himself as a power and a potency on the face of the earth , an embodied will , like a rush dark wind ? and hence , inevitably , she be but the stone of rest to his potency , his bed of sleep , the cave and lair of his male will . 

 what else ? to he there be nothing else . the star ! Don Ram n 's Morning Star be something that spring between he and she and hung shin , the strange third thing that be both of they and neither of they , between his night and her day . 

 be it true ? be she nothing , nothing , by herself ? and he , alone , fail his last manhood , without she be he nothing , or next to nothing ? as a fig tree which grow up , but never come to flower . 

 be this thing true , the same of both of they ? - that alone , they be next to nothing ? each of they , separate , next to nothing . apart in a sort of grey , mechanical twilight , without a star ? 

 and together , in strange reciprocity , flash darkly till the Morning Star rise between they ? 

 he would say to she , as Ram n have say of Carlota : ' soul ! no , you have no soul of your own . you have at good only half a soul . it take a man and a woman together to make a soul . the soul be the Morning Star , emerge from the two . one alone can not have a soul . ' 

 this Ram n say . and she know it convey what Cipriano really feel . Cipriano could not see Kate as a being by herself . and if he live a thousand more year , he would never see she as such . he would see she only as reciprocal to himself . as the balance of he , and the correspondence on the other side of heaven . 

 ' let the Morning Star rise between we , ' he would say . ' alone you be nothing , and I be manqué . but together we be the wing of the morning . ' 

 be it true ? be this the final answer to man 's assertion of individuality ? 

 be it true ? and be it her sacred duty to sit beside he in the green dress of Malintzi , in the church , the goddess admit her halfness ? her halfness ! be there no star of the single soul ? be that all an illusion ? 

 be the individual an illusion ? Man , any man , every man , by himself just a fragment , know no Morning Star ? and every woman the same ; by herself , starless and fragmentary . even in the relation to the innermost God , still fragmentary and unblest . 

 be it true , that the gate be the Morning Star , the only entrance to the innermost ? and the Morning Star rise between the two , and between the many , but never from one alone . 

 and be a man but a dark and arrowy will , and woman the bow from which the arrow be shoot ? the bow without the arrow be as nothing , and the arrow without the bow only a short - range dart , ineffectual ? 

 Poor Kate , it be hard to have to reflect this . it mean a submission she have never make . it mean the death of her individual self . it mean abandon so much , even her own very foundation . for she have believe truly that every man and every woman alike be found on the individual . 

 now , must she admit that the individual be an illusion and a falsification ? there be no such animal . except in the mechanical world . in the world of machine , the individual machine be effectual . the individual , like the perfect being , do not and can not exist , in the vivid world . we be all fragment . and at the good , half . the only whole thing be the Morning Star . which can only rise between two : or between many . 

 and man can meet only in the light of the Morning Star . 

 she think again of Cipriano and the execution , and she cover her hand over her face . be this the knife to which she must be sheath ? be it such a star of power and relentlessness that must rise between she and he ? he naked and paint , with his soldier , dancing and sweating and shout among they . herself unseen and nowhere ! 

 as she sit rock in her terrible loneliness and misgiving , she hear the drum on the tower , and the sound of rocket . she go to the gate . over the church , in the night sky , hang a spangling cloud of red and blue fire , the colour of Huitzilopochtli and Quetzalcoatl . the night of Huitzilopochtli would be over . the sky be dark again , and there be all the star , beyond , far , far beyond where the spangling have be . 

 she go indoor again , to retire . the servant have all run out to see the rocket . Ezequiel would be in with the man in church . 

 she hear footstep on the gravel walk , and suddenly Cipriano stand in the doorway , in his white clothe . he take off his hat , quickly . his black eye be sparkle , almost blaze to she , with a flashing of light such as she have never see . there be still smear of paint on his face . in the blazing of his eye he seem to be smile to she , but in a dazzling , childish way . 

 ' Malintzi , ' he say to she in Spanish . ' oh , come ! come and put on the green dress . I can not be the Living Huitzilopochtli without a bride . I can not be it , Malintzi ! ' 

 he stand before she , flickering and flash and strangely young , vulnerable , as young and boyish as flame . she see that when the fire come free in he , he would be like this always , flickering , flash with a flame of virgin youth . now , not will at all . sensitive as a boy . and call she only with his boyish flame . the living , flickering , fiery Wish . this be first . the Will she have see be subsidiary and instrumental , the Wish in armour . 

 she have be so used to fight for her own soul with individualistic man , that for a moment she feel old , and uncertain . the strange , flash vulnerability in he , the nakedness of the live Wish , disconcert she . she be use to man who have themselves well in hand , and be seek their own end as individual . 

 ' where do you want I to come ? ' she say . 

 ' to the church , ' he say . ' it be mine to - night . I be Huitzilopochtli : but I can not be it alone , ' he add with quick , wistful , watchful smile , as if all his flesh be flicker with delicate fire . 

 Kate wrap herself in a dark tartan shawl and go with he . he step quickly , in the short , indian way . the night be very dark . down on the beach some firework be flame , and the people be all watch . 

 they enter the yard of the church from the back , by the priest 's little gate . soldier be already roll up in their blanket , sleep under the wall . Cipriano open the little vestry door . Kate pass into the darkness . he follow , light a candle . 

 ' my soldier know I be watch to - night in the church , ' he say . ' they will keep guard . ' 

 the body of the church be quite dark , but the bluish white light burn above the statue of Quetzalcoatl , give not much light . 

 Cipriano lift his candle to the black statue of Huitzilopochtli . then he turn to Kate , his black eye flash . 

 ' I be Huitzilopochtli , Malintzi , ' he say in his low , indian Spanish . ' but I can not be it without you . stay with I , Malintzi . say you be the bride of the Living Huitzilopochtli . ' 

 ' yes ! ' she reply , ' I say it . ' 

 convulsive flame of joy and triumph seem to go over his face . he light two candle in front of Huitzilopochtli . 

 ' come ! ' he say . ' put on the green dress . ' 

 he take she to the vestry , where be many folded serape , and the silver bowl and other implement of the church , and leave she while she put on the dress of Malintzi she have wear when Ram n marry they . 

 when she step out she find Cipriano naked and in his paint , before the statue of Huitzilopochtli , on a rug of jaguar skin . 

 ' I be the live Huitzilopochtli , ' he murmur to she in a sort of ecstasy . 

 ' you be malintzi , ' he say . ' the bride of Huitzilopochtli . ' 

 the convulsion of exultance go over his face . he take her hand in his left hand , and they stand face the bluish light . 

 ' cover your face ! ' he say to she . 

 they cover their face in the salute . 

 ' now salute Quetzalcoatl . ' and he fling up his arm . she hold out her left hand , in the woman 's salute . 

 then they turn to the statue of Huitzilopochtli . 

 ' Salute Huitzilopochtli ! ' he say , bring his right fist down with a smash in the palm of his left hand . but this be the male salute . he teach she to press her hand together in front of her breast , then shoot they out towards the idol . 

 then he put a little lamp of earthenware between the foot of Huitzilopochtli . from the right knee of the idol he take a little black vessel of oil , make she take a little white vessel from the god 's left knee . 

 ' now , ' he say , ' together we fill the lamp . ' 

 and together they pour the oil from their little pitcher , into the saucer - shape lamp . 

 ' now together we light it , ' he say . 

 he take one of the two candle burn before the black idol , she take the other , and with the flame dripping and leap together , they kindle the float wick of the lamp . it burn in a round blue bud , then rise higher . 

 ' blow out your candle , ' he say . ' it be our Morning Star . ' 

 they blow out the two candle . it be almost dark now , with the slow light , like a snow - drop , of their united life float between the foot of Huitzilopochtli , and the everlasting - light burn small and bluish beyond the statue of Quetzalcoatl . 

 at the foot of the altar , beside the chair of Huitzilopochtli , a third chair be place . 

 ' sit in your throne of Malintzi , ' he say to she . 

 they sit side by side , his hand hold her hand , in complete silence , look down the dark church . he have place tuft of greenish flower , like thin , greenish lilac , above her chair , and their perfume be like a dream , strong , overpoweringly sweet on the darkness . 

 strange how naïve he be ! he be not like Ram n , rather ponderous and deliberate in his ceremonial . Cipriano in his own little deed to - night with she , be naïve like a child . she could hardly look at that bud of light which he say mean their united life , without a catch at her heart . it burn so soft and round , and he have such an implicit , childish satisfaction in its symbol . it all give he a certain wild , childish joy . the strange convulsion like flame of joy and gratification go over his face ! 

 ' ah , God ! ' she think . ' there be more way than one of become like a little child . ' 

 the flaminess and the magnificence of the beginning : this be what Cipriano want to bring to his marriage . the reel , powerful perfume of those invisible green flower , that the peon call buena de noche : good by night . 

 Strange - that which he bring to marriage be something flamey and unabashed , forever virginal . not , as she have always know in man , yearn and seek his own end . naïvely bring his flame to her flame . 

 as she sit in that darken church in the intense perfume of flower , in the seat of Malintzi , watch the bud of her life unite with his , between the foot of the idol , and feel his dark hand softly hold her own , with the soft , deep indian heat , she feel her own childhood come back on she . the year seem to be reel away in great circle , fall away from she . 

 leave she sit there like a girl in her first adolescence . the Living Huitzilopochtli ! ah , easily he be the live Huitzilopochtli . More than anything . More than Cipriano , more than a male man , he be the living Huitzilopochtli . and she be the goddess bride , Malintzi of the green dress . 

 ah , yes , it be childish . but it be actually so . she be perhaps fourteen year old , and he be fifteen . and he be the young Huitzilopochtli , and she be the bride Malintzi , the bride - girl . she have see it . when the flame come up in he and lick he all over , he be young and vulnerable as a boy of fifteen , and he would always be so , even when he be seventy . 

 and this be her bridegroom . here at last he be not a will . when he come clothe in his own free flame , it be not will that clothe he . let he be a general , an executioner , what he like , in the world . the flame of their united life be a naked bud of flame . their marriage be a young , vulnerable flame . 

 so he sit in silence on his throne , hold her hand in silence till the year reel away from she in flee circle , and she sit , as every real woman can sit , no matter at what age , a girl again , and for he , a virgin . he hold her hand in silence , till she be malintzi , and virgin for he , and when they look at one another , and their eye meet , the two flame ripple in oneness . she close her eye , and be dark . 

 then later , when she open her eye and see the bud of flame just above she , and the black idol invisibly crouch , she hear his strange voice , the voice of a boy hiss in naïve ecstasy , in Spanish : 

 ' Miel ! Miel de Malintzi ! - Honey of Malintzi ! ' 

 and she press he to her breast , convulsively . his innermost flame be always virginal , it be always the first time . and it make she again always a virgin girl . she could feel their two flame flow together . 

 how else , she say to herself , be one to begin again , save by re - find one 's virginity ? and when one find one 's virginity , one realize one be among the god . he be of the god , and so be i. why should I judge he ? 

 so , when she think of he and his soldier , tale of swift cruelty she have hear of he : when she remember his stab the three helpless peon , she think : why should I judge he ? he be of the god . and when he come to I he lay his pure , quick flame to mine , and every time I be a young girl again , and every time he take the flower of my virginity , and I his . it leave I insouciante like a young girl . what do I care if he kill people ? his flame be young and clean . he be Huitzilopochtli , and I be malintzi . what do I care , what Cipriano Viedma do or do not   do ? or even what Kate Leslie do or do not   do ! 

 

 

 CHAPTER XXV 

 Teresa 

 

 Ram n somewhat surprised Kate by marry again , a couple of month or so after the death of Doña Carlota . the new bride be a young woman of about twenty - eight , call Teresa . there be a very quiet civil wedding , and Ram n bring his new wife to Jamiltepec . 

 he have know she since she be a child , for she be the daughter of the famous hacienda of Las Yemas , some twelve mile inland from Jamiltepec . Don Tomás , her father , have be a staunch friend of the Carrascos . 

 but Don Tomás have die a year ago , leave the large , flourish tequila hacienda to his three child , to be administer by Teresa . Teresa be the young . her two brother have revert to the usual wasteful , spendthrift , brutal mexican way . therefore Don Tomás , in order to save the hacienda from their destructive hand , have especially appoint Teresa administrador , and have get the brother ' consent to this . after all , they be shiftless ne'er - do - well , and have never show the slight desire to help in the rather burdensome business of manage a large tequila hacienda , during their father 's lifetime . Teresa have be the one . and during her father 's illness the whole charge have devolve on she , while her brother waste themselves and their substance in the squashy prostitution - living of Mexicans of their class , away in the city . 

 no soon be the father dead , however , and Teresa in charge , than home come the two brother , big with their intention to be hacendado . by simple brute force they oust their sister , give order over her head , jeered at she , and in crush she united for once with each other . they be put she back into her place as a woman - that be to say , back into a secluded sort of prostitution , to which , in their eye , woman belong . 

 but they be bully , and , as bully , coward . and like so many Mexicans of that class , soft and suicidal towards themselves . they make friend with judge and general . they ride about in resplendent charro dress , and have motor - load of rather doubtful visitor . 

 against their soft , sensuous brutality Teresa could do nothing , and she know it . they be all soft and sensual , or sensuous , handsome in their way , open - handed , careless , but bully , with no fear at the middle of they . 

 ' make yourself desirable , and get a husband for yourself , ' they say to she . 

 in their eye , her great crime be that she do not make herself desirable to man of their sort . that she have never have a man , that she be not marry , make she almost repulsive to they . what be woman for , but for loose , soft , prostitutional sex ? 

 ' do you want to wear the trouser ? ' they jeer at she . ' no , Señorita ! not while there be two man on the place , you be not go to wear the trouser . no , Señorita ! the trouser , the man wear they . the woman keep under their petticoat that which they be woman for . ' 

 Teresa be use to these insult . but they make her soul burn . 

 ' you , do you want to be an american woman ? ' they say to she . ' go off to America , then , and bob your hair and wear breech . buy a ranch there , and get a husband to take your order . go ! ' 

 she go to her lawyer , but they hold up their hand . and she go to Ram n , whom she have know since she be a child . 

 it would have mean a hopeless and ruinous law - suit , to get the brother eject from the hacienda . it would have mean the rapid ruin of the estate . Ram n instead ask Teresa to marry he , and he carefully arrange her dowry , so that she should always have her own provision . 

 ' it be a country where man despise sex , and live for it , ' say Ram n. ' which be just suicide . ' 

 Ram n come with his wife , to see Kate . Teresa be rather small , pale , with a lot of loose black hair and big , wide black eye . yet in her quiet bearing and her well - close mouth there be an air of independence and authority . she have suffer great humiliation at the hand of her brother , there be still a certain wanness round her eye , the remain of tear of anger and helpless indignation , and the bitterness of insulted sex . but now she love Ram n with a wild , virgin loyalty . that , too , be evident . he have save her sex from the insult , restore it to she in its pride and its beauty . and in return , she feel an almost fierce reverence for he . 

 but with Kate she be shy and rather distant : a little afraid of the travel , experienced , rather assertive white - skinned woman , the woman of the other race . she sit in Kate 's salon in her simple white dress with a black gauze rebozo , her brown hand motionless in her lap , her dark neck erect , her dark , slender , well - shape cheek avert . she seem , Kate think , rather like a little sempstress . 

 but Kate be reckon without that strange quiescent power of authority which Teresa also possess , in her slight , dark body . and without the black , flash glance which rest on she from time to time , from Teresa 's eye , full of search fierceness and fiery misgiving . a fiery soul , in such a demure , slight , dark body . sometimes a muted word come from her mouth , and a constrain smile move her lip . but her burn eye never change . she do not even look at Ram n. 

 ' how much do you charge per word , Chica ? ' he ask she , with a sort of soft fondness .

 CHAPTER XXVI 

 Kate be a Wife 

 

 Kate be glad to get back to her own house , and to be more or less alone . she feel a great change be be work in she , and if it work too violently , she would die . it be the end of something , and the beginning of something , far , far inside she : in her soul and womb . the man , Ram n and Cipriano , cause the change , and Mexico . because the time have come . - nevertheless if what be happen happen too rapidly , or violently , she feel she would die . so , from time to time she have to withdraw from contact , to be alone . 

 she would sit alone for hour on the shore , under a green willow - tree that hang its curtain of pale - green frond , on the beach . the lake be much full and high up the shore , soft , more mysterious . there be a smell of the pile of water - hyacinth decaying at the water 's edge . Distance seem far away . the near conical hill be dot with green bush , like a japanese drawing . Bullock - wagon with solid wheel come roll to the village , high with sugar cane , draw by eight oxen with ponderous head and slowly swing horn , while a peon walk in front , with the guiding - stick on the cross - beam of the yoke . so slow , so massive , yet with such slight control ! 

 she have a strange feeling , in Mexico , of the old prehistoric humanity , the dark - eyed humanity of the day , perhaps , before the glacial period . when the world be cold , and the sea emptier , and all the land - formation be different . when the water of the world be pile in stupendous glacier on the high place , and high , high upon the pole . when great plain stretch away to the ocean , like Atlantis , and the lose continent of Polynesia , so that sea be only great lake , and the soft , dark - eyed people of that world could walk around the globe . then there be a mysterious , hot - blooded , soft - footed humanity with a strange civilization of its own . 

 till the glacier melt , and drive the people to the high place , like the lofty plateaux of Mexico , separate they into cut - off nation . 

 sometimes , in America , the shadow of that old pre - flood world be so strong , that the day of historic humanity would melt out of Kate 's consciousness , and she would begin to approximate to the old mode of consciousness , the old , dark will , the unconcern for death , the subtle , dark consciousness , non - cerebral , but vertebrate . when the mind and the power of man be in his blood and his backbone , and there be the strange , dark inter - communication between man and man and man and beast , from the powerful spine . 

 the Mexicans be still this . that which be aboriginal in America still belong to the way of the world before the Flood , before the mental - spiritual world come into being . in America , therefore , the mental - spiritual life of white people suddenly flourish like a great weed let loose in virgin soil . probably it will as quickly wither . a great death come . and after that , the living result will be a new germ , a new conception of human life , that will arise from the fusion of the old blood - and - vertebrate consciousness with the white man 's present mental - spiritual consciousness . the sinking of both being , into a new being . 

 Kate be more irish than anything , and the almost deathly mysticism of the aboriginal Celtic or iberian people lie at the bottom of her soul . it be a residue of memory , something that live on from the pre - flood world , and can not be kill . something old , and more everlastingly potent , than our would - be fair - and - square world . 

 she know more or less what Ram n be try to effect : this fusion ! she know what it be that make Cipriano more significant to she than all her past , her husband and her child . it be the leap of the old , antediluvian blood - male into unison with she . and for this , without her knowing , her innermost blood have be thud all the time . 

 Ireland would not and could not forget that other old , dark , sumptuous living . the Tuatha De Danaan might be under the western sea . but they be under the live blood , too , never quite to be silence . now they have to come forth again , to a new connection . and the scientific , fair - and - square Europe have to mate once more with the old giant . 

 but the change , Kate feel , must not come on she too soon and too suddenly , or it would rupture she and she would die . the old way have its horror . the heavy - footed ,    terre spirit of aboriginal Mexico could be so horrible to she , as to make her wicked . the slow , indomitable kind of exist and persisting , without hope or élan , which be in the aboriginal American , sometimes make her feel she would go mad . the sullen will persist over the slow , dark century , count the individual existence a trifle ! a tenacity of demon , less than human . and a sudden ferocity , a sudden lust of death rouse incalculable and terrible . 

 People who never really change . man who be not faithful to life , to the living actuality . faithful to some dark necessity out of the past . the actual present suddenly collapse in the soul of the man and the woman , and the old , black , volcanic lava burst up in violence , follow by a lava - rock indifference . 

 the hope ! the hope ! would it ever be possible to revive the hope in these black soul , and achieve the marriage which be the only step to the new world of man ? 

 but meanwhile , a strange , almost tear nausea would come over Kate , and she feel she must go away , to spare herself . the strange , reptilian insistence of her very servant . blood be one blood . we be all of one blood - stream . something aboriginal and tribal , and almost bad than death to the white individual . out of the dark eye and the powerful spine of these people , all the time the unknown assertion : the blood be one blood . it be a strange , overbearing insistence , a claim of blood - unison . 

 Kate be of a proud old family . she have be bring up with the English - germanic idea of the intrinsic superiority of the hereditary aristocrat . her blood be different from the common blood , another , fine fluid . 

 but in Mexico , none of this . her criada Juana , the aguador who carry the water , the boatman who row she on the lake , all look at she with one look in their eye . the blood be one blood . in the blood , you and I be undifferentiated . she see it in their eye , she hear it in their word , it ting their deference and their mockery . and sometimes it make she feel physically sick : this overbearing blood - familiarity . 

 and sometimes , when she try to hold herself up , in the proud old assertion : my blood be my own . noli I tangere , she would see the terrible ancient hatred in their eye , the hatred which lead they to atrocity and fearful maiming . 

 they would defer to her spirit , her knowledge , her understanding . they would give her deference , and a sort of grudging reverence for this . she belong to the rule race , the clever one . but back again they demand her acquiescence to the primeval assertion : the blood be one blood . we be one blood . it be the assertion that sweep away all individualism , and leave she immerse , drown in the grand sea of the live blood , in immediate contact with all these man and all these woman . 

 to this she must submit . or they would persist in the slow revenge . 

 and she could not submit , off - hand . it have to be a slow , organic process . anything sudden or violent would destroy she . 

 now she understand Ram n 's assertion : man be a column of blood : woman be a valley of blood . it be the primeval oneness of mankind , the opposite of the oneness of the spirit . 

 but Kate have always look upon her blood as absolutely her own , her individual own . her spirit she share , in the spirit she commune . but her blood stay by she in individuality . 

 now she be confront by the other great assertion : the blood be one blood . - it mean a strange , marginless death of her individual self . 

 now she understand why Ram n and Cipriano wear the white clothe and the sandal , and be naked , or half - naked , as living god . it be the acquiescence in the primitive assertion . it be the renewal of the old , terrible bond of the blood - unison of man , which make blood - sacrifice so potent a factor of life . the blood of the individual be give back to the great blood - being , the god , the nation , the tribe . 

 now she understand the strange unison she could always feel between Ram n and his man , and Cipriano and his man . it be the soft , quaking , deep communion of blood - oneness . sometimes it make she feel sick . sometimes it make her revolt . but it be the power she could not get beyond . 

 because , admit his blood - unison , Ram n at the same time claim a supremacy , even a godliness . he be a man , as the low of his peon be a man . at the same time , rise from the same pool of blood , from the same root of manhood as they , and be , as they be , a man of the pulsing blood , he be still something more . not in the blood nor in the spirit lie his individuality and his supremacy , his godhead . but in a star within he , an inexplicable star which rise out of the dark sea and shine between the flood and the great sky . the mysterious star which unite the vast universal blood with the universal breath of the spirit , and shin between they both . 

 not the rider on the white horse : nor the rider on the red . that which be beyond the rider and the horse , the inexplicable mystery of the star whence no horseman come and to which no horseman can arrive . the star which be a man 's innermost clue , which rule the power of the blood on the one hand , and the power of the spirit on the other . 

 for this , the only thing which be supreme above all power in a man , and at the same time , be power ; which far transcend knowledge ; the strange star between the sky and the water of the first cosmos : this be man 's divinity . 

 and some man be not divine at all . they have only faculty . they be slave , or they should be slave . 

 but many a man have his own spark of divinity , and have it quench , blow out by the wind of force or grind out of he by machine . 

 and when the spirit and the blood in man begin to go asunder , bring the great death , most star die out . 

 only the man of a great star , a great divinity , can bring the opposite together again , in a new unison . 

 and this be Ram n , and this be his great effort : to bring the great opposite into contact and into unison again . and this be the god - power in man . by this power you shall know the god in man . by none other . 

 Ram n be a man as the least of his peon be a man , with the beat heart and the secret loin and the lip close on the same secret of manhood . and he be human as Kate be human , with the same yearning of the spirit , for pure knowledge and communion , the soul in the greatness of its comprehending . 

 but only he have that starry power for bring together the two great human impulse to a point of fusion , for be the bird between the vast wing of the dual - create power to which man have access and in which man have his being . the Morning Star , between the breath of dawn and the deep of the dark . 

 man have try to murder he with knife . Carlota would have murder he with her spirit . each half separately want to commit the murder of he . 

 but he keep himself beyond . he be the live Quetzalcoatl , and the tiny sparkle of a star be rise in his own man , in his own woman . 

 the star between the two wing of power : that alone be divinity in a man , and final manhood . 

 Kate have a message from Cipriano to say he be come out to stay in the Villa Aragon . the Villa Aragon be the chief house on the lake , in small but rather beautiful ground with tuft of palm - tree and heavy hedge of jasmine , a garden keep always green by constant watering . the house be build rather like a little castle , absurd , yet its deep , spacious veranda opening on to the slope and knoll of the tree - cluster garden , above the lake , be pleasant .

 the Quetzalcoatl movement have spread in the country , but sinisterly . the Archbishop have declare against it , Ram n and Cipriano and their adherent be excommunicate . an attempt have be make to assassinate Montes .

Ram n labour ceaselessly . Cipriano appear in unexpected flash , in unexpected place . he manage to rouse the most discontent States , Vera Cruz , Tamaulipas , Yucatan , to a sort of religious frenzy . strange baptism take place in the sea , and a scarlet and black tower of Huitzilopochtli rise along the shore .

Kate be frightened , and she feel curiously hollow . even the queer , new , flash triumph and the sense of a new thing on the face of the earth could not quite save she . she belong too much to the old world of Europe , she could not , could not make herself over so quickly . but she feel that if she could go back to Ireland , and let her life and her body pause for a time , then she could come back and take her share . 

 for it be not her spirit alone which be change , it be her body , and the constitution of her very blood . she could feel it , the terrible katabolism and metabolism in her blood , change she even as a creature , change she to another creature .

 the strange , heavy , positive passivity . for the first time in her life she feel absolutely at rest . and talk , and think , have become trivial , superficial to she : as the ripple on the surface of the lake be as nothing , to the creature that live away below in the unwavere deep .

Chiefly , of the curious irritant quality of talk . and this he avoid . curious as it may seem , he make she aware of her own desire for frictional , irritant sensation . she realize how all her old love have be frictional , charge with the fire of irritation and the spasm of frictional voluptuousness . 

 Cipriano , curiously , by refuse to share any of this with she , make it become external to she . her strange seething feminine will and desire subside in she and sweep away , leave her soft and powerfully potent , like the hot spring of water that gush up , so noiseless , so soft , yet so powerful , with a sort of secret potency . 

 she realize , almost with wonder , the death in she of the Aphrodite of the foam : the seething , frictional , ecstatic Aphrodite . by a swift dark instinct , Cipriano draw away from this in she . when , in their love , it come back on she , the seethe electric female ecstasy , which know such spasm of delirium , he recoil from she . it be what she use to call she ' satisfaction . ' she have love Joachim for this , that again , and again , and again he could give she this orgiastic ' satisfaction ' , in spasm that make her cry aloud .

' what happen be dark and untellable . so different from the beak - like friction of Aphrodite of the foam , the friction which flare out in circle of phosphorescent ecstasy , to the last wild spasm which utter the involuntary cry , like a death - cry , the final love - cry . this she have know , and know to the end , with Joachim . and now this too be remove from she . what she have with Cipriano be curiously beyond her know : so deep and hot and flow , as it be subterranean . she have to yield before it . she could not grip it into one final spasm of white ecstasy which be like sheer know .

 now she find herself accept he finally and forever as the stranger in whose presence she live . it be his impersonal presence which envelop she . she live in his aura , and he , she know , live in her , with nothing say , and no personal or spiritual intimacy whatever . a mindless communion of the blood .

 he have to leave early one morning for Mexico City . the dawn come perfect and clear . the sun be not yet on the lake , but it catch the mountain beyond Tuliapan , and they shine magically distinct , as if some magic light be focusse on they . the green furrow of the mountain - side be as if in her own hand . two white gull , fly , suddenly get the light , and glitter . but the full , soft , noiseless dun lake be pallid , unlit .

 the Sons of the morning ! the column of blood ! a Red Indian . she look at he in wonder , as he move pure red and luminous far into the lake , unconscious . as if on fire ! 

 the Sons of the morning ! she let her effort at know slip away from her once more , and remain without effort , within the communion . 

 it be his race , too . she have notice before how the native shine pure red when morning or evening light catch they , rather level . as fire they stand in the water . the Red Indian .

 he be go , and for a while she feel the old nostalgia for his presence . not for he , exactly . not even to see he or touch he or speak to he . only to feel he about . 

 then quickly she recover . she adjust herself to the presence he leave behind with she . as soon as he have really go , and the act of go be over , his presence come back to she . 

 she walk a little while by the shore , beyond the breakwater wall . she love to be alone : a great deal alone , with a garden and the lake and the morning . 

 ' I be like Teresa , really , ' she say to herself . 

 suddenly before she she see a long , dark soft rope , lie over a pale boulder . but her soul be softly alert , at once . it be a snake , with a subtle pattern along its soft dark back , lie there over a big stone , with its head sink down to earth .

 and then what ! to sit in a London drawing - room , and add another to all the grimalkin ? to let the peculiar grimalkin - grimace come on her face , the most weird grimalkin - twang come into her voice ? horror ! of all the horror , perhaps the grimalkin woman , her contemporary , be the most repellent to she . even the horrid old tom - cat man of the civilized roof gutter , do not fill she with such sickly dread . 

 ' no ! ' she say to herself . ' my ego and my individuality be not worth that ghastly price . I would well abandon some of my ego , and sink some of my individuality , rather than go like that . ' 

 after all , when Cipriano touch she caressively , all her body flower . that be the great sex , that could fill all the world with lustre , and which she dare not think about , its power be so much great than her own will . but on the other hand when she spread the wing of her own ego , and send forth her own spirit , the world could look very wonderful to she , when she be alone . but after a while , the wonder fade , and a sort of jealous emptiness set in . 

 ' I must have both , ' she say to herself . ' I must not recoil against Cipriano and Ram n , they make my blood blossom in my body . I say they be limited . but then one must be limit . if one try to be unlimited , one become horrible . without Cipriano to touch I and limit I and submerge my will , I shall become a horrible , elderly female . I ought to want to be limit . I ought to be glad if a man will limit I with a strong will and a warm touch . because what I call my greatness , and the vastness of the Lord behind I , let I fall through a hollow floor of nothingness , once there be no man 's hand there , to hold I warm and limited . ah yes ! rather than become elderly and a bit grisly , I will make my submission ; as far as I need , and no far . ' 

 she call a man - servant , and set off down the lake in a row - boat . it be a very lovely November morning , the world have not yet go dry again . in the sharp fold of the steep mountain slope to the north - east , the shadow be pure corn - flower blue . below be the linger delicacy of green , already dry . the lake be full still , but subside , and the water - hyacinth have drift away . bird fly low in the stillness . it be very full and still , in the strong , hot light . some maize - field show sere stubble , but the palo - blanco flower be out , and the mesquite bush be frail green , and there be waft of perfume from the little yellow flower - ball , like cassia . 

 ' why should I go away ! ' say Kate . ' why should I see the bus on the mud of Piccadilly , on Christmas Eve , and the crowd of people on the wet pavement , under the big shop like great cave of light ? I may as well stay here , where my soul be less dreary . I shall have to tell Ram n I be sorry for the thing I say . I will not   carp at they . after all , there be another kind of vastness here , with the sound of drum , and the cry of Quetzalcoatl . ' 

 already she could see the yellow and reddish , tower - like upper story of Jamiltepec , and the rich , deep fall of magenta bougainvillea , from the high wall , with the pale spraying of plumbago flower , and many loose creamy - colour rose . 

 ' Están tocando ! ' say her boatman quietly , look up at she with dark , pregnant eye . 

 he have hear already the sound of the light drum at Jamiltepec . the boat row softly : and there come a sound of a man 's voice singing in the morning . 

 her boatman lift an oar , as a signal to the house . and as the boat round the curve into the basin , a man - servant in white clothe come run down to the little jetty . in the changeless sunshine be a scent , perhaps of datura and of rose , and an eternal mexican silence , which the noise of the drum , and the voice of singing , do not disturb . 

 ' be Don Cipriano here ? ' ask Kate . 

 ' está ! ' murmur the man , with a slight motion towards Ram n 's balcony , whence the singing come . ' shall I say you have come ? ' 

 he do not lift his voice above the murmur . 

 ' no ! ' say Kate . ' I shall sit here in the garden a while , before I come up . ' 

 ' then I will leave open the door , ' say the man , ' and you can come up when you will . ' 

 Kate sit on a seat under a big tree . a creep plant , with great snake - like cord , and big sulphur - and - brown trumpet flower , hang above . she listen to the singing . it be Ram n teach one of the singer . 

 Ram n have not a very good voice . he sing quietly , as if to the inner air , with very beautiful , simple expression . but Kate could not catch the word . 

 ' ya ? ' say Ram n , when he have finish . 

 ' ya , Patr n ! ' say the man , the singer . 

 and he begin , in his strong , pure voice that catch at the very bowel , to sing another of the Hymns . 

 

 ' my way be not thy way , and thine be not mine . 
 but come , before we part 
 let we separately go to the Morning Star , 
 and meet there . 

 I do not point you to my road , nor yet 
 call : " oh come ! " 
 but the Star be the same for both of we , 
 Winsome . 

 the good ghost of I go down the distance 
 to the Holy Ghost . 
 oh you , in the tent of the cloven flame 
 meet I , you I like most . 

 each man his own way forever , but towards 
 the hoverer between ; 
 who open his flame like a tent - flap , 
 as we slip in unseen . 

 a man can not tread like a woman , 
 nor a woman step out like a man . 
 the ghost of each through the leaf of shadow 
 Moves as it can . 

 but the Morning Star and the Evening Star 
 Pitch tent of flame 
 where we foregather like gypsy , none know 
 how the other come . 

 I ask for nothing except to slip 
 in the tent of the Holy Ghost 
 and be there in the house of the cloven flame , 
 Guest of the Host . 

 be with I there , my woman , 
 be bodily there . 
 then let the flame wrap round we 
 like a snare . 

 be there along with I , o man ! 
 reach across the hearth , 
 and laugh with I while the woman rest 
 for all we be worth . ' 

 

 the man have sing this hymn over several time , halting and forget , his pure , burn voice falter out ; then the low , rather husky voice of Ram n , with a subtler intensity , come in , as if hear from the centre of a shell ; then again the sudden rip sound of the true singer 's tenor , go like a flame through the blood . 

 her mozo , a man - servant , have follow she into the garden , and sit at a distance on his heel , under a tree , with his back to the trunk , like a crouch shadow clothe in white . his toe spread dark and hard , in his open huarache , and the black braid of his hat - string hang against his dark cheek . for the rest he be pure white , the white cotton tight on his thigh . 

 when the singing have finish above , and the drum be silent , and even the voice speak in low tone be silent , her mozo look up at Kate , with his black hat - string dangle at his chin , his black eye shin , and a timid sort of smile on his face . 

 ' Está muy bien , Patrona ? ' he say shyly . ' it be good , be not   it , Mistress ? ' 

 ' it be very good , ' she reply , with the infallible echo . but there be conflict feeling in her breast , and the man know it . 

 he look so young , when he smile that gay , shy , excited little smile . something of the eternal child in he . but a child that could harden in an instant into a savage man , revengeful and brutal . and a man always fully sex - alive , for the moment innocent in the fulness of sex , not in the absence . and Kate think to herself , as she have think before , that there be more way than one of ' become again as a little child . ' 

 but the man have a sharp , watchful look in the corner of his eye : to see if she be feel some covert hostility . he want she to acquiesce in the hymn , in the drum , in the whole mood . like a child he want she to acquiesce . but if she be go to be hostile , he would be quick to be first in the hostility . her hostile judgment would make a pure enemy of he . 

 ah , all man be alike ! 

 at that moment the man stand up , with soft suddenness , and she hear Cipriano 's voice from the balcony above : 

 ' what be it , Lupe ? ' 

 ' Está la Patrona , ' answer the servant . 

 Kate rise to her foot and look up . she see the head and the naked shoulder of Cipriano above the parapet of the balcony . 

 ' I will come up , ' she say . 

 and slowly she go through the great iron gate into the passage - way . Lupe , follow , bolt the door behind she . 

 on the terrace above she find Ram n and Cipriano both with their upper body naked , wait for she in silence . she be embarrassed . 

 ' I wait to hear the new hymn , ' she say . 

 ' and how do it seem to you ? ' say Ram n , in Spanish . 

 ' I like it , ' she say . 

 ' let we sit down , ' say Ram n , still in Spanish . he and she sit in the cane rocking - chair : Cipriano stand by the wall of the terrace . 

 she have come to make a sort of submission : to say she do not   want to go away . but find they both in the thick of their Quetzalcoatl mood , with their manly breast uncover , she be not very eager to begin . they make she feel like an intruder . she do not pause to realize that she be one . 

 ' we do not   meet in your Morning Star , apparently , do we ? ' she say , mocking , but with a slight quaver . 

 a deep silence seem suddenly to hold the two man . 

 ' and I suppose a woman be really de trop , even there , when two man be together . ' 

 but she falter a bit in the saying . Cipriano , she know , be baffle and sting when she taunt he . 

 Ram n answer she , with the gentleness that could come straight out of his heart : but still in Spanish : 

 ' why , Cousin , what be it ? ' 

 her lip quiver , as she suddenly say : 

 ' I do not   really want to go away from you . ' 

 Ram n look swiftly at Cipriano , then say : 

 ' I know you do not . ' 

 but the gentle protective tone of his voice only make Kate rebel again . she brim over with sudden tear , cry : 

 ' you do not   really want I . ' 

 ' yes , I want you ! - Verdad ! Verdad ! ' exclaim Cipriano , in his low , secret , almost mutter voice . 

 and even amid her tear , Kate be think to herself : what a fraud I be ! I know all the time it be I who do not   altogether want they . I want myself to myself . but I can fool they so that they shall not   find out . 

 for she hear the hot , phallic passion in Cipriano 's voice . 

 then come the voice of Ram n , like a chill : 

 ' it be you who do not   want , ' he say , in English this time . ' you need not   commit yourself to we . listen to your own good desire . ' 

 ' and if it tell I to go away ? ' she flash , defiant through the end of her tear . 

 ' then go ! oh certainly go ! ' 

 suddenly her tear come afresh . 

 ' I know you do not   really want I , ' she weep . 

 then Cipriano 's voice say , with a hot , furtive softness of persuasion : 

 ' you be not his ! he would not tell you ! ' 

 ' that be very true , ' say Ram n. ' do not   listen to I ! ' 

 he speak in Spanish . and Kate glance up sharply through her tear , to see he go quietly , but swiftly , away . 

 she wipe her face , suddenly calm . then she look with wet eye at Cipriano . he be stand erect and alert , like a little fighting male , and his eye glow black and uncannily as he meet her wet , limpid glance . 

 yes , she be a bit afraid of he too , with his inhuman black eye . 

 ' you do not   want I to go , do you ? ' she plead . 

 a slow , almost foolish smile come over his face , and his body be slightly convulse . then come his soft - tongue indian speech , as if all his mouth be soft , say in Spanish , but with the ' r ' sound almost lose : 

 ' Yo ! Yo ! ' - his eyebrow lift with queer mock surprise , and a little convulsion go through his body again . ' te quiero mucho ! mucho te quiero ! mucho ! mucho ! I like you very much ! very much ! ' 

 it sound so soft , so soft - tongue , of the soft , wet , hot blood , that she shiver a little . 

 ' you will not   let I go ! ' she say to he .
